##

MAR 1:1 Leya kweshcha shundǝ kǝ ɗar Yǝso kǝrǝsti hweya Fara.
MAR 1:2 Nda i yarandǝ tapǝnaa Ishaya hi tǝ ndatwa: "Ni thlǝn lǝ thlǝnda mban le na tahsandǝ mbanɗeku ɗi.
MAR 1:3 Ɓurata nifǝ le naka atfata hur loktara, le naka ndatwa tahsan mbanda lǝ Mwanda ɗi kǝ pupwenangnguni mbachikǝn'en hi."
MAR 1:4 Ɓak Yohanna nakna ɓasa hur loktarǝ tǝ ndatwa: "Chikawuni kǝtǝrǝnhi kǝ sangfichǝ Baptisma kǝ kalang fichǝ ɓǝɓichitfechi'enhi."
MAR 1:5 Nat nofchi Yahudiya tǝ Urshelima ɗǝknda ɓǝɗ'en tǝrkǝndǝhi saǝn baptisma kanda a suhwaɗ Urdun.
MAR 1:6 Yohanna njela'en pom ngelupa kǝnaǝn mumi'en tǝ poma, ɗǝsǝmtǝ'en mbecha tǝ ɗecha.
MAR 1:7 Ndakǝnwa yuna ɓata ɗiffitǝna le nak mwanchin mǝ njang chika sahǝt pahǝmchi'en sǝkwisi kǝ koppihi kǝ kwasayihiwa.
MAR 1:8 Saayi Baptisma kuni tǝ ama paɗ nakna sǝt ikǝn tǝ Chiɗchiɗ chit Shemeɗa.
MAR 1:9 Hanmunchiniyu ɓak Yǝso thlata Nazarat a thlet hǝmǝt Galili. Yohanna saǝn baptisma a suhwaɗ Urdun.
MAR 1:10 Nak Yǝso cheta kisha hur ama chatkichuyu nakǝn in'afshi hi ɓak Shemeɗa Fara hai kǝ ɗar indi'en nda ngungwiɗnga.
MAR 1:11 Sǝkkǝ nofchǝ ɓurata a afshi tǝ ndatwa: "Sokǝn naka hwe'engna le yahti paɗ lela sǝkti mbǝnkǝnfa."
MAR 1:12 Chatkichuyu pǝkkǝ Shemeɗa Farǝ ndǝ kǝ hur loktara.
MAR 1:13 Munɗǝ kumchit fwaɗa Sheɗanna kǝkaɗanda a hur loktara. Mǝla hur loktara tǝ ɗǝ hǝrǝmcha nak mala'ika Fara kǝssandǝsi.
MAR 1:14 Ɗiffitǝkǝn kǝsang fichǝ Yohanna, ɓak Yǝso kǝ hachahai Galili nakna ɓasǝ kweshcha shunda Fara.
MAR 1:15 Ndakǝnwa: "Ɓeɗ hanmunchǝkǝn nduk. Fara yehsǝ cheɗanda kuni wa kutur nakǝn. Chikawuni kǝ tǝrǝnhi, fǝram kit kǝ kwescha shunda Fara."
MAR 1:16 Nak Yǝso ɓǝrtǝhi tǝ mi suhwaɗ Galili, nakǝn Siman tǝ Andarawus hwanman Siman kanda muh langtanganga kǝthlǝm fa tumchǝ naknda.
MAR 1:17 Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Kuramnji ni sandǝkuni kǝfa ɓat tǝ nofcha mbǝɗengna."
MAR 1:18 Chatkichuyu malangndǝ tum tincha kurǝkǝndǝndǝ.
MAR 1:19 Nak Yǝso witǝ kǝ ɓan, nakǝn Yakubu hweeya Zabadi tǝ Yohanna hwanmankǝn a hur kommbawal, kanda tahsandǝ langtangchengnanda.
MAR 1:20 Akǝn kanda malkǝndǝ shinnandǝhi, Zabadi hur kommbawal tǝ tahǝt fa torcheng nanda kurǝkǝndǝndi.
MAR 1:21 Ɓaknda Kafarnahum, ɓak farǝ yipta Yahudawecha, yimkǝ Yǝso ɓǝt humta Yahudawechihi, nakna sakanda kandǝhar.
MAR 1:22 Shekɗa ng i'ndǝ kandǝ tǝ witǝ sakiniyu, nda nifǝ sǝkkǝsi, nga nda malndǝmcha thlahɓǝt Musa wa.
MAR 1:23 Nifǝsa hur ɓǝt humta Yahudawechikǝnhi tǝ ɓǝɓi Shemeɗa fa hwakǝn,
MAR 1:24 ndakǝnwa: "Mǝ kǝmukǝ tǝ kani Yǝso lǝ Nazarat ta? Ɓaku kǝ tǝkangnǝ kanihiwa? A shini ndu wunnaku. Sokǝn naku Chiɗchiɗ le ɓaka mbǝɗa Fara."
MAR 1:25 "Ɓokang Yǝso ɓǝɓi shemeɗkǝnhi ndaǝnwa ngasu ɓa, chukisha fat'en!"
MAR 1:26 Ɓǝɓi shemeɗkǝn nakna saktanda mǝla hwata cheknakisha fat'en.
MAR 1:27 Pǝɗang ǝnatkǝn nofchǝkǝnfa sahangndǝ ndani witǝ mǝ leya? Yuwa sakandaɗi tǝ sǝktǝsiwa? Ndangna ɓǝɓi shemeɗchǝkǝnwa kǝ chendakish paɗ sǝkkǝndǝndi.
MAR 1:28 Kusheng i sǝt Yǝso yu sǝkkǝficha a hachahai Galili nat.
MAR 1:29 Ɗiffitǝ chendengnanda kisha ɓǝt humta Yahudawechihi, pǝɗang Yǝso tǝ Yakubu tǝ Yohanna kǝ hura'a nda Siman tǝ Andarawus.
MAR 1:30 Nak thlaɓǝr Siman hahchin hafat kakǝnnda, chatkichuyu ɓwa'angnda Yǝso.
MAR 1:31 Ɗǝk Yǝso ɓǝsndi kǝskǝn har'en thlaǝn, chat kǝnkǝna ɗaɗi nakna sǝt tor ɗǝsǝmta.
MAR 1:32 Ɗiffitǝ hǝmta farǝhi ngomang ndǝ haacha tǝ fa ɓǝɓi luwurcha,
MAR 1:33 Nofchi hur hǝmǝtkǝn ngomkǝnda kish kǝ mi hura'a,
MAR 1:34 Kǝnang Yǝso hachǝkǝnaɗi tǝ fa ɓǝɓi luwurcha, paɗ malawutǝ fa ɓǝɓi luwurchǝkǝn kǝ shuwunndǝwa kǝthlǝm shinndǝndi.
MAR 1:35 Thlaakǝna ɓingtǝ tung, mwee ɓǝt shumma kǝ ɓǝt nguɗuk ka hwanda.
MAR 1:36 Siman tǝ tahǝt nofchǝkǝn naknda katndi.
MAR 1:37 Mbǝsangnda, ndangndǝwa: "Chikawun mǝla kassa."
MAR 1:38 Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Tama hwanhǝmchi naka ɓan, kǝnni ɓasa pǝnniyu paɗ ndǝkǝn cheka ɓat tǝ nji."
MAR 1:39 Wu'yaǝn hachahai Galili nak na ɓasa ɓǝt humta Yahudawechihi nak na chandǝ ɓǝɓi luwurcha kish.
MAR 1:40 Ɓak nifǝ tǝ tarkwinda fa, kopkǝnhi nakna hwanandǝ tǝ ndatwa: "Ma yehnǝsi kǝnitǝna ɗaɗi."
MAR 1:41 Haɗaǝn Yǝso fa, tǝka'ǝn harfa, ndakǝnwa: "Yehisi kǝnu ɗaɗi."
MAR 1:42 Chat kichuyu yimkǝ tarkwiinkǝnhi kǝnkǝnaɗi.
MAR 1:43 Ndang Yǝso wa pǝɗu kǝ mbwa'ana nifǝwa,
MAR 1:44 "Mbwa'ana chikawunwa, pǝɗu ɗu cheɗan faɗǝ ku Pǝrist kǝ fǝrnǝ i la fǝrtǝ ficha ma kǝnafichǝ nifa ɗaɗi nda ǝnnǝnǝ sakandǝ Musa kuni har yu, kǝ sokka ǝnnat sǝndǝwa kinnaɗi."
MAR 1:45 Pǝɗakǝn nakna mbwa'anda nofcha nakna fanandǝ shuwunkǝnhi ka'ǝn, kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn Yǝso mbǝla'utǝ kalǝfathi a thlet hwanhǝmchǝkǝnwa. Pǝndakǝn kǝ ɓǝt ngunduk, paɗ nak nofcha ɓata mbǝɗ'en chika tǝ teni.
MAR 2:1 Ɗiffitǝ hwanmunchǝkǝn ɗimek, ngǝrang Yǝso in kǝ Kafarnahum, sǝkkǝ nofchǝwa mǝlahuri.
MAR 2:2 Ɓak nofchǝ oi, paɗ mwa'u ɓǝtsǝwa taa kǝ mikǝnnda, mǝlan paɗ nakna ɓasa pathla Fara kanda.
MAR 2:3 Nɗǝkǝn ɓat nofcha mɓǝɗ'en tǝ tǝraɗ, nofchǝ fwaɗa tǝrkǝndi.
MAR 2:4 Mbǝsundǝ ɓǝt kǝ thlǝmatkǝn ndukwa, kǝthlǝm yakat nofcha tǝrkǝndǝ tǝ ɗar kǝtǝnkǝn, pahangndǝhi fǝrkǝndǝnda hai kǝ mbanitǝ Yǝso a ɗar ɓǝt hunat'en.
MAR 2:5 Nak Yǝso fǝr kitchiɗengnandǝhi, ndangna le sakaɗiyuwa: "Hweya kalu fichǝ ɓǝɓifechekuhi."
MAR 2:6 Malɗǝmchi fǝrkǝ kit kǝ kussa Musa yu nak ɗǝɗassa mbǝnniyu naknda yarandǝhi hur hanndǝkikecheng nanda.
MAR 2:7 "Kǝthlǝm mi nat nifiya shundǝ kichuyu? Mbwitǝ i nguchik keeke kǝ ɓǝɗa Fara, wunla kalang ɓǝɓichitfata nifǝhi manga Faruwa?"
MAR 2:8 Tangtang neɗ Yǝso hi hur shemeɗ'en i nannda yara, ndangna kandǝwa: "Kǝthlǝm mi natuni yarǝ kichuyu hur hanndǝkikechengnuni?
MAR 2:9 Len nak pa'pa i? kǝ ndangna le sakaɗiyuwa kalufichi ɓǝɓifandekuhiwa ndu kǝndangnǝwa thla'u tǝru ɓǝt hunaɗeku kǝ wii nǝ witekuwa?
MAR 2:10 Kǝthlǝm kǝsǝnuniwa alchita hweya nifǝsi kǝ kalǝn ɓǝɓifathi a hur kishi'iya, ndangna le sakaɗǝ tǝkǝnwa:
MAR 2:11 "Ndukiwa thla'u tǝru ɗǝngleku kǝ pǝɗana ɗaɗi kǝ hure'eku."
MAR 2:12 Thlaakǝn tukwas tǝrkǝn ndǝnglǝ'en cheknakissha hur hurǝkǝn, ɓanitǝ chikawuni, shekndang indǝ kanda naknda mwanandǝ Fara, ndangndǝwa: "Tamwuma nat ǝn kicheyawa."
MAR 2:13 Ngǝrkǝn chetakish paɗ kǝ mi hawurta, ɓak ngom nofcha ɓǝɗ'en, paɗ sakangnakandǝ har.
MAR 2:14 Nakna mbǝrtǝhi, nakǝn Lawi hweya Halfa ɗas ɓǝt thlǝt chamta, ndaǝnwa: "Kurunji" thlaakǝn kurukǝnndi.
MAR 2:15 Nak Yǝso sǝm'ǝna a hurhura'a Lawi tǝ fa thlǝt chamcha tǝ fa ɓǝɓichitfata, tǝ kimshechi'en kǝthlǝm nofchǝ ka'ǝn kurukǝndi.
MAR 2:16 Kǝ nat malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ ndelwercha Musa ɗi fichile naka Farisiyawecha, Yǝso mǝla sǝm'ǝn tǝ fa ɓǝɓifecha, tǝ fa thlǝt chamcha, ndangnda kimshechi'enwa kǝthlǝm mi natna sǝm'ǝn tǝ fa thlǝt chamcha paɗ tǝ fa ɓǝɓifecha?
MAR 2:17 Kǝ sǝktǝ Yǝso kandǝ kichuyu, ndangna kandǝwa: "Nofchi nak ngwalngwal hi, kǝmawu ǝn kandǝ tǝ lǝ fǝr hanɓǝɓaawa, fichile nak hahchin na kanndi. Ɓuwi kǝthlǝm kǝ i fichile fǝrkǝ kitwa, ɓaki kǝthlǝm fa ɓǝɓichitfata".
MAR 2:18 Nakǝnya kimshecha Yohanna tǝ Farisiyawecha kanda cherǝ ama. Ɓak nofcha mbǝɗa Yǝso sahangndǝwa: "Kǝthlǝm mi nat kimshecha Yohanna tǝ i Farisiyawecha cherǝ ama paɗ ichiwa kanda cherǝ amwa?
MAR 2:19 Ngǝmang Yǝso wa, tǝkǝnǝnat sǝmat pera nata thlǝmat shikechikǝn kǝnnda cherǝ ama? Ngu nat kichuwa, ma mwe sǝmat perǝkǝn tǝ kandǝwa.
MAR 2:20 Hanmunchǝkǝna ɓata le nat ficha tǝrandǝ sǝmat perǝkǝna thlǝmannda farinǝyu nanda cherǝ ama.
MAR 2:21 Nifǝsi na ɓumandǝ yuwa njela'a tǝ ɗohǝt njelaawa kǝthlem ma shiɗ kichu na ɗohǝt njelǝkǝna thlahtaɗi ka'ǝn.
MAR 2:22 Nifǝsi na thlǝr yuwa am innabi kǝ hur ɗohǝt kupat wa, kǝthlǝm nan fǝlta ɗi paɗ nu kuɓat i hurkǝnyu tǝ kupatkǝn nat. Kǝthlǝm ɗǝkǝn naku thlǝr yuwa am innabi kǝ hur yuwa kupata.
MAR 2:23 Farǝyipta nak Yǝso ɓǝrtǝhi tǝ hur hitǝ hwarma, nak kimshechi'ena ɓwerǝt hwarǝm kǝnna mi.
MAR 2:24 Ndang Farisiyawechǝwa: "Nu, kǝthlǝm mi nannda sǝt i ngǝmawuchit kustǝkǝn kǝ sǝficha farǝ yipta?"
MAR 2:25 Ngǝmaǝn kandǝwa: "Tamwuni changngandǝwowa, i sǝt Dauda yahkǝn ɗǝsǝmta kǝthlǝm mitafi'en, kandang tǝ nofchi'en fichile naka thlǝmatkǝnwa?
MAR 2:26 Yim kǝna kǝtǝn mwanandǝ Fara a thlahɓǝɗi nat Abiyata kǝ kapat Pǝrist, chiikǝn njohmi tahsandǝ fichihi kǝthlǝm kapat Pǝrist le kamuchiksi kǝ chii nifǝ somǝnwa, kapat Pǝrist ndak kamkǝsi kǝ chi'ǝn. Paɗ fǝrangna fichile naka thlǝmatkǝn yu.
MAR 2:27 "Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa, sǝk fichǝ Farǝyipta Yahudawecha kǝthlǝm nifa, su fichǝ nifa kǝthlǝm Farǝyiptǝwa."
MAR 2:28 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, Hweya Nifǝ mǝlan naka Lǝmwanda nat tǝ i Farǝyipta."
MAR 3:1 Farǝ le yimkǝ Yǝso ɓǝt humta Yahudawechihi, nakǝn nifa le sat har'enaɗi.
MAR 3:2 Nak nofcha kǝlandǝ ndu na Yǝso kǝnandaɗaɗi farǝ yipta kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsndǝ i nannda tǝramiyafa
MAR 3:3 Ndang Yǝso le sat har'ennaɗiyuwa: "Thla'u thlaru mbanitǝ nofcha."
MAR 3:4 Sahang Yǝso kanda: "Mǝ mbutǝ kustǝkǝn kǝsǝficha Farǝ Yipta? kafatwa ndu ɓǝɓichitfatwa, kǝ hǝrkang fichǝ shisshingtǝwa ndu kǝ ɓǝlang fichǝwa?" ngaskǝndǝ shetǝta.
MAR 3:5 Kǝlang Yǝso kandǝ tǝ sǝɓ hur ka'ǝn kǝthlǝm kwaakwaachit hanndǝkikechengnanda. Ndaǝnwa: "pupwanan harekuhi." Pupwanaǝn hi kǝnkǝnaɗi.
MAR 3:6 Chek Farisiyawecha tǝ wesha kǝ ɓǝnda nofcha Hiridus kǝthlǝm kǝ tahsangndǝ mbayihi nannda ɓǝlandǝ Yǝso.
MAR 3:7 Thlaakǝ Yǝso tǝ kimshechi'en kǝmi hawurta, kurǝkǝ nofchǝ ndǝ oi thlata Galili nat tǝ nofcha Yahudiya,
MAR 3:8 sǝkkǝndǝ ichi nat nanna sǝtta, yakat nofchǝ ka'ǝn ɓaknda mbǝɗ'en, thlata Urshelima, Edom tǝ hachahai Urdun taa kǝ Taya tǝ Sidon.
MAR 3:9 Kǝthlǝm rahanda njekthlǝ-njekthlǝchitta nofchihar, ndangna kimshechi'enwa ɗama kǝlam han kommbawal har ǝrta, kǝthlǝm terǝ nofcha mǝninda tǝkaharfa.
MAR 3:10 Kǝnannɗǝ nofcha ɗaɗi oi, nat fa hafecha nangnda ɓahtǝ nduk kǝthlǝm kǝ mbunangndǝharfa.
MAR 3:11 Chika kwat nat ɓǝɓi shemechikǝn ndi chat kopkǝndǝhi kanda kukwara ndangndǝwa: "Sokǝn naka hweya Fara."
MAR 3:12 Tiiɗaǝn thlǝmechengnanda kǝ mbwa'anda nifǝ ndu wunnakǝnwa.
MAR 3:13 Tǝrkǝna ɗargwiya akǝn fichile yahtǝn ɓaknda ɓǝsndi
MAR 3:14 Taɗkǝn nofchǝ kum ngǝrǝnsǝ chap akǝn kandǝwa kimshechi'en fichile na nat tǝndi, ɓahnan la thlǝnkanda kǝ ɗǝnda ɓasa.
MAR 3:15 Paɗ nuni mbǝs alchit chandǝ ɓǝɓi luwurcha kish.
MAR 3:16 Fichile taɗtǝn kum ngǝrǝnsǝ chap yu, Saminu (le ɗǝfandǝnwa Bitrus),
MAR 3:17 Yakubu hweya Zabadi tǝ Yohanna hwanmankǝn (le ɗǝfandǝn paɗwa Buwanarjis sakǝtkǝnwa hwecha ɓok era"),
MAR 3:18 Andarawus, tǝ Saminu, tǝ Filibus, tǝ Bartamalawus, tǝ Matiyu, tǝ Toma, tǝ Yakubu hweya Halfa, tǝ Taddawus, tǝ Saminu lǝ Kan'anata.
MAR 3:19 Tǝ Yahuda Iskariyoti le hi'yang Yǝso ɗi.
MAR 3:20 Chat pǝɗak Yǝso huri, ngǝrkǝ nofcha ngomtǝ oi, mǝlan tǝ kimshechi'en ɓǝsundǝ har sǝm ndǝsǝmtǝwa.
MAR 3:21 Kǝ sǝktǝ nofchi'en ɗǝknda kǝsanda kǝthlǝm nofcha ndatwa: "Tǝraa luwurcha."
MAR 3:22 Malɗǝmchǝ fa sakandǝ ɗelwercha Musa ɗi, fichile ɓaka a Urshelima ndangndǝwa: "Kutur luwurchǝ naka fi'en paɗ tǝ alchita kutur luwurcha la rǝktǝn luwurcha kish."
MAR 3:23 Ak Yǝso kanda, shuwunkǝn tǝ kanda hur sakǝtkǝn, ndakǝnwa tǝkǝni nat sheɗanna ɓǝla kǝtandǝ sheɗanna kish?
MAR 3:24 Ma shek kuturichithi chap, kuturichitkǝn ngu soktǝwa.
MAR 3:25 Kichu paɗ ma shek huraahi chap hurǝkǝn ngu thlarǝwa.
MAR 3:26 Sheɗan ma thla'aɗa fat'enfa kǝssakǝnhi ngu ɓǝla thlarǝwa kǝthlǝm ndukwat'en ɓaka.
MAR 3:27 Kitchitkǝn nifǝsina ɓǝla yimta hura'a lǝ alchit kǝ herka'ǝnwa, manga tǝ kǝnaǝn lǝ alchitkǝnhi kana mbǝla herkandǝwa.
MAR 3:28 Kitchikǝn tǝni mbwa'anda kuni nat ɓǝɓifechi sǝt nofcha na ficha kalandakandǝhi tǝ chika wun njirfat sǝtnda,
MAR 3:29 Chika tǝ kichu le njirkǝ Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗa ngu ficha kalandǝhiwa nakna nat kǝla ɓǝɓichitfat kǝ pware.
MAR 3:30 Mbukǝ Yǝso kichu kǝthlǝm lǝ ndangndǝwa: "Ɓǝɓi shemeɗ'ensi."
MAR 3:31 Ɓak mankǝn tǝ hwanmanchikǝn thlarkǝnda kish, thlǝnkǝndǝwa kǝɓan.
MAR 3:32 Yakat nofchi tauranghiyu shuwunkǝndǝ tǝ ndi ndangndǝwa, yatu tǝ hwanmanchiwa kanda katsa kish yehndǝ sa natsa.
MAR 3:33 Ngǝmaǝn kandǝwa: "Wun yaa tǝ hwanmanchina?"
MAR 3:34 Tǝɓǝrkǝnhi tǝ ɓǝɗa fichile ɗas ɗas yu ndangnakandǝwa: "Nam kandǝya fichileya naka nda yaa tǝ hwanmanchina"
MAR 3:35 Nat le sǝk i yahtǝ Fara mǝlan na hwanyaa tǝ yaa.
MAR 4:1 Paɗ tǝrkaakǝ Yǝso sakandaɗa mi kapat hawurta ngomkǝ nofchǝ ka'ǝn, tǝrkǝna hur kommbawal sokkǝnhi kǝ hurkǝn, nofchǝ oi a mi chicheng hawurkǝn.
MAR 4:2 Nakna sakandakandǝhara a hur sakǝtkǝn tǝ ndatwa.
MAR 4:3 Sǝkama! chek lǝ huɗata kish ka hǝfta
MAR 4:4 Nakna weshǝ witǝkǝn, funǝ witǝkǝn hǝmkǝnda hai kǝ hur mbanda, ɓak hanɗishcha chathlanda.
MAR 4:5 Funǝ witǝkǝn paɗ hǝhatkǝnnda ɗar fufurta ɓǝɗi nguchit furtǝsǝ ɗiichin, tifkǝnda kish leɗleɗ, kǝthlǝm ngafurtǝsa ɗarkǝn ɗiichinwa,
MAR 4:6 Tǝkkǝ hwatfarǝhi, lifirkǝndaɗi kǝthlǝm nga thlorǝ'ensǝ ɗiichinwa, hwarkǝnaɗi.
MAR 4:7 Paɗ funǝ hǝhatkǝnda hur ndahcha, mwankǝnda paɗ njekthlang ndahchiyu ɓǝla'utǝ sǝt hwechafuwa.
MAR 4:8 Funǝ paɗ hǝhatkǝndahai kǝ hachahai ɗiichin mbulkǝn sǝkǝn hwechafa, funǝ kumchit mǝkkan, funǝ kumchit tehhweth, funǝ paɗ kumchit kum.
MAR 4:9 Ndak Yǝso wa: "Le nat thlǝmat sǝktǝ'ensi kǝ sǝkkǝn."
MAR 4:10 Nak Yǝso ichitkǝn, fichile nduk tǝndǝ tǝ kimshechi'en kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap, sahahndǝ sakǝt shuniniyu.
MAR 4:11 Ndangnakandǝwa: "kunang ngǝmaficha kunisi kǝ sǝnnuni i naka ɓuɓweeta hur mwanda Fara, fichile nguchika hurnuni, chikamǝ naki mbwa'anda kanda hur sakǝtkǝn.
MAR 4:12 Nanda kǝllathi kǝ kǝllathi chika kichu ngunda natwa, kǝ kandǝ thlǝmathi kǝ kat thlǝmathi chika kichu ngunda sǝktǝwa. Kǝthlǝm ma shiɗndǝ kichu nanda tǝɓǝrtǝhi ɓǝnda Fara kǝ kalang fichi ɓǝɓichitfechengnanda kandǝhi.
MAR 4:13 Ndangnakandǝwa, awi sǝnwuni sakǝt shuniniyuwa? Nakuni sǝn yakat sakchikǝnwa kǝnni?
MAR 4:14 Lǝ huɗaɗiyu hiftǝ shunda Fara.
MAR 4:15 Fichile hǝhatkahai kǝ hur mbandǝyu, kandang naka sakǝt fichile hǝftǝ fichǝ shuwunkǝna hanndǝkikechengnandǝyu, kǝ sǝktǝnda chat kichuyu ɓak sheɗanna thlandǝ kandǝhar.
MAR 4:16 Kichu paɗ hanwitǝ hǝftǝ ficha hur fufurtǝyu, kandang naka fichile sǝkkǝ shuwunkǝn thlǝkndǝ tǝ mbǝnfata.
MAR 4:17 A nakǝn sutǝ thlora hanndǝkikechengnanduwa, nga alchindengnandǝsuwa, ma yimnda hur ɓahtǝ kǝthlǝm shuniniyu chikndǝ hansarǝhi.
MAR 4:18 Funǝ paɗ kandang naka sakǝt fichile hǝhatka hur ndahchiyu, kandang sǝkkǝ shuwunkǝn,
MAR 4:19 paɗ ǝnat kishita tǝ kǝnecha tǝ yah icha kishita, yimkǝndǝsi njaǝn shuwunkǝnna kanda suwa kweshchaǝnwa.
MAR 4:20 Fichile hǝhtǝ ficha hur furtǝ ɗiichinyu kandang naka sakǝt fichile sǝkkǝ shuwunkǝn thlǝknda, sǝkndǝ torsi mbǝskǝndǝ chekǝtkǝn, funǝ kumchit mǝkkan, funǝ kumchit tehhweth, funǝ kumchitkum.
MAR 4:21 Ɗǝk Yǝso mban tǝ ndanda kanduwa: "Mǝlapakaa la ɓak fichǝ tǝ tikesha huri kǝthlǝm kǝ supwang fichǝ tǝ i'naftǝwa, manga kichuwa kǝ ɗǝffichǝhi kǝka ɓǝt hunatwa? le ɓatunitǝkǝn kǝthlǝm kǝ ɗǝffuni kǝ ɓǝɗi la ɗǝftǝfichǝwa?
MAR 4:22 Ənsǝnaka ɓuɓweetǝ nguchit ficha chandakishwa, ǝnsa supta nguchit ficha kwallandandǝwa.
MAR 4:23 Le nat thlǝmat sǝktǝensi kǝ sǝkkǝn!''
MAR 4:24 Paɗ ndangna kandǝwa, ɗǝffam i'ndǝsi, kǝ ɗar ǝnǝnǝ sǝktuniyu, somǝɗi kǝkaɗtusi, tǝ ndǝkǝn nat ficha kǝkaɗutǝsi.
MAR 4:25 Kǝthlǝm le natǝn'ensi, mǝlan nat ficha chekanda, le nguchitǝn'ensi paɗ chikale naka har'en na ficha thlandǝhar kǝ chekang ficha le natǝnsǝ'en.
MAR 4:26 Ndakǝn paɗwa: "Mwanda Fara nakǝn nda nifǝ weshkǝ witǝ'enna hachahaya.
MAR 4:27 Kǝ hunanhi kǝ thlaǝn tifkǝ witǝkǝnna kish, mwankǝn, sǝnutǝ ndu sǝkǝn kǝniwa.
MAR 4:28 Furtǝ tǝ i'ndǝ'en la ɓǝlaakǝn mwanandǝ hwarma paɗ kǝ ɓulǝn, sǝn hwechafa.
MAR 4:29 Ma nihiɗi hwasaǝn tǝ chelta, kǝthlǝm shee thlahɓǝt nǝhatǝ'en."
MAR 4:30 Ndakǝn paɗwa, nakma kǝkaɗandǝ mwanda Farǝ tǝ mi? Manga kichuwa witǝ sakǝtmi natma kǝkaɗandǝfa?
MAR 4:31 Nakǝn nda hwan musdad, le nak nguɗeh a hur ichi la hǝftǝficha hachahaya.
MAR 4:32 Chika tǝ kichu ma hǝffa ficha, nan mwanda kǝ mbǝranka tahǝt afchihi hur hitǝkǝnyu, njarkǝnhi ka'ǝn paɗ kana hanɗishcha sokta kaaftǝ'en.
MAR 4:33 Tǝ sakǝt shuwunchǝ ka'ǝn mbutǝ Yǝso shunda Fara, kǝ sǝrǝt sǝndengnanda.
MAR 4:34 Mbwa'autǝ shunda kanda nga tǝ sakǝtkǝnwowa, paɗ mamǝlan ichitkǝn, la mbwa'angna kimshechi'en chikami.
MAR 4:35 Farǝniyu sǝk farǝhufta, ndangna kimshechi'enwa: "Chamǝn hawurkǝn kǝ mi chicheng le taatǝyu."
MAR 4:36 Malkǝndǝ ngomnofchikǝn ɗiffi'in, pǝɗakndǝ tǝnda hur kommbawal ichitkǝn, paɗ kurǝkǝ tahchikǝn kanda.
MAR 4:37 Ndǝkǝn thlatǝ husomba tǝrǝnna ka'ǝn, nak rǝnnikǝna hǝhrandǝ kommbawal tǝkǝn, nak ama hasa hur kommbawal tǝkǝn nda nan nǝhata.
MAR 4:38 Yǝso paɗ mǝla hur kommbawal tǝkǝn a ɗar ɓǝt sokta mǝla saɓweni, nahnang kimshechi'en ndangndǝwa: "Malɗǝm, nǝma tǝktǝhi, kǝmmuwowa?"
MAR 4:39 Nahǝnkǝn, ɓokangna rǝnnikǝnhi, ndangna rah amkǝnwa: "Thlarruhi! kǝ ngasnǝ kǝmma!" Ndǝkǝn thlartǝ rǝnnikǝnhi shǝyyet.
MAR 4:40 Ndangna kimshchi'enwa: "Kǝthlǝm mǝ lechituni kakǝchiuyu? Paa kǝnakǝnya ngafǝrkit engnunisǝwowa?
MAR 4:41 Lechitndaɗǝ kaka'ǝn, ndangndandaniwa: "Witǝ nifǝmǝkicheya, rǝnna'a tǝ ama kanda fǝra mwanda?
MAR 5:1 Kǝ chandǝndǝ suhwaɗa kǝ hachahai Garasinawecha.
MAR 5:2 Kǝ tǝrtǝ Yǝso haya hur kommbawal, thlaakǝ nifa le nak tǝ ɓǝɓi shemeɗa, mbǝt shok tǝ'en mbǝt thlohmurcha ɓakna mbǝɗa Yǝso.
MAR 5:3 Nifǝkǝn kwatmurcha naka mbǝt shoktǝ'en, nifǝsi la mbǝllakkǝ kǝnnanduwa chika tǝ chalalochiwa.
MAR 5:4 Kǝthlǝm kurɓafichǝ kǝnnandǝ harchi'en tǝ sarǝchi'en tǝ chalalocha, nat tǝkichu ɗǝɗahaǝn chalalo tǝkkǝnnaɗa sarǝ'en. Nga nifǝsi tǝ alchitafa la mbǝlakkǝ kǝssandǝhiwa
MAR 5:5 Nda fiɗikta tǝ fara la nakna kwat murchǝ tǝ ɗar shohlacha kǝnna nata tit ka'ǝn, paɗ kǝnna ɓursa ndǝ fat'enaɗi tǝ ngwicha.
MAR 5:6 Kǝ natǝn Yǝso langnga, paakǝnsi tǝ rahta ɗǝkna hǝmta mbanitǝkǝn.
MAR 5:7 Hwakǝn tǝ alchit tǝ kapat ɓurata ndakǝnwa: "Mǝ natu sǝtsa nji, Yǝso hweya Fara le nak mwanchin? A humuɗi tǝ Fara, mǝ fǝrinǝ pwanchiuwa.
MAR 5:8 Mbukǝn kichu kǝthlǝm nda Yǝso wa: "Chukisshafata nifiya sokǝn ɓǝɓi shemeɗa."
MAR 5:9 Ndǝkǝn sahandǝ Yǝso wa: "Thlǝmmuwa kǝni?" A ngǝmmanwa: "Thlǝmnǝwa terchin, kǝthlǝm nakani oi."
MAR 5:10 A hwanaǝn Yǝso tǝ ndatwa: "Mǝ rǝkinǝ kanda mbǝnniyuwa."
MAR 5:11 Kǝthlǝm mbǝnniyu kapat chaɓa katuchisi naka hǝrimtǝ nduk tǝ shohlata.
MAR 5:12 Ɓǝɓi shemechiyu hwanangnduwa: "Kǝ malaǝn kanda kǝ yimnda hur katuchiyu."
MAR 5:13 A ngǝmmang na kandǝsi. Thlaakǝ ɓǝɓi shemechiyu chekndakish, yimkǝnnda hur katuchiyu, katuchiyu shee ndǝ aru kumchit chap (2,000), a rah kǝnda ka hǝhhatta hur hawurta, tǝkkǝndǝhi nat ahur ama.
MAR 5:14 Kǝ nat fa hǝrǝm katuchiyu kichu, rah kǝnda ka mbuta hǝmta, tǝ han hǝmchikǝn chek nofchakish ka nat i sǝkka.
MAR 5:15 Kǝ ɓatnda thlǝmmat Yǝso, nak ndǝ nifi nak soh tǝ ɓǝɓi shemecha fǝyu, ɗas tǝ njelecha fa mǝlla hur iɗi'en thlaakǝnnda lechik nda.
MAR 5:16 Fichile sǝt fichi ǝnnat kǝnna hwaniteng na ndǝyu, ndǝkǝn chekandǝndǝ ɗwaachik kǝnna kanda, i kǝs kǝ lǝ ɓǝɓi shemeɗiyu tǝ katuchiyu.
MAR 5:17 Thlaakǝ nofchikǝn hwanang ndǝ Yǝso kǝ mallǝn thlet hǝmteng nandǝ hi.
MAR 5:18 Kǝ nat Yǝso yimta kommbawal, nifi soh nak tǝ ɓǝɓi shemeɗi fiiyu hwanaǝn Yǝso wa nan ɗǝtkakǝn.
MAR 5:19 Nat tǝ kichu Yǝso ngǝmmawusuwa, ndaǝnwa ɗu huri kǝ mbǝɗa fahchuwa, kǝ mbwa'angna kanda witǝ pǝktat ichi sutǝ Lǝmwanda tǝ haɗi haɗandufa.
MAR 5:20 Thlaakǝ nifiyu pǝɗakǝn ɗǝk na nata mbu i sandǝ ficha Dikafolis sakkǝtkǝn hǝmchǝ kum witǝ pǝktat i chi sandǝ Yǝso. Uf nofcha pǝɗang ǝnnatkǝn kandǝ fa.
MAR 5:21 Yim kǝ Yǝso hur kommbawal chaǝn kǝ mi chicheng le, ɓak nofchi oiya kǝtwurangndǝhi mǝllan paɗ mǝlla mi chicheng hawurkǝn.
MAR 5:22 Yunǝsǝ ǝrta naka kapat nifa a mbǝt humta Yahudawechihi, thlǝmkǝn wa Yayirus. Kǝ natǝn Yǝso himkǝnhi mbanitǝkǝn,
MAR 5:23 nakna hwanandǝ ka'ǝn tǝ ndatwa: "Hwe'engna le nak nguɗeh, kǝ nuhhweya mǝlla miya murta, nja hwanuta tama kǝ ɗǝnna tǝkaharfa kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝnkaɗi."
MAR 5:24 Pǝɗak Yǝso tǝndi, kuwurkǝ nofchi kandǝ oi nangnda njekkathlǝndi.
MAR 5:25 Nuhnifǝssa mbǝnniyu hurak kum ngǝrǝnsǝ chap tǝ hafat thlǝrfwara fa.
MAR 5:26 A sheetǝ pwanchǝ oi a hara fafǝr hamɓǝɓecha, tuɓwaɗǝ i nak sǝ'en nat, chika tǝ kichu mbǝsutǝ sǝmmǝchitwa hafatkǝn nakǝn kǝmban kǝmban.
MAR 5:27 Kǝ sǝktǝn kussheng Yǝso, ɗǝkǝn tǝ ɗifitǝkǝn tǝ hur terǝ nofchiyu tǝka'ǝn hara njela'enfa.
MAR 5:28 Nak na yarǝwa: "Matǝkaɗi hara njela'enfa ni kǝndaɗi"
MAR 5:29 Chatkichuyu thlarkǝ thlǝrfwarkǝn hi, sǝkkǝnsa fat'enwa kinaɗi.
MAR 5:30 Chatkichuyu sǝkkǝ Yǝso cheɗ alchǝta kishsha fat'en, tǝɓɓǝrkǝn hi hur terǝ nofcha ndakǝnwa: "Wun tǝkang hara njele'engnǝ fa?"
MAR 5:31 Ngǝmang kimshechi'en wa: "Sa nat nofchǝ njekthlǝnjekthla, kanna ndatwa, wun tǝkukǝ harfa?"
MAR 5:32 Kǝlak Yǝso hi kǝthlǝm kǝ nan ndu wun tǝkang harfa.
MAR 5:33 Nuhiyu kǝ sǝntǝn i sǝka fat'en lechikǝn, ɓakna mbǝsndi kopkǝnhi mbwaǝn nat kitchit i'sǝka.
MAR 5:34 Ndaǝnwa: "Hwe'engna, fǝrkitchiɗeku kǝnuɗaɗi. Pǝɗu ngwalngwal, kinhafaɗekuɗi."
MAR 5:35 Mǝlla ɗar shunda chat ɓak funa mbǝɗa Yayirus kapat nifa ndangnduwa: "Hwe'eku teppa miri! mǝ sǝk natu ɓahandǝ Malɗǝm paɗi?"
MAR 5:36 Nattǝ kicchu Yǝso ɗufutǝ i'nda i nannda mbutuwa, ndangna kapat nifǝkǝnwa: "Mǝlechinuwa, so kǝn fǝru kit ndak."
MAR 5:37 Malautǝ, chikka wun kǝ kurǝn ndǝwa tǝrkǝn Bitrus tǝ Yakubu tǝ Yohanna hwamman Yakubu.
MAR 5:38 Kǝ saatǝnda hura'a Yayirus kapat nifa, nak Yǝso nofcha kanda tita funa hwata.
MAR 5:39 Yimkǝnna hurikǝn, ndangnakandǝwa: "Kǝthlǝm mǝ natuni tita kǝ nuni nata hwata? Nuhhwaniya mǝruwa, tǝnakasaɓweni."
MAR 5:40 Nangnda masanda masǝ njirfata. Chaǝn nofchi kisha hurikǝn nat, akǝn shin hwankǝn tǝ mankǝn, tǝ kimshechi'en fichile naka thlǝmmatkǝn, yimkǝnnda mbǝɗi nat nuhhwaniyu.
MAR 5:41 Kǝskǝn har'en ndaǝnwa: "Talita kumi." (sakǝtkǝnwa: "Hannuhhweya, ndakiwa thla'u").
MAR 5:42 Chat kichuyu thlaakǝ nuhhwaniyu nakna witahi. (hurat'en kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap). Nofchi naka mbǝnniyu pǝɗang ǝnatkǝnkandǝfa.
MAR 5:43 Kahang Yǝso thlǝmmachengnandǝ tǝ ndatwa mǝ sǝni nifǝ isǝkyawa, fǝramǝn ɗǝsǝmtǝ kǝ sǝmǝn.
MAR 6:1 Malkǝ Yǝso mbǝnnihiyu ngǝraǝn inna hǝmtǝ'en, kimshechi'en paɗ kuwurkǝndǝndi.
MAR 6:2 Kǝ saatǝ farǝ yipta, tǝrkaakǝn sakandaɗa mbǝt humta Yahudawechihi. Nofchǝ oi naka kathlǝmmata, paɗ pǝɗang ǝnnatkǝn kandǝfa nakndandatwa: "A'ai mbǝstǝ nifiya witǝ ichiya? witǝ sǝnmǝ fǝra ndǝ fichǝ kicheya? ɓatna nata sǝt ǝnat sheka i'nniya?
MAR 6:3 Leya nga mǝllan naka lǝ kukwat ichiyuwa, hweya Maryamu hwamman nda Yakubu, tǝ Yusufu, tǝ Yahuda, tǝ Siman? Hwamman chikǝn kǝ nishcha nga kandang ni thlǝmmat nǝm yawowa?" Cherkǝndǝndǝfa.
MAR 6:4 Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Tapǝna'a ɓahutǝ mwanduwa manga himtǝ'en tǝ hur hwammanchikǝn, tǝ hur hura'enwa."
MAR 6:5 Yǝso mbǝla'u tǝ sǝt tor ǝnnat fǝr sheka i'nda mbǝnniyuwa, kǝnaǝnfunaɗi ɗimek hur fichile nak hahchin tǝ ɗǝffa hara kanda in.
MAR 6:6 Pǝɗang ǝnatkǝnfa tǝ ɓah fǝr kitchǝɗengnanda. A wu'yaǝn han hǝmcha, nakna sakanda kandǝ har.
MAR 6:7 Akǝn kimshechi'en kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap, thlinkǝn kanndǝ chap chap, a fǝraǝn alchita kanda i rǝk ɓǝɓi shemecha.
MAR 6:8 Ɓokang na kandǝwa makunna pǝɗata mǝtǝriɗuni ǝn inwa, chika ɗǝsǝmta, chika yokta, chika ɗǝngla, chika hanɗǝɓǝlta kǝ hur kwandangchengnuniwa, sǝssal ndak natuni tǝrta.
MAR 6:9 Tǝ paɗ kǝ puni pahamcha, mǝ hummaɗuni njelaa chapwa.
MAR 6:10 Ndangna kandǝ paɗwa: "Uf huri'i yimtunisi, kǝ sokkuni mbǝnniyu kǝ farinatuni thlata.
MAR 6:11 Uf mbǝɗi cher tǝ ndǝ kuni paɗ kawundǝ thlǝmmata kuniwa, manuni pǝɗata, kǝ tǝppanguni tǝnnayiɗa sarǝchengnuni kǝthlǝm kǝ sokka ǝnnat sinnda ɗar inndengnanda."
MAR 6:12 Pǝɗangda nataɓasanda nofchisi tǝ ndatwa kǝtǝrndǝhi kǝ malangndǝ ɓǝɓichitfechengnanda.
MAR 6:13 A chang ndǝ ɓǝɓi shemechakish oi, pa'angndǝ fiɗɗetafichile nak hahchin oi kǝnkǝnndaɗi.
MAR 6:14 Hiridus kutura sǝkkǝn kusheng shuwun Yǝso kǝthlǝm fen thlǝmkǝnhi chika tǝteni funa ndatwa: "Yohanna lǝsǝt Baptisma thla'a ndǝ ficha hur mǝmatcha, ndǝkǝn sǝk natǝn tǝ alchit sǝt ǝnnat fǝr sheka i'nda."
MAR 6:15 Ndakfunuwa: "Iliya tapǝna'a" funǝ paɗ ndakndǝwa, "Nda ǝrta hur tapǝnechi sohyu."
MAR 6:16 Kǝ sǝktǝ Hiridus shuwunkǝn, ndakǝnwa, Yohanna nǝyu, le thlendi i'ndǝ ennaɗi thlaaka hur mǝmatcha."
MAR 6:17 Kǝthlǝm Hiridus tǝ i'ndǝ'en mbukǝ tǝ ndatwa kǝ kǝssang fichǝ Yohanna, kǝ kǝnnang ficha kǝ ɗǝndǝ tǝnda pursuna. Sǝk Hiridus kichu kǝthlǝm Hirudiya, Nuh Filibus hwanmankǝn kahandǝn.
MAR 6:18 Kǝthlǝm Yohanna lǝnakna mbwa'anda Hiridus wa, "Ngǝmawu kus kǝ kahangnǝ nuh hwanyatuwa".
MAR 6:19 Awi Hirudiya mǝlla kǝs kommbǝl Yohanna a hur hanɗǝkiketǝ'en, a yahkǝn kǝ ɓǝllaǝn. Nat tǝkichu mbǝsutǝ mbandǝwa,
MAR 6:20 Kǝthlǝm Hiridus lechaɗa Yohanna, A shinwa mǝllan ka nifǝnakǝn, a shin tǝ ndatwa nakǝn chiɗchiɗ, lǝ ɗwachit paɗ, ndǝkǝn sǝk Hiridus kǝstǝn Yohanna har ndiichin, lǝ shekɗang i'nda ma mǝlla sǝk Yohanna mǝlla shundǝ tǝndi, nat tǝkichu lǝ nakna mbǝnandǝfa ma mǝlla sǝk shundǝ'en.
MAR 6:21 A mweshitkǝn ɓak Hirudiya mbǝs mbanda. A farǝ mbǝnfat thlahmbǝt ngǝtta Hiridus, akǝn pǝktat nofcha, funa ngomnati, funa hurfathlǝrhwata, tǝ pǝktat nofchi Galili.
MAR 6:22 Kǝ yimtǝ hweya Hirudiyasi kǝ nuhhweya, rǝmkǝn mbǝnang na Hiridus fa tǝ tahǝt romchi naksi. Ndang kutura nuhhwaniyuwa: "Hwanitǝn i yahtu, ni furuta."
MAR 6:23 Akǝn ichimi tǝ ndatwa, hwanitin i yahtu nifuruta chika mbuth kuturichiɗengna.
MAR 6:24 Thlaakǝ nuhhwaniyu cheknakish kambǝs mankǝn mbwa'ǝn tǝ ndatwa: "Mǝnati hwanada" Ngǝmmang mankǝnwa i'nda Yohanna lǝ sǝt Baptisma.
MAR 6:25 Chatkichuyu ngǝraǝn inna mbǝnda kutura tǝ wesha hwanan tǝ ndatwa, yahkǝsi nakǝn nakǝnya kǝ fǝrikǝnnǝ i'nda Yohanna lǝ sǝt Baptisma a hur tǝpɓi.
MAR 6:26 Sǝɓkǝ hanndǝkiketa kuturaɗǝ ka'ǝn. Paɗ ngu mbǝlla cherǝfuwa kǝthlǝm teppa eɗtǝ ichimi mbanitǝ nofcha, kǝthlǝm ngu mbǝlla talandǝ i mbutǝnwa.
MAR 6:27 Chatkichuyu thlǝnkǝn yuna hur fapundǝ har ndaǝnwa, kǝ ɗa ɓattǝ i'nda Yohanna, pǝɗak nifiyu kǝ pursunatǝkǝn ɗǝkna thlandǝ i'nda Yohanna,
MAR 6:28 ɓakǝn tǝ inkǝnna hur tǝpɓi fǝrangna nuhhwaniyu, thlǝk nuhhwaniyu fǝrangna mankǝn.
MAR 6:29 Kǝ sǝktǝ kimshecha Yohanna kichuyu, pǝɗaknda tǝr fatkǝn ɗǝknda thlohanda.
MAR 6:30 Kǝ ɓat fathlǝncha Yǝso ɗi ngomkǝndǝhi mbwa'ang ndǝ i sǝtndǝ uf, tǝ i sakandǝndaɗi.
MAR 6:31 Nak nofchǝ oiya ɓata funa pǝɗata, Yǝso tǝ fathlǝnchi'en mbǝsundǝ har sǝmɗǝsǝmtuwa. Ndǝkǝn ndandǝnna kanndǝwa tama katmbǝt har nguɗuk, kǝthlǝm kǝ yipuni.
MAR 6:32 Pǝɗaknda hur kommbawal kǝ mbǝt nguɗuk ichitnanda.
MAR 6:33 Awi neɗ nofchǝ kandǝ oi kanda pǝɗata, paɗ shinndǝ kanda, rahkǝnda tǝ sarǝcha a hur thlet hǝmchikǝn laknda mbǝɗi natnda ɗǝta.
MAR 6:34 Cheta Yǝso kissha hur kommbawaltǝkǝn, nakǝn nofchǝ oi haɗangndǝfa, kǝthlǝm nakndǝ nda shohrecha le nguchit lǝ hǝrǝmtǝsi. A tǝrkaakǝn saka ichakandǝhar oi.
MAR 6:35 Nak mbǝta hulta ɓak kimshechi'ena mbǝsndi, ndangndǝwa: "Mbǝɗi natǝmya nguɗuk nifǝsǝwa, tǝpaɗ mbǝta hulta.
MAR 6:36 Ndandǝna nofchiyawa kǝpǝɗanda kǝ kahǝmcha tǝthlet hǝmchi ndukndukya kǝɗǝnda hi i nanndasǝmta."
MAR 6:37 Paɗ ngǝmmang Yǝso tǝ ndatwa: "Kunang fǝramǝn ɗǝsǝmta kanndǝ kǝ sǝmnda." Ndǝkǝn ndandǝndǝwa, kǝ ɗani hi njohma i dinari aruchap kǝ fǝrangani kandǝ kǝ chiindǝwa?
MAR 6:38 Ndangna kandǝwa, njohmǝ kurmi naksengnuni? ɗama kǝllamǝn ɗǝknda kǝllanda ndangndǝwa, njohmǝ ɗurman tǝ tinchǝ chap.
MAR 6:39 Ndang Yǝso kimshechi'enwa kǝ ndangnda nofchiyuwa kǝ sokndǝhi tǝnglǝng-tǝnglǝng kǝ ɗar nduhwelecha.
MAR 6:40 A sokkǝndǝhi tǝnglǝng-tǝnglǝng, funǝ kumchit kum, funǝ paɗ kumchit ɗurman.
MAR 6:41 Tǝrkǝn njohǝmchi ɗurmanyu tǝ tinchi chap yu, kǝlangna afshi saǝn usoko Fara, saka'ǝnhi fǝrang na kimsechi'en, kǝ sakangnda nofcha. Sǝkǝn kichu tǝ tinchikǝn paɗ.
MAR 6:42 Uf nda sǝmkǝnnda ngalkǝnnda.
MAR 6:43 Ngomang kimshechi'en fishirchikǝn nihǝɗ inaftǝ kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap,
MAR 6:44 Terǝ nofchi sǝmkǝ ɗǝsǝmkǝn, hishchǝ, sheendǝ aru kumchit kum ɗurman (5,000).
MAR 6:45 Chatkichuyu ndang Yǝso kimsechi'en wa, kǝ yimnda hur kommbawal, kǝ landǝ cheta kǝ Betsaida, mǝlan paɗ kalkǝn terǝ nofchihiyu.
MAR 6:46 Ɗiffitǝ kalǝ nofchihi tǝrkǝna ɗar shohlata kǝthlǝm kǝ hwanǝn.
MAR 6:47 Sǝk farǝ hufta, kommbawal tiyu a hur ɗiffiti hawurta, Yǝso paɗ mǝlla hachahai i'chitkǝn.
MAR 6:48 Kǝ natin kimshechi'ena ɓahtǝhi tǝ koharǝkǝn, kǝthlǝm rǝnna'a ɓahandǝ kanda, keeke tǝ kukwara ɗekta katǝtɓǝta, mǝlla ɓata mbǝskandǝ tǝ wita ɗar hawurkǝn. Yarkǝnwa na lata mban.
MAR 6:49 Kǝ natndǝndi mǝlla wita ɗar ama, naknda muh hanhara naǝn kandǝhiwa ɗǝhanifa.
MAR 6:50 Kǝthlǝm ufnda neɗndǝndi, lechiknda, chatkichuyu "Shunaǝn kandǝ tǝ ndatwa ǝnsuwa, njeta, mǝ lechiɗuniwa."
MAR 6:51 Mbǝnniyu yimkǝna kommbawal tǝ kanda, chatkichuyu thlarkǝ rǝnnikǝnhi. Shekɗang i'ndǝkandǝ ka'ǝn.
MAR 6:52 Kǝthlǝm sunundǝ sakǝt sǝma'ǝn nofchi aru kumchit ɗurmanyu tǝ njohmǝwa, kǝthlǝm kwaakwaachit hanɗǝkikechengnanda.
MAR 6:53 Kǝ chandǝndǝ hawurkǝn kǝ kishitǝle, tǝrkǝnda haya a thlet hǝmǝt Jenisarat, kǝnangndǝ kommbawal tǝkǝnhi kǝmi chichengkǝn.
MAR 6:54 Kǝchet nda kisha hur kommbawal mbǝssang nofchuwa mǝllan.
MAR 6:55 Rahkǝnda hur hǝmchikǝn, naknda ɓat tǝ fichile nak haachin a ɗar mbǝt hunechengnanda kǝ mbǝɗi sǝktǝndǝwa mǝlla mbǝnniyu.
MAR 6:56 Nat mbǝɗi yimtǝn, thlet hwan hǝmchǝ tǝ hǝmcha, la naknda ɗǝt tǝ haachǝ kǝmbǝɗ'en paɗ tǝmi lumocha, a lanaknda hwananda kǝthlǝm kǝ tǝkangndǝ hara chika mi njela'enfa, nat le tǝkang harfa kǝnkǝnaɗi.
MAR 7:1 Farisawecha tǝ malɗǝmcha fichile la sakang kussa ɗi ɓaka Urshelima, ngomkǝnda thlǝmat Yǝso.
MAR 7:2 A mbǝssangndǝ tǝ ndatwa kimshechi'en kanda sǝmɗǝsǝmtǝ tǝ tǝkǝmharcha sapawundǝwa.
MAR 7:3 (Kǝthlǝm Farisawecha tǝ tahǝt Yahudawecha sǝmundǝ ɗǝsǝmtǝ kichu sapundǝ harwa, kǝthlǝm tor murta pǝktechengnanda nakǝn kichu.
MAR 7:4 Ma ɓennda ɗa lumo, manga tǝ fanndǝ nda i mbutǝ tor murtengnandǝwa ngunda sǝmɗǝsǝmtǝwa. Tor murtengnandǝsi paɗ lela kuwur tǝnda, nda sap tǝpsat 'amcha, tǝ ɓicha, tǝ kuppecha tǝ kǝtǝn sǝm'ǝna.)
MAR 7:5 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn sahang Farisawecha tǝ pǝktat malɗǝmcha fasakandǝ shuwun kussa Musaɗi: "Kǝthlǝm mi kimsecheku yahundǝ kuwur tor murcha pǝktechengnaniwa, mashiɗ kǝnnanda sǝmɗǝsǝmta tǝ tǝkǝmharcha?"
MAR 7:6 A ngǝmang Yǝso tǝ ndatwa: "Kohat nofcha keekesi fǝrtǝ Ishaya sakǝtkǝn kǝ ɗarnuni, nda i yarandǝ ficha. Nofchiya a mi ɗeng nannda mwanita, paɗ hanɗǝkikechengnanda nakǝn langnga tǝ nji.
MAR 7:7 Poffǝn lǝnannda mwanandǝ thlǝmna, kussi ti la natnda sakandaɗi, i nofchǝ ɗeng, ɗar ndatwa shunda Fara.
MAR 7:8 Lamallanguni i ndat Faruwa kǝ suni, nakuni kuwur tor murta nofcha."
MAR 7:9 Ndangnakandǝwa: "Awi nuni mbǝllamalandǝ kussi Fara kǝthlǝm kǝ kuruni tor murchengnuni!
MAR 7:10 Kǝthlǝm ndak Musa wa, 'fǝran mwanda suka tǝ yatu paɗ le erkǝ shinkǝn tǝ mankǝn keekesi kǝ ɓǝllang ficha.'
MAR 7:11 Paɗ landakuniwa: ''Nat i nat shinchinuni tǝ manchinuni ɓǝsta mbǝɗa nifǝ soh sokkǝn nda korban" (sakǝtkǝnwa fǝrraɗi Fara).
MAR 7:12 kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn mwawuni mallandǝ kǝ kǝssaǝn tora shinkǝnsi tǝ mankǝn wa.
MAR 7:13 Tǝkichu la natuni, cherǝ pathla Fara, tǝ pathlǝ kuwur tormurchengnuni, paɗ la nakuni ɗahhanda witǝ ichiniyu in.
MAR 7:14 Ngǝrkǝ Yǝso at nofcha mbǝɗ'en, ndangnakandǝwa kami thlǝmmat uffuni, paɗ kǝsununisi ndiichin.
MAR 7:15 Nga i lasǝmtǝ nifa hur na tǝkmandǝhiwa, i la cheka hur handǝkiketǝ la tǝkmang nifǝhi.
MAR 7:16 [Uf le nat thlǝmmatsǝktǝ'ensi kǝ sǝkkǝn.]
MAR 7:17 Kǝ saktǝnhi tǝ nofchi oiyu yimkǝnna huri, sahang kimsechi'en sakǝt i'sakandǝnaɗiyu.
MAR 7:18 Ndangnakandǝwa: "Awi kunang paɗ sǝnwuni sakǝtkǝn tǝ ndatwa i sǝmtǝ nifa hur, ɓahwa tǝkmandǝhiwa.
MAR 7:19 Kǝthlǝm nga la yimkǝnna hur hanɗǝkiketǝwa la yimkǝnna hur kǝhapangkaɗi. A hurra shuniya cheɗkǝ Yǝso wa i sǝka ɗǝsǝmta tǝkǝmtǝsa fi'enwa.
MAR 7:20 Ngǝr kǝnna ndatwa i lachekakissha hur hanɗǝkiketa nifa ndǝkǝn na tǝkmanghi.
MAR 7:21 Kǝthlǝm a hur hanɗǝkiketa nifa la chetɓǝɓi'ichakish, ndanda ɓǝɓiyara, fǝllawichita, herketa, tǝ ɓǝlfata,
MAR 7:22 Katnishcha nofcha, sǝɓfata, lekta, sǝrǝhta, mwa'inda, ɓokta, tǝ ɓomchita.
MAR 7:23 Uf ɓǝɓi'ichiniyu lǝ chekna hanɗǝkiketa, ndǝkǝn la tǝkmang nifǝhi.
MAR 7:24 Mbǝnniyu malkǝ Yǝso Galilihi pǝɗakna thlet hǝmmǝt Taya tǝ Sidon. yimkǝnna hura'a yuna, a yahu kǝ sǝnfichiwa. Nat tǝ kichu ɓuɓwe'iuwa.
MAR 7:25 Chatkichuyu nuhnifǝsi, tǝ hwe'ensi kǝ nuhhweya naktǝ ɓǝbi shemeɗafa, kǝ sǝktǝn kusheng Yǝso, ɓakna hǝmtǝhi mbanitǝkǝn.
MAR 7:26 Nuhhiyu witǝ Helinawechǝ nakǝn, a thlet hǝmǝt Finikiya ngǝttǝfichǝndi, a hachahai Suriya. A hwanaǝn Yǝso wa kǝ kǝtaǝn ɓǝɓi luwurchaɗa fa hwe'en.
MAR 7:27 Ndang Yǝso wa: "Suku kǝ ngal hwechǝ kwaɗǝn, kǝthlǝm kamusi kǝ tǝr fichǝ ɗǝsǝmta hwecha kǝ fǝrang ficha hǝɗechuwa."
MAR 7:28 A ngǝmang nuhiyu tǝ ndatwa: "Ə, kichuyu malɗǝm, chikatǝ kichu hǝɗecha la sǝmkǝnndǝ fishirchikǝnti ka tebǝr lela hǝhatka haya miya hwecha.
MAR 7:29 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Yǝso wa: "Kǝthlǝm shundeku, ɗuɗaɗi, ɓǝɓilura shekhi tǝ 'hwe'eku."
MAR 7:30 Ngǝrang nuhnifǝkǝn inna ɗi ɗǝkna mbǝssandǝ hwe'en ɗuk a mbǝthunata ɓǝɓi luriyu tepa keltǝndǝhi.
MAR 7:31 Malkǝ Yǝso thlet hǝmǝt Tayahi, kuwurkǝn tǝ Sidon ɗǝkna hawur Galili. A mbanda kwirtǝ thlet Hǝmchǝ shee Kum.
MAR 7:32 A mbǝnniyu ɓang ndǝ ɓomma, le lakweekǝ shunda, a hwanangnda kǝthlǝm kǝ ɗǝfaǝn hara in.
MAR 7:33 Kaɓkǝ Yǝso ɓommiyu kǝkǝllar, mbahkǝnndaɗa thlǝmat nofchiyu kǝ mbǝɗi nguchit nifǝsi. Pakǝn hanharchi'enna hur thlǝmmecha nifiyu, chahkǝn yahta hanhar'en, tǝka'ǝn hara hanshunda nifǝkǝn fa.
MAR 7:34 Kǝlak na afshi kahkǝn yiptǝ langnga, ndakǝnwa: "Iffata!" sakǝtkǝnwa: "Innuhi!"
MAR 7:35 Kǝ mbutǝn kichu inkǝ thlǝmmecha nifǝkǝnhi, i kǝnnang hanshundǝ'en paɗ kwaskǝnhi, tǝr kaakǝn shundǝ ndiichin.
MAR 7:36 Ɓokang Yǝso kandǝwa mǝ mbwa'anda chika wunwa, nattǝ ɓoki ɓokandǝnnakanda nak mbukǝnna chekta.
MAR 7:37 Shekɗang i'ndǝ kandǝ ka'ǝn, ndakndǝwa shiitǝ ichindiichin oi! Sokkǝn ɓomchasǝkmbǝta, tippengcha kanda shunda".
MAR 8:1 A hur hanmunchiniyu, nofchǝ oi paɗ ɓaka mbǝs Yǝso. A nakǝn ǝnsǝ nannda sǝmtǝwa, ak Yǝso kimshechi'en ndangna kandǝwa:
MAR 8:2 "Nofchiya haɗitǝfa, kǝthlǝm munkǝndǝ mǝkkan nakǝnya kanda thlǝmatna mwa'u ndǝsǝmtengnandǝsuwa,
MAR 8:3 Ma ɗeɗi nakǝnyawa kǝ pǝɗandaɗaɗi tǝ mita, na funa hǝhattǝhi mbacha. Kǝthlǝm funǝ ɓakndǝ langnga."
MAR 8:4 Ndǝkǝn ngǝmmandǝ kimshechi'enwa: "Nakma mbǝs njohma aiya hurhweli'iya na sǝmma ǝn nofchi natya?"
MAR 8:5 Sahang Yǝso kimshechiken'enwa: "njohmǝ kurmǝ naksengnuni?" Ngǝmangndǝwa: "Muɗ."
MAR 8:6 Ndangna nofchiyuwa kǝ sokndǝhi kǝ hachahaya. Ndǝkǝn hartǝn njohhomchi muɗ yu, saǝn usoko Fara, chichaǝnhi, fǝrangna kimshechi'en kǝ sakangnda nofchiyu, sǝk kimshechi'en kichuyu.
MAR 8:7 Tǝ paɗ tinchisǝ ɗimek. Yǝso saǝn usoko Fara, ndangna kimshechi'enwa leya paɗ sakamna kanda.
MAR 8:8 Sǝmkǝnda ngalkǝndǝ nda i yahtǝnda. Ɗiffitǝkǝn ngomang kimshechi'en fishirchikǝn inaftǝ muɗ.
MAR 8:9 A farǝkǝn shee nifǝ aru kumchit fwaɗɗa (4,000). Paɗ ndang Yǝso kandǝwa pǝɗama.
MAR 8:10 Chatkichuyu thlaakǝ Yǝso tǝ kimshechi'en yimkǝnda hur kommbawal pǝɗaknda thlet hǝmǝt Dalmanuta.
MAR 8:11 Ɓak Farisawecha tǝrkaakǝndǝ sahami Yǝso. Kǝthlǝm yahndǝssa kǝkaɗanda, sahangndǝ kǝ cheɗaǝn sakǝtkǝna kanda a hur afshi.
MAR 8:12 Kǝtkǝn yiptǝ langnga hur shemeɗ'en ndakǝnwa: "Kǝthlǝm mǝ nat nofchi kishi'i nakǝnya katsakǝtkǝn? Kitchitkǝn ni mbwa'anda kuni sakǝtkǝnsi nat ficha fǝranda kishi'i nakǝnyawa."
MAR 8:13 Thlaakǝn malkǝnkandǝhi, yimkǝnda hur kommbawal pǝɗakǝn kǝ chicheng le.
MAR 8:14 A nakǝn mbutandǝ kimshecha Yǝso kǝ tǝrndi njohmǝ in, njohmǝ ǝrtǝ ndak naka harengnanda hur kommbawal tǝkǝn.
MAR 8:15 Ndang Yǝso kimshechǝkǝn'enwa: "Ndǝfam ǝndisǝ ndiichin kǝ ndǝsǝcha Farisawecha tǝ i Hiridus nda mehnda."
MAR 8:16 Tǝrkaakǝndǝ shundǝ tǝndani tǝ ndatwa: "Mbukǝn i'ya kǝthlǝm njohmǝsa harrengnǝmwa."
MAR 8:17 Shin Yǝso i nat kimshechǝkǝna shunda ɗarkǝn, ndǝkǝn sahandǝn mǝ kandǝwa: "Kǝthlǝm mǝ natu ni ndandandaniwa njohmǝ nguchiksa harengnuni?" Awi paaya a sǝnwuniwowa? Tǝpaɗɗaa paaya a mbǝsawuniwowa? Paaya mwaakǝ hanndǝkikechengnuni kwaakwaawa?
MAR 8:18 Hwanichengnunisi, nuwuni mbǝtwowa? Thlǝmmechengnunisi, sǝkwuni mbǝtwowa? Kuɗukwunniharwowa?
MAR 8:19 Fari chichandi njohmihi ɗurman chiitǝ nofchǝ aru kumchit ɗurman yu, inaftǝ kurmi ngomanduni fishirchikǝn tiiyu?" Ngǝmang kimshechǝkǝn wa: "I'naftǝ kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap."
MAR 8:20 Ngǝrkǝn ndanda kandǝwa njohmi muɗ chichandǝhi chiiti nofchǝ aru kumchit fwaɗɗa yu i'naftǝ kurmi ngomanduni fishirchikǝn?" Ngǝmangndǝwa "i'naftǝ muɗ."
MAR 8:21 Paɗ sahaǝnmi kandǝwa: "Kananat paaya a mbǝsawuniwowa?"
MAR 8:22 Yǝso tǝ kimshechi'en ɓaknda Betsaida, ɓak nofchǝ tǝ nifǝ kǝ kukomta, hwanang nofchiyu kǝ tǝka'ǝn harfa.
MAR 8:23 Kǝskǝn haara kukomǝyu, chekǝntǝnda kish a hur thlet hǝmǝtkǝn. Chahkǝ Yǝso yahta hwanicha kukomǝyu sǝkkǝn harchi'enna hwanicha kukomǝyu, sahang Yǝso wa: "Sa nat mbǝt wa?"
MAR 8:24 Kǝllakna afshi a ndakǝnwa: "Nja nat nofcha nakndǝ nda afchǝ naka wiita."
MAR 8:25 Ngǝrkǝ Yǝso sǝt harchi'enna hwanicha kukomǝyu, nakǝnya kǝllak nifiyu ndiichin, ǝnkǝ hwanichi'en hi nakna nat chikamǝhi chiɗchiɗ.
MAR 8:26 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Yǝso wa: "Ɗuɗaɗi kǝ huri, mǝ ngǝrina thlet hǝmǝɗiniyuwa."
MAR 8:27 Thlaakǝ Yǝso tǝ kimshechi'en kǝ thlet hǝmcha hachahai Kaisariya Filibi. Nak nda wita ndǝkǝn sahandǝn kimshechi'enwa: "La tǝrkǝ nofchuwa wunnaki?"
MAR 8:28 Ngǝmang funǝ la ndakndǝwa: "Sokǝn Yohanna lǝ sǝt Baptisma, funǝ la ndakndǝwa Iliya tapǝna'a, funǝ paɗ la nɗakndǝwa naku ǝrta hur tapǝnecha."
MAR 8:29 Ndǝkǝn sahandǝ Yǝso kimshechi'enwa kunang kǝni: "La ndakuniwa wun naki?" Bitrus Ngǝmanwa sokǝn naka Kǝrǝsti."
MAR 8:30 Ɓokang Yǝso kandǝ ndatwa: "Mǝ mbwa'anda yunǝ ndu wun nakǝnwa."
MAR 8:31 Tǝrkaakǝ Yǝso sakandakandǝhar tǝ ndatwa: "Hweya nifǝ nan ɓahtǝhi tǝ ichi somsomǝn, paɗ kǝ cher pǝktechǝndi tǝ pǝktat pǝristochicha, tǝfa sakandǝ ɗalwer tǝ kussa Musa ɗi. Nanda ɓǝllanda, ɗiffitǝ mundǝ mǝkkan nan thlata.
MAR 8:32 Mbwa'ǝn ichiniyu kimshechi'en a ɗwachitkǝn. Ɓak Bitrussa kahndi kǝ kǝlar ɓoka'ǝn kǝ ɗar mbuwitǝ'ichiniyu.
MAR 8:33 Tǝɓǝrkǝ Yǝso hi nakna kǝllandǝ kimshechi'en, ɓokangna Bitrus hi tǝ ndatwa: ''Mbahhu thlǝmatna Sheɗan, yareku nga i Farǝwa i nifa."
MAR 8:34 Akǝn nofchǝ tǝ kimshechi'en, ndangna kandǝwa: "Nifi yahkǝssa kuwurnji kǝ cherǝn i'ndǝ'en, kǝ tǝrǝn palitǝ'en kǝ kurǝn nji."
MAR 8:35 Kǝthlǝm chikawun yahkǝssa hǝrkandǝ shisshingtǝ'en nan shekɗanda, paɗ chǝkawun shekɗang shisshingtǝ'en kǝthlǝm njang tǝ kushengshundǝ mbǝnchin, nan hǝrkandi shisshingtǝ'en.
MAR 8:36 Mǝ naka mbǝs ǝnhara nifa ma mbǝssandǝ kisshita kǝ ɓahhǝn shisshingta.
MAR 8:37 Mǝnat nifa fǝrta kǝthlǝm shisshingtǝ'en?
MAR 8:38 Chǝkawun la harandǝfat kǝthlǝm njang tǝ shundengna a kishi ɓahkitchiɗiya tǝ ɓǝɓichit faɗi nakǝnya, hweya nifa nan sǝk harǝfat'en paɗ ma ɓeɗa hur mwanda Shinkǝn tǝ mala'ikachǝ chiɗchiɗ.
MAR 9:1 Ndǝkǝn ngǝrtǝ Yǝso ndanda kandǝwa: "kittǝkǝn nja mbwa'anda kuni, funǝsa a hurnuni mbǝɗya ngunda mǝrtǝwa sema neɗndǝ kuturichita Fara ɓeɗ tǝ alchita."
MAR 9:2 Ɗiffitǝ mundǝ tehheth, harkǝ Yǝso nda Bitrus tǝ Yakubu tǝ Yohanna, ɗǝkǝn tǝ kanda shohlatǝ lenak njang, nakndǝ ichitnanda mbǝnniyu. Naknda nata kǝllathi chat mbumbweɗkǝ fata Yǝso hi a mbanitǝnanda,
MAR 9:3 sǝk njelechi'en hendǝɗa nakna kǝstǝfǝ nda hwatfara, nguchit nifa mbǝlla sapandǝ njelechi'en tǝ pachau kichuyu a hur kishi'iya.
MAR 9:4 Chatkichuyu ɓak nda Iliya tǝ Musa, cheɗkǝndǝ faɗengnanda paɗ kanda shundǝ tǝ Yǝso.
MAR 9:5 Ndang Bitrussa Yǝso wa: "Malɗǝm ɓaɗengnǝma mbǝdya ndiichinsi, tahsam kǝtǝnchǝ mǝkkan, ǝrtǝ iyuwa, ǝrtǝ i Musa, ǝrtǝ i Iliya."
MAR 9:6 Mbukǝn iniyu kǝthlǝm sǝnutǝ'i'natna mbutǝwa, kǝthlǝm a lechiɗnda.
MAR 9:7 Ɓak husomba'a haya kǝ ɗar inchengnanda ngǝlaǝn kanda, chek mburata kissha hur husombikǝn tǝ ndatwa: "Ka hweengnǝniya leyahti kamǝn thlǝmmata."
MAR 9:8 Chat kǝllakndǝhi chika tǝteni nundǝ nifǝ somǝnwa, se Yǝso ndak naka thlǝmat nanda.
MAR 9:9 Naknda tǝrtahaya a shohlayiyu, ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Mǝ mbwa'anduni nifǝ i'nattuniyawa, se fari thlaatǝ hweya nifa hur mǝmatcha."
MAR 9:10 Kǝskǝndǝ I'har mbwa'andǝnna kanda, paɗ naknda sahandǝ ndanichǝ tǝ ndatwa: "Mǝ naka sakǝt thlata a hur mǝmatcha."
MAR 9:11 Sahang ndǝ mi tǝ ndatwa: "Kǝthlǝm mǝ ndat malɗǝmchǝ fa sakandǝ kus tǝkǝnnaɗi, Iliya na tǝrka thlata?"
MAR 9:12 Ngǝrkǝ Yǝso sǝwa: "Kittǝkǝn Iliya na tǝrka thlata kǝthlǝm kǝ tahsaǝn chikamǝhi. Chika tǝ kichu, kǝthlǝmmǝ ndat laulawatkǝnwa hweya nifa nan sat pwanchǝ ka'ǝn tǝ paɗ kǝ njirndǝndi?
MAR 9:13 Paɗ nja mbwa'anda kuni ndatwa, Iliya tepi ɓeɗi sa nofchǝ i'ngǝmtǝ hurengnanda nda i'natna a hur laulawatkǝn kǝ ɗar i'ndi'en.
MAR 9:14 Kǝnatnda ngǝrta mbǝɗa tahǝt kimshechi'en, nakndǝ nofchǝ oi, a taurangndǝ kandǝhi, paɗ funǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kus tǝ tǝrɓanda Fara ɗi kanda halǝ'i'ndǝ tǝ kanda.
MAR 9:15 Kǝnat nofchiyu Yǝso, pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfa, rahkǝnda thlǝmatkǝn ndangndǝ ǝna.
MAR 9:16 Ndǝkǝn sahandǝ Yǝso kandǝwa: "Mǝnatuni halǝ'i'ndǝ tǝ kandǝ kǝ ɗarkǝn?"
MAR 9:17 Yuna hur nofchiiyu shuwunkǝn tǝ ndatwa: "Malɗǝm ɓuɗi hwe'engna kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝnangɗi ɓǝɓi shemeɗɗa fat'en njandǝ shunda.
MAR 9:18 Ma ɓeɗ ɓǝɓi shemeɗkǝnna fi'en la muhkǝnndǝhi kǝ hachahaya. Mi'enna hupta kǝna chi hanthlanchi'en, chat mbǝsku titiɗhi. Ndaɗi kimshecheku wa kǝ rǝkangndǝ ɓǝɓishemechikǝnna kish mbǝlla'undǝwa."
MAR 9:19 Ngǝmang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Kunang nofchǝ fa ɓahfǝrkit! Kǝkwat natmanata ɓǝt ǝrtǝ tǝ kuni? Kǝ kwat natinata kǝrǝstǝ tǝkuni? Ɓamitǝn hwankǝn."
MAR 9:20 Ɓangndǝ hwaniyu. Kǝnat ɓǝɓi shemeɗiyu Yǝso, tǝpkǝn hwanihiyu hachahaya mǝla takarǝhi mi'enna hupta.
MAR 9:21 "Ndǝkǝn sahandǝ Yǝso mi shin hwanniyuwa?" Ɓǝt kǝnni kǝstǝ'i'ndiya?" Ngǝmanwa: "Thlata hwanchit'en.
MAR 9:22 Kurɓandǝ nata muhnda hur am tǝ hwata tǝna mbǝlanda. Paɗ manu mbǝllata kǝsanna kanisi kǝ handukanifa."
MAR 9:23 "Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Yǝso wa kǝthlǝm mǝnatu ndatwa mani mbǝllata?" Chikamǝ nan sǝtta kǝ mbǝɗa le fǝrkǝ kit."
MAR 9:24 Chatkichuyu shin hwanniyuwa tǝkǝn ndakǝnwa, a firi kit, paɗ kǝsitǝnsi tǝ ɓah fǝr kitchiɗengna."
MAR 9:25 Kǝ nat Yǝso nofchǝkǝna chektǝ oi, kanda ɓat tǝ rahta, ɓokangna ɓǝɓi shemeɗkǝnhi tǝ ndatwa: "Sokǝn ɓǝɓi shemeɗɗi njang sǝkɓǝt tǝ shunda hwaniya nja ndutuwa chukisha fat'en mǝ tamina ngǝr yimta fat'enwa."
MAR 9:26 Ɓǝɓi shemeɗɗiyu hwakǝn, tǝpkǝn hwanihiyu fat'enna saktatfa chekna kish. Nak hwanniyu ɗuk nda tǝ mǝrrǝn, nak nofcha hurrumta paɗ terchin ndangwa tǝ mǝrrǝn.
MAR 9:27 Kǝskǝ Yǝso hara hwanniyu kǝsaansi thlarkǝnhi kit.
MAR 9:28 Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn, Yǝso tǝ kimshechi'en i'chitnanda a huri, sahang kimshechi'en miya a ɓuɓweeta: "kǝthlǝmmi mbǝla'uchitani kǝtandǝ ɓǝɓi shemeɗɗiyu?"
MAR 9:29 Ngǝmang Yǝso wa: "Witǝkǝn ngu chetakish kichuwa se tǝ hwanda."
MAR 9:30 Malkǝndǝ mbǝnnihiyu cheknda kish tǝ hurhuri Galili. kǝthlǝm yahu Yǝso kǝ sǝn nifǝ mbǝndi natǝnwa,
MAR 9:31 nakna sakanda kimshechi'en har tǝ ndatwa: "Na ficha fǝr hweya nifa kǝ harra attikrechikǝn, nanda mbǝllanda paɗ ɗiffitǝ mundǝ mǝkkan nan thlata hur mǝmatcha."
MAR 9:32 Nakǝn mbǝsawundǝ i'mbutǝnwa tǝ paɗ kanda lechit kǝ sahangndǝ i'natna yara.
MAR 9:33 Ɓak nda Kafarnahum sokkǝndǝhi a huri sahang Yǝso kimshechi'enwa: "Mǝnatuni shunda ɗarkǝna mbandiyu?"
MAR 9:34 Mbǝla'undǝ fǝra ngǝmkǝnwa, kǝthlǝm a mbanda helndǝ i'ndǝ tǝ ndani ndatwa wun nak mwanchinna hurnanda.
MAR 9:35 Sokkǝnhi, akǝn kimshechi'en kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap yu, ndangnakandǝwa: "Chikawun yahkǝsa nata mban kǝ naka ɗiffi paɗ kǝ saǝn fat'en kǝ mafata nofchǝ nat."
MAR 9:36 Tǝrkǝn hwe har, thlaraanhi hurɗifitǝnanda tǝrkǝnndǝ, ndangna kandǝwa:
MAR 9:37 "Chikawun thlǝk hwe kicheya a hur thlǝmna thlǝtǝnji, paɗ chikawun thlǝknji, thlutǝnji ɗengwa thlǝkǝn tǝ Papati thlǝnkǝnji."
MAR 9:38 Ndang Yohanna Yǝso wa: "Malɗǝm neɗani nifa rǝk ɓǝɓi luwurcha a hur thlǝmwa, ndangnganiwa kǝ malaǝn kǝthlǝm nga nakna hurnaniwa"
MAR 9:39 Ndǝkǝn ndat Yǝso wa: "Mǝ njaɗuniwa, nifǝsi na sǝt witǝ torǝniyu a hur thlǝmna mashiɗ kǝ tǝɓrǝnhi kǝ mbuǝn ɓǝɓi'icha i'ndengniwa."
MAR 9:40 Chikawun nguchika atikrechit tǝ kǝm mǝlan i'nǝm.
MAR 9:41 Kittǝkǝn nati mbwa'anda kuni, nat nifi fǝrang amsata kuni kǝthlǝm kunang 'i Kǝrǝsti nan thlǝt kǝnikǝn.
MAR 9:42 Chikawun ɗǝfkǝ ǝrta hur hwanchi fǝrkǝ kit kǝ ɓǝɗengniya kǝ sǝn ɓǝɓichitfata, kweshaɗa nifiniyu kǝ wokang fichǝ fǝnhata ɓur kǝ muh fichǝnda hur hawurta.
MAR 9:43 Ma hareku la ɗǝfkǝsa sǝt ɓǝɓichitfata thlandinaɗaɗi. Kweskǝn kǝ yimna pwan nga harsǝ ǝrtǝwa mǝni muhsa hwata tǝ harchǝ hwaa.
MAR 9:44 Hwaɗi la lǝfuchik kǝ pwaree.
MAR 9:45 Ma sareku la ɗǝfkǝsa sǝt ɓǝɓichitfata, thlandǝnaɗi kweshkǝn kǝ yimna pwan nga sarǝsǝ ǝrtǝwa mǝni muhsa hwat tǝ sarǝchi hwaa.
MAR 9:46 Hwanɗi la lǝfuchik kǝ pwaree.
MAR 9:47 Ma hwaniteku la ɗǝfkǝsa sǝt ɓǝɓichitfata, kǝtandǝnaɗi kweshkǝn kǝ yimna mwanda Farǝ tǝ hwanitǝ ǝrta mǝni muhsa hur hwat tǝ hwanichǝ hwaa.
MAR 9:48 Mbǝɗi la mǝruchit hweecha, paɗ hwatkǝn tamwa liftǝwa.
MAR 9:49 "Kǝthlǝm chikawun nak ficha kikeɗandǝ tǝ hwata.
MAR 9:50 "Mannda ndiichin, paɗ ma tǝr mbǝndǝ'ennaɗi, naku mbǝlla ngǝranda kwarkǝn kǝ manndawa kǝni? Kǝnuni mbinchin tǝ ndani nda i nat mannda, paɗ kǝ sokuni yuyur tǝ ndani."
MAR 10:1 Yǝso malkǝn thlet hǝmǝɗkenhi pǝɗakna thlet hǝmǝɗ Yahudiya chaǝn suhwaɗ Yodan. Humkǝ nofchǝ oi kǝ thlǝmatkǝn, nakna nata sakanda nofchiharyu nda i la sǝtǝn kǝnding.
MAR 10:2 Ɓak Farisawecha mbǝsndi kǝthlǝm kǝ kikeɗangnda, sahangndǝ mi wa: "Keekesi kǝ kal hishnifǝ nuhkǝnhiwa?"
MAR 10:3 Ngǝmang Yǝso kandǝ tǝ sahmi paɗ ndatwa: "Mǝ mbutǝ Musa a hur kus tǝkǝn kǝ ɗar sak reta?"
MAR 10:4 Ngǝmang "Musa fǝrandǝn mbanda hishnifa kǝ yaraǝn ɗelwera nuhkǝnsǝ kǝ fǝraǝn kǝ rǝkǝnndǝ."
MAR 10:5 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Yǝso kandǝwa: "Yarangna kunisǝ kichuyu kǝthlǝm kwaakwaachit hanndǝkikechengnuni.
MAR 10:6 Paɗ thlata tǝrkakǝn tinkǝ Farǝ kandǝ, nuhnifa tǝ hishnifa.
MAR 10:7 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn hishnifǝ nan malǝ shinkǝhi tǝ mankǝn kǝ nandǝ ǝrtǝ tǝ nuhkǝn.
MAR 10:8 Chapndǝyu hwimndǝhi kǝ ǝnǝrta. Nga nakndǝ chap paɗwa nakndǝ ǝrta.
MAR 10:9 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn i'humandǝ Fara mǝ saka nifǝhiwa.
MAR 10:10 Kǝnatǝn i'chitkǝn tǝ kimshechi'enna huri sahangndǝ mi kǝ ɗar shuniniyu paɗ.
MAR 10:11 Ndangnakandǝwa: "Chikawun cherkǝ nuhkǝn kahkǝn somǝn shiɗtǝ fǝlawichit tǝ ndi
MAR 10:12 Paɗ ma cher nuhnifǝ sǝmaha kahkǝn yunǝ somǝn, shiɗtǝ fǝlawichita."
MAR 10:13 Farǝ le ɓang parchǝ hwechengnanda Yǝso kǝthlǝm kǝ tǝka'ǝn harra kandǝfa kǝ fǝraǝn mbǝsǝnhara kanda. Nak kimshechi'enna njanda parchiyuwa mǝ ɓindǝ tǝ hwanchiyu mbanitǝkǝnwa.
MAR 10:14 Kǝnat Yǝso kichuyu, sǝɓkǝ hur'ennaɗi, ndangna kandǝwa: "Malamǝn hwecha kǝ ɓanda mbǝndengna, mǝ njanduni kandǝwa, kǝthlǝm kuturichita Fara i'witǝ fichile nak nda kandang.
MAR 10:15 Kitchitkǝn nati mbwa'anda kuni chikawun thluchik mwanda Farǝ nda hweya, ngu yimtǝsǝwa."
MAR 10:16 Mbǝnniyu harkǝn hwanchiyu sǝkǝn harcha inchengnanda fǝraǝn mbǝs'ǝna kandahar.
MAR 10:17 Yǝso tahǝskǝnfa na ɓǝɗata Urshelima, ɓak kimsha'a lǝ kǝnaa tǝ rahta, sǝkǝn kurumchihi ɓanitǝkǝn sahaǝnwa: "Ka Malɗǝm, mǝ natisǝta kani ɓǝs shisshingtǝ le kǝ pware?"
MAR 10:18 Sahang Yǝso wa: "Kǝthlǝm mǝ atunjiwa ka malɗǝm?" "Nifǝsǝ naka katkǝnwa se Farǝ ndak.
MAR 10:19 Kǝ ngǝmayi sahmiyeku a shinnǝ kuschikkǝnwa! Mǝ mbǝlǝnifatwa, mǝ sǝni fǝlawichitwa, mǝ herkinǝwa, mǝ thlerna ɗar yuna a ɗar lektǝwa, mǝ ndathlana nifafuwa, kǝ fǝrrangnǝ mwanda nda suk tǝ yatu."
MAR 10:20 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝnwa: "Malɗǝm, a hǝrmi i'chiniharyu nat thlata hwanchiɗengna."
MAR 10:21 Kǝlang Yǝso kimshi'iyu tǝ hwanitǝ mbǝnfata ndaǝnwa: "Ən ǝrtǝ tahhuka, ɗu hi'yan i'chiɗǝ nakseku nat kǝ sakangnǝ hanndǝɓǝlkǝna fa ɓahcha, nu mbǝs hurmichita hur afshi, kanna ɓata kuwurnji."
MAR 10:22 Kǝ sǝktǝn shuninuyu, ɓǝɗakǝn tǝ sǝɓhura, kǝthlǝm lǝ kǝnaa nakǝn ka'ǝn.
MAR 10:23 Kǝlak Yǝso hi ndangna kimshechi'enwa: "'Yang'yangnga fa hurumta kǝ yimka kuturichita Fara!"
MAR 10:24 Pǝndang ǝnna kimshechifiyu tǝ shuwunkǝn. Ndǝkǝn ngǝrtǝ Yǝso ndanda kandǝ paɗwa: "Hwecha, yimta kuturichita Farǝ 'yang'yang.
MAR 10:25 Nannat paapa'a fa ngelupa kǝ 'yimǝn tǝ kwat lipir mǝni hurumta kǝ yimka kuturichita Fara."
MAR 10:26 Kǝ sǝktǝ kimshechǝkǝn'en shuniniyu, pǝndang ǝn kandǝfǝ ka'ǝn sahkǝndǝwa: "Ma nakǝn kichu wunhacha na hǝrǝkta hurkishi'iya?"
MAR 10:27 Kǝllang Yǝso kandǝ ndakǝnwa: "Mbǝɗa nifa ngu nat paapaawa, mbǝɗa Fara chikamǝ nan nat paapaa."
MAR 10:28 Tǝrkaakǝ Bitrus ndandǝwa: "Kanang melani i'chi hi nat kana kuwursa."
MAR 10:29 Ndǝkǝn ndat Yesowa: "Kittǝkǝn nja mbwa'anda kuni, chǝkawun malkǝ huraahi, ndu hwanmanchǝkǝn kǝ hishcha tǝ nishcha, ndu shinkǝn ndu mankǝn, ndu hwechi'en, ndu pwatarcha kǝthlǝm njang tǝ ka kusheng shunda,
MAR 10:30 nan mbǝs ǝn arucha a kishi'i nakǝnya, hurecha, hwanmancha, parcha, hwecha tǝ pwatarcha tǝ pwenecha nan mbǝs shisshingta a hurrechi na ɓatyu,
MAR 10:31 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, terchin fichile naka mban nakǝnya naknda nata ɗiffi, fichile naka ɗiffi paɗ naknda nata mban."
MAR 10:32 Kanda pǝɗata Urshelima, Yǝso lak na mbanitǝnanda. Pǝɗang ǝnnatkǝn kimshechi'enfa, nofchi naka kuwur kanda ɗiffi paɗ lechiknda. Thlarkǝ Yǝso hi akǝn kimshechi'en kumngǝrǝnsǝ chapyu kǝ kǝlar, mbwa'angna kandǝ nat i' na mbǝsndi.
MAR 10:33 Ndakǝnwa: "Sǝkama, nakǝnya nǝma ndǝta Urshelima, kǝ mbǝndǝ nat ficha fǝr hweya nifa, kǝ harra pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kus tǝkǝnnaɗi. Nanda thla kitasǝ i'mǝrtaɗi kǝ fǝrndǝndi kǝ harra punofcha.
MAR 10:34 Nanda sa welǝm, chahangndǝ yahta fa, tǝppangnda, kǝ mbǝllangnda. Hur mundǝ mǝkkan nan thlata."
MAR 10:35 Nda Yakubu tǝ Yohanna hweecha Zabadi ɓaknda ɓǝsndi ndangndǝwa: "Maldǝm, ǝnsǝ yahtanisa hwanuta kǝ sangnǝ kani."
MAR 10:36 Sahaǝn kandǝwa: "Mǝ yahtuni kǝ sayi kuni?"
MAR 10:37 Ndangndǝwa: "Fari natu yimta kuturichiɗeku hur afshi kǝ sokǝm rǝmma, ǝrta harsǝmteku ǝrtǝ paɗ a hishingteku."
MAR 10:38 Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Sǝnwuni i natuni hwandǝwa. Nuni mbǝla sat ɓahhi nati satyawa? Nuni mbǝla thlǝt baptisma ti nati thlǝtyawa?"
MAR 10:39 Ngǝmangndǝwa: "Aa nani mbǝlata." Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Nuni mbǝla sat ɓahi nati sata, kǝ thluni baptisma ti nati thlǝta.
MAR 10:40 Paɗ alchiɗengnǝsǝ nati ndatwa leya na sokta a harsǝmtengna ndu hǝshingtengnǝwa. Farǝ tahsaǝn ɓichiniyu kǝ i' fichile taɗtǝnhar."
MAR 10:41 Kǝ sǝktǝ tahǝt kimshechi'en kumyu shuniniyu sǝɓkǝ hurchengnandaɗi kǝ ɗar Yakubu tǝ Yohanna.
MAR 10:42 Ak Yǝso kandǝ nat, ndangna kandǝwa: "Shinuniwa, fichile naka kuturcha a kishi'iya la sǝkndǝ tor tǝ alchindengnanda kǝ ɗar nofchengnanda, paɗ pǝktechǝkǝn la sǝkndǝ tor tǝ mwaɗengnanda kǝ ɗar nofchengnanda.
MAR 10:43 Ngu nat kichu a hurnuniwa. Paɗ le yahkǝsa nat mwanchin a hurnuni, kǝ sǝka mafata tahchǝkǝn.
MAR 10:44 Tǝ paɗ le yahkǝssa nata mban, kǝ naka mafata nofchǝ nat.
MAR 10:45 Kǝthlǝm chika hweya nifa a ɓu kǝ sang fichǝ torwa, ɓakǝn kǝ saǝn tora nofcha, paɗ kǝ fǝrǝn shisshingtǝ'en kǝ thlǝn nofchandǝ oi."
MAR 10:46 Yǝso tǝ kimshechi'en saakǝnda Yeriko. Naknda malǝ Yerikohi tǝ nofchǝ oi, lǝ hwandǝsǝ paɗ kukomta thlǝmkǝnwa Bartimawus, hweya Timawus, ɗas a mi mbanda,
MAR 10:47 Kǝ sǝktǝ Bartimawus wa Yǝso Lǝnazarat naka mbǝrtǝhi, ndǝkǝn thla'andǝn mburata ndatwa: "Yǝso hweya Dauda, kǝ handukǝfa."
MAR 10:48 Ɓokang nofchihi oiyu ndangndǝwa kǝ ngasǝn ɓa. Thlat tǝkichu i'naǝn mburathi ka'ǝn: "Hweya Dauda kǝ handukifa!"
MAR 10:49 Sǝkkǝ Yǝso ndi thlarkǝn hi ndakǝnwa: "Ndamǝnwa kǝ ɓaka mbǝɗya." Nofchiyu ndangnda kukomiyuwa: "Kwallu hacha," "Aɓu mǝla atsa."
MAR 10:50 Chatkichuyu thlakǝ kukomiyu muhaǝn ndǝ suptǝ'enaɗi, ndǝkna mbǝs Yǝso.
MAR 10:51 Ndǝkǝn sahandǝ Yǝso miya: "Mǝyahtusǝ kǝ sukǝ?" Ndǝkǝn ngǝmandǝ kukomiyuwa: "Malɗǝm, Yahkǝsi kǝ mbǝsi natmbǝta."
MAR 10:52 Ndang Yǝso wa: "Ndu, fǝrkitchindeku kǝnuɗaɗi." Chatkichuyu inkǝ hwanichi'enhi kuwurkǝn Yǝso pǝɗaknda.
MAR 11:1 Kǝnatnda satǝ nduk kǝ Urshelima, a Betafaji, tǝ Betani, tǝ shohla Zaitun, thlinkǝ Yesu kimshechi'en chap,
MAR 11:2 Ndangna kanduwa, yimmama thlet hǝmǝɗini taata mbanitǝnuniyu, nda yimtengnunisi nuni nat hwan kware kǝnda, le tamuchit ficha pǝrtǝsi. Kǝ kwasuni ɓunitǝkǝn.
MAR 11:3 Chika wun sahang mi kuni wa kǝthlǝm mi, natuni sǝt kichu? Ndangnguniwa shinnǝm naka yahta, paɗ nan ɓattǝkǝn nakǝnya.
MAR 11:4 Ndǝkǝn pǝndat kimshechi'en ndǝknda ɓǝssandǝ hwan kware tǝkǝnna miɓanga a kǝlarǝ mbanda, kwassang ndǝ hi.
MAR 11:5 Nofchi nak kitkita mbǝnniyu, ndangnda kanduwa: "Kǝthlǝm mi natuni kwasǝ hwan kware ti ya?
MAR 11:6 Mbwa'angnda kandǝ I ndandǝ Yǝso kandǝwa kǝ mbunda, malang nofchikǝnkanda pǝndakndǝtǝkǝn.
MAR 11:7 Ɓangndǝ hwan kware tǝkǝna Yǝso supkǝndǝ njelenjengnanda ɗar hwan kware tǝkǝn pǝrkǝnsi.
MAR 11:8 Nofchǝ oi supkǝndǝ ndǝ supcheng nanda mbanda, funǝ paɗ thlithlahkǝndǝ swikangrechi har somkǝndǝhi.
MAR 11:9 Fichile ɓan tǝ fichile naka ɗiffi naknda whata, funa kukwara tǝ ndatwa, Hosanna! ɓǝs'ǝnna har shok kǝ ndukwatkǝn kǝɓǝɗa lǝɓatta hur thlǝm Lǝmwanda.
MAR 11:10 Ɓǝs'ichisǝ har a ɗar ɓata kuturichita kakatnǝm Dauda! Mwanamǝn Fara le naka afshi
MAR 11:11 Yim kǝnna Urshelima, kǝ kapat hura'a Fara, kǝllaǝn chikami, Sǝk farǝhufta, chekna kish pǝɗak na Betani tǝ kimshechi'en kum ngǝrrǝnsǝ chap.
MAR 11:12 Ɓingǝtkǝn naknda malǝ Betanihi, nak mita fa Yǝso.
MAR 11:13 Anakǝn affǝt shuɓwat tǝ swa'en kundummǝ kuɗkuɗ langnga, ndǝkǝn ndǝtǝn ka nata naǝnhiwa nan mbǝs hwecha ɓuratkǝn. Swechǝ ndaknaksi, kǝthlǝm sa'u farǝ ngǝttǝ'enwa.
MAR 11:14 Ndang Yǝso affǝtkǝnwa: "Mǝ ngǝri nifa chi hwecheku paɗwa." A shik kimshechi'en i mbutǝn.
MAR 11:15 Ɓakndaɗi kǝ Urshelima, yim kǝ Yǝso kǝ kapat hura'a Fara, rǝkkǝn fa hita tǝ fa hi'yandǝ ichaɗa hur kapat hurikǝnna Fara, paɗ wuwelaǝn hanafcha fa hi'yandǝ Tattabaracha ndǝ tǝ fa mbumbwe hanndiɓǝlcha.
MAR 11:16 Paɗ thlaraǝn chika wunhi naka sǝt tortǝ kapat huri kǝnna Fara nda mbǝt hi'yandǝ ichaɗi.
MAR 11:17 Ndangna kandǝwa: "Ndak yaratkǝnwa, 'Hure'engna nak ficha atwa mbǝt hwanda a hǝmchǝnat, ɓakuni tǝɓrandǝhi kǝ mbǝt sokta harcha."
MAR 11:18 Kǝ sǝktǝ pǝktat pǝrischǝ tǝ malɗǝmcha i laulawatkǝn i sǝt Yǝso, kakndǝ mbayi natnda mbǝllanda. Sokkǝn lechanda kǝthlǝm nofchi humkǝyu pǝɗa'ǝnkandǝfǝ tǝ saktǝ'en.
MAR 11:19 A Farǝhuffǝɗiniyu chek Yǝso kisha hǝmǝtkǝn tǝ kimshechi'en.
MAR 11:20 Kanda mbǝrtǝhi a ɓingǝtkǝn tǝ thlǝmat affǝɗi mbutǝn ǝn kǝ ɗarkǝnyu, mbǝssang kimshechi'en affǝt shuɓwatkǝn hwerandǝ kǝ thlorǝkǝn.
MAR 11:21 Kuɗukkǝ Bitrus i mbutǝ Yǝso kǝ ɗar shuɓwaɗiyu a farǝle ndakǝnwa: "Malɗǝm, kǝllu shuɓwandǝ sǝɓandundǝ tǝ hanngalǝ shunda hweraɗi paɗ miraɗi."
MAR 11:22 Ngǝmang Yǝso kimshechi'en wa: "Nam tǝ fǝrkitta mbǝnda Fara.
MAR 11:23 Ni mbwa'a kittǝkǝna kuni, chikawun ndannga shohlayiya wa, 'thla'u hǝmu hur hawuriyu, nan hǝmtǝsi. Paɗ waat kǝ fǝrnǝkit kǝna sǝtkichu, mǝninǝ tǝ hanɗǝkiketǝ chap chap wa.
MAR 11:24 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn nja mbwa'anda kuni, chika mǝ katuni hur hwanda, ma firuni kitsi tepa mbishuni, nan sokta innuni.
MAR 11:25 Paɗ ma thleruni hi kuna hwanda, ma yunǝ si natuni tǝnda a hurhanɗǝkiketa, kǝ kaluni ndǝhi, kǝ thlǝm shinnuni ti naka hur afshi nan kala ɓǝɓichitfechengnuni kunǝhi.
MAR 11:26 Paɗ ma kalawuni ɓǝɓichitfechengnanda kandǝhiwa, shinnuni hur afshi ngu kala ɓǝɓichitfechengnuni kunihiwa.
MAR 11:27 Ngǝrkǝ nda yimta Urshelima. Nak Yǝso wi'yandǝ kapat hura'a Farǝhi, pǝktat Pǝrischǝ tǝ pǝktat malɗǝmcha fichile la sakang kus tǝ tǝrmbandaɗi, tǝ fa ɓanita ɓaknda ɓǝɗ'en.
MAR 11:28 Ndangndǝwa: "Mbǝsku alchit sǝt ichinatya ayi? Wun fǝrukǝ mbanda kǝ sǝni kanda?"
MAR 11:29 Ngǝmang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Ni sahami kuni ǝrta, ma fǝrinduni ngǝmkǝn kani ɓwa'anda kuni ndu wun fǝrikǝ alchit ichi nati sǝtya.
MAR 11:30 Ɓwa'ami ɓǝskǝ Yohanna alchit sa Baptisma nofcha ayi mɓǝnda Farǝ wa, ndu ɓǝɗa nifa?"
MAR 11:31 Tǝrkaakǝndǝ halǝi'nda tinnanda mǝnat ma ndata? Ma ngǝmandǝm wa ɓǝnda Fara, nan ndatwa mǝ sǝk fǝruchituni kitta Yohanna?
MAR 11:32 Paɗ ma ɗendǝm wa ɓǝnda nifa kanda lechanda nofcha kǝthlǝm tǝrkǝ nofchuwa, Yohanna tapǝnaa nakǝn.
MAR 11:33 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝnda Yǝso wa: "Sǝnwaniwa. "Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Njang paɗ ngi mbwa'andakuni ndi tǝ witǝ alchit mǝ la sittǝ pǝktat torchiyawa."
MAR 12:1 Tǝrkaakǝ Yǝso shunandǝ kandǝ tǝ sakǝt shundǝ ndakǝnwa: "Nifǝsǝ nat hitǝ inabi ensi, tauraǝn hi tǝ thlara, rekǝn mbǝt yimmandǝ hwanchi inabi tǝkǝnsi, a tinkǝn kǝtǝn pu hitǝkǝnhar. Fǝrang na funǝ fa huɗatkǝn, kana pǝɗata hachahai somǝn.
MAR 12:2 Saakǝ farǝ ɗamhwanchi inabi tǝkǝn, thlǝnkǝn mafat'en har ǝrtǝ kǝ mbǝɗa fichile tǝr kǝ hitiyu, kǝthlǝm kǝ thlangndǝ hwanchi inabi chiyu a hitǝkǝn.
MAR 12:3 Fa tǝr hitǝkǝn kǝsagndǝ mafaɗiyu tǝpangnda, kalkǝndǝndǝhi pǝɗakǝn har chaa.
MAR 12:4 Ngǝrkǝ lǝ hitiyu thlǝnna mafata kandǝ somǝn, erkǝndǝndi tǝpangnda in, sangndǝ ǝnnat harǝ fata.
MAR 12:5 Ngǝrkǝna thlǝn yuna, leya paɗ mbǝllangnda. Nakǝn kichu tǝ yakat fichile thlǝntǝn, funǝ tǝ tǝpangnda kanda funǝ tǝ mbǝllangndǝ kanda.
MAR 12:6 A tahkǝn nifǝ ǝrta, hwan lelǝ mbǝntǝn fatkǝn ka'ǝn. A mweshitkǝn lǝ hitiyu thlǝnkǝn ndi kǝ mbǝɗengnanda tǝ yarǝwa kittǝkǝn nanda fǝra mwanda hwe'engna.
MAR 12:7 Fichile tǝrkǝ hitiyu ndangndandaniwa, Ale na sokta lǝ hitǝkǝnya a ɓama ɓǝma ɓǝllanda, kǝ sok hitǝkǝna i'nǝm.
MAR 12:8 Kǝssangnda a ɓǝllangnda, muhangndi murrut kǝnaɗi kǝ ɗiffitǝ hitǝkǝn."
MAR 12:9 Sahang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Saǝnkunifǝwa mǝnat lǝ hitiyu sǝta? Ni mbwa'anda kuni-nan mbǝlandǝ fa hundechiniyu kǝ fǝraǝn hitikǝna funǝ somǝn.
MAR 12:10 Tamwuni changngandǝ iya hur yarat shiwuncha Farǝwowa? Ngwiyi chertǝ fatinda sokka kukuwun tinda.
MAR 12:11 Ndǝsǝta Lǝmwandǝniyu, paɗ ǝnat pǝɗandǝ kǝmfa hwanichengnǝm.
MAR 12:12 Pǝktat fatǝr mbanda yahkǝndǝsa kǝsandǝ Yǝso kǝthlǝm mbǝssandǝwa fǝrkǝn sakǝt ɓǝɓi fa huɗechiniyu kǝ ɗar inchengnanda. Anakǝn kanda lechanda nofchi oiyu, kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn mallangnda pǝɗaknda.
MAR 12:13 Farǝle, thlǝnkǝ pǝktechǝ funa hur Farisiyawecha tǝ nofcha Hiridus, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsangndǝ chit'hansara Yǝso hi, a hur shiwunchi nat na mbuta ɓah nanda kǝsanda.
MAR 12:14 Satengnanda, ndangndǝwa: "Malɗǝm, shinani wa sokǝn lǝkitchita. Nofchǝ uf ǝrta mbǝɗeku yah i'ndekusǝwa. Lasakawu mbanda Fara ɗi a ɗar kitchita. Nakǝnya mbwa'ana kani keekesi kǝ kwanani chamta ɓǝɗa Kaisar kapat kutura Romacha ndu nga keekesuwa?
MAR 12:15 Anakǝn a mbǝssa Yǝso sakta kohat nofchǝkǝn, ndangnakandǝwa: "Kǝthlǝmmǝ natuni ndǝfi kantara mban? Ɓamitǝn hanndǝmbǝlta Romawecha kǝ ni."
MAR 12:16 Ndǝkǝn ɓandǝndǝ ǝrta, sahkǝnwa, mirshingngiya tǝ thlǝmmǝ ɗarkǝnya i wuni?" Ndangndǝwa: "I Kaisar."
MAR 12:17 Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Fǝramna Fara i naka i Fara paɗ fǝranguni Kaisar i naka i Kaisar." Pǝɗang ǝnatkǝn kandǝfǝ ka'ǝn tǝ ngǝmtǝ'en.
MAR 12:18 Ɓak Sadukiyawecha mbǝs Yǝso, pǝktat fa tǝrmbanda fichile ndakwa thlatǝsa ɗiffitǝ mǝrtaɗǝwa. Sahangndǝmi tǝ ndatwa:
MAR 12:19 "Malɗǝm, yarang Musa kus tiya kanisi ndatwa, ma mir hwanman nifǝ kǝ hishnifa, meltǝ nuhnifihi nga hwechi'ensuwa, hwanmankǝn kǝ hishnifa nan kǝna reta kǝ ngalaǝn hwecha hwanmankǝntisǝ mǝrkǝyu, kǝthlǝm kǝɗa thlǝm hwanmankǝna mban.
MAR 12:20 Hwanmanchisi muɗ kǝ hishcha, hwalat'hwankǝn thlekǝn perra, mǝrkǝn malutǝ hwehiwa,
MAR 12:21 Chapatǝkǝn tǝrkǝn nuhmuruɗiyu kǝ nuhkǝn, mǝlan paɗ mǝrkǝn malutǝ hwehiwa. Sokkǝn kichu tǝ mǝkkatǝkǝn.
MAR 12:22 Nakna mban kichuyu tuɓwaǝn hwanmanchi muɗyu malundǝ hwehiwa. A mweshitmikǝn ɓak nuhiyu mǝrta.
MAR 12:23 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn mbwa'ana kani, a thlata mǝmatcha nakna nat kǝ nuh wuni? Kǝthlǝm ufndǝ muɗ reɗndǝ tǝndi."
MAR 12:24 Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Ndǝkǝn sǝk la suchituni keeke kǝthlǝm sǝnwuni yarat shunda Faruwa, Paɗ sǝnwuni alchita Farǝwa.
MAR 12:25 Thlahmbǝɗi nat mǝmatcha thlata, mwa'u hishcha ret nishchǝwa, nishchi paɗ mwa'u ficha fǝrkanda kanwa. Naknda soktǝ nda fathlǝncha Fara hur'afshi.
MAR 12:26 Ɗar pathlǝ thlata mǝmatcha, awi tamwuni changnganda a hur ɗelwercha Musa wowa, a hur kusheng shiwun hurhwelii kǝskǝ hwatyu? Ndatwa njang naka Fara Ibrahim, Ishaku tǝ paɗ i' Yakubu."
MAR 12:27 Mǝlan nga Fara mǝmatchǝwa, i' fa shisshingcha. Shiɗɗuni i'nguchik Keeke."
MAR 12:28 Ərta hur malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kussa Musa ɗi, thlarkǝnhi mbǝnniyu nakna sǝkkanda halǝ'i'ndǝ tǝ ndani. Mbǝssaǝn tǝndatwa Yǝso firtǝ ngǝmtǝ ndiichin, sahkǝnwa: "Yen kus tǝni cheka nat mwanchina hur kuschi ufya?"
MAR 12:29 Ngǝmang Yǝso wa: "Le nak mwanchin ndǝkǝn naka, Sǝkama, Kunang Israilawecha, Lǝmwanda Farengnǝm mǝlan ǝrta na Lǝmwandǝ ndak.
MAR 12:30 Waat kǝ mbǝnnǝfat Lǝmwanda Fareku tǝ hanndǝkiketǝku uf, tǝ shisshingteku uf, tǝ yareku uf tǝ paɗ alchiɗeku uf.'
MAR 12:31 Chapatǝkǝn paɗ ndǝkǝn naka, 'Kǝ yahnǝ le nattuni nduknduk nda i'yahtu i'ndeku.' Nga kussi si mbǝrangnga fichilehiya tǝ mwandǝwa."
MAR 12:32 Ndǝkǝn ngǝrandǝ malɗǝmti la sakangnga ɗǝwa: "Keeke mbuutu malɗǝm. Mbwi nǝ kittǝkǝn ndatwa Farǝ ǝrta yunǝsǝ paɗwa.
MAR 12:33 Paɗ ashini ndiichinsi kǝ yah fichindǝ tǝ hanɗǝkiketǝ uf tǝ mbǝssandengnǝ uf, tǝ alchit uf, tǝ paɗ kǝ yahnǝ fichile natuni nduknduk nda i yahtu i'ndeku. Ndǝkǝn nak ndiichin oi sheraɗa fǝr us'i'chi tǝ fǝr pofǝnti yahtǝ ficha hur kustǝkǝn."
MAR 12:34 Kǝ mbǝsandǝ Yǝso wa nifiniyu a mbǝssaɗǝ ngǝmtǝ'en tǝ ɗathla, ndaǝnwa: "Nganaku lanngǝ tǝ kuturichitta Farǝwa. "Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn yunǝsǝ sǝk alchit hanndǝkiketǝ kǝ ngǝrǝn sahhami paɗwa.
MAR 12:35 Nak Yǝso sakandaɗa hur kapat hura'a Fara, sahkǝnwa: "Tǝkǝni lanat malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kus Musaɗi ndatwa, "kǝrǝsti hweya Dauda nakǝn?
MAR 12:36 Kǝthlǝm Dauda tǝ i'ndi'en a hur Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, ndakǝnwa: "Lǝmwanda ndangna Lǝmwandengnǝwa, sokuhi tǝ harsǝmtengna, kǝ fari nati ndǝf atikrechǝuwa ka sarǝcheku."
MAR 12:37 Dauda tǝ i'ndi'en eɗtǝndǝwa Lǝmwanda, tǝ kǝnǝ natna sokta hwe'en?" Kapat humtǝhi kathlǝmat tǝ mbǝndǝfa.
MAR 12:38 A sakandǝ'enaɗi ndakǝnwa: "Mbǝramsa malɗǝmcha fa sakaɗǝ kus tǝ tǝrɓandaɗi, la yahkǝnda witǝ tǝ pǝktat njelecha, kǝthlǝm kǝ ndang fichi ǝnna kandǝ tǝmwanda lumocha.
MAR 12:39 Paɗ la mbǝnangfata kanda kǝ mbǝsndi mbǝtsokchi ndiichin a mbǝt humta Yahudawechihi, tǝ mbǝt rǝɓcha.
MAR 12:40 Kandang harǝfatsǝwa la naknda sǝmandǝ i'cha ndǝlat nishchi mǝrtǝ hishchengnanda, tǝ hwandǝ toltol a hur nofcha nda ka fa tǝrmbanda. Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn nanda sat ɓahtǝ ka'ǝn."
MAR 12:41 Sokkǝ Yǝso nduktǝ yokǝt ngom hanndǝmbǝlta a kapat hura'a Fara, nakna nata kǝlandǝ nofchi naka muh hanndǝmbǝltengnanda hur yokǝt fǝr poffǝn tǝkǝn. Hurrumchi oi muhkǝ hanndǝmbǝlchǝ ka'ǝn.
MAR 12:42 A ɓak nuhnifǝ lǝ ɓahta le mǝrtǝ sǝmahha, somkǝn mbuthl kopo chap kǝ hurkǝn, le sokka pene ǝrta.
MAR 12:43 Ak Yǝso kimshechi'en kǝ thlǝmatkǝn, ndangna kandǝwa: "Kitchitkǝn nati mbwa'anda kuni, i'fǝrtǝ ndǝlat nuhhi mǝrtǝ sǝsmahya, mbǝranda i'chika wunhi uf.
MAR 12:44 Kandang ufya fǝrkǝnda hur kǝnechengnanda, mǝllan paɗ a hur ɓahtǝ'en fǝrtǝn uf i'tahangsa nat'en."
MAR 13:1 Nak Yǝso malǝ kapat hura'a Farǝhi, ǝrta hur kimshechi'en ndakǝnwa: "Malɗǝm, nu witǝ pǝktat ngwichiya tǝ pǝktat tinchiya."
MAR 13:2 Ndang Yǝso wa: "Nga neɗnǝ pǝktat tinchiyawa? Nga yunǝsǝ natficha mala mbǝnniyu chika ǝrtǝwa paɗ ngwisǝ nat ficha mala ɗar shekkǝn nguchitficha wuwellandǝhiwa."
MAR 13:3 Paɗ sokkǝnna ɗar shohla Zaitun le naka kǝllarǝ kapat hura'a Fara. Bitrus, Yakubu, Yohanna tǝ Andarawus ɓakndǝ i'chitnanda ɓuɓweeta sahangndǝwa:
MAR 13:4 "Mbwa'andǝna kani, kwat nat i'chiya sǝta? Mǝnaka sakǝtkǝn na chetǝwa a shee farǝ sǝta i'chiniya?"
MAR 13:5 Ngǝrkǝ Yǝso sǝwa, "Ndǝffam i'ndǝsi mǝ shekɗa yunǝ kuniwa.
MAR 13:6 Kǝthlǝm nofchǝ oi na ɓata hur thlǝmnǝ tǝ ndatwa, 'njang naka kǝrǝsti.' Nanda lǝm nofchǝ oi.
MAR 13:7 Paɗ ma shikunǝ pathlǝ mbecha tǝ kusheng mbecha, mǝ lechiɗuniwa. Waat i'chiniyu nat kǝssǝn kichu, paɗ mweshitkǝn sa'u kwandǝnwa.
MAR 13:8 Hǝmtǝ nan thla'anda hǝmtǝ fa, kuturichit paɗ nan thla'anda kuturichita fa. Na ficha sǝk hǝhǝrta hachahaifa mbechǝ somsomǝn a kisshita, tǝ paɗ na mita natsi. I'chininatyu tǝrka pwanchǝ kwaɗǝn, mwee funa ɓata.
MAR 13:9 "Kǝ sokuni tǝ tahhasǝfa ma i'chiniyu tǝrka thlata. Nanda ndǝttǝkuni kǝ mbǝt sakmicha, paɗ nanda tǝppanda kuni a mbǝt humta Yahudawechahi, paɗ nuni thlara ɓanitǝ pǝktat nofcha tǝ kuturcha kǝthlǝm thlǝmna, paɗ nuni mbǝs mba mbwa'a kusheng shunda kandǝ kǝ ɗar i'ndengna.
MAR 13:10 Kǝthlǝm kusheng shundǝ mbinchin nat ficha tǝrka ɓassanda hǝmchǝ nat.
MAR 13:11 Ma harandǝ kuni ɗǝɗndǝ tǝ kuni mbǝt shunda, mǝ thla'i hur in'chengnuni kǝ ɗar i'natuni mbutǝwa. Mbwa'am i'mbwa'andǝ Fara kuni a mbǝnniyu, kǝthlǝm nga kunang na shundǝwa Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗ ndak na shunda.
MAR 13:12 Paɗ hwanmanda nan fǝr hwanmankǝn kǝ ɓǝlang ficha, Shindǝ paɗ nan fǝr hwe'en, paɗ hwecha nanda thla'anda parchinandǝ fa, kǝ ɗǝfndǝ kǝ tǝkang fichǝ kandǝhi.
MAR 13:13 Paɗ chikawun nan cherǝ kuni kǝthlǝm thlǝmna. Paɗ le kǝrǝskǝ kǝ ndukwatkǝn nan hǝrǝkta.
MAR 13:14 "Farǝkǝnaɓata ma mbishuni ǝnat tǝkǝmta le na ɓat tǝ pwancha a thlerhi mbǝɗi kamuchiksi, (Lǝ changngatkǝn kǝ sǝnǝn): "Fichile naka Yahudiya kǝ rahnda shohlacha.
MAR 13:15 Le naka afshi a ɗar kǝnnda mǝ tǝriɗahai kǝ yimka huriwa nan tǝr ǝnwa.
MAR 13:16 Le naka hi mǝ ngǝriɗa huri wa nan tǝr ǝnat suptǝ'enwa.
MAR 13:17 Ai kǝmbǝɗa nishcha fichile tǝ hwechahur tǝ fichile tǝ hwecha hǝsǝr a hur munchiniyu.
MAR 13:18 Hwanama mǝ si ichiniyu a hur mbitǝuwa.
MAR 13:19 A thlah mbǝɗiniyu, na pwancha natsi le tamu chit ficha nata kǝ sǝt Farǝ kishita kǝ ɓukweya, paɗ ngu ficha ngǝrandǝwa kǝ ndukwatkǝn.
MAR 13:20 Manga i'nakǝn tahha Lǝmwandǝ hanmunchikǝnhiwa nifǝsi na hǝrǝktǝwa, Paɗ kǝthlǝm tachikǝnharti taatǝn, ndǝkǝn sǝk tahandǝn hanmunchikǝnhi.
MAR 13:21 Mǝnda yuna kuniwa, "Nama, a Kǝrǝstiya, ndu 'mǝlan taatiyu' mǝ fǝriɗuni kitsǝwa.
MAR 13:22 Kǝthlǝm fa lekchisi na chetakish wa kandang naka kǝrǝsti, tǝ tapǝnecha i'lekta, paɗ kǝnanda sǝt ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa kǝthlǝm kǝ shekɗangndǝ nofcha, manan sǝta chika tachikǝnhara Fara.
MAR 13:23 Kǝ ndǝfuni i'ndǝsi, mbwa'aɗi chikama kuni leɗya.
MAR 13:24 Ɗiffitǝ Pwanchini hanmunchiniyu, hwatfarǝ nan yimta hulta, ndǝrra'a ngu fǝr ɗwachitwa,
MAR 13:25 Handǝrechǝ paɗ nanda nata hǝhatta haya afshi, alchita afshi nan hǝhǝrtǝfa.
MAR 13:26 Ɗif fitǝkǝn chikawun nannat hweya nifa ɓata hur hussomɓa tǝ kapat alchit tǝ mwanda.
MAR 13:27 Kana thlǝn fathlǝnchi'en kǝ ngommangndǝ tachikǝn'en chika aya hurkishita, thlata ndukwat kukunchi fwaɗa a kishita thlata ndukwat kishitǝ kǝ le.
MAR 13:28 Nakǝnya sakam ǝna ɗar affǝt shuɓwata. Ma mbisshuni tirkeetǝ njarǝhi mǝla titita, kǝ sǝnunisǝwa fektǝ ndukhi.
MAR 13:29 Kichu paɗ, ma neɗnduni ichiya sǝta kǝ sǝnunisǝwa ɓat'en ndukhi mǝla mi kǝnnda.
MAR 13:30 Kitchitkǝn nati ɓwa'anda kuni, naɗihi nakǝnya ngu mbǝrtǝhiwa, sema shiɗ i'chinatyu.
MAR 13:31 Afshi tǝ kishita nanda thlǝrǝttaɗi, paɗ shundengnǝ ngu tamta thlǝrǝttaɗǝwa.
MAR 13:32 Paɗ nifǝsǝ sǝnkǝ farǝkǝn ndu hanthlikǝn kurmi fari nat i'chiniyu sǝta, chika fathlǝnchikǝna hur afshi ndu hwankǝn tǝ'i'ndǝ'en. Shindǝ sǝnkǝ ndak.
MAR 13:33 Nakǝn sǝnwuni fari nat farǝkǝna ɓatwa, sokam tǝ tahhasǝfa.
MAR 13:34 "Ɓata hweya nifa naknanat nda nifǝ na sǝt witǝ langnga, ma meltǝ huraahi, saka'ǝn tora mafechi'en, chika wun tǝ tor'en, ndangna lǝ pu mimbangkǝnharwa, kǝ ndǝfǝn i'ndǝsi kǝ fari natna ngǝrandǝ'in.
MAR 13:35 Chika kunang kǝ ndǝfuni i'ndǝsi, kǝthlǝm sǝnwuni fari nat lǝ hura'a ɓataɗǝwa, ndu farǝhufta, hurɗiffitǝ findǝkta, katǝt ɓǝta, mbahya ɓingta.
MAR 13:36 Ma ɓeɗ kurukchuk mǝ ɓiɗa mbǝsandǝ kuni saɓweniwa.
MAR 13:37 I la ɓwa'aɗi kuni, la ɓwa'ayi chikawuni kǝ sokuni tǝ tahhasǝfa."
MAR 14:1 Tahkǝ mundǝ chap kǝ safichǝ chohhǝmtala tǝ i'chi njohma le nguchit mehɗǝsafi'en. Le nak mwanchina hur pǝrischa tǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kussa ɗi, naknda kat mba kǝsandǝ Yǝso ɓuɓweeta kǝthlem kǝ ɓǝlangnda.
MAR 14:2 Kǝthlǝm lǝ ndakndǝwa: "Ngǝma sǝt iya hur njohhǝmiyawa, mǝni nofcha thla'andǝhur'i'nda."
MAR 14:3 Yǝso mǝla Betani hura'a Siman le nat tarkwindafi'en soh. Mǝla ɗar sǝm'ǝna, yimkǝ nuhnifǝsi tǝ kwescha kupat tahǝstǝfichi tǝ pundala, tǝ fiɗeta hurkǝn le nat satǝ'en mbinchinfa la atfichuwa nardi, la hiikǝfichǝ tǝ hanɗǝɓeltǝ oi, chaǝn kupaɗihiyu thlǝraǝn fiɗetkǝna Yǝso in.
MAR 14:4 Nofchi naka mbǝnniyu sǝɓkǝ hanɗǝkikecheng nandaɗi tǝ i sǝt nuhiyu, ndangndandaniwa: "Kǝthlemmǝ natna sǝɓandǝ fiɗeɗiɗǝ lahiitǝfichǝ tǝ hanɗǝɓeltǝ oi kicheya?
MAR 14:5 Matǝ hi'yangfichaɗiya manaficha mbǝs hanɗǝɓelta i sherangnga aru kumchit kum mǝkkan, kǝ fǝrangficha fa ɓahcha." Ɓokangnda nuhihiyu ka'ǝn.
MAR 14:6 Ndak Yǝso wa: "Malamǝn nuhhiniyu! Kǝthlemmǝ natuni ɗahandǝ'in? Shiɗtǝ'ǝn ndiichin.
MAR 14:7 Faɓahcha pware a hurnuni, nuni mbǝlla kǝsandakandǝsi chikakwat yahtuni. Paɗ nga njang tǝ kuni pwareewa.
MAR 14:8 Nuhhiya shiɗtǝ i natna mbǝla sita. Thlǝriɗǝ fiɗetafa a tah'saɗǝ faɗengnǝ kǝ fari natficha thlohita.
MAR 14:9 Kitchitkǝn mbwa'andi kuni, uf mbǝɗi nat nofcha ɓasǝ kusheng kashunda hur kishitǝ nat, nanda mbu i sǝt nuhhiya, kǝthlem kǝ kuɗukfichǝndi."
MAR 14:10 Yahuda Iskaryoti ǝrta hur kimshecha Yǝso kumkǝngǝrǝnsǝ chap, ɗǝkna mbǝɗa Pǝktat Pǝristchǝkǝn kǝthlǝm kǝ hi'yangka ɗi.
MAR 14:11 Sǝkkǝndǝ i yahtǝna sǝta naknda kwala, ndǝkǝn tahsaɗǝɗǝhiwa nani fǝrru hanɗǝɓǝlta. Mbǝnniyu ngagtǝ Yahuda kat mbayi natna hi'ya Yǝso kanda.
MAR 14:12 Saakǝ tǝrka farǝ chi njohǝm chohhǝmtala le nguchit mehnɗǝsa fi'en, le lǝ thlet fichǝ ɓurat hanshohrata, ndang kimshechi'enwa: "A ai yahtusi kǝ tahsukani mbǝt chi njohǝm chohhǝm talǝkǝnsi?"
MAR 14:13 A thlǝnkǝn kimshechi'en chap ndagnna kaɗewa: "Ɗama hur hǝmta, nuni kǝmtǝ tǝ nifǝ mǝla rǝf ɓǝt ama, kurunindi,
MAR 14:14 uf huri'i yimtǝn, ndangnguni lǝ hurikǝn wa: "Ndak malɗǝm wa a ai kǝtǝn romchi natti chi njohhǝm chohhǝmtala kanang tǝ kimshechengna?'
MAR 14:15 Nan cheɗa kapat kǝnnda kuni afshi le taptǝficha kǝ tahsangficha. Mbǝnniyu natuni tahsǝ njohǝmkǝna kǝmsi."
MAR 14:16 Kimshechiyu malkǝdǝ mbǝnnihiyu pǝɗaknda hur hǝmta, ɗǝknda mbisandǝ uf ichi sǝka nda i mbutǝ Yǝso. Tahsangndǝ chohhǝmtalǝkǝnhi.
MAR 14:17 Ɗiffitǝ hǝmta fara Yǝso tǝ kimshechi'en kum kǝngirǝnsǝ chap ɓaknda hurikǝn.
MAR 14:18 Kanda ɗar sǝm'ǝna, ndak Yǝso wa: "Kitchitkǝn nati mbwa'anda kuni, ǝrta hurnuni nan hi'itaɗi, le natani sǝm'ǝn tǝndi."
MAR 14:19 Kǝ sǝktǝ kimshechi'en kichu sǝɓkǝ hanɗekiketeng nandaɗi, tǝrƙaakǝnda sahandǝ ǝrtǝ ǝrta tǝ ndatwa: "Njang wa?"
MAR 14:20 Ngǝrkǝnsuwa, ǝrta hurnuni kumkǝngǝrǝnsi chap le natani sǝmta hur tǝɓi ǝrta.
MAR 14:21 Andiya hweya nifǝ nan ɓǝɗata, nda i yarandǝfichǝ kushengkǝnhi nattǝ kichu, ai kǝ mbǝɗa nifi yahkǝsa fǝr hweya nifa! Kweshkǝna ngǝtufichǝndǝwa."
MAR 14:22 Naknda ɗar sǝm'ǝna, tǝrkǝn njohma saǝn usoko Fara, chichaǝnhi fǝrangna kimshechi'en, ndagna kandǝwa: "Thlama; leya faɗegna."
MAR 14:23 Ɗiffitǝkǝn tǝrkǝn tǝpsat ama, a sǝkǝn usoko, a fǝrangna kanda sakndǝ ufnda
MAR 14:24 "Leya fwarengna le thlerandiɗi kǝthlem nofchǝ oi."
MAR 14:25 "Tǝni mbwa'a kitchitkǝna kuni thlatǝ nakǝnya kǝ mban mwaawi sat ǝnwa magnga fari natisat yuwakǝnna hur mwanda Farǝ wa."
MAR 14:26 In'kǝndǝ imsha, pǝɗaknda kish kǝ shohla Zaitun.
MAR 14:27 Kanda ɗar wita ndang Yǝso kandǝwa: "Uffuni nuni rahta maluni nji i'chitna. Nda i yarandǝ fichǝ ndatwa, 'Ni ɓǝlandǝ la hǝrǝmta, shohrechikǝn nanda wuwelǝhi.'
MAR 14:28 Ɗǝk na mban tǝndandǝ wa ɗiffitǝ thlatengna tǝ shisshingta ni lata Galili mǝ kunang".
MAR 14:29 Ndang Bitrussa Yǝso wa: "Njang ngi malǝsǝhiwa chika rahkǝ tahchikǝn nat."
MAR 14:30 Ndang Yǝso Bitrus wa: "Kitchitkǝn nati mbu'uta fiɗǝkiya kǝ kukwara ɗektǝ chap nu kurɓadǝ halǝ indǝ mǝkkan tǝ ndat wa sǝnunǝ njiwa."
MAR 14:31 Chika tǝ kichu nak Bitrussa kurɓandǝ mbuta tǝ alchita ndatwa, chika tǝna ficha tǝkkandǝkǝmhi hwaa ngi tamta halǝ i'ndǝwa sǝnwisǝwowa!" Natnda ndakndǝ kichu.
MAR 14:32 Ndǝkǝn saatǝnda mbiɗǝ la atfǝchiwa Getsemani. Ndangna kimshechi'en wa: "Sokamhi mbiɗya, kǝ ɗi hwanda."
MAR 14:33 Tǝrkǝn Bitrus, Yakubu tǝ Yohanna, tǝrkaakǝn sǝk ɓahtǝ ka'ǝn, mirfat'ennaɗi.
MAR 14:34 Ndangnakandǝwa: "Shisshingtengna mǝlla nat pwanchǝ ka'ǝn. Thlaramhi mbiɗya kǝ nuni kǝlathi."
MAR 14:35 Ɗǝkna mban nguɗeh hǝmkǝnhi hachaya nakna hwandǝ tǝ ndatwa: "Ma mbandǝsi mǝ niɗi pwene ti naka ɓatyuwa."
MAR 14:36 Ndakǝnwa: "Papa, Papa, ǝnsǝ nak 'yang'yang nga mbǝɗekuwa. Tǝrran pwene tiɗaɗi fi'engnǝya. Chika tǝ kichu nga i yahti natu sǝtwa iu'wa.
MAR 14:37 Ndǝkǝn ngǝrandǝn ina thlemat kimshechi'en ɗǝkna mbǝsandǝ kanda sa ɓweni. Ndangna Bitrus wa: "Bitrus, nanna sa ɓweni? Awi nguna mbǝlla soktǝ tolla a kǝlat chika i hanthliktǝ ǝrtǝwa?
MAR 14:38 Sokam tǝ tahasǝfa kǝ nuni hwanda kǝthlǝm mǝhǝmiɗuni hur yah'ichǝwa. Paɗ tir shemeɗa nat tǝkichu fatkǝn tǝrruwa."
MAR 14:39 Ngǝrkǝnna ngǝrrandǝ'in kǝthlǝm kǝ hwanin, nakna ngǝrrandǝ shuni shuwuntǝn soh.
MAR 14:40 Ngǝrkǝna ɓata thlemat nanda ɓakna mbǝsandǝ kanda saɓweni, kǝthlǝm uf nda nǝhǝɗ ɓweni hwanichengnandǝ ka'ǝn, ɓahkǝndǝ i nan nda mbwa'anda.
MAR 14:41 Ngǝrkǝna thlǝmatnanda i mǝkkatǝkǝn, ndangna kandǝwa: "Paaya mwakuni saɓweni kǝnuni yipta? Shik kichu, shee farǝkǝn. A fir fichi hweeya nifa kǝ hara fa ɓǝɓichitfata.
MAR 14:42 Thla'ama, tama. nama, nifina hiiyandaɗaɗi mǝlanya!"
MAR 14:43 Chatkichuyu, kǝ nanna ngǝlandǝ mi'en, ɓak Yahuda ǝrta hur kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap tǝkǝn tǝ nofchǝ oi tǝ thlohcha tǝ sǝssalcha, pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kusaɗi, tǝ pǝktechi thlenkǝ kanda.
MAR 14:44 Kǝthlǝm nifi hi'yangngaɗiyu teppa mweshandǝ tǝ ndatwa: "Le natti mbǝnfatkǝnyu mǝlan naka nifǝkǝn. Kǝ kǝsangnguni kǝ pǝɗuni tǝnda har."
MAR 14:45 Kǝ saatǝn ɗǝkna mbǝs Yǝso ndaǝnwa: "Lǝ hura'a." Nakna mbǝnfatkǝn tǝ kǝmmiya.
MAR 14:46 Chatkichuyu njo'angnda kǝsangnda.
MAR 14:47 Ərta hurnandǝ le nak kit, kǝtkǝn thlohtǝ'en chathlaǝn thlemata mafata kapat Pǝrist tǝkǝnnaɗi.
MAR 14:48 Ndang Yǝso kandǝwa, ɓakuni tǝ thlohcha tǝ sǝssalcha kǝthlem kǝ kǝsikuni nda tǝni hara?
MAR 14:49 Hanmunchikǝn kǝm nang tǝ kuni nja sakandaɗa hur kapat hura'a Fara, nattǝ kichu kǝsiwuniwa. Sǝk fichǝ kichuyu kǝthlǝm kǝ nǝhɗang fichǝ i mbutǝ laulawatkǝn.
MAR 14:50 Mbǝnniyu ɓak kimshechi'ena cherǝndǝfa, rahkǝnda.
MAR 14:51 Han kimshasi tǝ ɗǝ supta fa, kuwurkǝn ndi. Njo'angnda,
MAR 14:52 mǝllan mallaǝn ɗǝ supkǝna kanda, rahkǝn tamkwal.
MAR 14:53 Mbǝnniyu Pǝɗak ndǝ tǝ Yǝso kǝ mbǝɗa kapat pǝrist. Nat pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ fambanicha tǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kussa ɗi ngomkǝnda thlǝmmatkǝn.
MAR 14:54 Bitrus nakan langnga nattǝkichu kuwurkǝnndi, kǝ hura'a kapat pǝrist tǝkǝn sokkǝnna thlemat fa pu hurikǝnhar nakna tǝk hwata.
MAR 14:55 Mbǝnniyu pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ pǝktat fasakmichǝ uf nda naknda kat sakǝt shuni nannda ɗǝftǝ kǝ ɗar Yǝso, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsndǝ kǝ ɓǝlangnda, nattǝkichu mbǝsundǝ mbandǝwa.
MAR 14:56 Paɗ nofchǝ oi shuwunkǝ lekta ɗar i'ndi'en paɗ ɓu miyengnandǝ ǝrtǝwa.
MAR 14:57 Ɗiffitǝkǝn paɗ thlaakǝ funǝ tǝ lektǝ kǝ ɗar i'ndi'en ndatwa:
MAR 14:58 "Shikanindi ndatwa, 'ni hokkandǝ kapat hura'a Farǝhi le tintǝ fichǝ tǝ harcha, paɗ hur mundǝ mǝkkan ni tinnanda kwarkǝn nga tǝ harchǝwa."
MAR 14:59 Chika tǝ kichu shundengnandǝ ɓu ǝrtǝwa.
MAR 14:60 A mbǝnniyu thlaakǝ kapat pǝrist thlarkǝnhi kit kǝ hurɗifitǝnanda sahaǝn mi Yǝso tǝ ndatwa: "Nga ngǝmtekusǝwowa? A ɗar witǝ i'chi mbutǝ ficha i'ndekuyawowa?"
MAR 14:61 Ngaskǝn ɓa ngǝrawusǝwa. Ngǝrkǝ kapat pǝrist tǝkǝnna sahandǝ paɗ: "Sokǝn naka Kǝrǝsti, hweya Farǝwa?"
MAR 14:62 Ndak Yǝso wa: "Njang." "Tǝpaɗ nuni nat hweya nifa ɗassa harsǝmta le nak mwanchin mǝla ɓatahaya hur afshi hur husomba'a."
MAR 14:63 Ndǝkǝn thlǝthlahandǝ kapat pǝrist tǝkǝn njela'enaɗi, ndakǝnwa mǝnatma ngǝrkata mbǝɗ'en paɗi.
MAR 14:64 "Sǝkam witǝ njir faɗi sǝtǝn: "Mǝ nattuni?" Uf nda thlangndǝ kitahi tǝ ndatwa keekesi kǝ mǝrkaɗi.
MAR 14:65 Chatkichuyu tǝrkaakǝ funa chaha yahtafa, kǝnangndǝ hwanichi'en, tǝtǝpangndǝfa, ndangndǝwa: "Mbwa'ana kani wun tǝpkǝsa." Fa pu kapat hurikǝnhar mbwaltakǝnndi.
MAR 14:66 Bitrus mǝllan ndassa hachahaya fǝlhura'a, ɓak nuhhwee ǝrta hur mafecha kapat pǝrist.
MAR 14:67 Nakkǝn Bitrussa tǝk hwata, nakna kǝllandǝ ndakǝnwa: "Sokǝnma, kunang nak tǝ Yǝso Lǝnazarattaɗiyu." "Ndaǝnwa kunang nak tǝ Yǝso Lǝnazarattaɗiya.
MAR 14:68 Paɗ halkǝn i'ndǝ ndakǝnwa: "Njang sǝnwi i natu shunda ɗarkǝnwa. Paɗ mbǝssawiwa!" Cheknakish kǝ mi mbanga. Chatkichuyu kukwarkǝ ɗekta.
MAR 14:69 Mafat nuhhwaniyu nakǝnndi, ngǝrkǝn ndanda fichile kitkitta mbǝnniyuwa: "Nifiya mǝlla hur nanda."
MAR 14:70 Ngǝrkǝna halǝ i'nda. Toppǝ kicha paɗ fichile kitkityu ndangnda Bitruswa: "Kitchitkǝn sokǝn paɗ naku ǝrta hurnanda, kǝthlǝm sokǝn lǝ Galiliyawata."
MAR 14:71 Nakna cherǝ i'ndi'en kǝnna nata at'i'chimi tǝ ndatwa: "Sǝnwi nifi natuni shunda ɗarkǝnwa."
MAR 14:72 Chatkichuyu kukwarkǝ ɗekta i chapatǝkǝn. Kuɗukkǝ Bitrus tǝ shuni mbwa'andǝ Yǝso ndatwa: "Kǝ kukwara ɗǝktǝ chap nu kurɓandǝ halǝ i'ndǝ mǝkkan ndatwa sununǝ njiwa." Kǝ kuɗǝktǝn shuwunkǝn chat nakna tita.
MAR 15:1 Kǝnat ɓǝta wenda mbingtǝ tung, pǝktat pǝristchikǝn tǝ pǝktat fambanicha tǝ malɗǝmchǝ fa sakandǝ kussa Musa ɗi, tǝ pǝktat fasakmicha tahsangndǝ hi. Ɗǝkǝn kǝnandǝɗǝ Yǝso pǝɗakndǝ tǝnda mbaniti Bilatus.
MAR 15:2 Sahang Bilatus mi Yǝso tǝ ndatwa: "Sokǝn naka kutur Yahundawechǝwa?" Ngǝmaǝn'en tǝ ndatwa: "A mbwinǝ keeke."
MAR 15:3 Nak pǝktat pǝristchikǝnna nata muh hanharkǝn kǝ ɗar i'chǝ oi.
MAR 15:4 Ngǝrkǝ Bilatus sahami tǝ ndatwa: "Nga ngǝmtǝsi natu ngǝrtǝsǝwowa? Nu yakat kohat shuwunchi nannda mbutǝ kǝ ɗar i'ndekuyu."
MAR 15:5 Yǝso paaya ngǝrausǝwa, pǝɗang ǝnnatkǝn Bilatus fa.
MAR 15:6 Ma shee farǝ chohhǝmtala Bilatus lakalkǝn nifǝhi ǝrta hur pursunacha le sahtǝnda.
MAR 15:7 Hur fa thlahur in'chi pursunayu yunǝsǝ mbǝlkǝfata le la atfichǝwa Barnabas.
MAR 15:8 Ɓak ngom nofchǝ oi tǝrkaakǝndǝ hwanandǝ Bilatus kǝ saǝn kandǝ nda i'sǝntǝnhi tǝ sandǝ kanda.
MAR 15:9 Ndǝkǝn ngǝmmandǝn engnanda: "Yahkunisi kǝ kallayi kutur Yahundawecha kuni hiwa?"
MAR 15:10 Kǝthlem mbǝssaɗiwa tǝ nan'nda sǝrǝhndi, ndǝkǝn nat pǝktat pǝristchikǝna fǝrndi.
MAR 15:11 Pǝktat pǝristchikǝn chikangndǝ nofchikǝn, kweshkǝn kǝkalaǝn Barnabassa kandǝ hi.
MAR 15:12 Ngǝrkǝ Bilatussa ndanda kandǝwa: "Mǝnati sandǝ nifi lǝ atuniwa kutur Yahundachiya?"
MAR 15:13 Ngǝrkǝndǝ hwata tǝ ndatwa: "Kukanhi!"
MAR 15:14 Ndang Bilatussa kandǝwa: "Kǝthlem mi? witǝ ɓǝɓifat mǝ sǝtǝn?" Chika tǝ kichu thla'angndǝ mburat uf ndǝ tǝ alchita ndakndǝwa: "Kukamǝn hi!"
MAR 15:15 Bilatus yahkǝnsa tǝra hur ngom nofchihiyu kalaǝn Barnabassa kandǝ hi. Ɗifitǝ tǝppi tǝpandǝ fathlǝrhwecha Yǝso fǝrangna kanda kǝ kukwangndǝhi.
MAR 15:16 Pǝɗak fathlǝrhwechǝ tǝndi kǝ huri kuturichita, kǝ hur huri kuturichita, akndǝ tahǝt fathlǝrhwatkǝn nat.
MAR 15:17 Pangndǝ njeli kuturichit ngah nda am fi mbillehsheta, tahǝskǝndǝ fwa'in ndahha pangnda in.
MAR 15:18 Tǝrkaakǝndǝ nda ǝnna: "Mbwarǝ shisshingta kǝ mbǝɗeku kutur Yahundawecha!"
MAR 15:19 Naknda rǝrro'a ndǝffa'in tǝ sǝssala, naknda chahha yahta fa, tǝpaɗ naknda kopandǝhi wa tǝnnda fǝra mwanda.
MAR 15:20 Kǝ mweshandǝndǝ njirndi, kǝtangndǝ njeli'ihi fi'en ngah nda am fi mbillehshetyu pangndǝ ikǝn. Pǝɗakndǝ tǝndǝ kǝthlem kǝ ɗǝnda kukwandǝhi ɗar palita.
MAR 15:21 Kanda ɗar mbǝrtǝhi tǝ Yǝso mǝlla rǝf palitǝ'en, chat a nifiya lenat thlemkǝn wa Siman lǝ Sayirinta, shinnda Alekzanda tǝ Rufus, mǝla ɓata thlet hǝmta ɗǝfkǝndǝndi waat kǝtǝrǝn palita Yǝso.
MAR 15:22 Pǝɗakndǝ tǝ ndi kǝ mbǝɗi lǝ atfichǝwa Golgota (sakatkǝn wa mbǝt tǝɓ i'nda").
MAR 15:23 A mbǝnniyu fǝrrangndǝ am'innabi le kurtandǝndǝhi tǝ mur, cherkǝn sata.
MAR 15:24 Kukangndǝhi ɗar palita, sakangndǝ njela'en hi thlerǝnanda, naknda tata kǝthlem kǝ sǝnndǝ i'nat chikawuna mbǝsta.
MAR 15:25 Kukangndǝhi tǝ hanthlǝktǝ hanherta i'ɓingta.
MAR 15:26 A yarandǝ ǝnat sǝnkǝn kǝ ɗarkǝn: "Kutur Yahudawecha."
MAR 15:27 Mbǝnniyu kukangndǝ hi tǝ harchǝ chap, ǝrta harsǝmtǝ'en ǝrta hishingtǝ'en.
MAR 15:28 Leya ndǝkǝn na nǝhata laulawathi, ndakwa a thlǝkfichǝnda hur fa cherǝ thlǝn i mbutǝ kus."
MAR 15:29 Nat nofchi naka mbǝrtǝhi tǝ mbǝnniyu, naknda hǝhrandǝ i'nda kǝnnda shuwun ɓǝɓi icha ɗar Yǝso tǝ ndatwa: "Yu! sokǝn ti ndakwa, nu hokandǝ kappat hura'a Farǝhi paɗ kǝ tinangna hur munchǝ mǝkkan,
MAR 15:30 hǝrkandǝn i'ndeku hacha, kǝ tǝrnahaya ɗar pali'iya!"
MAR 15:31 Kichu paɗ pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kussa ɗi, lǝ naknda shuwun njirndi a thlerǝnanda, lǝ naknda ndatwa: "Hǝrkaɗǝfuna: "Ngu hǝrkandǝ i'ndi'enwa.
MAR 15:32 Kǝ tǝr Kǝrǝsti haya kutur Isra'ilawecha, kǝ tǝrkahaya ɗar palikǝn chetchetya, tǝkichu natma nata kǝ fǝrǝmkita ɗarkǝn." Fichile kukandǝ fichikandǝ tǝndi i'erandǝfa.
MAR 15:33 Hanthlǝktǝ kumkǝngǝrǝnsi chap i hur fara, ngǝlang hultǝ hachahaikǝn nat, kǝ hanthlǝktǝ mǝkan i farǝhufta.
MAR 15:34 Kǝ saatǝ hanthliktǝ mǝkan, tik Yǝso tǝ kapat mburata, ndakǝnwa: "Eloi, Eloi, lama sabatani?" sakǝtkǝn wa: "Ai Fara, Ai Fara, mǝsǝk chertunji?"
MAR 15:35 Fichile thlarkǝ nduk tǝndi kǝsǝktǝndǝ kichu ndakndǝwa: "Sǝkama mǝla at Iliya."
MAR 15:36 Rahkǝ yuna hurnanda ɗǝkna tǝnnandǝ ǝn nda hussunnjela'a, tǝ am tamnda fakkǝna sǝssala, fǝrangna Yǝso kǝ san, ndakndǝwa, "Pwa'ama, kǝnǝm ma na Iliya ɓata tǝrandahaya ɗar pali'i'ya."
MAR 15:37 Chatkichu shuwunkǝ Yǝso tǝ kapat mburata, kanna kalǝ shisshingtǝ'enhi.
MAR 15:38 Kuwuri kǝntǝ ficha kapat hura'a Fara thlahkǝn hi chap, thlata ɗarkǝn kǝ kakǝn.
MAR 15:39 Kapat fathlǝehwechǝkǝn le nak kitta mbǝniyu a kǝlanda nakǝn mǝri'mǝrtǝn ndakǝnwa: "Kitchitkǝn nifiya hweya Farǝ nakǝn!"
MAR 15:40 Nishchǝsi thlarkǝ langnga naka nat kanda nishchǝkǝn nda Maryamu le ɓaka a Magdala, Maryamu man Yakubu le nak nguɗɗeh mǝ Yusufu, tǝ Salomi.
MAR 15:41 Kandang kuwurkǝndǝ, naɗi natnda hachahai Galili, kwirndǝndǝ tǝpaɗ fǝrandǝ mwanda, tǝ yakat nishchi oiyu ɗǝfkǝndǝ kǝ Urshelimayu kanda mbǝnniyu.
MAR 15:42 Sǝk farǝ hufta, ɓakna soktǝ kǝ farǝ tahasǝfa kǝthlǝm ishkichitkǝn farǝ yipta Yahudawecha,
MAR 15:43 Nifǝsi lǝ atfichǝwa Yusufu ɓakna hǝmǝt Armatiya, nakǝn ǝrta hur fichile lǝ fǝrandǝ fichǝ mwanda, lenaka pu mwanda Fara, sǝkǝn alchit hanɗǝkiketa ndǝkna mbǝnda Bilatus, sahaǝn murǝt Yǝso.
MAR 15:44 Pǝɗang ǝnatkǝn Bilatus fa ndu a teppa mirri, thlǝnkǝn kǝ angfichile nak mwachina hur fathǝrhwechǝkǝn, sahaǝn miya: "Tǝkit Yǝso teppa mirwa?"
MAR 15:45 Kǝ sǝktǝn kichu miya kapat fathlǝrhwechǝkǝn tǝ ndatwa teppa mirri, fǝraǝn murǝt fatkǝnna Yusufu.
MAR 15:46 Hiikǝ Yusufu njeli thlohmurta, tǝraǝn fata Yǝso haya, fwaɗaǝn tǝ njeli thlohmurundǝyu, ɗǝfkǝna hur kwata le retficha fa ngwiya. Pwatkǝn paplata ngǝlaǝn mi kwatkǝnsi.
MAR 15:47 Maryamu le ɓaka a Magdala tǝ Maryamu man Yusufu neɗndǝ mbǝɗi hunandǝ ficha.
MAR 16:1 Kǝ mbǝrkǝ farǝ yipta Yahundawechǝ hi, Maryamu le ɓaka a Magdala, tǝ Maryamu man Yakubu, tǝ Salomi, hiikǝndi fiɗeɗi nat satǝ'en mbinchinfa kǝthlem kǝ ɗǝnda pa'anda Yǝso fa.
MAR 16:2 A farǝ Lati ɓingtǝ tung, kǝnat fara cheta pǝɗaknda mi kwatkǝn.
MAR 16:3 Nangnda ndandandani chiuwa: "Wun na pwatandǝ paplatkǝn engnǝmaɗa mi kwatkǝn?"
MAR 16:4 Kǝ thla'andǝndǝ i'nda nak ndǝ paplatkǝn a teppa pwatafichaɗi nakǝn mwanchin.
MAR 16:5 Kǝnannda yimta hur kwatkǝn, nakndǝ hwankimsha'a ɗas tǝ harsǝmta, tǝ heɗɗi njela'a pǝɗang ǝnatkǝn kandǝfa.
