MAR 16:6 Ndangna kandǝwa mǝ pǝɗa ǝnkunifǝwa nuni kat Yǝso Lǝnazaratta, le kukkwandǝfichǝhi. A thle'i, mǝlansa mbǝnniyuwa, kǝlama mbǝɗi hunandǝficha.
MAR 16:7 Ɗama mbwa'amna kimshechi'en tǝ Bitrus, tǝndatwa nan lata Galili mǝ kandang, mbǝnniyu nuni nanndi nda i mbwa'a'ndǝnakuni."
MAR 16:8 Nishchǝkǝn paɗ shekɗa'indǝ kanda kandǝ saktatfa Cheknda kish tǝ rahta, a hurkwatkǝn fechengnanda rǝptǝfa shekɗa'indǝ kandǝ ka'ǝn. Mbwa'aundǝ ǝna nifuwa kǝthlǝm kanda lechita.
MAR 16:9 [Kǝ thlattin tǝ shisshingta fa ɓingtǝ tung a farǝ Lati, tǝrkaakǝn ɓata mbǝs Maryamu le ɓaka a Magdala, nuhi rǝktǝ Yǝso lǝwurchǝ muɗa fet'en.
MAR 16:10 Mǝlan paɗ ɗǝkna mbwa'anda fichile natndǝ tǝ Yǝso soh kana mǝrta ɗǝkna mbǝssandǝkanda sǝɓ hura tǝ paɗ kanda tita.
MAR 16:11 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝwa Yǝso mǝllan tǝ shisshingta fa, tǝpaɗ neɗtǝndi, cherkǝnda fǝrkitsi.
MAR 16:12 Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn cheɗkǝn fat'enna mbǝnda funǝ chap hurnandǝ tǝ witǝ natsomǝn, kanda ɗar pǝɗata thlethǝmta.
MAR 16:13 Nofchi chapyu ngǝrangndǝ'in ɓaknda mbwa'anda tahchikǝn, chika tǝkichu fǝrundǝ kitsi kǝ ɗar i mbutǝndǝwa.
MAR 16:14 Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn ɓak Yǝso mbǝs kimshechi'en kumkǝngǝrǝnsǝ ǝrta shokndǝhi kanda sǝm ɗǝsǝmta, ɓokkangna kandǝhi kǝ ɗar ɓah fǝrkitchiɗeng nanda, tǝ kwaakwaachit hanɗǝkiketa, kǝthlem cherndǝ fǝrkitta ɗar fichile naknda a ɗiffitǝ thla'i'thlattǝn.
MAR 16:15 Ndangna kandǝwa ɗama hur kishitǝ nat kǝ ɓassuni kwescha shunda kǝ mbǝɗa nofchǝ nat.
MAR 16:16 Uf nifi fǝrkǝkit sangfichǝ baptisma nan hǝrǝkta, paɗ le cherkǝ fǝrkit na ficha fǝra pwancha.
MAR 16:17 Na ficha nat sakǝt i'chiiya tǝ mbǝɗa fichile fǝrkǝkit: nanda chandǝ ɓǝɓi lǝwurchakissha hur thlemna, nanda shuwun yuwamichǝ somsomǝn,
MAR 16:18 Nanda harǝ huthlǝnchahar tǝ paɗ chika witǝ ɓǝɓi i'natma sandǝ ngu tamta sa ǝnkanduwa; nanda sa harcha nofcha in fichile nak hahchin nanda kǝndaɗi."
MAR 16:19 Ɗiffitǝ shuni shunandǝ Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso kanda, tǝrrang ficha afshi, sokkǝnna har sǝmta Fara.
MAR 16:20 Pǝɗak kimshechikǝnna nata ɓasǝ kwashchǝ shunda Fara chika ayi, Lǝmwanda nakna kǝsanda kandǝsi. Tǝ mbǝɗa ǝnnat sheka inchi nannda sǝtyu cheɗkǝnwa kweshcha shuni nannda ɓassǝyu ɓakna mbǝɗa Fara.]
ACT 1:1 Hur tǝrka ɗelwer engna, le yarutisi sokǝn Tiyofalus, yaraɗi ichihi nat tǝrkaatǝ Yǝso sǝta tǝ fichile tǝrkaatǝn sakandaɗi,
ACT 1:2 kǝ fari tǝrtǝ fichinda afshi, ɗifitǝ fǝra kussa fathlǝnchi'en taɗtǝnhar tǝmbǝɗa Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ.
ACT 1:3 Hur mundǝ kumchit fwaɗa, ɗifitǝ ɓahtǝ'enhi tǝ mǝrtǝ'en, kurɓaɗǝ cheɗa fat'enna kanda a mbachǝ somsomǝn ndatwa tǝkit a thlee tǝ shisshingtafa, paɗ mbwa'aɗǝ pathlǝ mwanda Fara kanda.
ACT 1:4 Naɗi natǝn tǝ kandǝyu, ndangna kandǝwa: "Mǝ malindǝ Urshelima hiwa, kǝ pundǝ kǝ nǝhhǝɗ ɗǝfshuni ɗǝftǝ shinkǝn hiiyu, nda i mbwa'andǝna kanda,
ACT 1:5 Kǝthlǝm Yohanna sǝkǝn baptisma tǝ ama, a hanmunchǝ ɗimek nakficha sa baptisma kuni tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ."
ACT 1:6 Kǝnat Yǝso humtǝhi tǝ fathlǝncha, sahangndǝwa: "Lǝmwanda, nakǝnya natu ngǝr fǝra kuturichit'ena Israila ɗǝwa?"
ACT 1:7 Ndangna kandǝwa: "Nga innuni kǝ sǝnuni thlet hanmunchǝ tǝ hanthlǝkchǝkǝnwa, papa ndak nak tǝ alchitkǝn.
ACT 1:8 Nuni mbǝs alchita ma ɓeɗ Shemeɗ kǝ ɗar inchengnuni. Nakuni nat kǝ shetachengna, kǝ nuni mbwa'a pathlengna nofcha a hur Urshelima tǝ hachahai Yahudiya nat tǝ Samariya tǝ sǝrǝt kishitǝ nat."
ACT 1:9 Kǝ mbuutǝn kichu, kanda ɗar kǝlanda, tǝrangficha afshi kǝ hur husomba'a, ɓakna shekata hwanichengnanda mwa'unda ngǝr nanndǝwa.
ACT 1:10 Kanda ɗar kǝlata afshi, mǝlan paɗ mǝla pǝɗata, ɓak nofchi chappa thlara thlǝmatnanda, tǝ njelechǝ heɗǝɗa.
ACT 1:11 Ndangnda kandǝwa: "Hishcha Galilicha, kǝthlǝmmǝ natuni kikit kǝnuni kǝlata afshi? Yǝso ti tǝrrandǝ ficha hurnuni kǝ afshiya, farǝyuna nan ngǝr ɓata nda i natuni pǝɗat'ena hur afshi."
ACT 1:12 Thlaakǝnda malkǝndǝ shohla Zaitunhi ngǝrangndǝ'ina Urshelima nakǝn nga langngǝwa, witǝ nduk ka mel ǝrta.
ACT 1:13 Kǝ nannda sata hǝmǝtkǝn, tǝrkǝnda huri afshi kǝ mbǝɗi nanndǝ ɗǝndas. nda: Bitrus, Yohanna, Yakubu, Andarawus, Filibus, Toma, Bartalamawus tǝ Matiyu, Yakubu hweya Halfa tǝ Saminu lǝ mbat thlǝt inda punofcha ɗi tǝ Yahuza hweya Yakubu.
ACT 1:14 Humkǝndǝhi natyu tǝ yarǝ ǝrta, naknda nata hwandǝ kǝnding, tǝ Maryamu man Yǝso tǝ nischǝ terchin tǝ hwanmanchǝ Yǝso.
ACT 1:15 A hanmunchiniyu, ngomkǝ fafǝrkithi aru tǝ kumchitchap kǝ mbǝt ǝrta, thlaakǝ Bitrus kit a hurnanda, ndakǝnwa:
ACT 1:16 "Hwanmanchina, sokkǝn waat kǝ nǝhɗangfichi ihi mbuutǝ shunda Farǝ soh tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ ɓak tǝ miya Dauda kǝ ɗar Yahuda le hǝmka mbanna hur fichile kǝsang Yǝso.
ACT 1:17 Kǝthlǝm nakna hurnǝm soh, paɗ fǝra fichi i natna sǝta hur toriya.
ACT 1:18 (Yahuda, tǝkǝni ɓǝɓi tor'en hiitǝn mbǝtsi, hǝmkǝnhi tǝ inda, ɗathlkǝ hur'en ɓak hanheɗechi'ena haiya.
ACT 1:19 Kusheng shiwun mǝrta Yahuda sǝkkǝ nofcha Urshelima nat, ak fichi mbǝtkǝnwa Akaldama tǝ miyengnanda, sakǝtkǝnwa mbǝt fwara.)
ACT 1:20 Ɗǝk Bitrussa mban tǝ ndatwa: Nakna hur yaratkǝn kichuyu a hur Zabura, ndatwa: "Nak huraa'ena nata kǝtǝn kuffi, mǝ soki nifa hurkǝnwa: paɗ mbǝt soktǝ'en a hur torkǝn kǝ tǝr yuna."
ACT 1:21 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn sokkǝn waat kǝ taɗim yunihara a hur nofchi natǝm tǝ kandǝ nat farǝ natma witǝ tǝ Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso yu.
ACT 1:22 Thlata fari sandǝ Yohanna baptisma kǝ fari tǝrtǝndǝndi a hurnǝm kǝ afshi. Chikawun tǝrtǝ ficha, nan sokta sheta tǝkǝm kǝ ɗar thlata Yǝso a hur mǝmatcha.
ACT 1:23 Harkǝndǝ nofchi chap: Yusufu lela atfichǝwa Barsabas, lela atndǝ paɗwa Yustus tǝ Matiyas.
ACT 1:24 Hwankǝnda tǝ ndatwa: "Ai Lǝmwanda, lǝ sǝn hanndǝkiketa chika wuni, cheɗɗu le taɗtuhara hur nofchi chapya.
ACT 1:25 Kǝ sokka lǝ thlǝnda hur torkǝn, kǝ tǝrǝn mbǝtsokta Yahuda le lengkǝhi pǝɗaka mbǝɗi ɓatǝn yu.
ACT 1:26 'Yimkǝnda tata, sǝmkǝ Matiyas ɗǝfkǝfichinda hur fathlǝncha, humang fichi tǝ fichile kumngǝrǝnsǝ ertǝyu.
ACT 2:1 Kǝ saatǝ farǝ pentekos, uf fa fǝrkit hwimndǝhi mbǝt ǝrta.
ACT 2:2 Sutolluwa, sǝkkǝ fichi tit ǝna hur afshi nda kapat rǝnna'a nǝhɗaɗǝ huri'i nannda hurkǝn ɗǝɗas.
ACT 2:3 Cheɗkǝ ichi fechengnanda nda hanshuwun hwata, kanda saktǝhi, kanda ɗǝta ɗar inchengnanda.
ACT 2:4 Nǝhɗang fichi kandǝ nat tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, tǝrkaakǝndǝ shundǝ tǝ michǝ somsomǝn, ɗa i fǝrandǝ Shemeɗ shunda kanda.
ACT 2:5 A thlahmbǝchiniyu, Yahudawechisi fa mwanandǝ Farǝ kaǝn, ɓaka a hachahaichǝ somsomǝn a hur kishita nak tǝ sokta a Urshelima.
ACT 2:6 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ iniyu, humkǝndǝhi ngomkǝnda mbǝt ǝrta kǝthlǝm a kwehǝr sokkǝnaɗi, chikawun mǝla sǝktǝ kanda shundǝ tǝ miyengnanda.
ACT 2:7 Pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfa paɗ shekɗang'indǝ kanda, ndakndǝwa: "Awi fa shuni natya nga Galilawechiwowa?"
ACT 2:8 Sǝk ǝnikǝni natma sǝk kanda shundǝ tǝ miya chikawuni?
ACT 2:9 kǝmnangya, Fartiyawecha tǝ Madiyawecha, tǝ Elamawecha tǝ nofcha hachahai Mesofotamiya tǝ Yahudiya tǝ Kafadokiya tǝ i Fantus tǝ Asiya,
ACT 2:10 tǝ Firijiya tǝ Bamfiliya tǝ Masar tǝ fichile nak nduknduk tǝ Sayirin a hachahai Libiya tǝ romchi ɓaka Roma. Yahudawecha tǝ fichile yimka tǝrmbandengnǝm.
ACT 2:11 Paɗ kǝmnang Kiritawecha tǝ Larabawecha, nat kǝmna sǝk kanda shundǝ tǝ miyengnǝm kǝ ɗar pǝktat ichi sǝt Fara."
ACT 2:12 Pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfǝ natnda kohǝrkǝ inchengnandaɗi, ɗakndǝwa: "Mǝnaka sakǝt iya?"
ACT 2:13 Chang funǝ mi kandǝhi ndatwa: "Tǝ sandǝ am inabi ngalkǝndǝ ɓeng."
ACT 2:14 Thlaakǝ Bitrus kit tǝ tahǝt fathlǝnchi kumngǝrǝnsǝ'ǝrtǝyu, i'naǝn ɓurathi ɓassangna kandǝsi, ndakǝnwa: "Hwanmanchina Yahudawecha tǝ fichile naktǝ sokta Urshelima nat sǝkamnji, paɗ kǝ ɗǝffuni i'nda i nati mbwa'anda kuni.
ACT 2:15 Nofchiya nga tǝ tǝrang ǝna kandǝ nda i tǝrtuniwa, nakǝn mwee mbǝta ɓingtǝyawa: hanthlikkǝn hanhertǝ ndak.
ACT 2:16 I natuniya ndǝkǝn mbutǝ tapǝnaa Yowel ndatwa:
ACT 2:17 "'Ndak Farǝ wa, a mweshit hanmunchikǝn ni thlǝr Shemeɗengna ɗar inda nofchi nat. Hwechengnuni kǝ nishchi tǝ hishcha nanda mbu icha le mbwa'andǝ Fara kanda. Kimshechengnuni nanda nat'ichi tamuchitnda nata, tuɓurnofchengnuni nanda sǝnnata.
ACT 2:18 A hanmunchiniyu ni thlǝr shemeɗengna kǝ ɗar inda mafechengna hishchi tǝ nishchi nat, paɗ nanda mbu icha le mbwa'andǝ Fara kanda.
ACT 2:19 Ni che ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa a hur afshi, tǝ i na che sakǝt ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nofchǝfa a kishita, naknanat fwara tǝ hwata tǝ ǝnnda husomba'a.
ACT 2:20 Hwatfarǝ nan yimta hulta, ndǝra'a nan tǝɓǝrtǝhi ngah nda fwara, kana fari Lǝmwandiyu ɓata, kapat fari nak mwanchin.
ACT 2:21 Farini hachiyu, chikawun hwanka hur thlǝm Lǝmwanda nan hǝrǝkta.
ACT 2:22 Hwanmanchina, Israilawecha, sǝkam shuniya. Yǝso lǝ Nazaratta, nifi cheɗandǝ Fara kuni tǝ pǝktat torcha tǝ ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa tǝ che ichi somsomǝn a hurnuni tǝ mbǝɗ'en, nda i sǝntuni tǝ indengnuni.
ACT 2:23 Yǝso tiya, fǝrkǝ fichindi tepi tehishhi paɗ tǝ sǝnda Fara, kunang kukwang kǝ ɓǝllangnda tǝ mbǝɗa ɓǝɓi nofcha.
ACT 2:24 Ɓak Fara thla'anda ɗifitǝ ɓohandǝ hanmurtǝɗa i'ndi'en, kǝthlǝm ngu sǝtta hanmurta kǝ kǝsǝnndǝharwa.
ACT 2:25 Dauda kutura mbwitǝ ǝn kǝɗarkǝn ndatwa: "A neɗi Lǝmwandǝ mǝla thlǝmmatnǝ kǝnding. Ngi hǝhǝrtǝfuwa, kǝthlǝm mǝla harsǝmtengna.
ACT 2:26 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, hanndǝkiketengna sǝk mbǝndǝfa, hanshundengna in immish mbǝnfata. Tǝ paɗ thlarkǝ faɗengna ɗar ɗǝf'inda mbǝɗa Fara.
ACT 2:27 Kǝthlǝm nguna malǝ faɗengna hur mǝmatchiwa, ndu kǝ mallangnǝ iuti nak Chiɗchiɗ kǝ yirakaɗa kwatwa.
ACT 2:28 Cheɗinǝ mba shisshingta. Nu nǝhɗitǝ tǝ mbǝnfata naku tǝnji kǝnding.
ACT 2:29 "Hwanamanchina, ni mbǝlla mbwa'anda kuni tǝ kitchitwa kakannǝm Dauda, ndatwa miri a thlohaficha, kwat'en mwakǝna thlǝmmatnǝm kǝ ɓukweya.
ACT 2:30 Nakǝn kǝ tapǝnaa, paɗ a shinwa ɗǝffa Farǝ shundǝhi tǝ at'ichimi ndatwa kachit Dauda na sokta mbǝt sok kuturichit'en.
ACT 2:31 Ɓak Dauda nathi kichuyu, paɗ a shuwun kǝ ɗar thlata Almasihu a hur mǝmatcha. Nakna ndatwa Farǝ ngu malǝnda hur mǝmatchuwa ndu kǝmalǝn fat'en kǝ yirakaɗa kwatwa.
ACT 2:32 Thlaa Farǝ Yǝso a hur mǝmatcha, kanang natani shetachǝ nakani.
ACT 2:33 Nakǝn mwanaficha nakna harsǝmta Fara, Paɗ shinkǝn nda i ɗǝftǝn shundǝhi, fǝraǝn Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ kǝ thlǝrka ɗar inchengnǝm nda i sǝktuni paɗ natuni ɓukweya.
ACT 2:34 Nga Dauda tǝrka hur afshiwa, chika mǝlan ndakǝnwa: "Lǝmwandǝ ndangnga Lǝmwandengnǝwa, soku harsǝmtengna,
ACT 2:35 Kani ɗǝf atikrechiwa ishangnǝkanda ka sarǝcheku."
ACT 2:36 "Kǝthlǝmndǝkǝn chikawuna hur Isra'ila kǝsǝnǝn tǝkitwa Yǝso ti kukwandunihiyu, ngǝra Fara Lǝmwanda tǝ Almasihu."
ACT 2:37 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ shuniniyu, thlǝhǝrkǝn kanda hanɗǝkiketa, ndangnda Bitrus tǝ tahǝt fathlǝnchikǝnwa: "Hwanmancha, mǝnatani sǝta?"
ACT 2:38 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Bitrussa kandǝwa: "Kǝ tǝrunihi kǝ sangfichǝ baptisma kuni a hur thlǝm Yǝso kǝrǝsti kǝthlǝm kǝ kallangfichi ɓǝɓichitfechengnuni kunihi, kanuni thlǝt Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ.
ACT 2:39 Kǝthlǝm ɗǝfshunihiya innuni tǝ hwechengnuni, tǝ fichile nak langngǝ paɗ, chikawun at Lǝmwanda, Farengnǝm."
ACT 2:40 Ɗǝk Bitrussa mban tǝ ɓassanda kandǝ kǝ tolta, nakna ndanda kandǝwa: "Hǝrkamǝn fechengnuni hura sǝɓ kishi'iya."
ACT 2:41 Fichile fǝrkǝkit kǝ ɗar shunda Bitrus, sangfichǝ baptisma kanda. A farǝniyu chekkǝ nofchǝ kǝ ɗar fafǝrkit nduk aru kumchit mǝkkan.
ACT 2:42 Ɓaknda ɗǝf inchengnanda sakini fathlǝnchiyu, lǝ humkǝndǝhi kǝnnda chi johma, paɗ kǝnnda hwanda.
ACT 2:43 Kǝsang lechit chikawuni, sǝk fathlǝnchikǝn ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nofchifǝ tǝ sakchikǝn kaǝn.
ACT 2:44 Nat fafǝrkit kanda mbǝt'ǝrta, chikamengnanda paɗ ǝrta.
ACT 2:45 Hi'yangndǝ ichiɗǝ naksengnandǝ nat, sakangndǝ handǝɓǝlkǝna chikawuni, nda i yahtǝn.
ACT 2:46 I sǝkka wembǝta kanda ɗǝta kapat hura'a Farǝ tǝ ndani rǝmma, kǝnnda chi njohma a hurechengnanda, kǝnnda sǝm'ǝna mbǝt ǝrta tǝ mbǝndǝfa tǝ hanɗǝkiketǝ yuyur.
ACT 2:47 Kanda mwanandǝ Fara, nangnda mbǝs hamta mbǝɗa nofchinat. I sǝka wembǝta Lǝmwanda cheka fichile hǝrkandǝfich kanda.
ACT 3:1 Farǝle nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna pǝɗata kapat hura'a Fara ka hwanda a farǝhuftǝ, hanthlǝkkǝn mǝkkan.
ACT 3:2 Bakndǝ tǝ nifǝ le ngǝttǝ fichǝ kǝ tǝraɗ kǝnding la ɓaknda ɗǝfndǝhi nduk kǝ mi ɓang kapat hura'a Fara lela atndǝwa chamare tǝ mimbangnga, kǝthlǝm kǝ hwanǝn fǝr poffǝnna harra fa yimta kapat hura'a Fara.
ACT 3:3 Kǝnatǝn nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna yimta kapat hura'a Fara, hwanaǝn fǝr poffǝn kanda
ACT 3:4 Nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna nak nda kǝllanda, ndak Bitrus wa: "Kǝllan kani."
ACT 3:5 Ngǝrkǝ hur'indǝ'en nat kǝfaɗengnanda, naǝnhiwa nan mbǝs'ǝna harengnanda.
ACT 3:6 Ndak Bitrus wa: "Hanɗǝɓǝltengnǝsǝwa, i'naksengna ndǝkǝn nati fǝrruta. A hur thlǝm Yǝso Almasihu Lǝnazartta, thla'u wi'iu."
ACT 3:7 Kǝskǝ Bitrus harsǝmtǝ'en thla'a'ǝn. Chatkichuyu sarrǝchi'en tǝ sanglamchi'en sǝkndǝ alchita.
ACT 3:8 Thlaakǝn pǝrkǝna afshi thlarkǝnhi tǝrkaakǝn wita, yimkǝna kapat hura'a Farǝ tǝ kanda, mǝla wita mǝla pǝrta afshi, mǝla mwanandǝ Fara.
ACT 3:9 Nat nofcha nakndǝndi mǝla wita mǝla mwanandǝ Fara.
ACT 3:10 Mbǝssangndǝwa mǝlanni lǝ sokka a chamare tǝ mimbang kapat hura'a Fara kǝnna hwafǝrpoffǝnyu. Pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfǝ kǝ ɗar i'ndi'en.
ACT 3:11 Kǝskǝn Bitrus tǝ Yohanna har, ngomkǝ nofchǝ nat kǝ thlǝmatnandǝ tǝ rahta a hur kǝttǝn para Sulemanu, kǝthlǝm a pǝɗa'ǝnkandǝfa paɗ kwehǝr hur'inchennandaɗi.
ACT 3:12 Kǝnat Bitrus kichu, kahaan hur'inda nofchǝ tǝ ndatwa: "Israilawecha, mǝsǝk pǝɗandǝ'ǝnkunifǝ kǝ ɗar iya? Kǝthlǝmmǝ natuni kǝlandǝ kani nda tǝ alchiɗ'indengnani wiitǝ nifiya ndu kuwur Farengnani sǝk wiitǝ nifiiya?
ACT 3:13 Fara Ibrahim tǝ Ishaku tǝ Yakubu, Fara kakechinǝm nat, mǝlan mwanang mafat'en Yǝso, le chertuni paɗ fǝrtunindi a mbanitǝ Bilatus yu, chikama sokkǝnwa tirwa nan kalǝndǝhi.
ACT 3:14 Cherkuni le nak chiɗchiɗ lǝ kafata, hwankuni kǝ kallangfichi lǝ ɓǝlfata kunihi.
ACT 3:15 Ɓǝlangnguni le nak tǝ mba shisshingta har, thla'ang Fara hur mǝmatcha, kanang shetacha ɗar kitchitkǝn.
ACT 3:16 "Tǝ mbǝɗa fǝrkit hur thlǝm Yǝso, kǝntǝ nifiɗiya, sǝntuni sohwa tǝraɗ. Kittǝkǝn fǝrkitchiɗi tǝmbǝɗa thlǝm Yǝso kǝnang nifiɗiya a hwanitengnuni nat.
ACT 3:17 Nakǝnya hwanmancha, mbǝssaɗiwa i sanduni Yǝso sǝkuni hur ɓahsǝnda, nda i sǝt fa hǝmɓanichengnuni.
ACT 3:18 Tǝkichu nǝhɗandǝ Farǝ ɗǝfshundǝ'enhi tǝ miya tapǝnechǝ nat, ndatwa Kǝrǝsti nan sat ɓahta.
ACT 3:19 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn kǝ tǝrunihi kǝ tǝɓrunihi ɓǝɗa Fara, kǝthlǝm kǝ sapang fichǝ ɓǝɓichitfechengnuni ɗi, Lǝmwanda nannata cheka alchit hanɗǝkiketa kuni.
ACT 3:20 Paɗ nan thlǝn Kǝrǝsti ti taɗandǝnakunisi soh, mǝlan naka Yǝso.
ACT 3:21 Waat kǝ sokka hur afshi kǝ fari natficha mbumbweɗandǝ ichihi nat kǝ yuwachikǝn, nda i ɗǝftǝ Farǝ shiwunkǝnhi kǝsoh tǝ mbǝɗa tapǝnechi'en chiɗchiɗ.
ACT 3:22 Ndak Musawa: "Farǝ Lǝmwanda nan thla'a tapǝna'a kunisi a hur nofchengnuni, nda i thla'itǝn. Waat kǝ ɗǝffuni inda i nat mbwa'andǝna kuni nat."
ACT 3:23 Nakna sokta chikawun kawuchik thlǝmmata tapǝni'iniyu na ficha sǝɓandaɗa hur nofcha.
ACT 3:24 Tapǝnechi mbukǝ ichi nat, thlata Samaila ka kǝs fichilesi ɓaka ɗifi, mbwindǝ ichi naka sǝt nat a hanmunchi nakǝnya.
ACT 3:25 Kunang naka hwecha tapǝnechiniyu paɗ kuna hur ɗǝf shunini ɗǝfandǝ Fara kakechǝnǝmhiyu. Kǝthlǝm ndang Fara Ibrahim wa: "Tǝ mbǝɗa kachitwa na nofcha kishita natta mbǝs ǝnhar.
ACT 3:26 Kǝ thla'andǝ Farǝ mafat'en Yǝso, tǝrkaakǝn thlǝnndi kǝ mbǝɗengnuni Israilawecha, kǝthlǝm kǝ fǝraǝn mbǝs ǝnhara kuni tǝ mbǝɗa tǝɓrandǝ chikawuna hurnuni kǝ malaǝn ɓǝɓi ɗǝsǝchi'en."
ACT 4:1 Pǝrischa tǝ la hǝmmbanita fa pu kappat hura'a Farǝ har tǝ Sadukiyawecha, ɓaknda mbǝsnda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna kanda hur shunandǝ nofcha.
ACT 4:2 Shiɓhurchengnandaɗi kǝthlǝm kanda sakanda nofchihar tǝ sǝnanda kandǝsǝwa mǝmatcha nanda thlatǝ tǝ shisshingchafa nda i thlaatǝ Yǝso.
ACT 4:3 Kǝsangndǝ kanda, ɗǝkndǝ tǝ kanda kǝttǝn pursuna kǝ ishki, nakǝn tepa shiɗ farǝhufta.
ACT 4:4 Yakat fichile sǝkkǝ ɓassikǝn, fǝrkǝndǝkitsi. Nofchi fǝrkǝkittǝkǝn sheendǝ aru kumchitɗurman.
ACT 4:5 Ɓingǝtkǝn, fa yarandǝ ichihi a kuturchitkǝn uf tǝ fa hǝmmbanita tǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kussaɗi, ngomkǝndǝhi a Urshelima.
ACT 4:6 Tǝ Hanana kapat pǝrist tǝ Kayafa tǝ Yohanna tǝ Alekzanda, nat ta fichile naka hur ngitikta kapat pǝrist.
ACT 4:7 Ɓakndǝ tǝ Bitrus tǝ Yohanna, thlarangndǝ kandǝhi kǝ hur ɗiffi, sahangndǝ kandǝwa: "Tǝ alchitmi ndu tǝ thlǝm wuni sǝtuni ichiya?"
ACT 4:8 Bitrus, nǝhǝɗkaɗǝ tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, ndangnakandǝwa: "Kuturcha tǝ pǝktat nofcha,
ACT 4:9 Sahangnguni mi kani ɓukweya kǝthlǝm kachiɗi sandani tǝraɗtiyawa tǝ mbayi kǝntǝna ɗiyawa?
ACT 4:10 Yahkisi kǝ sǝnuni nattuni tǝ Israilawecha, ndatwa tǝ thlǝm Yǝso Almasihu Lǝnazaratta, le kukwandunihi thla'andǝ Fara hur mǝmatcha, kǝntǝ nifiɗi ngwalngwal kita mbanitǝnuniya.
ACT 4:11 Mǝlan naka: "Ngwiyi chertuni kunang fa tincha, ndǝkǝn sokka kukuwun tinda."
ACT 4:12 Nifǝsi na mbǝssa kaɓi nifǝ chika ǝrtǝwa, kǝthlǝm thlǝmsa hur kishi'inatya fǝrandǝ ficha nifa le na mbǝssakaɓikǝmwa."
ACT 4:13 Kǝ natndǝ alchit shunda nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna, paɗ mbǝssangndǝwa nga fa sǝn'ǝnwa, paɗ fa ɓahcha, pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfa. Ɓeɗnda mbǝssandǝ paɗwa kǝsoh nakndǝ tǝ Yǝso.
ACT 4:14 Kǝnannda nat nifi kǝnandǝndaɗaɗi kita hurnanda, ɓahkǝndǝ i nannda mbuta.
ACT 4:15 Ndangnda nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna wa kǝ chendakisha kǝttǝn yarangndǝ ichihi, kǝ yarangndǝ ichihi kǝ ndani.
ACT 4:16 Ndakndǝwa: "Nakma sandǝ nofchiya kǝni? Mbandǝsǝ namma ndatwa sundǝ ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfuwowa, kǝthlǝm chikawuni a Urshelima shinwa shiɗ fichǝ ǝn kichu.
ACT 4:17 Kǝthlǝm kǝ njaam ɗǝttǝkǝna kanda mban, ɓokamna kanda, mǝ ngǝrinda shunandǝ nifa hur thlǝmmiyawa."
ACT 4:18 Akndǝ fathlǝnchikǝn, ɓokangnda kanda mǝ ngǝrinda shunandǝ nifǝ ndu kǝ sakangnda nifǝhar hur thlǝm Yǝso wa.
ACT 4:19 Ngǝrang nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna kandǝsǝwa: "Keekesa mbanitǝ Fara kǝ sǝkani innuni kǝ cherani i Farǝwa, Kǝlamǝn kǝnuni.
ACT 4:20 Kǝthlǝm kanang ngani malandǝ mbu i natani tǝ i sǝktaniwa."
ACT 4:21 Ngǝrkǝndǝ chekandǝ ɓokanda kanda kalkǝndǝ kandǝhi, kǝthlǝm sǝnundǝ mbayi nannda fǝra ɓwenne kandǝwa kǝthlǝm nofcha. Kǝthlǝm chikawun mǝla mwanandǝ Fara kǝ ɗar i sǝka.
ACT 4:22 Nifi mbǝskǝ kǝndaɗaɗi tǝ mbanda ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa, sheraɗa hurat kumchit fwaɗa tǝ ngǝtta.
ACT 4:23 Kǝ kaltǝndǝ kandǝhi, nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna pǝɗaknda mbǝs fahchinanda, mbwa'angndǝ i kandǝ mbutǝ pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ pǝktecha.
ACT 4:24 Kandang paɗ kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu, thla'angndǝ ɓurechengnanda mbǝɗa Fara hurhwanda, ndakndǝwa: "Lǝmwandǝ lǝ alchitnat, sokǝn sǝk hur afshi tǝ kishita tǝ hawurta tǝ ichi naka hurkǝn nat.
ACT 4:25 Tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, tǝ miya kakannani Dauda, mafaɗeku ndatuwa: "Kǝthlǝmmǝ sǝɓɓandǝ punofcha huraɗi? Kǝthlǝmmǝ nat nofcha kike kohat i'cha?
ACT 4:26 Kuturcha kishita tehishndǝfa mbata, fa hǝmmbanita humandǝ inda kǝ ɗar Lǝmwanda tǝ Kǝrǝsti paɗ."
ACT 4:27 "Kittǝkǝn a hur hǝmǝɗiya Hiridus tǝ Buntus Bilatus humandǝ inda tǝ punofcha tǝ nofcha Isra'ilawecha kǝ sangndǝ ɓǝɓichitfatfa nat kǝ ɗar mafaɗeku Yǝso le taɗtuhar.
ACT 4:28 Humangndǝ inda kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝndǝ ichi taptu kǝ tahsangnǝhi tǝ alchiɗeku tǝ yahtekuwa nan sǝta.
ACT 4:29 Nakǝnya Lǝmwanda, kǝlandǝn kah thlemmaɗengnanda kǝ Fǝrangnǝ mbaɓǝs shundeku mafecheku tǝ alchita.
ACT 4:30 Kǝlla tiɗɗangnǝ harekuhi i kǝndaɗi, kǝ sani ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa tǝ sakchikǝn tǝ mbǝɗa thlǝm mafaɗeku chiɗchiɗ, Yǝso."
ACT 4:31 Ɗifitǝ hwandengnanda, mbǝɗi humtǝndǝhi hǝhǝrkǝnfa, nǝhɗang fichi kandǝ tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ. Ɓǝskǝndǝ pathla Farǝ nga lecgitfuwa.
ACT 4:32 Sǝrǝt fichile fǝrkǝkit, humkǝndǝhi hanɗǝkiketǝ ǝrta tǝ yarǝ ǝrta. Ngusǝ ndakwa i naksǝ'enwa ikǝnwa, chikamǝ naksengnanda innandǝ nat.
ACT 4:33 Fathlǝnchǝkǝn fǝrkǝndǝ sheta tǝ thlata Yǝso Lǝmwanda hur mǝmatcha tǝ alchita, paɗ Kachita Farǝ kaǝn a ɗar nandǝ nat nda.
ACT 4:34 Ngusa hurnandǝ ɓahkǝ ǝnwa, kǝthlǝm nat fa hurecha tǝ hicha hiyandaɗi ɓakndǝ tǝ hanɗǝɓǝlkǝn.
ACT 4:35 Ɓakndǝ tǝ hanndǝɓǝlkǝn, fǝrangnda fathlǝnchǝkǝn, sakang ficha nofchinat chikawun keeke a i yahtǝn.
ACT 4:36 Nifǝsi thlǝmkǝnwa Yusufu, lǝ Lawita kachitkǝn lǝ Kubrustǝ nakǝn, la at fathlǝnchǝkǝnwa Barnabas (sakitkǝnwa: "Hwan cheka alchita hanɗǝkiketa")
ACT 4:37 Hiyaǝn hitǝ'enaɗi, ɓakǝn tǝ hanndǝɓǝlkǝnna ɓanitǝ fathlǝnchikǝn.
ACT 5:1 Nifǝsǝ thlǝmkǝnwa Hananiya tǝ nuhkǝn Safiratu, hi'yaǝn mbǝt enaɗi.
ACT 5:2 Ɓuɓweekǝn hanɗǝɓǝlkǝn har tǝ sǝnda nuhkǝnsi, ɓakǝn tǝ tahhǝtkǝn ɗǝfkǝnhi mbanitǝ fathlǝncha.
ACT 5:3 Ndǝkǝn ndat Bitrus wa: "Sokǝn Hananiya, mǝsǝk malandu Sheɗan kǝ nǝhɗaǝn hanɗǝkiketeku kǝ lekangna Shemeɗsǝ Chiɗchiɗ, ɓuɓweetu hanɗǝɓǝltǝ harra hur hanɗǝɓǝl hiti hi'yanduɗi?
ACT 5:4 Thlateku kǝ ɗǝna hi'yandaɗaɗi, nga iuwowa? Ɗifitǝ hi'yaɗekuɗi, hanɗǝɓǝlkǝn nga iuwowa? Mǝsǝk ɗǝftu lekta hanndǝkiketeku? Nga nifǝ lekandusǝwa, Fara."
ACT 5:5 Kǝ sǝktǝ Hananiya shuniniyu, hǝmkǝnhi mǝrkǝn. Nat fichile sǝkka kǝsang lechit kandǝ kaǝn.
ACT 5:6 Ɓak kimshecha tǝranda kish, fwaɗangndǝ tǝ njeli thlohmurta pǝɗaknda thlohhanda.
ACT 5:7 Ɗifitǝ nda hanthlǝkkǝn mǝkkan, yimkǝ nuhkǝnsi, sǝnutǝ i sǝkwa.
ACT 5:8 Ndǝkǝn sahandǝ Bitrus wa: "Ɓu'i'tǝn, hi'yangnguni hitiɗiyu kichawa?" Ngǝmanwa: "Aa, kichuyu."
ACT 5:9 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Bitrus wa: "Mǝsǝk humanduni mi kǝ kikeɗangnguni Shemeɗa Lǝmwandǝ kicheya? Suku kwarsara fichile pǝɗaka thlohhandǝ sǝmatu, kanda mikǝnnda, nanda tǝrruta kish paɗ."
ACT 5:10 Chatkichuyu, hǝmkǝnhi mǝrkǝn. Kǝ yimtǝ kimshechikǝnsi, mbǝssangndǝ kǝ murǝtkǝn, tǝrkǝndǝndi kitangnda kish pǝɗangnda thlohhanda thlǝmat sǝmaha.
ACT 5:11 Kǝssang lechit kǝttǝn hwakǝn kaǝn nat ta fichile sǝkkǝ ichiniyu.
ACT 5:12 Shiɗ fichi ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa tǝ sakchikǝn kaǝn a hur nofcha tǝ ɓǝɗa fathlǝncha. Nat fafǝrkit la ngomkǝndǝhi kǝttǝn para Sulemanu tǝ yarǝ ǝrta.
ACT 5:13 A hur tahhǝt nofcha, ngusǝ cheɗkǝ nda nan yimta hurnandǝwa, chika kichu la fǝrang nofchǝ mwanda kanda.
ACT 5:14 Nak fafǝrkitta chektǝ kaǝn kǝ ɓǝɗa Lǝmwanda, sheraɗa le soh, hishchǝ tǝ nishchǝ nat.
ACT 5:15 Ala ɓakndǝ tǝ hacha mimbacha, funa mbǝt'hunecha funa ɗǝngǝlcha, kǝthlǝm ma Bitrusa mbǝrtǝhi, chika mirshingtǝ'en kǝɗǝn tǝ ɗar funa.
ACT 5:16 Nofcha a thlet mbichi somsomǝn taurang Urshelima hiyu naknda ngomta, kanda ɓat tǝ hacha tǝ fichile nat ɓǝɓilǝwurcha ɓahandǝ kanda, kǝnang fichi kandaɗǝ natnda.
ACT 5:17 Thlaakǝ kapat pǝrist tǝ fichile naka thlǝmatkǝn, fa tǝrmbanda Sadukiyawecha, nakndǝ tǝ sǝrǝhtafǝ kaǝn.
ACT 5:18 Kǝsangndǝ fathlǝnchikǝn, ɗǝkndǝ tǝ kanda pursuna.
ACT 5:19 Sokkǝn a fiɗɗikta, ɓak Mala'ika Lǝmwanda i'nandǝ mikǝtǝn pursunechikǝnhi, chaǝn kanda kish ndangna kandǝwa:
ACT 5:20 "Ɗama kapat hura'a Fara ɗuni thlarǝhi hurkǝn kǝ mbwa'angnguni nofcha pathlǝ yuwa shisshingta kanda."
ACT 5:21 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu yimkǝnda kapat hura'a Fara ɓingta naknda sakandaɗi. Kapat pǝrist tǝ fichile naka thlǝmatkǝn chekndakish, akndǝ fa sakandǝ ichihi tǝ fa hǝmmbanita Isra'ilawecha, thlǝnkǝnda pursuna kǝ ɓafichi tǝ kanda.
ACT 5:22 Kǝ ɗǝt fa pu pursuna tǝkǝn, mbǝsawundǝ kandǝsǝwa, ɓaknda ɗaɗi ndakndǝwa:
ACT 5:23 "Ɗǝkkani mbǝssandi pursuna tǝkǝna kuɓultǝ ndiichin, fa putǝhar kandǝsi a mikǝttǝnchikǝn, kǝ i'nandanihi mbǝssawani nifa hurkǝn chika ǝrtǝwa."
ACT 5:24 Kǝ sǝktǝ kapat lǝ pu kapat hura'a Farǝ har kichu tǝ pǝktat pǝristchikǝn, kohǝrkǝ inchengnandaɗi, naknda sakandǝhi mǝna kuwurɗifitǝkǝn.
ACT 5:25 Ɓakyuna ndanda kandǝwa: "Nofchi somtuni pursunayu kanda hur kapat hura'a Fara kanda sakanda nofchihar."
ACT 5:26 Fa pu kǝttǝn hwakǝn har tǝ kapat nanda pǝɗaknda ɓat tǝ fathlǝnchikǝn, paɗ ngatǝalwa, kǝthlǝm pǝktechikǝn kanda lechita mǝmǝmuhanda kandǝfǝ tǝ ngwichǝwa.
ACT 5:27 Kǝ ɓatndǝ tǝkanda, thlarangndǝ kandǝhi a mbanitǝ fa sakandǝ ichihi. Nak kapat pǝristsa sahami kanda.
ACT 5:28 Ndakǝnwa: "Ɓokandǝmakuni, mǝ ngǝriɗuni sakanda nifihar a hur thlǝm nifiyawa, chika kichu nǝhɗaɗuni Urshelima ɗi tǝ saktengnuni kǝ ɗarkǝn, a yahkunisǝ nakǝnya kǝ tǝrranǝ hakke tǝ fwara nifiya kǝ ɓa ɗar inchengnani."
ACT 5:29 Bitrus tǝ tahǝt fathlǝnchikǝn ngǝmangndǝwa: "Sokkǝn waat kǝ sani i mbutǝ Fara nga i mbutǝ nifuwa.
ACT 5:30 Fara kakechinǝm thla'ang Yǝso hur mǝmatcha, le mbǝlanduni tǝ mbanda kukwandǝhi ɗar palita.
ACT 5:31 Mǝlan mwanandǝ Fara ɗǝfkǝnndǝ tǝ harsǝmtǝ'en, sangna lǝ hǝmmbanita paɗ lǝ thlǝt nofchaɗi. Sǝkǝn iniyu kǝthlǝm Isra'ilawecha kǝ mbǝsndǝ mba tǝrtǝhi kǝ kalangfichǝ ɓǝɓichitfechengnanda kandǝhi.
ACT 5:32 Kanang shetacha kǝ ɗar ichini natyu, kichu paɗ tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, fǝrandǝ Fara fichile la kuwurkǝ ichi la mbutǝn."
ACT 5:33 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu, sǝɓkǝ hurchengnandaɗi kaǝn, yahkǝndǝsa ɓǝllandǝ kanda.
ACT 5:34 Yunǝsa mbǝnniyu lǝ Farisiyawata nat thlǝmkǝnwa Gamaliyel, lǝ ɓassǝ kus, le la fǝrandǝ nofchinat mwanda, thlaakǝn kit a hur fa sak'michikǝn ndakǝnwa chamǝn nofchikishya kwandǝn.
ACT 5:35 Kanna ndanda kandǝwa: "Hwanmanchina Isra'ilawecha, mbǝramsa i yahtunisa sandǝ nofchiya.
ACT 5:36 Hurechi mbǝrkǝhiyu, ɓak yunǝ kichu wa mǝlan Tuɗas, tǝrkǝn indǝ'en nda ǝnnakǝn, nifǝ aru fwaɗa ɗǝk kakǝn, ɓak ficha ɓǝllanda, fichile ɗǝk kakǝn nat wuwelkǝndǝhi.
ACT 5:37 Ɗifitǝ mǝlan paɗ, fari nat ficha thlikandǝ nofcha, ɓak yuna wa mǝlan Yahuda lǝ Galilita, chikaǝn funa kuwurkǝndǝndǝ, mǝlan paɗ thlǝrǝtkǝnaɗi. Fa kuwurndǝ tǝkǝn wuwelkǝndǝhi.
ACT 5:38 Chikale nakǝnya, ni mbwa'andakuni, chamakisha mbanda nofchiya, ma i natnda sakta i nifa, ngu ndǝta mbahwa:
ACT 5:39 Ma i Fara, nguni mbǝla sa'ǝnkandǝwa. Na ficha mbǝssandǝ kuni kuna mbat tǝ Fara."
ACT 5:40 Ngǝmangndǝ shundǝ'en, akndǝ fathlǝnchikǝnna hurkǝn, tǝppangnda kanda. Ndangnda kandǝwa mǝ ngǝrǝnda shundǝ tǝ thlǝm Yǝso wa, kannda kalǝ kandǝhi.
ACT 5:41 Fathlǝnchikǝn malkǝndǝ mbanitǝ fa sakandǝ ichihi, kanda sǝt mbǝnfata a ɗar ndatwa shǝkndǝsi kǝ sandǝ ɓahta kǝthlǝm thlǝm Yǝso.
ACT 5:42 Chikayen wembǝta, ndu hur kapat hura'a Fara ndu huri, malaundǝ sakandaɗi tǝ fǝr kusheng shundǝ mbinchin kǝ ɗar Yǝso wa mǝlan naka Kǝrǝstiwa.
ACT 6:1 A hanmunchiniyu nak fa fǝrkitta chektǝ oi, nak hurumtǝsǝ kaǝn. Yahudawecha fa shuwun Helenanchi naknda hurmanda Ibraniyawechǝfa, fa shundǝ tǝ mi Helenanchi, wa kǝlundǝsa nishchengnandǝ fichile mǝrtǝ hishchengnanda ka sak ichi kǝnding wa.
ACT 6:2 Fichile kumngǝrǝnsǝ chapyu akndǝ fa fǝrkit ndakndǝwa: "Kamusǝ kimnang kǝ malaam ɓassǝ pathla Farǝ kǝ yimma pathlǝ ndǝsǝmtǝ wa.
ACT 6:3 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, hwanmanchina, taɗam nofchihar muɗ a hurnuni, fichile la fǝrandǝ fichǝ mwanda kanda, paɗ nihiɗndaɗi tǝ Shemeɗa tǝ sǝnda, kǝ sǝmkanda ɗar toriya.
ACT 6:4 Kǝmnang nakma nata ɗar hwanda tǝ sakandǝ shuwunkǝnaɗi."
ACT 6:5 I mbutǝnda mbǝnangna nofchifǝ nat. Ndǝkǝn taɗtǝndǝ Istifanus, nifi nǝhiɗkǝ tǝ fǝrkit tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Filibus tǝ Burokoras tǝ Nikanor tǝ Timan tǝ Barminas tǝ Nikolas lǝ Antakiyata le yimka tǝrmbanda Yahudawecha.
ACT 6:6 Fichileya ɓanndǝ tǝ kanda mbǝɗa fathlǝncha, hwankǝnda ɗǝffaǝn harra kanda in.
ACT 6:7 Nak pathla Fara nata ɗǝta mban. Fa fǝrkit naknda chekta a Urshelima kaǝn, pǝristchǝ terchin fǝrkǝkit.
ACT 6:8 Istifanus, nifi nǝhǝɗkaɗǝ tǝ kafata tǝ alchita, shiɗtǝ pǝktat icha tǝ ǝnat sakchikǝn kaǝn a hur nofcha.
ACT 6:9 Funǝsi a mbǝt humta Yahudawechihi lela atfichiwa kǝttǝn hwanda fichile kaltǝfichihi, thla'angnda Istifanus fa tǝ halǝ'inda, Yahudawechǝ ɓaka Sayirin tǝ Alekzandariya tǝ funa hachahai Kilikiya tǝ Asiya.
ACT 6:10 Nakǝn tǝ sǝnǝnafǝ fǝrandǝ Shemeɗ i shunda, ngusǝ mbǝlaakǝ thlarǝhi kǝ halǝn'indǝ tǝndǝwa.
ACT 6:11 Shipangndǝ yipta funa hur a ɓuɓweeta kǝ mbundǝ lektǝ kǝ ɗar Istifanus ndatwa: "Shikanindi mǝla erǝ Musa tǝ Fara."
ACT 6:12 I'nǝyu thla'andǝ hur'inda nofcha, tǝ fa hǝmmbanita, tǝ malɗǝmcha fa sakandǝ kussaɗi. Kǝsangndǝ Istifanus ɓakndǝ tǝnda mbanitǝ fa sakandǝ ichihi.
ACT 6:13 Ɓakndǝ tǝ fa fǝr sheta tǝ lekta, ndakndǝwa: "Nifiya kǝnding la nakna mbu sǝɓ'icha kǝ ɗar mbǝɗi chiɗchiɗya tǝ kuscha Musa,
ACT 6:14 Kǝthlǝm shikanindi mǝla ndatwa Yǝso Lǝnazareta nan fǝffalandǝ mbǝnɗiɗiya, kǝ mbumbweɗaǝn ɗǝsǝchengnǝmhi le malandǝ Musa kǝmhi."
ACT 6:15 Kǝ sǝktǝ nofchi nat sokkǝhi ɓǝt humkǝnhi, thlǝrangndǝ hwanichafa, nakndǝ chumwandǝ'en nda i Mala'ika
ACT 7:1 Kapat pǝristǝkǝn, sahaǝn mi Istifanus wa: "Ichi natnda chitsǝhi ɗarkǝnya kitwa?"
ACT 7:2 Ngǝmang Istifanus wa: "Hwanmanchina tǝ shinchina, sǝkamnji. Farǝ lǝmwanda cheɗang fat'ena kakatnǝm Ibrahim a Mesofotamiya, kana ndǝta sokta a Haran.
ACT 7:3 Ndaǝnwa: "Chukisha hachahaiyeku tǝ parchǝwa kǝ yimna hachahaiyi nati cheɗuta.
ACT 7:4 Thlaakǝn malkǝn hachahaiya Kaldiyawechǝ hi kǝ hachahai Haran kǝ farǝ mǝrta shinkǝn. Kana Fara ɓattǝnda ɓǝɗi natunisǝ nakǝnya.
ACT 7:5 Fǝrawu Farǝ mbǝta mbǝnniyu kǝ ikǝn chika ishtǝ ǝrtǝwa, ndǝffaǝn shundǝhi tǝ ndatwa, kǝmban hachahaikǝn nat nan sokta'ikǝn tǝ kachitkǝn chika nguchik hwe'ensiyu.
ACT 7:6 Ngǝrkǝ Farǝ shunandǝ ndatwa, na kachitwa ɗǝta sokta a hachahai somǝn kǝ mafecha, nanda sat ɓahtǝ kaǝn kǝ hurat aru fwaɗa.
ACT 7:7 Nifǝra ɓahta hachahaiyi sang nofcheku kǝ mafechiyu, ndak Farǝwa, 'a mweshikǝn nanda chetakish kǝ ɓanda mwanita a mbǝɗya.'
ACT 7:8 A hanmunchiniyu ɗǝffang Fara shunda Ibrahim hi i hesha. Ngǝtkǝ Ibrahim Ishaku, heshaǝn a mundǝ foɗfoɗa. Naknamban kichuyu, Ishaku heshaǝn Yakubu, Yakubu heshaǝn hwanchi'en kumngǝrǝnsi chap kakechinǝm.
ACT 7:9 "Kakechǝnǝm tǝkǝn naknda sǝrǝh Yusufu, hi'yang ndandǝ kǝ Masar anakǝn Farǝ tǝndi.
ACT 7:10 Thlǝkkǝnndaɗa hur ɓahta, fǝrang Farǝ mbǝs'ǝnhar tǝ sǝnda a mbanitǝ Fir'auna kutur Masarcha, fǝrang kuturkǝn mwanda a hachahai Masar uf paɗ fǝraǝn huraa'ena har.
ACT 7:11 Ɓak mita yimta hachahai Masar tǝ Kan'ana, tǝ ɓahtǝ kaǝn sokkǝn kakechinǝm ɗǝsǝmtengnandǝsǝwa.
ACT 7:12 Sǝkkǝ Yakubu wa ɗǝsǝmtǝsa Masar, thlǝnkǝn hwechi'en kakechinǝm kǝ Masar kǝthlǝm kǝ ɗǝnda hi ndǝsǝmta paɗ tǝrka ɗǝɗengnanda.
ACT 7:13 Chapatǝ ɗǝɗengnanda, cheɗang Yusufu fata hwanmanchikǝn, paɗ cheɗang Yusufu hwanmanchikǝna Fir'auna.
ACT 7:14 Thlǝnkǝ Yusufu wa shinkǝn tǝ tahhǝt witǝnandǝ nat, nifǝ kumchitmuɗ ngǝrǝnsǝ ɗurman, kǝ ɓanda hai kǝ Masar.
ACT 7:15 Pǝɗak Yakubu kǝ Masar, mǝrkǝna mbǝnniyu nda i mǝrtǝ kakechinǝm.
ACT 7:16 Kohkǝ fichǝ mǝmatchinanda kǝ Shekem ɗǝkficha thlohandǝ kanda a hur kwaɗi hiitǝ Ibrahim tǝ hanɗǝɓǝlta a hara hwecha Hamor a Shekem tǝkǝn.
ACT 7:17 Nak farǝ ɗǝf shunda Farǝ hi tǝ Ibrahim satǝ nduk, Yahudawechikǝna a Masar chekkǝndǝ kaǝn.
ACT 7:18 Tǝrkǝ kutursǝ somǝn a Masar tǝkǝn le sǝnuchik ǝn kǝɗar Yusufu
ACT 7:19 Kuturǝniyu a pupwiktǝ nofchengnǝmhi oi paɗ a fǝraɗǝ ɓahta parchinǝm, la ɗǝfkǝn kandǝ kǝ somangndǝ hanngwa'yarchengnandaɗi kǝthlǝm kǝ mǝmatnda.
ACT 7:20 A thlahɓǝchiniyu ngǝttǝfichǝ Musa, hwee ndiichin a mbanitǝ Fara. Kǝskǝ parchikǝn ndǝhar ndǝraa mǝkkan a hurhura'a shinkǝn.
ACT 7:21 Kǝ muhandǝndaɗi ɗǝk hweya Fira'una tǝrta saǝn nda hwe'en mwanaǝn.
ACT 7:22 Sakangfichǝ sǝnda Musahar i Masarawechi nat, paɗ alchit'ensi a hur torchǝ tǝ shunda.
ACT 7:23 "Saakǝn hurat kumchit fwaɗa, ndakǝnwa kemsǝ kǝɗa nat fahchikǝn Israilawecha.
ACT 7:24 A farǝle nakǝn lǝ Masarta ɓahandǝ hwanmankǝn, thlǝkǝn hwanmankǝn ɓǝlaǝn hwan lǝ Masartiyu.
ACT 7:25 Naǝn Musa hiwa hwanmanchikǝn Israilawecha mbǝsandǝwa Farǝ naka sǝt tor tǝndi kǝ chaǝn kanda kissha hur ɓahta, a nakǝn ɓǝssawundǝwa.
ACT 7:26 Wenkǝɓǝta ngǝrkǝn chetakish, nakǝn hwanmanchikǝn Israilawechi chap kanda mbata, 'yahkǝnsa mbǝnandǝ kanda, ndakǝnwa: 'Hishcha' nakuni hwanmani mǝsǝk natuni mbata?''
ACT 7:27 Lenaka fǝra ɓahta shekkǝnyu njingtaǝn Musa ɗi ndakǝnwa, 'Wun ɗǝfkǝsa kutura tǝ lǝ sakmi kǝ ɗarnani?'
ACT 7:28 'Yahnǝsa ɓǝlitǝ nda i ɓǝlandu lǝ Masarti ɓǝraa'yuwa?
ACT 7:29 Kǝsǝktǝ Musa kichu, rahkǝn malkǝn hachahaikǝnhi pǝɗakna hachahaya Midiyanacha sokkǝn kǝ romma ɓǝnniyu paɗ ngaǝlngǝn hweechi chap kǝ hishcha.
ACT 7:30 Ɗifitǝ hurat kumchitfwaɗa, cheɗang mala'ika fat'ena Musa tǝ mbǝnda hanshuwun hwata, naka kǝsta ɗar hanafta a loktara nduk tǝ shohla Sina'i.
ACT 7:31 Kǝnat Musa i'niyu pǝɗangǝnfa mbǝnniyu. Ɓahkǝn nduk kǝthlǝm kǝnanhi ndiichin, sǝkkǝn ɓurata Lǝmwanda:
ACT 7:32 'Njang naka Fara kakechuwa, Fara Ibrahim, Ishaku tǝ Yakubu.' Lechik Musa, nakna saktatfa tǝraǝn hwanitaɗi.
ACT 7:33 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Lǝmwandǝwa, 'Mbasan pahǝmchekuhi, kǝthlǝm mbǝɗi thlartusiyu chiɗchiɗtǝ mbǝta.
ACT 7:34 A neɗi ɓahta nofchengnǝhi a Masar. Shiki tiɗengnanda, Ɓakihaiya kǝthlǝm kǝthlǝ kandaɗi. Nakǝnya ɗu ni thlǝnsa kǝ ngǝrangnǝinna Masar
ACT 7:35 "Musati chertǝnda ndatwa: 'Wun ɗǝfkǝsa kutura tǝ lǝ sakmiya?' Mǝlan thlǝntǝ Farǝ nakǝnya kǝ naka kutura tǝ lǝ thlǝtkandaɗi tǝ mbǝɗa mala'ika cheɗang fat'en tǝ mbanda hwata ɗar hanafta.
ACT 7:36 Nifiniyu chang kanda kish a Masar, ɗifitǝ sǝt ichi pǝɗang nofchifǝ kaǝn, paɗ tǝ i sǝtna a fi hawurta tǝ loktara, tǝrkǝ ndǝ hurat kumchit fwaɗa.
ACT 7:37 Musa tǝkǝn ndangna Israilawechǝ wa, 'Na Fara thla'a'ndǝ yuna hurnuni kǝ tapǝna'a nda njang.'
ACT 7:38 Nifikǝn nakna hurnuni fari ngomtunihi a loktarǝ tǝ kakechinǝm tǝ mala'ika ɓaka shunanda a shohla Sinaiyu tǝ shinchinǝm. Mbǝnniyu thlǝt Musa shuwun nathi kana ɓata fǝranda kǝm.
ACT 7:39 Kakechinǝm tǝkǝn cherkǝnda fǝra mwanda, kawundǝ thlǝmatwa. Cherkǝndǝndi a 'yahkǝndǝsa ngǝrandǝinna Masar.
ACT 7:40 Ndangnda Haruna wa kǝ tahsaǝn ɗǝhhacha kandǝsi, fichile na nata mban. Kǝthlǝm sǝnwum i kǝskǝ Musa ti chang kǝma kishsha Masar wa.
ACT 7:41 Tinkǝndǝ ɗǝhhata nda hwalata, thlangndǝ ɓurat ɗǝhǝrǝmcha ɗǝhhakǝn i mbǝnfata kǝ ɗar i tahǝstǝndǝ tǝ harchengnanda.
ACT 7:42 Tǝɓrang Farǝ hǝsǝra kandǝfa malkǝn kandǝhi kǝnnda mwanandǝ handǝrecha afshi nda farengnanda, nda i natna hur yaratkǝna tapǝnecha, kunang Israilawecha, njang thlanduni ɓurat ɗǝhǝrǝmcha mwananduni ɗǝhhacha a loktarǝ hurat kumchitfwaɗa wa?
ACT 7:43 Harkuni kǝttǝn ɗǝhhachengnuni Molek tǝ ɗǝhha handǝra'a Refan, nakuni witǝ tǝ kanda, ɗǝhhachi tahǝstuni tǝ harcha kǝthlǝm kǝ mwanangnguni kanda, njang paɗ ni harandi kuni kǝ ɗifitǝ Babila.
ACT 7:44 Soh kakechinǝm tenti engnandǝsi a loktara, le cheɗkǝwa lanak Fara mbǝnniyu. Ndǝkǝn na tenti tǝ ndandǝ Fara Musa wa kǝ tahsǝn, tahǝskǝndǝ nda i ndandǝ Fara kanda.
ACT 7:45 Ɗifitǝ hurecha, kakechinǝm ti thlǝk iniyu, ɓakndǝ tǝkǝna hachahayi fǝrandǝ Fara kanda, ɗifitǝ rǝki rǝktǝ Farǝ nofchi naka hachahaikǝn, fari nat Joshua kǝ lǝ hǝm mbanita. Tenti tiniyu nakna mbǝnniyu kǝ thlahmbǝɗi sǝt Dauda kuturichita.
ACT 7:46 Dauda tǝkǝn mbishtǝ ɗwachita mbǝɗa Fara a hwankǝnwa nan tina hura'a Fara Yakubu si.
ACT 7:47 Sokkǝn Sulemanu tinang hurikǝnsi.
ACT 7:48 A nakǝn Kapat Lǝmwanda sokwa hurǝ'i tintǝ nifǝ tǝ harwa, nda i ndat tapǝna'a,
ACT 7:49 "Hur afshi mbǝt soktengna, hachahaya mbǝt sǝt sarǝchengna, witǝ hurǝmǝ natuni tinitǝsi? Paɗaa witǝ mbǝt yipmi natuni tinitǝsi?"
ACT 7:50 Nga harchengnǝ tingkǝ ichi natyawowa?
ACT 7:51 Kunang fa kwaakwachit hur i'ncha, tǝ fa kwaakwachit hanɗǝkikecha, tǝ fa kwaakwachit thlǝmecha, kǝ nding kuna cherami Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗ fa. Sǝk kakechinuni kichuyu a nakuni sǝtkichu kunang paɗ
ACT 7:52 A hur tapǝnecha, wun fǝrawuchit kakechinuni ɓahta? Ɓǝlandǝ fichile mbukǝ ɓata lǝ kafatchiɗchiɗ. kunang paɗ fǝrkunindǝ a ɓǝllangnguni.
ACT 7:53 Thlǝkuni kuscha Fara cherkuni hǝrǝmtǝhar keeke.
ACT 7:54 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu sǝɓkǝ hurchengnandanɗi, nangnda cha'andǝ hanthlanchengnandǝ kǝ ɗarkǝn.
ACT 7:55 A nakǝn Istifanus a nihiɗaɗi tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, kǝlakna hur afshi a nakǝn mwanda Fara, paɗ Yǝso kita harsǝmta Fara.
ACT 7:56 Ndǝkǝn ndat Istifanus wa: "Nama, a neɗi afshi inhi paɗ hweya nifa kita harsǝmta Fara."
ACT 7:57 Thlaakǝndǝ tǝ kapat kukwara, ngǝlangndǝ thlǝmechengnandǝ tǝ harchengnanda ngomangndafa.
ACT 7:58 Changnda kish kǝ hǝsǝr hura'a ndǝknda mumuhwandafa. Fichile mumuhwangfiyu malkǝndǝ ichengnanda mbǝnniyu hara kimshaa lela atfichiwa Shawulu.
ACT 7:59 Naknda mumuhwanda Istifanusafa, hwankǝn ndatwa: "Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso, thlu shemeɗengna."
ACT 7:60 Hǝmkǝna ɗar weɗchi'en, i'naǝn ɓurathi kaǝn, ndakǝnwa: "Lemwanda, mǝ thlikani ɓǝɓichitfechiya a ɗar inchengnandǝwa." Mbukǝn i'niyu, mǝrkǝn.
ACT 8:1 Huneɗ Shawulu ɗar ɓǝl Istifanus. A farǝniyu thlaakǝ kapat ɓahtǝ kǝ ɗar fa tǝrmbayi naka Urshelima. Wuwelkandǝhi kǝ thlet hǝmǝt Yahudiya tǝ Samariya, fa thlǝnchǝ ndak maltǝndǝsi.
ACT 8:2 Funǝ nofchisi fa mwandǝ Fara ndǝknda thlohandǝ Istifanus, tikndǝ kaǝn kǝ mǝrti'en.
ACT 8:3 A nakǝn Shawulu ndǝkna mban tǝ fǝra ɓahta fa tǝrmbanda nda hishchǝ tǝ nishcha, la yimkǝn huraahura'a, mǝla somkanda pursuna.
ACT 8:4 Fichile wuwelandǝ fichi kandǝhiyu, pǝɗaknda thlet mbichǝ somsomǝn naknda ɓassǝ pathla Fara.
ACT 8:5 Pǝɗak Filibus kǝ hurhuri Samariya ɗǝkna nata ɓassanda nofchisi kǝ ɗar Kǝrǝsti.
ACT 8:6 Nofchi oi tǝ hanɗǝkiketǝ ǝrta sǝkkǝnda, nakndǝ ǝnat pǝɗadǝfaɗifǝ natna sǝta, naknda kathlǝmata i nat Filibussa mbuta.
ACT 8:7 Ɓǝɓi shemechi naka chetakishyu naknda kukwara. Tǝraɗcha tǝ fichile sakkaɗi kanda kǝɗaɗi.
ACT 8:8 Nak mbǝnfatsǝ kaǝn a hǝmǝɗiniyu.
ACT 8:9 Nifǝsa mbǝnniyu thlǝmkǝnwa Saminu, lǝ sǝt tor kullata, lafǝraǝn ǝnat pǝɗandǝ Samariyawechafa, la tǝrkǝnwa kapat nifǝ nakǝn.
ACT 8:10 Chikawuni, hanhwe tǝ kapatnifa nat a fǝrandǝ hur'inda tǝ ndatwa: "Nifiya alchita Fara la atfichǝwa kapat Mwanda."
ACT 8:11 A fǝrangndǝ hur'indǝ kaǝn, kǝthlǝm a mwin tirǝɓ mǝla sǝt ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nofchifa tǝ ǝnat kullechi'en.
ACT 8:12 Paɗ kǝ ɓat nofchiyu fǝrkitta ɓassa Filibus kǝ ɗar kusheng shundǝ ɓinchin kǝ pathlǝ kuturichita Fara tǝ thlǝm Yǝso Kǝrǝsti, sangndǝ baptisma kanda, hischi tǝ nishchi nat.
ACT 8:13 Chika Saminu tǝ i'ndǝ'en a firtǝkit, saǝn baptisma nakna witǝ tǝ Filibus kalutǝndǝhiwa. Saminu nakna nat ichi natna sǝta i pǝɗandǝ nofchifa, mǝlan paɗ pǝɗang ǝnfa.
ACT 8:14 Kǝ sǝktǝ fathlǝnchi Urshelimayuwa, Samariyawecha a thlǝɗndǝ pathla Fara, thlǝnangndǝ nda Bitrus tǝ Yohanna kanda.
ACT 8:15 Satengnanda, hwanangnda kaɗǝsi kǝthlǝm kǝ thlǝndǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ.
ACT 8:16 Kǝthlǝm Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗkǝn tǝrwahai kǝ ɗar inda yunǝ kwandǝnwa, tǝ sang fichi baptisma kandǝ ndak a hur thlǝm Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso.
ACT 8:17 Ndǝkǝn sandǝ Bitrus tǝ Yohanna harcha kanda in thlǝkndǝ Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗa.
ACT 8:18 Kǝnat Saminuwa tǝ ɓǝɗa ndǝfhara'inna fathlǝnchǝ la mbǝstǝ fichi Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗa, fǝraǝn hanndǝɓǝlta kanda.
ACT 8:19 Ndakǝnwa: "Njang paɗ fǝramitǝn alchiɗiya, kǝthlǝm chikawun ndǝfandi hara'in kǝ thlǝn Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗa."
ACT 8:20 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Bitrus wa: "Sokǝn tǝ hanndiɓǝlteku kǝ thlǝrtuninɗi, mbah sukǝnfǝwa nu mbǝs fǝrta Farǝ tǝ hanndiɓǝlta.
ACT 8:21 Sǝssa hur torchiyawa, kǝthlǝm hanndǝkiketeku nga keeke kǝ mbǝɗa Farǝ wa.
ACT 8:22 Tǝrruhi hur ɓǝɓi ndǝsǝcheku kǝ hwanangnǝ Lǝmwanda ma mbandǝsi kǝ kallukǝn ɓǝɓi yarekuhi.
ACT 8:23 Kǝthlǝm kǝlayi sokǝn cheku nat ɗǝhɗǝh, paɗ naku chingching hur ɓǝɓifata."
ACT 8:24 Ngǝmang Saminuwa: "Hwanamitǝnsi kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda kǝthlǝm ichi mbutuni natya, mǝ ɓiɗa ɗar indengnǝwa."
ACT 8:25 Kǝ mbwa'andǝ Bitrus tǝ Yohanna kanda i natnda, ɓassangndǝ pathla Lǝmwanda kaɗǝsi le nak ɓinchin, naknda ngǝrangndǝ'ina Urshelima, ndǝkndǝ tǝ ɓassa a thlet hǝmchǝ somsomǝn, a hachahai Samariya oi.
ACT 8:26 Ndang mala'ika Lǝmwanda Filibuswa: "Thla'u ɗu tǝ kukuwun hishingteku kǝ tǝrnǝ mbayi thlaaka Urshelima kǝ Gaza yu, naka mba loktariyu."
ACT 8:27 Thlaakǝn pǝɗakǝn, kǝmkǝn tǝlǝ Itiyofiyata mbanda, kullaɓta, kapat nifa a hur kuturichita Kandis, kutur nishcha a Itiyofiyata, mǝlan na lǝ kǝs ndǝɓǝltǝhar. Ɓakna Urshelima kǝthlǝm kǝ mwanaǝn.
ACT 8:28 Nakna ngǝrandǝ i'naɗi ɗassa hur ǝnat sokta a Pirish keeke'en, mǝla changngat ɗelwerra Ishaya tapǝna'a.
ACT 8:29 Ndang Shemeɗa Filibuswa: "Ɗuɗuk tǝ Pirish keeketiyu."
ACT 8:30 Rahkǝ Filibus kǝ thlǝmmatkǝn, nakna sǝk i nat nifiyu changngata a hur ɗelwerra Ishaya tapǝna'a. Sahang Filibus wa: "Shinnǝ sakǝt i natu changngatyawa?"
ACT 8:31 Ngǝmang nifiyuwa, "Naki sǝndǝwa kǝni manga nifi tausang engnǝwa?" Ndǝkǝn ndandǝna Filibus wa kǝ tǝrǝnsi kǝ ɗa mbǝssndi kǝ sokndǝ rǝmma.
ACT 8:32 I natna changngata a hur ɗelwertǝkǝn ndatwa: "Kahkǝ fichindi nda shohrata kǝ mbǝt thletɓurata. Nda i lanat hwan Shohrat ɓa a hara lǝ hǝsta, nakǝn kichu chika miya i'nawuhiwa.
ACT 8:33 Njirkǝndǝndi paɗ njangndǝ kitchitkǝn. Wunna mbǝla mbu kachitkǝn? Kǝthlǝm thla fichǝ shisshingtǝenhi hur kishita."
ACT 8:34 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ kullaɓiyu Filibuswa: "Wunnat tapǝni'iya shunda ɗarkǝn, kǝ ɗar'i'ndi'enwa ndu kǝ ɗar yunǝ somǝn?"
ACT 8:35 Tǝrkaakǝ Filibus shunda tǝrta mbǝɗi changngat nifiyu, nakna mbwa'a kweshcha kusheng shundǝ kǝ ɗar Yǝso.
ACT 8:36 Naknda ɗar wita hur mbanda saakǝnda mbǝɗi nat amsi, ndak nifiyuwa: "A amya mǝna njat kǝ sikǝ fichi baptisma?"
ACT 8:37 Ndak Filibus wa, "Ma firnǝkit tǝ hanɗǝkiketǝ ǝrta sukǝ ficha: "Ngǝmang nifiyuwa Firikit Yǝso Almasihu hweya Farǝ nakǝn."
ACT 8:38 Chatkichuyu ndak nifiyuwa kǝ thlarang fichi Pirish keeketihiyu. Nda Filibus tǝ kullaɓiyu tǝrkǝnda haya, yimkǝnda hur ammiyu, sang Filibus baptisma.
ACT 8:39 Kǝ natnda cheta hur amkǝn, tǝrang Shemeɗa Lǝmwanda Filibus. Kullaɓiyu ngǝrutǝ natndǝ paɗwa, kǝskǝn mbandǝ'en pǝɗakǝn tǝ mbǝnfata.
ACT 8:40 A nak fichi Filibus a Azotus. Nakna ɓǝrtǝhi ɓasskǝn kusheng shundǝ mbinchinna thlet hǝmchini natta mbǝnniyu saakǝnna Kaisariya.
ACT 9:1 Ɗǝk Shawulu mban tǝ fǝraa lechita fa tǝrmbanda Lǝmwandǝ kaǝn, ndatwa nan ɓǝllandǝ kanda, ɗǝkna ɓǝɗa kapat pǝrist.
ACT 9:2 Hwanaǝn kǝ yaraǝn ɗelwerchisi kǝ mbǝt humta Yahudawechihi a Dimaska, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝssǝn mba kǝsandǝ nofcha fa tǝrmbakǝn, hishchǝ tǝ nishchǝ nat kǝɗǝn tǝkanda Urshelima a kǝnda.
ACT 9:3 Mǝla pǝɗata, shee nduk tǝ Dimaska tǝkǝn chat kichuyu ɓak ɗwachita haya afshi tauraǝn Shawulu tǝkǝnhi.
ACT 9:4 Hǝmkǝnhi hachahaiya sǝkkǝn ɓurata ndatwa: "Shawulu, Shawulu, kǝthlǝmǝ natu ɓahita?"
ACT 9:5 Mǝlan paɗ ndakǝnwa: "Wunnaku Lǝmwanda?" Ndǝkǝn ɗandǝnwa: "Njang Yǝso le natu fǝra ɓahtiyu.
ACT 9:6 Thla'u kǝ yimna hurhura'a, mbǝnniyu nanda mbu'u i natu sǝta."
ACT 9:7 Nofchi nannda witǝ rǝmmǝyu, thlarkǝndǝhi kǝmma kanda shundǝsuwa, kanda sǝk ɓuratkǝn nakǝn kanda nat nifǝwa.
ACT 9:8 Thlaakǝ Shawulu a hachahaiya, i'naǝn hwanichi'enhi mbǝla'utǝ nat ǝnwa. Nofchi nannda witǝyu kǝskǝndǝ har'en, ndǝkndǝ tǝnda hurhuri Dimaska.
ACT 9:9 Mundǝ mǝkkan mǝla natmbǝtwa, paɗ sǝmutǝ'ǝnwa sutǝ amwa.
ACT 9:10 Lǝ tǝrɓandǝsa Dimaska lǝ atfichiwa Hananiya, ndang Lǝmwanda a hur ǝn nda sǝnnatǝwa: "Hananiya." Ngǝmanwa: "A njangya Lǝmwanda."
ACT 9:11 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Lǝmwandǝwa: "Thla'u kǝ ɗǝnna mbayi la atfichiwa Ndellengnga, kǝ sahnǝ hura'a Yahuda nifi ɓaka Tarsus la atfichiwa Shawuluyu. Nakǝn kicheya mǝla hur hwanda.
ACT 9:12 A neɗɗa hur ǝn nda sǝnnatǝwa nifa ɓata la atfichiwa Hananiya, ma shee nansa harcha in kǝthlǝm kǝ ngǝrǝn nat mbǝta."
ACT 9:13 Ngǝmang Hananiya wa: "Lǝmwanda, a shiki nofchi oiya mbu ɓǝɓi icha ɗar nifinǝyu le sandǝn fa tǝrmbanda a Urshelima:
ACT 9:14 Paɗ pǝktat pǝristchiyu fǝrandǝ alchita kǝ kǝssaǝn chikawun naka at thlǝmwa."
ACT 9:15 Ndǝkǝn ɗandǝ Lǝmwandǝwa. "Ɗu, kǝthlǝm teɗindi kǝ sokka ǝnat torrengna, kǝ ɗǝn tǝ thlǝmna mbǝɗa punofcha tǝ kuturcha, paɗ tǝ Isra'ilawecha.
ACT 9:16 Ni cheɗa witǝ ɓahhi natna satta kǝthlǝm thlǝmna."
ACT 9:17 Pǝɗak Hananiya, ndǝkna mbǝssandǝ Shawulu. Saǝn harcha in, ndakǝnwa: "Hwan'yaa Shawulu, Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso cheɗukǝ fat'ena mbandǝyu thlinkǝnji kǝthlǝm kǝ ngǝrnǝ natmbǝta paɗ kǝ nǝhǝɗnǝ tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ."
ACT 9:18 Chat kichuyu ichi nda ɓwar tinda hǝhatkǝnda haya a hwanichi'en, ngǝrkǝna nata natmbǝta. Thlaakǝn sangfichi baptisma.
ACT 9:19 Sǝmkǝn ǝna ɓak alchit'enaɗi. Sokkǝ Shawulu hi a Dimaska, i hanmunchi ɗǝmek tǝ fa tǝrmbanda.
ACT 9:20 Chatkichuyu tǝrkaakǝn nata ɓasǝ Yǝso, a mbǝt humta Yahudawechihi ndatwa, mǝlan naka hweya Fara.
ACT 9:21 Nat fichile sǝkkǝndi, pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfa, ɗakndǝwa, "Awi nga nifiya wuwelang fa tǝrmbanda Yǝso ɗa a Urshelima wa? Ɓakna mbǝɗya kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝssaǝn kanda kǝ ɗǝn tǝ kanda kǝ mbǝɗa kapat pǝristchikǝn?"
ACT 9:22 Ɓassa Shawulu nakǝn kǝ chektǝ kǝ chektǝ tǝ alchita, paɗ shiwunchi'en kǝ ɗar Yǝso nakǝn tǝɓraɗǝ hur'i'nda Yahudawechihi naka Dimaska.
ACT 9:23 Ɗifitǝ hanmunchi kaǝn, humang Yahudawechi miwa nanda mbǝllanda.
ACT 9:24 Kanda ngunguɗndi fiɗiktǝ tǝ farǝ nat, a mimbangnga kǝthlǝm kǝ ɓǝllangnda, a nakǝn kusheng shiwunkǝn himma thlǝmata Shawulu.
ACT 9:25 A fiɗikta kimshechi'en hǝrkangndǝ tǝ tinkuɓata hur changlangta.
ACT 9:26 Kǝ saatǝ Shawulu Urshelima, sǝkǝn i natna sǝta kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝmndǝ tǝ fa tǝrmbanda, a nakǝn natnda kanda lechanda. Fǝrundǝ kitsuwa shiɗa lǝ tǝrmbandiwa.
ACT 9:27 Ndǝkǝn kǝstǝ Barnabas har'en, ɓakǝn tǝnda mbǝɗa fathlǝncha, paɗ mbwa'angna kandǝ kǝmmi kǝmtǝ Shawulu tǝ Lǝmwanda, a mba Dimaska tǝ witǝ shuni shunandǝ Lǝmwanda. Ngǝrkǝn ndanda kandǝ paɗwa ɓesh Shawulu tǝ alchitafa a hur thlǝm Yǝso a Dimaska.
ACT 9:28 Sokkǝ Shawulu tǝ kanda, wu'yaǝn kandǝ nat nda hurkǝn tǝ ɗifitǝkǝn a Urshelima, nakna ɓassǝ tǝ alchitafa a hur thlǝm Lǝmwanda.
ACT 9:29 A lanakna shundǝ tǝ Yahudawecha fa sǝk Helenanchi kǝna sǝt thlangǝtmi tǝ kanda, yahkǝndǝsi kǝ ɓǝsɗǝ mbanda mbah nanda ɓǝllangnda.
ACT 9:30 Kǝɓat fahchikǝnna mbǝssandǝ kichu, tǝrkǝndǝndi kǝ Kaisariya, paɗ thlingkǝndǝndi kǝ Tarsus.
ACT 9:31 Sokkǝn fa tǝrmbayi a Yahudiya tǝ Galili tǝ Samariya yu, ɓeɗnda mbǝs yuyurchita, naknda ɗǝta mban tǝ torchengnanda tǝ alchitafa, kǝthlǝm fa tǝrmbakǝn naknda wita hur lechanda Lǝmwanda. Paɗ tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗɗa kǝssanda kandǝsi naknda chekta.
ACT 9:32 Nak Bitrussa nata wiyandǝ mbichi somsomǝn a hurnanda, ɓakna mbǝs hwecha Fara a Lidda.
ACT 9:33 Mbǝnniyu ɓatna mbǝssandǝ nifi la atndǝwa Iniyas, ndukka mbǝthunat hurat foɗffoɗa sheɗ sarǝchi'enaɗi.
ACT 9:34 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Bitrus wa: "Iniyas, kǝnnu Yǝso Kǝrǝsti ɗi, thla'u tǝrru mbǝthunaɗeku." Chatkichuyu thlaakǝn.
ACT 9:35 Uf nofchi naktǝ sokta a Lidda, tǝ Sharon nakndǝ Iniyas mǝla witǝhi tǝɓǝrkǝndǝhi kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda.
ACT 9:36 Lǝ tǝrmbandǝsa Yoffa thlǝmkǝnwa Tabita le nat sakǝtkǝnwa Dokas. Kafat'ensi paɗ fǝrchin'ǝna.
ACT 9:37 A hanmunchiniyu haɗkǝn, mǝrkǝn, fanang ficha ndǝknda ndǝfnda kǝttǝn afshi, kǝthlǝm kǝ thlohahnda.
ACT 9:38 Lidda nakǝn nduk tǝ Yoffa. Sǝkkǝ fafǝrkit wa Bitrussa mbǝnniyu. Thlingkǝndǝ nofchi chap kǝ mbǝɗ'en ndatwa: "Komkom weshu ɓana mbǝs kani nga tǝ kǝfatichitfuwa."
ACT 9:39 Thlaakǝ Bitrus pǝɗakndǝ tǝ fichile thlintǝnda. Kǝ saatǝn, ɗǝkndǝtǝnda hurǝ afshitǝkǝn. Kǝttǝnkǝn nihiɗaɗi tǝ ndǝlat nishchi fichile mǝrtǝ hishchengnanda, kanda tita paɗ cheɗangndǝ njelechi tǝ tahhǝt ichi 'yahmandǝ Dokas tǝkǝna kandǝsi, thlahɓǝndǝ natǝn tǝ kanda.
ACT 9:40 Chang Bitrus nofchakissha kǝttǝnkǝn uf, sǝkkǝn kurumchihi, hwankǝn. Kǝ tuɓwandǝn hwakǝn, tǝɓǝrkǝnhi fa murutkǝn ndakǝnwa: "Tabita, thla'u." Chatkichuyu inaǝn hwanichihi, kǝ natǝn Bitrus, thlaakǝn ɗas.
ACT 9:41 Kǝskǝ Bitrus har'en thla'aǝn. Ndǝkǝn atǝn ndǝlat nishchi mǝrtǝ hishchengnandǝyu, nat tǝ fafǝrkit, fǝraǝn Tabita tǝkǝnna kanda tǝ shisshingtafa.
ACT 9:42 Kusheng shiwunkǝn fankǝnhi a Yoffa nat, paɗ nofchǝ terchin fǝrkǝkit kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda.
ACT 9:43 Sokkǝ Bitrus hi a Yoffa tǝkǝn hanmunchi kaǝn, hura'a Saminu lǝ tahhasǝ pomcha.
ACT 10:1 Nifǝsa a Kaisariya thlǝmkǝnwa Karneliyus. Kapat nifa a mbǝt thlǝrhwata Italiyacha la atfichiwa: "Hum'i'nda fa thlǝrhwecha Italiya."
ACT 10:2 Mǝlan lǝ tǝrmbanda Fara, paɗ lalechengna Fara, mǝlan tǝ nofchi'enna huraa'en. La fǝraǝn icha nofcha tǝ har chaa, paɗ la nakna hwanandǝ Farǝ noknok.
ACT 10:3 Farǝle tǝ farǝhufta hanthlǝkkǝn mǝkkan, nakǝn mala'ika Fara ndaa hursǝnnata mǝla ɓata mbǝsndi, ndaǝnwa: "Karneliyus."
ACT 10:4 Kǝllang Karneliyus tǝ lechitafa, ndakǝnwa: "Mi, Lǝmwanda?" Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ mala'ikawa: "Hwandeku tǝ fǝr'ǝnneku shee'a mbǝɗa Fara, ǝnat kuɗuktǝhar a mbanitǝ Fara.
ACT 10:5 Nakǝnya, thlǝnu nofchǝ kǝ Yoffa kǝ andǝ Saminu lelǝ atfichiwa Bitrus.
ACT 10:6 Nakna sokta mbǝɗa Saminu lǝ tahhasǝ pomcha, le nat huraa'ena mi hawurta."
ACT 10:7 Kǝ pǝɗat mala'ika ti shunangyu, ak Karneliyus nofchihar chap a hur mafechi'en, fa sa tora huraa'en, tǝlǝ thlǝrhwata lela lechangnga Fara, hur fichile lǝ sang tor kǝnding.
ACT 10:8 Mbwa'aǝn chikama kanda, thlǝnkǝn kanda Yoffa.
ACT 10:9 Ɓingǝtkǝn, nofchi thlǝntǝ Karneliyusyu ndukndǝhi kǝ hurhura'a, pǝɗak Bitrussa hurǝ afshi, ɗǝkna nata hwanda a hurfara.
ACT 10:10 Nak mita fi'en, paɗ yahkǝnsa sǝm'ǝna, ficha nǝha'ǝna chat yimkǝnna hur ǝn nda sǝnnata.
ACT 10:11 Nakǝn afshi inhi, ǝna ɓatahai nda kapat ɗǝ supta, firficha hai tǝ kukuwunchi'en fwaɗɗa.
ACT 10:12 I sǝka ɗǝhǝrǝmta neesa hurkǝn, fa sarǝchǝsǝ fwaɗɗa, tǝ fa kah hurcha hachahaya tǝ ɗishcha.
ACT 10:13 Sǝkkǝn ɓurata ndanduwa: "Thla'u, Bitrus: thliu ɓurata kǝ chiina."
ACT 10:14 Ndǝkǝn ndat Bitruswa: "Auwa Lǝmwanda, kǝthlǝm tamwi chi i nguchik chiɗchiɗ ndu ndǝɗuwowa."
ACT 10:15 Ngǝrkǝn sǝk ɓuraɗiyu i chapatǝkǝn ndatwa: "I tahsandǝ Farǝhi tamina ndatwa nga chiɗchiɗwa."
ACT 10:16 Kurɓang iniyu sǝt mǝkkan. Chat kichuyu kahang fichi ǝnatkǝnaɗi kǝ afshi.
ACT 10:17 Nak Bitrussa hur ɓweechitfat kaǝn, kǝ ɗar i'ni nda sǝnnatiyuwa nakna sokta mi? Chat nofchi thlǝntǝ Karneliyusyu sheenda hura'a Saminu, thlerkǝndǝhi kikkita mimbangnga.
ACT 10:18 Akndǝfata sahkǝnda, nifi la atfichiwa Saminu Bitrusyu, ndu tǝrkǝna haya mbǝnniyu.
ACT 10:19 Kǝnat Bitrussa yarandǝ i'nihi nda sǝnnatiyu, ndang Shemeɗwa: "Sǝku, ɓeɗ nofchǝ mǝkkan kanda katsa.
ACT 10:20 Thla'u, tǝruhaya, kǝ pǝɗuni tǝ kanda, mǝ ndǝrminǝwa kǝthlǝm njang thlǝngkǝ kanda."
ACT 10:21 Ndǝkǝn tǝrtǝ Bitrussa hai kǝ mbǝɗa nofchiyu, ndakǝnwa: "Njangya njang natuni kata. Kǝthlǝm mǝ ɓatuni?"
ACT 10:22 Ndǝkǝn ndatndǝwa: "Karneliyus kapat nifa a Romacha thlǝngkǝkani. Kanifǝ nakǝn, paɗ lǝ mwana'ǝn Farǝ noknok, Yahudawechǝ nat la fǝrangndǝ mwanda. Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Mala'ikachǝ ndangwa, kǝ thlǝnukǝn fata kǝ ɗina huraa'en kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝkǝn i natu mbuta."
ACT 10:23 Sang Bitrus marapa kanda, ndangna kandǝwa kǝ hunandǝhi ke wenmbǝta. Ɓingǝtkǝn, thlaakǝn pǝɗakndǝ tǝ nochiyu, funǝ hwanmanchisa Yoffa ndǝfkǝndǝndi.
ACT 10:24 Saakǝnda Kaisariya ɓingǝtkǝn. Karneliyus mǝla pukanda, paɗ ngomandǝ hwanmanchikǝn tǝ shikechikǝn.
ACT 10:25 Kǝnat Bitrussa yimta hurǝkǝn, sang Karnǝliyus marapa, himkǝna mbanitǝkǝn nakna mwananda.
ACT 10:26 Thla'ang Bitrus, ndaǝnwa: "Thla'u, njangma nifǝnaki nda sokǝn."
ACT 10:27 Bitrussa ɗar shundǝ tǝndi yimkǝnda huri, ɗǝknda mbǝstǝ hwim nofchǝ oi.
ACT 10:28 Ndangna kandǝwa: "Kunang tǝ inchengnuni shinuniwa, keekesuwa lǝ Yahudawat kǝ sǝn shikechit ndu kǝ humndǝhi tǝ punofchǝwa. Farǝ cheɗikǝwa mǝ tǝrǝndi chikawun wa nga chiɗchiɗwowa.
ACT 10:29 Ndǝkǝn sǝk ɓati kaɗi katfichinji a cherwifǝwa. Mbwa'amitǝn i sǝk thlǝnitunifata:
ACT 10:30 Ndǝkǝn ngǝrtǝ Karneliyus sǝwa: "Munǝ fwaɗɗa mbǝrkǝhiyu nja hwandǝ hure'engna, hanthlǝkkǝn mǝkkan i farǝhufta a hure'engna, ɓak nifa mbǝsnji tǝ furnjelechafa lela tǝrang hwanita, thlarkǝnhi mbanitina.
ACT 10:31 Ndakǝnwa, Karneliyus, ngǝmma Farǝ hwaɗeku tǝ fǝr'ǝneku, shokka ǝnat kuɗukta mbǝɗa Fara.
ACT 10:32 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, thlǝnu nifi nakǝnya kǝ Yoffa kǝ afichi Saminu lǝ atfichiwa Bitrusyu, tǝrkǝna haya a hura'a Saminu lǝ tahhasǝ pomcha, nduk tǝ mi hawurta.'
ACT 10:33 Chat kǝ thlǝnuti fata, a ndǝrmunǝwa ɓaku. Nakǝnya kanang naka mbǝɗya, nakani mbanitǝ Fara, kǝ sǝkani i fǝrrutǝ Lǝmwanda kǝ mbwa'angna kani."
ACT 10:34 Ndǝkǝn tǝrkaatǝ Biturssa shunandǝ kandǝ tǝ ndatwa: "Nakǝnya ɓǝsaɗi tǝ ndatwa Farǝ taɗuharwa.
ACT 10:35 La thlǝkǝn fichile lalechanga, tǝ fichile la sǝk i nak keeke kǝ ɓǝɗa nofcha.
ACT 10:36 Shinuniwa shuniya thlǝnkǝ Fara mbǝɗa Isra'ilawecha, ficha ɓassa kashuwun yuyurchita kandǝsi tǝ mbǝɗa Yǝso kǝrǝsti. Le naka Lǝmwandǝ nat.
ACT 10:37 Shikuni i sǝka a hachahai Yahudiya nat, tǝrkata a hachahai Galili, ɗifitǝ ɓassǝ baptismati sǝt Yohanna.
ACT 10:38 Paɗ shinuni kusheng Yǝso Lǝnazaratta, witǝ i sǝt Farǝ kǝ ɗarkǝn fǝrandǝn Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ tǝ alchita. Ɗǝk Yǝso mban tǝ ka torcha, mǝla kǝnadǝ nofchandǝ nat fichile kǝsti Sheɗan har, kǝthlǝm Farǝ tǝndi.
ACT 10:39 Kanang na shetacha, kǝthlǝm neɗani ichi sǝttǝn nat a Yahudiya tǝ Urshelima. Ɓǝllangnda tǝ mba kukwandǝhi ɗar palita.
ACT 10:40 Thla'ang Farǝ tǝ shisshingtafa a farǝ mun mǝkkatǝkǝn. Malaǝn paɗ kǝ cheɗin fat'en.
ACT 10:41 Cheɗutǝ fat'en kǝ mbǝɗa nofchi natwa, paɗ kǝ mbǝɗa fichile taɗtǝ Farǝ har kǝ soh, kanang hacha, sǝmkǝ'ǝn tǝ sat'ǝn tǝndi ɗiffitǝ thlatǝ'ena kwata.
ACT 10:42 Fǝraǝn tora kani kǝ ɓasangani nofchisi chika tǝteni, paɗ kǝ cheɗani tǝ kitwa, Yǝso mǝlan taɗtǝ Fara lǝ thlakita chikawunsa hur fa shisshingtǝ tǝ mǝmatcha.
ACT 10:43 Mǝlan shiwuntǝ tapǝnecha inkǝn ndatwa: "Chikawun fǝrkǝkit kǝ mbǝɗ'en, na ficha kala ɓǝɓifechi'enhi hur thlǝmkǝn."
ACT 10:44 Nak Bitrusa hur shiwunchiniyu, ɓak Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗa ɗar chikawun naka sǝk shiwunchi'en.
ACT 10:45 Yahudawechǝ fa tǝrmbandǝ ɓaka Yoffa ndǝfkǝ Bitrus yu, pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfa, kǝthlǝm a thlǝr Farǝ Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗ hi chika kǝ ɗar punofcha.
ACT 10:46 Kǝthlǝm shikndǝ kandǝ kanda shundǝ tǝ michǝ somsomǝn, kanda mwanandǝ Fara. Ndǝkǝn sahtǝ Bitrus wa:
ACT 10:47 "Yunisi na njat kǝ sangfichi baptisma nofchiyawa, taɓkǝn kǝ thlǝndǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ nda i thlǝtani?"
ACT 10:48 Ndǝkǝn ndatǝnwa kǝ sangfichi baptisma kanda a hur thlǝm Yǝso kǝrǝsti. Ɗiffitǝkǝn ndǝkǝn ndandǝnda Bitruswa kǝ chekaǝn munchi ɗimek kicha a thlǝmatnanda.
ACT 11:1 Fathlǝncha tǝ fa fǝrkitti naka Yahudiya, sǝkkǝndǝwa thlǝɗ punofchǝ pathla Fara.
ACT 11:2 Kǝ ɗǝt Bitrussa Urshelima, thla'ang pǝktat Yahudawachǝfa, fichile fǝrkǝkit kǝ ɗar hesha, ndatwa:
ACT 11:3 "Yimku hura'a punofcha fichile heshuchika sǝmku ǝn tǝ kanda"
ACT 11:4 Mbwa'ang Bitrussa kandǝ keeke nat i sǝka.
ACT 11:5 "Nja hǝmǝt Yoffa nja hwanda, naki'ǝn ndaa hur'sǝnnata, naki ǝna ɓata haya hur'afshi nda kapat ǝnat supta, firficha haya hur'afshi tǝ kukuwunchi'en fwaɗa, saakǝn nduk tǝnji.
ACT 11:6 Kǝ kǝlandi nduk a naki ɗǝhǝrǝmcha, tǝ hanthlucha hurhwela'a tǝ fa kah hura hachahaya tǝ ɗishcha.
ACT 11:7 Sǝkki ɓurata nditǝwa: "Thla'u, Bitrus: ɓǝllu kǝ chiina.'
ACT 11:8 Ndakiwa auwa Lǝmwanda, tamu kohat ǝnkichu ndu i nguchik ndiichina yimta hurmiyengnuwa.
ACT 11:9 Ngǝmang ɓurata hur'afshi, shuwunkǝn i chapatǝkǝn, ndatwa: "I sǝt Farǝ chiɗchiɗ kǝ ndǝnuwa ndǝɗuwowa.'
ACT 11:10 Kurɓang iniyu sǝt mǝkkan, kana ficha ngǝr kahanda hur'afshi.
ACT 11:11 Chatkichuyu ɓak nofchǝ mǝkkan kǝ huri'i natanisi, thlǝntǝ fichǝ kanda a Kaisariya kǝ mbǝɗengna.
ACT 11:12 Ndak Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗwa, kǝɗi tǝ kanda mǝtaɗiɗiharwa. Ɗǝfkǝ hwanmanchǝ nji tehhethl, yimkani hura'a nifikǝn.
ACT 11:13 Mbwa'angna kani naɗi natǝn mala'ika kitta hura'en ndakǝnwa, 'Thlǝnu nofchǝ kǝ Yoffa kǝ afichi Saminu nat thlǝmkǝn paɗwa Bitrus:
ACT 11:14 Mǝlan na mbu shuni na fǝru hǝrǝkta, sokǝn tǝ nofchi hure'eku nat.
ACT 11:15 Kǝ tǝrkaati ka shunda, ɓak Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗa hai kǝ ɗar inchengnandǝ nat nda i ɓatna hai kǝ ɗar inchengnani a tǝrkakǝn.
ACT 11:16 Kuɗukki shunda Lǝmwanda nda i ndatǝnwa, 'Sǝk Yohanna baptisma tǝ ama, kunang nak ficha sa baptisma kuni tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ.'
ACT 11:17 Sokkǝn fǝrra Fara kandǝ keeke tǝ le sandǝn kǝm, fari fǝrtǝm kit kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso Kǝrǝsti, wun njang na ndanda Farǝ wa nga kichuwa?"
ACT 11:18 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu ɓahkǝndǝ i natnda mbuta, mwanangndǝ Fara ndatwa: "Awi chika punofchima i'na Farǝ mba tǝrtǝhi kandǝsi tǝ mbǝs shisshingta."
ACT 11:19 Fichile wuwelkǝhi kǝthlǝm pwanchi thlaakǝ kǝ ɗar Istifanusyu, pǝɗakndǝ kǝ hachahai Finikiya tǝ Sayifurus tǝ hǝmǝt Antakiya, naknda ɓassa shuwunkǝna Yahudawechisǝ ɗeng nga chika wunwa.
ACT 11:20 Funǝsa hurnanda Sayifuruscha, tǝ Sayirincha, kǝ saatǝnda Antakiya ɓassangnda punofchisi, naknda mbwa'a kweshcha kusheng shunda kandǝ kǝ ɗar Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso.
ACT 11:21 Hara Lǝmwandǝ tǝkanda, nofchǝ oi fǝrkǝ kit tǝɓǝrkǝndǝhi mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda.
ACT 11:22 Kusheng shuwun i sǝka, saakǝna thlǝmata fa tǝrmbanda a Urshelima, thlǝngkǝndǝ Barnabas kǝ Antakiya tǝkǝn.
ACT 11:23 Kǝ saatǝn paɗ a neɗtǝ kafaɗi sandǝ Farǝ kanda, sǝkǝn mbǝnfat kaǝn paɗ chekaǝn alchita kandǝ tǝ ndatwa, kǝ thlarndǝ tǝ alchitafa hur fǝrkit kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda tǝ hanndǝkikechengnandǝ nat.
ACT 11:24 Kǝthlǝm Barnabas kanifǝ nakǝn, nihǝɗaɗi tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ paɗ tǝfǝrkit. Chekkǝ nofchǝ oi kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda.
ACT 11:25 Pǝɗak Barnabassa Tarsus kakat Shawulu.
ACT 11:26 Kǝ mbǝssandǝn, ɓakǝn tǝnda Antakiya. Hurata, nda Barnabas tǝ Shawulu kanda kǝmtǝ kǝ mbǝt ngǝlhwanita, kanda sakanda nofchihar oi. A Antakiya tǝrkaatǝ ficha at fa tǝrmbachǝwa Kǝrǝstacha.
ACT 11:27 A hanmunchiniyu funǝ tapǝnechǝsi ɓaka Antakiya thlata Urshelima.
ACT 11:28 Ərta hurnanda thlǝmkǝnwa Agabus, thlaakǝn kit shuwunkǝn tǝ alchit Shemeɗa fa ndatwa, na mita natsǝ kaǝn hur kishitǝ nat, sǝk mitǝkǝna thlahmbǝt kuturichita Kalaudiyus.
ACT 11:29 Ndǝkǝn tǝrtǝ fa tǝrmbandǝhurwa, chikawun nan fǝr ǝna keeke a alchit'en kǝthlǝm kǝ thlǝnang ficha hwanmanchi naka hachahai Yahudiya.
ACT 11:30 Sǝkndǝ kichu, thlǝnangnda pǝktechi mbǝnniyu tǝ hara Barnabas tǝ Shawulu.
ACT 12:1 Nda mbǝt kicheeya, Hiridus kutura tǝrkaatǝn fǝrra ɓahta funǝ fafǝrkit a mbǝt ngǝlhwanita.
ACT 12:2 Ɓǝllaǝn Yakubu hwanman Yohanna tǝ thlohta
ACT 12:3 Kǝ natǝn ǝnatkǝn mbǝnaɗa Yahudawechǝ fa, thlaakǝn kǝssaǝn Bitrus paɗ, sǝk i'niyu a thlahmbǝt chohhǝm sǝmɗǝsǝmta le nguchit mehndǝsa fi'en.
ACT 12:4 Kǝ kǝsandǝn muhkǝnnda pursuna, fǝrangna fathlǝrhwecha har, fathlǝrhwechǝ fwaɗa fwaɗa sakkǝn fwaɗa, tǝ yarǝwa ma mbir chohhǝmkǝnhi kana ɓattǝnda mbanitǝ nofcha.
ACT 12:5 Kuɓlang fichǝ Bitrus kǝ hur pursuna, nak fangǝlhwanicha hwananǝndǝ Farǝ tǝkit kǝ ɗarkǝn.
ACT 12:6 A fiɗikiniyu manat Hiridussa chandǝ Bitrussa kish, mǝla saɓweni a thlerǝ fa thlǝrhwechǝ chap. A kǝnandǝ tǝ chalaluchǝ chap. Fa thlǝrhwatkǝn kanda ɗar tor kiikit a mimbang pursuna.
ACT 12:7 Chatkichuyu, ɓak mala'ika Lǝmwanda thlarǝ nduktǝndi, yimkǝ ɗwachita hurkǝttǝnkǝn. Tǝkang mala'ika tǝkǝn harra Bitrus fa mumi thla'a'ǝn, ndaǝnwa: "Thla'u leɗleɗ." Chalaluchi har'enyu kwaskǝndǝhi chuthla.
ACT 12:8 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ mala'ika tiiyuwa: "Kǝnan ɗǝ kǝndeku kan ndiichin, kǝ panǝ pahǝmcheku." Sǝkǝn kichuyu. Ndang mala'ikawa: "Suppu ndǝ supteku fa kǝ kuwurnǝnji."
ACT 12:9 Chekna kissha pursuna tǝkǝn nakna kuwur mala'ika tǝkǝn. Ichini natyu sǝnuwa kitwa, naǝnhiwa ǝnnda sǝnnata natna hurkǝn.
ACT 12:10 Kǝ pǝɗandǝnda fa pumbǝtkǝnhar i tǝrkakǝn tǝ'i chapatǝkǝn saakǝnda mimbangngi sǝtfichi tǝ tǝpassa lela chetfichi chat kǝ hurhura'a, inangna kandǝsǝ ichitkǝn. Chekndakish naknda wita hurmbakǝn, chatkichuyu mala'ika tǝkǝn malkǝnndǝhi.
ACT 12:11 Kǝ ɓat Bitrussa ndǝ kǝ hur'indi'en, ndakǝnwa: "Nakǝnya sǝntiwa tǝ kit Lǝmwandǝ thlǝngkǝ mala'ika'en, kǝ ɓa hǝrkǝta a hara Hiridus tǝ ɓǝɓi sakta Yahudawecha."
ACT 12:12 Kǝ mbǝsandǝn kichu, pǝɗakna hura'a Maryamu, man Yohanna la atfichiwa Markus, mbǝɗi humtǝ nofchǝhi oi kanda hwanda.
ACT 12:13 Kǝ fuɗandǝ Bitrus mimbangkǝn, ɓak hwanhura'a kish kǝ nuhhweya nat thlǝmkǝnwa Roda, kǝthlǝm kǝ nan ndu wuni.
ACT 12:14 Kǝ mbǝssandǝn kǝ ɓurata Bitrus, ngǝraǝn'in kǝ huri inawutǝ mimbangkǝnhiwa, kǝthlǝm mbǝnfata, ndangna nofchiiyuwa: "Bitrus kita mimbangnga."
ACT 12:15 Ndangndǝwa: "Tǝrru luwurcha!" Mǝlan paɗ nakna nata ɗahanda kandǝ'in wa mǝlan. Ndǝkǝn ndatndǝwa: "Nakna nat kǝ mala'ika'en."
ACT 12:16 Bitrus paɗ nakna nata fuɗandǝ mimbangngiyu. Kǝ inaandǝndǝ mimbangkǝnhi nakndǝ kǝ mǝlan, pǝɗang ǝn kandǝfa.
ACT 12:17 Mǝlan paɗ thla'aǝn hara kanda kǝ ngasndǝɓa, mbwa'angna kandǝ chayi chandǝ Lǝmwanda kissha pursuna. Ndakǝnwa: "Kǝ mbwa'anguni Yakubu tǝ tahhǝt hwanmancha ichini sǝk natyu." Pǝɗakna mbǝt somǝn.
ACT 12:18 Wendambǝta, nga hwan thlahur'indi thlaaka hurɗifitǝ fa thlǝrhwechiyuwa kǝ ɗar i kǝskǝ Bitrus.
ACT 12:19 Kǝ kat Hiridus ndi mbǝssawuwa, nakna tawasǝ kitchitkǝnna mbǝɗa fa pukǝnhar. Fǝrkǝn mi tǝ ndatwa kǝ mbǝllangfichi kanda. Ɗiffitǝkǝn thlaakǝ Hiridus a Yahudiya pǝɗakna Kaisariya, sokkǝnna mbǝnniyu kǝ farǝyuna.
ACT 12:20 Nakǝnya shiɓhura Hiridussa ɗi tǝ nofcha Taya tǝ Sidon. Nak nofchini kichuyu ɓaknda mbǝɗ'en, ɗiffitǝ kahhandǝ hur'inda Bilastus le nak mwanchina hura'a kutura, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsndǝ sok yuyurchita paɗ la mbǝskǝndǝ ndǝsǝmta a furta Hiridus tǝkǝn.
ACT 12:21 A farǝle fari tahsandǝ fichihi kǝmtǝ tǝ kutura, pak Hiridus njeli kuturichit'en, sokkǝna mbǝt sok kuturichita shunaǝn nofcha.
ACT 12:22 Nofchi humkǝyu hwaknda ndatwa: "Leya nga ɓurata nifǝwa, ɓurata lura."
ACT 12:23 Chatkichuyu tǝpkǝ mala'ika Lǝmwandǝ Hiridus hi, kǝthlǝm fǝrautǝ mwanda Farǝ wa. Mbǝnniyu cha'ang hwacha Hiridus mǝrkǝn.
ACT 12:24 A nak shunda Fara nata fandǝhi chika tǝteni, nakna ndǝta mban nak fa fǝrkitta chekta.
ACT 12:25 Kǝ tǝɓwandǝ nda Barnabas tǝ Shawulu i natnda sǝta a Urshelima, ngǝrangndǝ'in kǝ Antakiya, tahkǝndǝ Yohanna in la atfichiwa Markus.
ACT 13:1 A kǝtǝn whayi a Antakiyayu Tapǝnechǝsi tǝ malɗǝmcha, Barnabas, Samiyon la atfichǝwa pukǝn, Lushiyus le ɓaka Sayirin, tǝ Manayen, le mwantǝnda mbǝt ǝrtǝ tǝ Hiridus kutura tǝ Shawulu.
ACT 13:2 Naknda mwananɗǝ Lǝmwanda tǝ kǝrkushimta, Ndak Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ wa: "Ɗǝffaam Barnabas hi tǝ Shawulu kǝllar kǝthlem tori ati kanda."
ACT 13:3 Ɗiffitǝ kǝrkushimta tǝ hwanda sangndǝ harcha kanda in ndangnda kandǝwa pǝɗama.
ACT 13:4 Kandang paɗ kǝ thlǝntǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ kanda, pǝɗaknda hai kǝ Salukiya, thlaakǝndǝ kǝ Sayifurus hur kommbawal.
ACT 13:5 Kǝ saatǝnda Salamis, ɓaskǝndǝ pathla Fara hur kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechǝhi. Yohanna mǝlan tǝkanda nakna kǝsanda kandǝsi.
ACT 13:6 Kǝ wiyangndǝn hachahaikǝn nat ɓaknda Bafos, kǝmkǝndǝ tǝlǝ Yahudawata lǝ kulata, tapǝna'a lǝ lekta, thlemkǝnwa Bar Yoshuwa.
ACT 13:7 Le humandǝndǝ i'ndǝ tǝle kǝskǝ hachahaikǝn har, Sarjiyus Bulus, mǝlan ti naka lǝ sǝn'ǝnna. Ngomna tǝkǝn akǝn nda Barnabas tǝ Shawulu, kǝthlem yahsa sǝk pathla Fara.
ACT 13:8 Paɗ Alimas lǝ kulata (kǝthlem sakǝt thlemkǝn kichu tǝ miya Heliniyawecha), fǝrautǝ hum'inda kandǝwa, nakna katkǝ tǝpraǝn hur inda ngomnatǝkǝnhi a hur fǝrkitchiɗiniyu.
ACT 13:9 Nakǝn Shawulu la atfichǝ paɗwa Bulus, nihiɗ tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, kǝlaǝn Alimas ndongnga kǝ hur hwanita.
ACT 13:10 Ndakǝnwa: "Sokǝn hweya sheɗan, atikretǝ ichi nak ndiichin nat. Lǝ lektǝ naku paɗ lǝ shekɗaɗǝ nofcha. Nguna malandǝ tǝɓrandǝ kitchit mbanda Lǝmwandǝhiwowa?
ACT 13:11 Nakǝnya haraa Lǝmwanda sǝt atikrechit tǝssa, paɗ nukukomta nguna mbǝlla nat hwatfarǝwa, kǝ hanthlikchi ɗemek: "Chatkichuyu hussoɓa tǝ hulta ngǝlangndǝ hwanitǝ'en. Nakna tapta kǝna kat le na kǝssandǝsi.
ACT 13:12 Kǝ nat ngomna tǝkǝn i sǝka fǝrkǝn kit, kǝthlem pǝɗa'ǝnatkǝnfǝ oi kǝ ɗar sakta Lǝmwanda.
ACT 13:13 Nakǝnya Bulus tǝ shikechǝ witǝ'en, thlaakǝnda Bafos a hur kommbawal, pǝɗaknda Ferga chaa tǝ hachahai Famfiliya. Yohanna malkǝnkandǝhi ngǝraǝn inna Urshelima.
ACT 13:14 Ɓǝrkǝɗǝhi kǝ ɓan thlata Ferga, pǝɗaknda Antakiya tǝ hachahai Bisindiya. Farǝ yipta Yahudawecha yimkǝnda kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechihi sokkǝndǝhi.
ACT 13:15 Ɗiffitǝ changngata hur kus tǝ ɗelwercha tapǝnecha, fambanichikǝnna hur kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechikǝn, thlǝnangnda kanda ndatwa: "Hwanmancha ma shundengnunisi lena kǝssanda nofchǝsi mbwa'ama."
ACT 13:16 Thlaakǝ Bulus kit thla'a'ǝn haraa kǝ ngas nofchǝ ɓa, ndakǝnwa: "Kunang hwanmanchǝnǝ Isra'ilawecha, tǝ kunang ti lalechangnga Fara, kam thlǝmathi.
ACT 13:17 Fara nofcha Isra'ila, taɗkǝ kakechengnǝm teraǝn kandǝ oi. A thlahmbǝɗi natnda soktǝ nda romcha a hachahai Masar, paɗ tǝ kapat alchita chandǝn kandakish a hachahaikǝn.
ACT 13:18 Kǝrǝskǝn kandǝ hurat kumchit fwaɗa a hur loktara.
ACT 13:19 Ɗiffitǝ thlǝrtandǝ hachahaichaɗǝ muɗ hur Kan'ana, fǝraǝn hachahaikǝnna Isra'ilawecha kǝ sokka innanda.
ACT 13:20 Sǝk i'ya a hur hurat aru fwaɗa tǝ kumchit ɗurman. Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn fǝraǝn fa sak miya kanda kǝ thlahɓǝt tapǝnaa Samaila.
ACT 13:21 Hwankǝndǝ kǝ fwaɗangfichǝ kutura kandǝsi, fǝrang Farǝ Shawulu kanda. Hweya Kish, kachit nda Bilyaminu, le sokkǝ kuturichit hurat kumchit fwaɗa.
ACT 13:22 Kǝ kǝtandǝ Farǝ Shawuluhi, tha'a'ǝn Dauda kǝ sokka kuturreng nanda. Le fǝrtǝ Farǝ sheta kǝɗarkǝn ndatwa: "A mbǝshi Dauda hweya Yessi, nifǝ lǝwitǝ hanɗǝkiketengna, le na sǝt i yahti nat.'
ACT 13:23 "Hur kachit nifǝniyu, ɓat Farǝ tǝ lena Thlǝt Isra'ilawechaɗi, Yǝso, nda i ɗǝftǝn shuwunkǝnhi.
ACT 13:24 Ɓassa Yohanna nofchǝsǝ nat a Isra'ila kǝtǝrndǝhi, kǝ sangfichǝ baptisma kanda, kanna Yǝso ɓata.
ACT 13:25 Kǝ nat Yohanna nduk tuɓandǝ tor'en, ndakǝnwa, lanaǝn kunihiwa wunnaki? Njang nga mǝllanwa. Auwa, yunaɓata ɗifitǝna, le sukuchitisi kǝ kwassayi sahǝtpahǝmchi'enhi."
ACT 13:26 "Hwanmancha, kachit Ibrahim, tǝ fichile hurnuni lalechangnga Fara, kǝ mbǝɗengnǝm thlǝntǝfichǝ kusheng shuwun hǝrǝkiya.
ACT 13:27 Nofchi nak tǝ sokta hur Urshelima tǝ fambanichengnanda, mbǝssaundǝwa mǝllanwa, paɗ sunundǝwa mǝllan shuwuntǝ tapǝnecha ɗarkǝn, la changkandǝfichǝ pwaree a farǝ yipta Yahudawecha, nǝhɗangndǝ shuwunkǝnhi tǝ kiitati thlandǝndǝsi.
ACT 13:28 Chika mbǝssauchikndǝ tǝ chithansarǝhiyu, le kamkǝsi kǝ mǝrrǝn, chika tǝkichu hwanangndǝ Bilatus kǝ ɓǝllangficha.
ACT 13:29 Kǝ nǝhɗandǝndǝ ichihi yaratfichǝ kǝ ɗarkǝn nat, tǝrangndahaya ɗar palita hunangnda hur kwata.
ACT 13:30 Thla'ang Fara hur mǝmatcha.
ACT 13:31 Munchǝ terchin mǝla cheɗafat'ena fichile ɓatndǝtǝndi, thlata Galili kǝ Urshelima, kandang naka shetachi'en nakǝnya kǝ mbǝɗa nofcha.
ACT 13:32 Paɗ kanang ɓangngani kweshcha shuniya kuni tǝndatwa, ɗǝfshuni ɗǝffandǝ Fara shinchinǝmhi.
ACT 13:33 Nǝhɗaɗǝngnǝm hi, kǝmnangti naka hwechengnanda, tǝ mbǝɗa thla'andǝ Yǝso a hur mǝmatcha. Nda i natna hur yaratkǝn, a hur chapatǝ Zabura ndatwa: "Sokǝn naka hwe'engna, ɓukweya sokkǝ kǝ sukka."
ACT 13:34 Pathlǝ thla'ai thla'andǝna hur mǝmatcha, ndatwa: "Ngu ngǝr mǝrtaɗi ndu kǝ ngǝrǝn yirata hurkwatwa." A i mbutǝnya, ni fǝrru chiɗchiɗchita tǝ kitchit mbǝs'ǝnharra Dauda.
ACT 13:35 Kǝthlem ndǝkǝn ngǝrkǝn ndat paɗa hur Zabura tǝllewa: "Ngu malandǝ le nak chiɗchiɗ kǝ yiraka hur kwatwa.'
ACT 13:36 Kǝ mweshandǝ Dauda tori fǝrandǝ Fara, a thlahmbǝt tor'en mǝrkǝn, thlohhangficha, mbǝɗi thlohhandǝfichǝ shinchikǝn, yiraknaɗa hur kwata.
ACT 13:37 Le thla'andǝ Fara a yirruwa.
ACT 13:38 Kǝ sǝnnunisi hwanmancha, ndatwa tǝ mbǝɗa Yǝso natficha kalla ɓǝɓichitfechengnuni kunihi.
ACT 13:39 Chikawun fǝrkǝkit tǝ mbǝɗ'en mbishtǝ hǝrǝkta. Hur chikamǝnat le nguchittu hǝrǝktǝ tǝ kussa Musa.
ACT 13:40 Kǝthlem ndǝkǝn ɗǝffam'indǝsi, mǝɓi i mbutǝ Fara hur ɗelwercha tapǝnecha kǝ mbǝssǝnkuniwa ndatwa:
ACT 13:41 "Namma, kunang fa njirfata, kǝ pǝɗang'ǝnkunifa, kǝ mǝrruni kǝthlem ni sǝt tora hanmunchengnuni, tori nguchittuni fǝrkitchitsi, chika mbwa'ang yuna kuni."
ACT 13:42 Kǝ chetnda Bulus tǝ Barnabassa kish, hwanang nofchǝkǝn kandǝ ndatwa, kǝ ngǝrnda ɓata mbwa'a ichiniyu kanda, a farǝ yipta Yahudawechi na ɓatyu.
ACT 13:43 Ɗiffitǝ wuwela nofchǝ hi, Yahudawechǝ oi tǝ fichile fǝrkǝ inndǝ kaǝn, kǝtǝr mbanda yahudawecha, kuwurkǝndǝ Bulus tǝ Barnabas, shunang ndǝ kanda. Paɗ ndangnda kandǝwa, kǝ ɗǝndamban tǝ nata hur kafata Fara.
ACT 13:44 Ngǝrkǝ farǝ yipta Yahudawecha sata, sokkǝn chikawuna hur hǝmǝtkǝn, hwimndǝhi kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝkndǝ pathla Fara.
ACT 13:45 Paɗ kǝ nat Yahudawechǝ nofchǝ oi, nǝhǝɗkǝ hanɗǝkikecheng nandaɗi tǝ sǝrǝhta, naknda halǝ'inda kǝ ɗar i'mbuttǝ Bulus, paɗ naknda njirndi.
ACT 13:46 Bulus tǝ Barnabas shuwunkǝndǝ tǝ alchita, ndatwa: "Kunang kamkǝsi kǝ tǝrkaafichǝ ɓassa pathla Fara kunisi. Sokkǝn a cheruni, cheɗkuniwa, kamusi kǝ mbǝssuni shisshingtǝ lekǝ pwareewa, nakǝnya nani tǝɓǝrtǝhi kǝ mbǝɗa punofcha.
ACT 13:47 Kǝthlem Lǝmwanda tepa ɗǝftǝkanisi ndakǝnwa: "Ɗifikuni kǝnuni ɗwachita punofcha, kǝthlǝm kǝ sokǝnwa tǝ mbǝɗengnuni nat kishita hǝrǝkta."
ACT 13:48 Kǝ sǝktǝ punofchǝkǝn kichu, sǝkndǝ mbǝnfat kaǝn, tǝpaɗ mwanangndǝ shunda Fara, fichile ɓaka soktǝwa nanda mbǝs shisshingta. Le kǝpwaree fǝrkǝndǝkit.
ACT 13:49 Fankǝ shunda Lǝmwandǝhi chikatǝteni a sǝrǝt hachahaikǝn nat.
ACT 13:50 Yahudawecha ɗǝknda chikandǝ nischa, fa lechanda Fara, paɗ fichile la nat ficha fǝraa mwanda kanda, tǝ pǝktat nofcha hǝmǝtkǝn. Tǝrkaakǝndǝ fǝraa pwancha nda Bulus tǝ Barnabas, tǝpaɗ rǝkkǝndǝ kanda a sǝrǝt thlet hǝmtengnanda.
ACT 13:51 Tǝpangndǝ tǝnnayiɗa sarǝchengnanda, kǝ sokka sheta ɗar inchǝngnanda, pǝɗaknda hǝmǝt Ikoniya.
ACT 13:52 Sokkǝn fafǝrkit, nǝhhǝɗkǝndǝ tǝ mbǝnfat oi, paɗ nǝhhǝɗkǝndǝɗi tǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ.
ACT 14:1 A Ikoniya, Bulus tǝ Barnabas yimkǝnda mbǝt humta Yahudawechǝhi, ɓaskǝndǝ pathla Farǝ tǝ alchitafa, tǝrkǝ nofchǝhi oi, Yahudawechǝ tǝ punofchǝ nat fǝrkǝndǝkit.
ACT 14:2 Yahudawechi fǝruchikkit, kurtangndǝ hur i'nda punofchǝhi, sǝɓangndǝ hurɗifitǝnaɗaɗi kǝ ɗar hwanmanchinandǝ fafǝrkit.
ACT 14:3 Bulus tǝ Barnabas tǝrkǝndǝ hanmunchǝ oi a mbǝnniyu. Kanda ɓassǝ lechitfuwa kǝɗar Lǝmwanda, lefǝrkǝ sheta tǝ shuwun kafat'en, tǝ mba sǝt ǝnnat pǝɗandǝ nofchǝfa, tǝ sakchikǝn tǝ mbǝɗengnanda.
ACT 14:4 Nofchi naka hǝmmǝtkǝn sakkǝndǝhi, funa mbǝɗa Yahudawecha, nak funa mbǝɗa fathlǝnchǝkǝn.
ACT 14:5 Punofchǝ tǝ Yahudawechǝkǝn, tǝ fahǝm mbanichengnanda, tahsangndǝhi wa nanda fǝrra pwancha kanda, paɗ kǝ mumuhhwangnda kandǝfa.
ACT 14:6 Kǝ sǝkkǝndǝ i naka sǝta, rahkǝnda thlet hǝmǝt Listira tǝ Darbe, a hachahai lkoniya, tǝ tahhǝt hǝmchǝ nak nduknduk,
ACT 14:7 a mbǝnniyu ɗǝknda mban tǝ ɓassǝ kweshcha shiwunkǝn.
ACT 14:8 A Listira nifǝsi nak ɗas kǝ tǝraɗ, tamwa sǝt tor tǝ sarǝchǝ'enwa, nakǝn kichuyu kǝ ngǝttǝ'en tamwa witǝuwa.
ACT 14:9 Nakna sǝk ɓassa Bulus, nak Bulussa kǝlandǝ ndongnga, kǝnatǝn fǝrkit'en kemsi kǝ kǝnangfichaɗi.
ACT 14:10 I'naǝn ɓurathi kaǝn ndakǝnwa: "Thla'u thlarnǝhi kit kǝ ɗar sarǝcheku. "Thlaakǝn tǝrkaakǝn wita.
ACT 14:11 Kǝ nat nofchi oiyu i sǝt Bulus i'nangndǝ ɓurechǝhi, ndakndǝ tǝ mi Likoniyachitwa: "Ɓeɗ luwurchahai kǝ mbǝɗengnǝm nda nofcha!"
ACT 14:12 Ɗǝffangndǝ Barnabas wa Zeyus, Bulus paɗ wa Hermes, kǝthlem mǝlan naka kapat lǝ shuwunkǝn.
ACT 14:13 Pǝrissa Zeyus ɗǝhhayu, le nak kapat kǝtǝn ɗǝhhakǝnna ɗifiti hǝmta, ɓakǝn tǝ lecha tǝ fitǝ icha, kǝ mimbang hǝmǝtkǝn, yahhǝnsa fǝr poffǝn'en ɓweet tǝ nofcha.
ACT 14:14 Kǝ sǝktǝ fathlǝnchikǝn nda Barnabas tǝ Bulus i naka sǝta, thlǝthlahhangndǝ njelechengnandaɗi, rahkǝnda hur nofchiyu, thla'angndǝ ɓurata ndatwa:
ACT 14:15 "Nofcha mǝ sǝk natuni sǝt iya?" Kanang nofchǝ nda kunang! Tǝ ɓangngani kweshcha kusheng shunda kuni, kǝthlem kǝ tǝɓrunihi, hurwitǝ ɓǝɓiɗǝsǝchiya kǝ mbǝnda Fara, le nak tǝ shisshingta, le sǝk afshi tǝ kishita, hawurta tǝ ichi nat naka hurchikǝn.
ACT 14:16 Hursoh ti mbǝrkǝhi, malaɗǝ nofchǝ nat kǝ wii nda mbachi yahtǝnda.
ACT 14:17 Chikka tǝ kichu malutǝ fat'en nga ǝ'nat sheta sǝwowa. Kǝthlǝm shiɗtǝ ǝnndiichin, tǝ mba fǝrra ercha kuni afshi tǝ fekchǝ ndiichin, ngalaǝn kuni tǝ ɗǝsǝmta, paɗ mǝlla fǝrra mbǝnfata kuni.
ACT 14:18 Nat tǝ shuwunchiniyu ɓehndǝhi, kan'nda njat fǝr poffǝnti yahtǝ nofchiyu fǝrta, kǝthlǝm kandang.
ACT 14:19 Ndǝkǝn ɓat Yahudawecha a Antakiya tǝ Ikoniya, lǝmkǝndǝ nofchi ngomkǝhiyu, mumuhangnda Bulus fa, paɗ kahangnda kishsha hur hǝmǝtkǝn, naǝn kandǝhiwa miri.
ACT 14:20 Kǝ ɓat fa fǝrkitta taurandǝhi, thlaakǝn paɗ ngǝraǝn i'nna hurhura'a. A ɓingǝtkǝn mǝlan tǝ Barnabas pǝɗaknda Darbe.
ACT 14:21 Ɗiffitǝ ɓassǝ kwescha kusheng shiwunkǝn kǝ hǝmmǝtkǝn, mbǝskǝndǝ fichile fǝrkǝkit oi, ngǝrangndǝ'ina Listira tǝ Ikoniya paɗ tǝ Antakiya,
ACT 14:22 Mbǝnniyu sakandǝnda nofchǝhar tǝndatwa, kǝ sokndǝ tǝ alchitafa hur fǝrkit. Chekangnda kandǝ tǝ ndatwa, tǝ sat ɓahtǝ kaǝn natma mbǝs yimta kuturichita Fara.
ACT 14:23 Bulus tǝ Barnabas taɗangndǝ pǝktecha kandǝsi, a hur chikayen kǝtǝn hwanda, tǝmbǝɗa hwanandǝ Fara tǝ kǝrkushimta, fǝrkǝndǝ kanda hara Lǝmwanda, le fǝrtǝndǝ kitchitta mbǝɗ'en.
ACT 14:24 Ɓǝrkǝndǝhi tǝ hur Bisidiya ɓaknda hur Famfiliya.
ACT 14:25 Kǝ ɓastǝndǝ shiwunkǝn hur hǝmǝt Ferga, pǝɗaknda hai kǝ Ataliya.
ACT 14:26 Mbǝnniyu yimkǝnda hur kommbawal ngǝrrangndǝ'ina Antakiya, mbǝɗi soh hwanandǝ fichǝ kafata Fara kandǝsi, kǝthlǝm kǝ hǝrmǝn kandǝhar hur tori tuɓandǝndǝ nakǝnya.
ACT 14:27 Kǝ saatǝnnda Antakiya, ngomangndǝ fa tǝr mbandakish, kǝ mbǝt ǝrta, nbwa'angnda kandǝ nat i sǝt Farǝ tǝ mbǝɗengnanda, paɗ tǝ mbayi i'nandǝn mikǝtǝn fǝrkitchithi kǝ mbǝɗa punofcha.
ACT 14:28 Sokkǝnnda mbǝnniyu hammunchǝ oi tǝ fatǝrmbanda.
ACT 15:1 Ɓak funǝ nofcha a Yahudiya tǝ Antakiya, naknda sakanda fa tǝrmbandǝ har, ndatwa: "Manga tǝ heshangfichǝkuni nda i mbutǝ ɗǝssǝta Musa wa, nguni mbǝs hǝrǝktǝwa."
ACT 15:2 Nga hwan halǝ'indǝ yimka thlerǝ nda Bulus tǝ Barnabas tǝ nofchiyuwa, harkǝ fichǝ nda Bulus tǝ Barnabas tǝ funǝ fa tǝrmbanda kǝ ɗǝnda Urshelima kǝ ɓǝɗa fathlǝncha tǝ pǝktecha, kǝthlǝm kǝ tausangndǝ shuninihiyu.
ACT 15:3 Nofchǝ thlǝntǝfichǝyu, pǝɗangndǝ tǝ hurhuri Finikiya tǝ Samariya, naknda mbu tǝɓǝrta punofchihi kǝ mbǝɗa Fara, fǝrang ndǝ ɓǝnfata fa tǝrmbandǝ kaǝn.
ACT 15:4 Kǝ sa'atǝnda Urshelima, fa tǝrmbanda tǝ fathlǝncha, tǝ pǝktecha sangndǝ marapa kanda, kandang paɗ mbukǝndǝ uf i sǝt Farǝ tǝ mbǝɗengnanda.
ACT 15:5 Funǝ fafǝrkitsi naka hur mbanda Farisiyawecha, thla'akǝnda ndankndǝwa: "Sokkǝn waat kǝ heshangfichǝ punofcha, paɗ kǝ ɗǝffichǝ kanda kǝ kǝsndǝ kussa Musa har."
ACT 15:6 Fathlǝncha tǝ pǝktecha fa tǝrmbanda ngomkǝndǝhi, kǝthlem kǝ tausangndǝ shuninihiyu.
ACT 15:7 Ɗiffitǝ shuni shiwuntǝnda ɗarkǝn kaǝn, thlaakǝ Bitrus kit ndangna kandǝwa: "Hwanmancha shinuniwa thlata tǝrkakǝn, teɗ Farǝ nja hurnuni ndatwa, tǝmbǝɗengnǝ nat punofcha ɓǝs kusheng shunda kǝ fǝrndǝkitsi.
ACT 15:8 Fara le sǝnkǝ hanndǝkiketa cheɗkǝwa a thliiɗtǝ kanda tǝ mba fǝrra Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗa kanda, nda i fǝrra ndǝnakani.
ACT 15:9 Paɗ cheɗutǝ sǝmsǝmchita thlerǝnanda tǝ kaniwa, kǝ sapaɗǝn hanɗǝkikechengnandaɗi tǝɓǝɗa fǝrkit.
ACT 15:10 Kǝthlem ndǝkǝn, mǝsǝk natuni kikeɗandǝ Fara, tǝmbǝɗa ɗǝffa rǝfta kimshechi'ena ɓur, le nguchit shinchinǝm tǝkǝmna mbǝlla tǝrta?
ACT 15:11 Paɗ firǝm kitwa, nakma mbǝs hǝrǝktǝ tǝ mbǝɗa kafata Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso, nda i mbǝstǝnda."
ACT 15:12 Uf nofchi ngomkǝhi ngaskǝndǝ ɓa, naknda kathlǝmmata nda Barnabas tǝ Bulus, nak nda mbu alchiɗi fǝrandǝ Fara kanda, kǝ sǝndǝ ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nofchǝ fa, tǝ ǝnat sheka'inda a hur punofcha.
ACT 15:13 Ɗiffitǝ mweshandǝ shundǝngnanda, ngǝrkǝ Yakubu si tǝ ndakǝnwa: "Hwanmancha sǝkam nji.
ACT 15:14 Mbwa'a Siman Bitrussa kǝm laɗi lat Fara ɓata mbǝɗa punofcha, paɗ hertǝ funǝharra hurnanda kǝthlǝm thlǝmkǝn.
ACT 15:15 Leya ɓakna soktǝ keeke tǝ shunda tapǝnecha, nda i yarandǝ fichihi tǝndatwa,
ACT 15:16 'Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn ni ngǝr ɓata tǝpaɗ ni ngǝr tinandǝ hura'a Dauda le hǝmkǝhi. Kǝ ngǝri tinandǝ thlarǝ'enna kwarkǝn kǝnan kit.
ACT 15:17 Tahhǝt nofchi nat katnji, njang Lǝmwanda, nat tǝ punofchǝ la atfichǝ tǝ thlimna, ndat Lǝmwanda le sǝk i'chiya.
ACT 15:18 Sǝntǝ fichǝ kǝ soh.
ACT 15:19 "Kǝthlǝm ɗǝkǝn a kǝlandengna, kamusǝ kǝ thla'am hur'inda punofchi naka tǝɓǝrtǝhi kǝ ɓǝɗa Farǝwa.
ACT 15:20 Makǝ yarangma kandǝsi ndatwa, kǝ malangndǝ ɗǝsǝmta ɗǝhacha. Mǝsǝmindǝ chaɗnguwa, mǝsindǝ fǝllawichitwa, paɗ mǝ sǝmindǝ i ɓekrandǝfichǝ mɓurat'enwa.
ACT 15:21 Kǝthlǝm hur soh, a thlet hǝmchǝ somsomǝn fa ɓassǝsi tǝ ɗelwercha Musa, paɗ la changngandǝ fichǝ kanda chika yen farǝ yipta Yahudawecha, a kǝtǝn hwacha ɓeshfichǝ kussa Musa, a hur chikayen hǝmta i hurechǝ terchin, tǝpaɗ la changangficha isǝka farǝ yipta Yahudawecha, a kǝtǝn humchengnanda.
ACT 15:22 Fathlenchǝkǝn tǝ pǝktecha, nat tǝ fa tǝrmbanda kǝllangndǝwa ndiichinsi, kǝ taɗɗǝ nofchihar a hurnanda, kǝ thlǝnndǝ kanda Antakiya tǝ Bulus tǝ Barnabas, fichile taɗtǝnda nda Sila tǝ Yahuda lela atfichǝndǝwa Barsaba. Kandangti naka fambanicha fafǝrkit.
ACT 15:23 Fǝrangndǝ yarat ɗelwera kanda, kǝ ɗangnda kanda le naka ndatwa: "Kanang hwammanchǝnuni, Fathlǝncha tǝ fambanicha, kǝmbǝɗa hwammancha fichile naka punofcha, hur Antakiya tǝ Suriya tǝ Kilikiya, Ndat'ǝn kaǝn.
ACT 15:24 A shikani wa nofchisi thlaaka hurnani, mbǝɗya thla'andǝ hur inchengnuni tǝ shuwuncha. Chika sokkǝn thlǝnwani kandǝwa,
ACT 15:25 Hwimanihi yaraɗanihi ndiɗchinsi kǝ taɗani nofchihara hurnani, kǝ thlǝnani kanda mbǝɗengnuni, tǝ kaa shikechǝnǝm Barnabas tǝ Bulus.
ACT 15:26 Nofchiya tepa fǝrndǝ shisshingchengnanda, kǝthlem thlǝm Lǝmwandengnǝm Yǝso Kǝrǝsti.
ACT 15:27 Kǝthlem ndǝkǝn thlinnani Yahuda tǝ Silas, kandang tǝ inchengnanda nanda mbwa'a nda kuni tǝ miya, witǝ ǝn'ǝrta tǝ i natani yarata.
ACT 15:28 Keekesi mbǝɗa Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, tǝ kanang neɗɗaniwa ndiɗchinsi, mǝ ɗǝfaɗani kapat lǝkta kuni'inwa kǝ sherangka ichi sokkǝ waatwa:
ACT 15:29 Kǝ lenganguni ichihi thlithlandǝficha ɗǝhacha, tǝ i'sǝka thluwa ɗǝhǝrǝmtǝ mǝrkǝ nga fwarsafǝwa, tǝ i'sǝka thluwa ɗǝhǝrǝmi ɓekrandǝfichǝ ɓurat'en. Tǝpaɗ mǝ siɗuni fǝllawichitwa. Ma hirmuni ichini haryu, nuni sǝt ichǝ ndiichin. Kǝ sokuni ngwalngwal."
ACT 15:30 Kǝ thlǝntǝfichǝkanda, pǝɗak ndǝ hai kǝ Antakiya, ngommangndǝ fa tǝrmbanda, fǝrangndǝ yarat ɗelwer tǝkǝna kanda.
ACT 15:31 Kǝ changngandǝnda sǝkndǝ mbǝnfata, kǝthlǝm alchiɗi chekandǝnda kanda.
ACT 15:32 Yahuda tǝ Silas kandangti naka tapǝnechǝ paɗ, shunangndǝ kandǝ ka'ǝn, paɗ chekangndǝ alchita hwammancha, tǝ shiwunchǝ oi.
ACT 15:33 Ɗiffitǝ hangmuncha mbǝnniyu, malkǝndǝ kandǝhi ngwalngwal, ngǝrandǝ'ina mbǝɗa fǝchile thlǝnkǝ kanda.
ACT 15:34 Kǝllang Silaswa keekesi, mǝllan kǝ sokka mbǝnniyu.
ACT 15:35 Bulus tǝ Barnabas tǝngkǝnda hur Antakiya, naknda sakandaɗi tǝ ɓassǝ shunda Lǝmwanda, tǝ nofchǝterchin paɗ.
ACT 15:36 Ɗiffitǝ hanmuncha, Bulus ndangna Barnabas wa: "ngǝramǝn'in ɗǝmma kǝlandǝ hwanmancha hur chikayen hǝmta mbichi ɓastǝm shunda Lǝmwanda, tǝpaɗ kǝnǝm ndu nakndǝ kǝni."
ACT 15:37 Barnabas yahkǝnsi kǝ pǝdandǝ ɓweet tǝ Yohanna, lǝ atfichǝwa Markus.
ACT 15:38 Bulus yaraǝnhi kamusuwa kǝ pǝɗandǝ tǝle saktǝndǝhi a hur Famfiliya, tǝpaɗ chertǝn ɗǝta mbet tortǝkandǝyuwa.
ACT 15:39 Mbenniyu thla'akǝ ɓǝɓi somsommǝnchitta hanɗǝkiketa thlerǝnanda, kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn sakkǝndǝhi tǝ ndani, Barnabas tǝrkǝn Markus, yimkǝnda kombawal pǝɗaknda Sayifurus.
ACT 15:40 Bulus taɗkǝn Silas, ɗiffitǝ fǝri fǝrtǝ hwanmanchǝ kanda, ƙǝ kafata Lǝmwanda pǝɗanda.
ACT 15:41 Pǝɗak Bulus tǝhur hachahai Suriya tǝ Kilikiya, nakna cheka alchita kanda kǝtǝn hwachikǝn.
ACT 16:1 Bulus ɓakǝn paɗ kǝ Darbe tǝ Listira. Lǝ fǝrkitsa mbǝnniyu, thlemkǝnwa Timoti, hweya nuhnifǝ lǝ Yahudawata shinkǝn lǝ Helenawata.
ACT 16:2 Fafǝrkitti naka Listira tǝ Ikoniya lanaknda hamndi.
ACT 16:3 Yahkǝ Bulus kǝ ɗǝf Timoti ndi, tǝrkǝnndi tǝ paɗ hesha'ǝn, kǝthlem Yahudawechi naka mbechiniyu nat nda shinndǝwa shinkǝn lǝ Helenawata.
ACT 16:4 Naknda ɗar pǝɗata wiikǝndǝ hǝmtǝ hǝmta, naknda mbwa'anda nofcha ichi yarandǝ fathlenchikǝnhi, tǝ pǝktecha fichile naka Urshelima, ndangnda fafǝrkitwa kǝ kuwurndǝ i yarandǝndǝhi.
ACT 16:5 Tǝkichu nofchǝ fatǝrmbanda, chekkǝndǝ tǝ alchita hur fǝrkit, chikayen para kanda tera.
ACT 16:6 Bulus tǝ nofchi'en wiyangndǝ sǝrǝt hachahai Firijiya tǝ Galatiya, kǝthlem Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ njanda kanda, mǝ ɓasindǝ pathla Fara hur Asiya wa.
ACT 16:7 Kǝ ɓatndǝ kǝ sǝrǝt hachahai Misiya, yahkǝndǝ ɗǝt tǝhur hachahai Bitiniya, chikakichu paɗ Shemeɗa Yǝso ngǝmawa kandǝsǝwa.
ACT 16:8 Mbǝrkǝndǝhi tǝ kǝllari Misiya, pǝɗaknda hai kǝ Toruwas.
ACT 16:9 A fiɗikkǝn ɓak ǝna ɓǝs Bulus ndaa hur sǝnata, nakǝn nifǝ lǝ Makidoniyata, kit nakna hwananda tǝ ndatwa: "Aɓu Makidoniya kǝ kǝsangnakanisi."
ACT 16:10 Kǝ nat Bulus i'ni nda sǝnnatǝyu, chatkichuyu kakkani mbanda Makidoniya, mweshangngani tǝndatwa Farǝ nakka atkǝm, kǝ ɓassaam kweshcha shunda kandǝsi.
ACT 16:11 Pǝɗakani hur kombawal, thlata Toruwas kǝ Samotiras, wendambǝt paɗ pǝɗakani Niyafolis.
ACT 16:12 Thlata mbǝnniyu paɗ ɗǝkani Filibi, le naka kapat hǝmta Makidoniya, nat Romawecha sǝt kutǝrichitkǝn. Shiɗani hanmunchǝ ɗǝmek a hur hǝmǝɗiniyu:
ACT 16:13 Farǝ yipta Yahudawecha, chekani kish kǝ mimbang hǝmǝtkǝn, ɗǝkani mi'ama, mbǝɗi natani yarǝwa na mbita natsi i hwanandǝ Fara, mbǝnniyu sokkanihi shunangngani nishchi ngomkǝhi.
ACT 16:14 Ərta hur nishchi naka sǝkkani, thlemkǝnwa Lidiya, ɓakna hǝmǝt Tayatira, lǝ hiiyandi fi njelechaɗi, lǝ mwanandǝ Farǝ naken. I'nang Lǝmwandǝ hanɗǝkiketǝ'enhi, ɗǝfkǝn hur'i'nda i nat Bulussa mbuta.
ACT 16:15 Kǝ sandǝfichǝ baptisma tǝ fichile naka huraa'en, hwanang Lidiya kani, tǝndatwa: "Ɓaknasoktǝwa ngǝmaɗuniwa njang lǝ fǝrkit kǝmbǝnda Lǝmwanda, ɓam tama hure'engna kǝ sokkunihi." Tǝkichu kahandǝn hur i'ɗǝngnani.
ACT 16:16 Farǝle nakani pǝɗata mbǝt hwanda, kǝmkani tǝ mafat nuhhweya, lenat shemeɗ luwurchǝsa fi'en, la kulakǝn, tǝpaɗ la mbǝskǝn hanɗǝɓǝlta, kǝ fǝrangka nofchi naka thlǝmatkǝn, tǝ ɓǝɗa kulat'en.
ACT 16:17 Nakna kuwur kani tǝ Bulus mǝlla hwata, ndatwa: "Nofchiya mafecha Fara le sherkǝ tǝ mwanda, kanda ɓassa mba hǝrǝkta kunisi."
ACT 16:18 Ɗǝknamban tǝ sǝt i'niyu i mundǝ tǝrchin. Tǝkichu sǝɓkǝ hanndǝkiketa Bulussa ɗǝ kaǝn, tǝɓǝrkǝnhi ndangna shemeɗiwa: "Nja ɗǝfsǝ waat hur thlem Yǝso Kǝristi chukishsha fat'en." Chatkichuyu cheknakish.
ACT 16:19 Kǝnat fa nuhwani natna hure'engnandǝyu, resh mba mbǝs ǝ'nengnandaɗi, kǝsangndǝ Bulus tǝ Sila, tǝpaɗ kahkǝndǝ kanda milumo, ndǝkndǝ tǝ kanda mbanitǝ fichile nak tǝ kuturichit hachahaikǝna har.
ACT 16:20 Kǝ ɗǝtndǝ tǝ kanda mbanitǝ fa sakmicha, ndakndǝwa: "Nofchiya Yahudawecha, naknda kanda shekɗa i'ndǝ hǝmtengnani.
ACT 16:21 Kanda sakandǝ ɗǝssǝchaɗi kamuchǝksi, le kamuchiksi kanang Romawecha kǝ thlani."
ACT 16:22 Ɓak terǝ nofcha humangndǝ miya kǝ ɗar walǝkanda, fa sak michikǝn thlethlahangndǝ njelecha nda Bulussa ɗi tǝ Sila, ndankndǝwa kǝ tǝpangficha kandǝ kaǝn.
ACT 16:23 Ɗiffitǝ tǝpanda kandǝ kaǝn, somkǝndǝ kanda pursuna, ndangficha lǝ pu pursunatǝkǝn harwa, kǝ kǝlansakandǝ kaǝn, mǝninda hǝrǝkta.
ACT 16:24 Kǝ thlǝtǝn shuwunkǝn, ɗǝkǝn tǝ kanda kakǝ hur kǝtǝn pursunatǝkǝn kǝnaǝn sarǝchengnanda thleri peh'afta.
ACT 16:25 A ɗar fiɗikta, Bulus tǝ Sila kanda hwanda, tǝ in i'mish mwanandǝ Fara, tahǝt pursunachikǝn kanda kathlǝmmata kanda.
ACT 16:26 Su tollǝwa, sǝkkǝfichǝ kapat hǝhǝrta kisshitǝfa, njun kǝtǝn pursuna tǝkǝn hǝhǝrkǝnfa. chatkichuyu mikǝtǝn pursuna tǝkǝn inkǝndǝhi nat, tǝpaɗ uf challaluchi kǝnandǝfichǝ pursunachikǝnsi hǝhhatkǝndahaiya.
ACT 16:27 Kǝ thlaatǝ lǝpu pursuna tǝkǝnhar, anakǝn in mikǝtǝnchǝkǝnhi nat. Yarkǝnwa reh pursunachikǝn, kǝtkǝn thlohtǝ'en, tǝna ɓǝllandǝfat'en.
ACT 16:28 Shuwunkǝ Bulus tǝ kapat ɓurat ndatwa: "Mǝsanǝ mboro i'ndekufuwa, kana mbǝɗya nattani."
ACT 16:29 Lǝpu pursunatǝkǝnhar ndakǝnwa, kǝɓa fichǝ tǝ tikkesha, tǝpaɗ weshkǝna rahta hurkǝn, mǝla saktatfa tǝ lechita ɗǝkna hǝmta mbanitǝ Bulus tǝ Sila.
ACT 16:30 Mbǝnniyu chaǝn kanda kish ndangnakandǝwa: "Famwanda, mǝnati sǝt kǝthlem kǝ mbǝsi hǝrǝkta?"
ACT 16:31 Ndangndǝwa: "Fǝrukit kǝ ɓǝnda Lemwandǝ Yǝso, nu mbǝs hǝrǝkta tǝ chikawuna hur hure'eku."
ACT 16:32 Shunangndǝ pathla Lemwanda, nat tǝ fichile naka hur huraa'en.
ACT 16:33 Chika nakna fiɗiktiyu, lǝpu pursunatǝkǝnhar kileɗsa kanda tǝpaɗ sapaɗǝ ndindichengnandaɗi. Chatkichuyu mǝlan tǝ fichile naka hur hura'en sangfichǝ baptisma kanda.
