ACT 16:34 Ɓakǝn tǝ kanda hur huraa'en, tǝpaɗ saǝn ɗǝsǝmta kanda mban, mǝlan tǝ fichile naka hur huraa'en, naknda sǝt mbenfata kǝthlem firndǝkit kǝmbǝnda Fara.
ACT 16:35 Wenda mbǝta fa sak michikǝn thlǝnkǝndǝ hansǝsalchǝ ndatwa: "Kǝ kalndǝ nofchihiyu!"
ACT 16:36 Lǝpu pursunatǝkǝnhar ndangna Bulus wa: "Ndak fa sak michikǝnwa, kǝ kalfichǝ kunihi nakǝnya, chamakis pǝɗam ngwalngwal."
ACT 16:37 Ngǝrkǝ Bulussǝwa: "Tǝpangnda kani a ɓaniti nofchǝ talyar, sahhawundǝ mikaniwa, a nakǝn kanang Romawecha, paɗ pǝkkǝndǝkani pursuna. Nakǝnnya yahkǝndǝ kalǝkanihi ɓuɓweta? Auwa! Kǝ ɓanda harandǝ kanikish tǝ i'ndengnanda."
ACT 16:38 Kǝ ɗǝt hansǝsalchiyu mbu i'niyu, nak fa samichikǝnna lechita, ɓaknda sǝndǝwa Bulus tǝ Sila Romawecha.
ACT 16:39 Ɓaknda tǝrandakandǝhi. Kanda harandǝ kandakish, tǝpaɗ hwanangndǝkanda kǝmalndǝ hǝmǝtkǝnhi.
ACT 16:40 Ɗiffitǝ cheta nda Bulus tǝ Sila kishsha pursuna, ngǝrangndǝ'ina hura'a Lidiya. Humkǝndǝhi mbǝnniyu tǝ fichile fǝrkǝkit mbwa'angndǝ shuwuncha kanda, paɗ ɓaknda soktǝ tǝ alchit hanɗǝkiketa. Pǝɗaknda.
ACT 17:1 Kuwurkǝndǝ tǝ Amfibolis tǝ Afolloniya, saakǝndǝ Tassalonika kǝ mbǝɗi nat kǝtǝn humta Yahudawecha.
ACT 17:2 Bulus yimkǝna thlǝmmatnanda nda i sǝntǝnhi, mbǝraɗ farǝ yiptǝhi mǝkkan mǝlla halǝ'i'ndǝ tǝ kanda a hur ɗelwercha Fara.
ACT 17:3 Nakna chekanda kanda, paɗ kǝna sǝnanda kandǝsi tǝ ndatwa, keekesi kǝ saa Kǝrǝsti pwene, paɗ kǝ thlaaka hur mǝmmatcha, ngǝrkǝn ndatwa. Yǝso ti nati mbwa'andakunniya, mǝllan naka Kǝrǝsti.
ACT 17:4 Paɗ funǝ Yahudawecha, kahhafichi hur'inchengnanda, hummangndǝ i'ndǝ tǝ Bulus tǝ Sila, kichupaɗ sǝt Helinawechǝ oi fa lechanda Fara, tǝ kichupaɗ sǝt pǝktat nischǝ oi fa mbutǝ kǝ sǝkficha.
ACT 17:5 Nak Yahudawechikǝna sǝrǝhta, ngommang ndǝ hwanchǝ rǝnnecha a lumo. Kǝ ngomtǝnnda, tǝrkaakǝndǝ thla'andǝ hur'i'nda a hur hǝmmǝtkǝn. Yimkǝnnda hurhura'a Yason nak nda kat Bulus tǝ Sila kǝthlǝm kǝ ɓandǝ tǝ kanda mbanitǝ nofcha.
ACT 17:6 Kǝ ɓǝssawuchitndǝ kanda, kahkǝndǝ Yason tǝ funǝ hwanmancha, ɗǝkndǝ tǝ kanda mbanitǝ fa sak miiya, nak nda hwatta kanda ndatwa: "Nofchiya naka thlahur'i'nda chika ayi hurkisshita, ɓeɗnda mbǝɗya paɗ.
ACT 17:7 Yason thliɗtǝ kanda, ufnda kǝllundǝssa kussa Kaisarwa, ndatwa yunǝ kutursi, thlǝmkǝnwa Yǝso."
ACT 17:8 Thlaakǝ hur'i'nda Nofcha tǝ fa sakmicha kǝ sǝktǝndǝ ichiniyu.
ACT 17:9 Kǝ thlǝɗ ndǝ hanɗǝɓǝl punofchǝhar a harra Yason tǝ tahǝt nofcha kalkǝndǝ kandǝhi kǝ pǝɗanda.
ACT 17:10 Chat kǝ sǝt fiɗikta, ɗǝfkǝ hwanmancha ndǝ Bulus tǝ Sila kǝ pǝɗanda Biriya. Kǝ saatǝnda mbǝnniyu yimkǝnnda kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechihi.
ACT 17:11 Yahudawechi naka ɓǝɗya pǝɗanda fichilehi naka Tasalonika tǝ hur'i'nda, kǝthlǝm thliɗndǝ shuwunkǝn tǝ harchǝ chap chap, lanaknda tausandǝ shunda Farǝ wembǝta kǝ nandǝ ndu i mbutǝ Bulusyu kit.
ACT 17:12 Oiya hur Yahudawechi fǝrkǝkit, Paɗ tǝ funǝ nishchǝ Helinawecha fichile naktǝ mwanda tǝ hishchǝ paɗ.
ACT 17:13 Kǝ sǝktǝ Yahudawechi naka Tassalonikayu, tǝ ndatwa Bulussa ɓassǝ pathla Fara a Biritiya, ɗǝknda nata chikandǝ kanda kǝnnda thla'andǝ hur'i'nda nofcha.
ACT 17:14 Chatkichuyu ɗǝfkǝ fafǝrkit Bulus kǝ pǝɗaka mihawurta, nda Sila tǝ Timoti thlarkǝndǝhi mbǝnniyu.
ACT 17:15 Fichile ɗǝfkǝ Bulusyu saakǝndǝ tǝndi kǝ Atina. Naknda ngǝrandǝ'in thlǝkndǝ thlǝnda ɓǝɗa Bulus ndatwa, yehsi nda Sila tǝ Timoti kǝ ɗǝnda mbǝsndǝ leɗleɗ, pǝɗaknda.
ACT 17:16 Kǝ nat Bulussa pu kanda a Atina, sǝɓkǝ hanɗǝkiketǝ'enaɗi kaǝn, kǝ natǝn hǝmǝtkǝn nihiɗaɗi tǝ ɗǝhhacha.
ACT 17:17 I sǝka para la nakna halǝ'i'nda kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechǝhi kandang tǝ funǝ Helinawecha fa lechanda Fara. Chika ɓǝɗi nat lumo fichile la ɓǝlaakǝ nata ɓǝnniyu.
ACT 17:18 Funǝsǝ paɗ Abikuriyawecha tǝ Sitokiyawecha fa mbǝr'ǝna halkǝndǝ'i'ndǝ tǝ ndi. Funengnanda ndakndǝwa: "Mǝ yahtǝ lǝ ɗaakiya mbuta?" Ndakfunǝwa: "Nda lǝɓassǝ ɗǝhhacha nofcha." "Mbukǝndǝ kichu kǝthlǝm Bulussa ɓassǝ Yǝso tǝ thlata mǝmatcha.
ACT 17:19 Tǝrkǝndǝndi ɗǝkndǝ tǝnda ɗar Arasa, ndakndǝwa: "Ndu nu mbǝlla mbwa'andakani witǝ yuwa sakayiɗi natu sakandaɗiya?
ACT 17:20 Kǝthlǝm ɓanǝ yuwa icha thlǝmechengnani, yahkanisi kǝ sǝnnani i naka sakchikǝn."
ACT 17:21 Nakǝnya nat Atinawecha tǝ romchi naka mbǝɗengnanda, ǝnsǝ lǝ sǝnndǝ kǝ sherangka mbu yuwa shuwuncha tǝ sǝk yuwa icha.
ACT 17:22 Thlaakǝ Bulus thlarkǝnhi hurɗifitǝ Arasacha, ndakǝnwa: "Kunang nofchi Atinacha, a mbǝssaɗi wa kunang fa tǝr mbandǝ chika tǝ teni.
ACT 17:23 Kǝthlǝm manja mbǝrtǝhi tǝ hǝmǝtkǝn, lanaki ichi natuni mwananda, a naki mbǝt fǝr pofǝn tǝ yarata ɗarkǝn ndatwa: "Kǝthlǝm Fari sǝnuchit ficha. Lenatuni mwanandǝ sǝnuchituniyu, mǝllan nati mbwa'anda kuni.
ACT 17:24 Fara letinkǝ kisshita tǝ ichinaka hurkǝn uf, mǝllan naka Lǝmwanda afshi tǝ kisshita, shokwa kǝtǝn kapat hura'a Farǝ letintǝ nifǝwa.
ACT 17:25 Kichu paɗ ɓahwa kat nifǝ kǝ kǝssaansǝ tǝ harchǝ'enwa, ɓahwa yah ǝnwa, kǝthlǝm mǝllan tǝ i'ndi'en la fǝrang shisshingta nifa, tǝ yipta tǝ ichi natna yahtǝ nat.
ACT 17:26 Mǝllan paɗ tinkǝ yakat terǝ nofcha tǝ mbǝɗa nifǝ ǝrta, kǝthlǝm kǝ soknda hur kisshitǝ nat, tahsaǝn sǝrǝt naɗengnandǝhi, tǝ sǝrǝt hǝmchengnanda.
ACT 17:27 Sǝk Farǝ kichuyu kǝthlǝm kǝ kandǝndi, mbahya nanda taptǝ kǝ mbǝssangnda, chika sokkǝn nga nakǝn langngǝ tǝkǝmwa.
ACT 17:28 Kǝthlǝm: "Tǝ mbǝɗ'en natǝmhi, lanatma yipta, paɗ tǝ mbǝɗ'en mwaatǝmhi. Nda i mbutǝ funengnuni fa at imshi ndatwa: "Kitchitkǝn, kǝmnang ma witǝkǝn nakǝm.'
ACT 17:29 "Nakǝn kǝmnang witǝ Fara, kamusi kǝ yarǝm tǝ ndatwa Farǝ nakǝn nda zinariya ndu azurfa ndu ngwiya, le tahhǝstǝ nifǝ tǝ ɗathlǝ'enwa.
ACT 17:30 A hur soh tǝrra Farǝ chumwandǝ'enaɗi a ɗar tor ɓomchita. Nakǝnya mbwa'aɗa nofchǝ nat, chika tǝ tee'ǝn kǝtǝrndǝhi.
ACT 17:31 Kǝthlǝm tahsaɗǝ farihi natna ɓata sa kiita kisshitǝsi, i kitchitkǝn tǝ mbǝɗa nofchi tahsaɗǝnhi, kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn firtǝ kitchitkǝn kǝ mbǝɗa chika wunni, tǝ thla'a nda hur mǝmatcha."
ACT 17:32 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ shuwun thlata mǝmatcha, funengnanda njirkǝndǝndi, ndak funǝ paɗwa: "Yahkani kǝ ngǝrani sǝk i natu mbuta kǝ ɗar shuniya paɗ."
ACT 17:33 A mbǝnniyu saktǝ Bulushi tǝ kanda ɓǝɗakǝn.
ACT 17:34 Funengnanda ngǝrang ndǝ'ina mbǝɗa Bulus, fǝrkǝndǝ kit. A hurnanda Diyonisiyus, lǝ sakmicha, tǝ nuhnifa le nat thlǝmkǝnwa Damaris, tǝ funǝ paɗ fichile naka thlǝmatnanda.
ACT 18:1 Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn, malkǝ Bulus Atinahi pǝɗakna Korinti.
ACT 18:2 Kǝmkǝndǝ tǝ lǝ Yahudawata mbǝnniyu nat thlǝmkǝnwa Akila lǝ Fontusta. Le ɓak nakǝnya a Italiya, kandang tǝ nuhkǝn le nat thlǝmkǝnwa Biriskila, kǝthlǝm Kalaudiyus firtǝ kus ndatwa nat Yahudawecha kǝ malndǝ Romahi. Ɗǝk Bulussa mbǝskanda.
ACT 18:3 Nakǝn tor harengnandǝ ǝrtǝ tǝ nofchiyu, tor tahhasǝ tenti, sokkǝnna thlǝmatnanda naknda sǝt torra.
ACT 18:4 I'sǝka farǝ yipta Yahudawecha, la yimkǝna kǝtǝn humta Yahudawecha, a la nangna kahandǝ hur'inda Yahudawechǝ tǝ punofcha.
ACT 18:5 Kǝ ɓaɗnda Sila tǝ Timoti a Makidoniya, ɓaknda mbǝs Bulus firtǝ fat'enna ɓassa, mǝlla cheɗanda Yahudawecha tǝ kitwa, Yǝso naka Kǝrǝsti.
ACT 18:6 Halangndǝ'i'nda nak nda i'erandǝfa, tǝppaǝn njelechi'ennaɗi ndangna kandǝwa: "Hekke tǝ fwarchengnuni tǝ inchengnuni! njang cheɗikish. Thlata nakǝnya kǝ mban ɗǝki mbǝɗa punofcha."
ACT 18:7 Malkǝn mbǝnnihiyu pǝɗakna hura'a nifǝ lǝ atfichiwa Titiyus Yustus, lǝmwanandǝ Fara, huraa'en nduk tǝ mikǝtǝn humta Yahudawecha.
ACT 18:8 Kirisbus, kappat nifa mbǝt humta Yahudawecha, fǝrkǝn kit kǝmbǝɗa Fara, kandang tǝ nofchi huraa'ennat. Korintiyawechi oi sǝkkǝ ɓassa Bulus, fǝrkǝndǝkit sanfichǝ baptisma kanda.
ACT 18:9 Farǝle fiɗikta, chenɗang Lǝmwanda Bulus hur'ǝn nda sǝnnatawa: "Mǝlechinuwa, ɗumban tǝ ɓasseku paɗ mǝngasinǝ ɓaawa,
ACT 18:10 Kǝthlǝm njangtǝsa, paɗ nifǝsǝ na walǝsa kǝ sukǝn'ǝnwa, kǝthlǝm nofchengnǝsi oi hur hǝmmǝɗiya."
ACT 18:11 Sokkǝ Bulushi mbǝnniyu, hurat'ǝrta tǝ ndǝraa tehethl, mǝlla sakandǝ pathla Fara ɗi a hurnanda.
ACT 18:12 A fari nat Galiyo sǝt kuturichita furǝt Akaya, thla'ang Yahudawechǝ Bulussafa, ɓakndǝtǝnda mbanitǝ fasakmiya.
ACT 18:13 Ndakndǝwa: "Nifiya mǝlla kahhandǝ hur'i'nda nofcha, kǝ mwanangndǝ Fari nguchik keeke tǝ kus."
ACT 18:14 Kǝ nat Bulus nduk kǝ shunǝn, ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Galiyo Yahudawechǝkǝnwa: "Makǝthlǝm sǝt'ǝn nduɗuwa ndu kapat ɓǝɓi'ǝna, mani kathlǝmmatakuni.
ACT 18:15 Nakǝn pathlǝ sahmi kǝ ɗar shuwuncha, tǝ thlǝmcha tǝ paɗ kus engnuni, kǝllamǝn kunang tǝ inchengnuni. Njang ngi mbǝlla thlandǝ shundǝhi kǝ ɗar witǝ ichiyawa."
ACT 18:16 Rǝkkǝn kanda kǝtǝn sakmikǝn.
ACT 18:17 Nat nda kǝsangndǝ Sostanus lǝhǝm mbanita a mbǝt humta Yahudawechǝhi, tǝppangnda a mbanitǝ fa sakmikǝn. Kǝmmawuchik'ǝn Galiyo kǝ ɗar i'sǝtnda
ACT 18:18 Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn sokkǝ Bulushi hanmunchǝ oi tǝfafǝrkit a mbǝnniyu, ndangna kandǝwa nan malǝkandǝhi, a yimkǝnna kommbawal, ɓǝɗakna Suriya kandang tǝ Biriskila tǝ Akila. Kǝ saatǝnda Kankiriya, hǝsaǝn hwasǝ indǝ'enaɗi, kǝthlǝm kǝ nǝhɗaǝn shunihi mbuɗtǝn.
ACT 18:19 Saakǝnda Afisa, malkǝn Biriskila tǝ Akila mbǝnniyu, mǝllan tǝ i'ndǝ'en yimkǝnna kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechihi, nakna tausandǝ shuwunkǝn tǝ Yahudawechikǝn.
ACT 18:20 Hwanangndǝwa kǝ sokka mbǝnniyu hanmunchǝ oi, cherkǝnfa.
ACT 18:21 Nakna pǝɗata ndangnakanduwa: "Ni ngǝrandǝ'inna mbǝɗengnuni ma ngǝmma Fara." Yimkǝnna kommbawal pǝɗakna Afisa.
ACT 18:22 Kǝ tǝrtǝnahaya a Kaisariya, pǝɗaknashi ɗǝkna nda'ǝnna fa tǝrmbanda, pǝɗatahai kǝ Antakiya.
ACT 18:23 Ɗifitǝ munchi sǝtna mbǝnniyu, thlaakǝn wiyaan furǝt Galatiya tǝ Firijiya nakna kuwur hǝmtǝ hǝmta, kǝna cheka alchita fa tǝrmbandǝ nat.
ACT 18:24 Lǝ Yahudawatsi thlǝmkǝnwa Afolos ɓaka Afisa. Mǝllan lǝ Iskandariyatǝ nakǝn. Lǝ mbǝr shunda shintǝ'ǝnkaǝn, nat tǝ yarat shunda Fara.
ACT 18:25 Sakafǝchǝ pathlǝ mbanda Lǝmwandǝhar, paɗ nakǝn tǝ alchita fa hur Shemeɗa, la mbukǝn paɗ kǝ sakaan'ichaɗi kǝ ɗar Yǝso keeke, nat tǝ kichu baptisma Yohanna ndak sǝntǝn.
ACT 18:26 Tǝrkaakǝn shundǝ tǝ alchitafa, a kǝtǝn humta Yahudawecha, kǝ sǝktǝ nda Biriskila tǝ Akila ndi, tǝrkǝndǝnda huri, chekangndǝ mbwa'a pathla Farǝ kaǝn.
ACT 18:27 Kǝ yahtǝ Afollossa ɗǝta Akaya, chekang hwanmanchǝ alchita, paɗ yarangndǝ ɗelwera fa tǝr mbandǝsi kǝthlǝm kǝ thlǝndǝndi tǝ harchǝchap. Kǝ saatǝn, kǝssangna fichilesi fǝrkǝkit kaǝn, tǝ mbǝɗa kafata.
ACT 18:28 Kǝthlǝm sheraɗa Yahudawecha tǝ alchit kaǝn, fǝraan harǝfata kanda mbanitǝ nofcha, la cheɗkǝnwa hur pathla Fara Yǝso naka Kǝrǝsti.
ACT 19:1 A thlahmbǝɗi nat Afollossa korinti, Bulus wuyaǝn hur thlet hǝmǝtkǝn saakǝna Afisa, mbǝɗi mbǝsandǝn tahhǝt kimshechǝkǝn.
ACT 19:2 Ndangna kandǝwa: "A thlinduni Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ a thlahmbǝɗi fǝrtuni kitwa?" Ndangndǝwa: "Auwa, ɓahwani tamta sǝktǝwa Shemeɗsi Chiɗchiɗwa."
ACT 19:3 Ndakǝnwa: "Witǝ baptisama tǝmǝ sandǝfichǝkuni?" Ndakndǝwa baptisma Yohanna."
ACT 19:4 Ndak Buluswa: "Yohanna sǝkǝn baptisma kǝchendǝnwa tǝrnifǝhi, nakna ndanda nofchuwa kǝ fǝrndǝ kit kǝ mbǝɗa le na ɓata ɗiffitǝkǝn, naka Yǝso."
ACT 19:5 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu, sang fichǝ baptisma kanda a hur thlǝm Lǝmwanda Yǝso.
ACT 19:6 Kǝ ɗǝffandǝ Bulus hara kanda in, ɓak Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ kǝ ɗarnanda, naknda shundǝ tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝn, paɗ naknda mbu'icha.
ACT 19:7 Ufnda nak ndǝ nifǝ kumngǝrǝnsi chap.
ACT 19:8 Yimkǝ Bulussa kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechihi nakna ɓassa lechitfuwa shee ndǝraa mǝkkan, mǝlla halǝ'i'ndǝ tǝ kanda, nakna kahhandǝ hur'inchengnanda kǝ ɗar mwanda Fara.
ACT 19:9 Paɗ funǝsa hurnanda tǝ kwaakwachit i'nda cherkǝnda fǝrkit, naknda njirandǝ mbanda Lǝmwananda mbanitǝ nofcha, kǝthlǝm kichu Bulus sakkǝnhi tǝkanda, pǝɗakǝn tǝ fa fǝrkit, nakna sakandaɗi i sǝkka wembǝta a makaranta Tiranus.
ACT 19:10 Hurat chap mǝlla sǝt kichu, tǝ kichu nat nofchi naka hǝmǝt Asiya shikndǝ pathla Lǝmwanda, Yahudawecha tǝ punofcha.
ACT 19:11 A shiɗ Farǝ ǝnat sheka i'ndǝ oi tǝ mbǝɗa Bulus le tamuchit ficha nata.
ACT 19:12 Chika mayani'en ndu njelaa'en, le tǝkanghara fat'enfa, la ɗangficha hacha kǝ kǝnda hur hafaɗeng nanda, paɗ kǝ sakndǝhi tǝ ɓǝɓishemecha.
ACT 19:13 Funǝ Yahudawecha fichile la naka wiyandǝ hǝmǝtkǝn, la naknda rǝk ɓǝɓishemecha, la sǝkndǝ tor tǝ thlǝm Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso, a ɗar fichile nak tǝ ɓǝɓishemechikǝnafa la ndangndǝwa: "A hur thlǝm Yǝso lela ɓastǝ Bulussa ɗarkǝn chamakish."
ACT 19:14 A hurnanda hwechǝsi muɗ kǝ hishcha, naka i kapat pǝrist lǝ Yahudawata le nat thlǝmkǝnwa Sikeba, uf nda lasǝkndǝ kichu.
ACT 19:15 Ngǝmang ɓǝɓishemeɗ kǝn kandǝwa: "A shini Yǝso paɗ a shini Bulus, kunang paɗ kunang miicha?"
ACT 19:16 Nifi nak tǝ ɓǝɓishemeɗɗǝ fiyu pǝrkǝnna ɗarnanda, sherangna kandǝ tǝ alchita, cheknda kissha hurikǝn tǝ wesha tamkwal tamkwal paɗ ɓǝskǝndǝ ndindicha.
ACT 19:17 Fichile nak tǝ sokta a Afisa, Yahudawecha tǝ punofcha, kǝ sǝktǝndǝ i sǝkyu kǝsang lechit kandǝ nat, mwanang ndǝ thlǝm Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso.
ACT 19:18 Oi a hur yuwa fafǝrkit, ɓaknda nata mbu ɓǝɓi ɗǝssǝcheng nanda tallara.
ACT 19:19 Nofchǝ oi fa kulecha ɓakndǝ tǝ ɗelwercheng nanda, 'yangndaɗaɗi a mbanitǝ nofchǝ uf, kǝ sakandǝndǝ hanɗǝɓǝl ɗelwerchi ikkaɗi, mbǝssang ndǝwa a shee azurfa aru kumchit kum ɗurman (50,000).
ACT 19:20 Shunda Lǝmwanda nakna ɗǝta mban tǝ alchitafǝ kaǝn.
ACT 19:21 Ɗiffitǝ ichini sǝknatyu, Bulus yarkǝnna hanɗǝkiketi'enwa niɗǝttǝ Makidoniya, tǝ Akaya ka cheta Urshelima, ndakǝnwa ma ɗiɗi mbǝnniyu waat kǝ ɗi hǝmmǝt Roma."
ACT 19:22 Thlǝnkǝn funǝ chap hur fa kǝssa torchǝsi, nda Timoti tǝ Arastus, kǝ Makidoniya, mǝllan thlarkǝnhi a hǝmmǝt Asiya tolla.
ACT 19:23 A hanmunchiniyu thlakkǝ kapat thla hur'i'nda, kǝ ɗar pathlǝ fa tǝrmbanda Yǝso.
ACT 19:24 Thla hur'inkǝn ɓakǝn tǝ mbǝɗa lǝ ɓǝlta, le nat thlǝmkǝnwa Dimitiriyus, lelǝ sǝk tor tǝ hurita, kǝnna ɓǝl kǝtǝn ɗǝhhacha Artemis. Lanakna mbǝssa hanɗǝɓǝlta fa torharkǝnsǝ kaǝn.
ACT 19:25 A ngomaǝn kandǝ nat tǝ fichile nat witǝ torhareng nandǝ ǝrta, ndakǝnwa: "Nofcha, ashinuniwa tǝ tori engnaniya mbǝsti kǝnnecha.
ACT 19:26 Kuna nata kuna sǝkta nga Afisa ɗengwa nat tǝ Asiya, Bulus kahhaɗǝ hur'i'nda nofchǝ oi, paɗ tǝɓrandǝ nofchihi oi, tǝ ndatwa ɗǝhachi lǝ tintuni tǝ harcha nga Farǝwa.
ACT 19:27 Mbǝrramsi mborro ɓata naficha sǝɓandǝ thlǝm torengnǝmmaɗi. Ɗiffitǝ ndǝkǝn paɗ tǝ kǝttǝn nuhɗahata kapat alliya a Artemis, nan soktǝ nga ǝnwa, paɗ nan saktǝhi tǝ mwandǝ'en, mǝllan ti lamwanandǝ hǝmmǝt Asiya tǝ kishitǝ nat."
ACT 19:28 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝkichu sǝɓkǝ hurcheng nandaɗi, naknda hwat tǝ ndatwa: "A shok kapat mwanda Artemis a Afisawecha!"
ACT 19:29 Nǝhǝɗkǝ hǝmǝtkǝnaɗǝ tǝ sheka i'nda, rahkǝndǝ kǝ mbǝt terǝkǝn, kǝssangndǝ Gayus tǝ Aristarkus, shikechǝ wita Bulus a Makidoniya.
ACT 19:30 Yeh Bulus si kǝ yimka hur nofchǝkǝn, ngǝmauchik fa fǝrkit.
ACT 19:31 Kuturchǝsa Asiya naka shikechǝkǝn, thlǝnangndǝ shundǝ tǝ ndatwa, mǝ ɓahiɗa yimta hur nofchi oi yuwa.
ACT 19:32 Yakat nofchi ngomkǝhiyu, kanda hur sheka'i'nda, kǝthlǝm shekndǝhi, funǝ tǝ mbǝɗyu funǝ paɗ tǝ mbǝɗya, sokkǝn terchin fichile sǝnuchik i humang kandǝhi.
ACT 19:33 Funǝ Yahudawechǝsi pǝkkǝndǝ Alekzanda mban. Mǝlan paɗ thla'a'ǝn hara kǝthlǝm kǝ ngasfichǝ ɓa, mbah nan mbwa'anda kandǝ i sǝka.
ACT 19:34 Kǝ mbǝssandǝndǝwa lǝ Yahudawat nakǝn, hanthlikchǝ chap ufndǝ kanda hwata, tǝ kapat ɓurata ndatwa: "Kapat mwanda Artemis a shoka Afisawecha!"
ACT 19:35 A mweshitkǝn, lǝ yaratkǝnna hǝmǝtkǝn ngassaǝn nofchihiyu, ndakǝnwa: "Kunang Afisawecha, wun sǝnuchikwa hǝmmǝt Afisa naka hǝrǝm kǝttǝn ɗǝhhacha kapat Artemis, tǝ kweshcha ngwiyi hǝmka haya afshi?
ACT 19:36 Nda i natǝm ichiniyu, kamusi kǝ halǝm i'ndǝwa, kamkǝnsi kǝ ngassuni ɓa mǝ wesshiɗuniwa.
ACT 19:37 Ɓakuni tǝ nofchiya ɓǝɗya, chika sokkǝn herkunda kǝtǝn ɗǝhhachengnǝm, ndu kǝ mbundǝ ɓǝɓi'ǝn kǝ ɗar nuhɗǝhhachengnǝmwa.
ACT 19:38 Ma Dimitiriyus tǝ shikechǝkǝn tǝ fa sǝt torchi'en, ma ǝnsa thlerǝnandǝ tǝ yuna, a i'nafichǝ kǝtǝn sakmichǝhi, paɗ fa sakmikǝnsi ɗǝknda muh hanhara.
ACT 19:39 Ma ǝnsǝ yahtunisa ɓattǝkǝn kǝ mban, ɗǝk ma mweshanda mbanitǝ pǝktecha.
ACT 19:40 Kittǝkǝn kǝmna hur lechit ngǝm muhhanhar thlahur inni ɓukweya, kǝthlǝm ngǝma mbǝlla mbu i ɓaktǝ thlahuri'ndǝ kǝ ɗarnandǝwa.
ACT 19:41 Kǝ mbutǝn ichiniyu kalkǝn nofchǝkǝnhi.
ACT 20:1 Kǝ tuɓwat thlahur'i'nda, Bulus akǝn fafǝrkit, chekaǝn alchita kanda hur hanɗǝkiketa, ɗǝkǝn ndandǝnakandǝwa sefarǝyuna, pǝɗakna hǝmmǝt Makidoniya.
ACT 20:2 Kǝ wiyandǝn thlet hǝmchikǝn, chekaǝn alchita fafǝrkit kaǝn, ɓakna hǝmmǝt Hellas.
ACT 20:3 Sǝkǝn ndǝraa mǝkkana mbǝnniyu, nakna harǝfa kǝ pǝɗaka Suriya a hur kombawal, nak Yahudawecha yaraa ɓǝɓi'ichafa. Ndǝkǝn yartǝnwa nan ngǝrandǝ in tǝ Makidoniya.
ACT 20:4 Nofchi ɗǝfkǝ Bulus nda: Sufata hweya Farus lǝ Biriyata, tǝ Aristarkus tǝ Sakundus, Nofcha Tassalonika, tǝ Gayus nangna Darbe, tǝ Timoti, nat tǝ Tikikus tǝ Tarofimus, nofcha Asiya.
ACT 20:5 Fichile lak pǝɗata ɓan puukǝndǝ kani a Toruwas.
ACT 20:6 Kanang paɗ malkani Filibihi yimkani kommbawal, ɗiffitǝ chi njohmi nguchit mehndǝsa fi'en, hur mundǝ ɗurman ndǝkani mbǝskanda a Toruwas sokkani ɓǝnniyu mundǝ muɗ.
ACT 20:7 Tǝrka mundǝmuɗ ngomkani uf kǝthlǝm kǝ chichangani njohmǝhi. Thlaakǝ Bulus ɓassangna kandǝsi. Nakna harǝfǝ kǝthlǝm yehsa pǝɗata ɓingǝtkǝn, nakna ɓassǝ toltol taa kǝ ɗar fiɗikta.
ACT 20:8 A kǝtǝni ngomtani a huri afshi tikkeshchisǝ oi.
ACT 20:9 Hwan kimshaasi thlǝmkǝnwa Aftikos sokkǝn ɗassa tinkummbata, kǝssang ɓweni kaǝn. Bulussa ɗar ɓassǝ toltol yimkǝna ɓweni kasat, hǝmkǝnnahaya mǝkkatǝ tǝrkǝtǝnkǝn, tǝrkǝ fichiɗǝ kǝ murǝtkǝn.
ACT 20:10 Tǝrkǝ Bulussa haya kǝ ɓǝɗi nat hwaniyu, ɓirkǝnhi ɗarkǝn tǝrkǝnnda kapahɓa ndakǝnwa: "Mǝ thla'i hur'i'ɗengnuniwa mwe tǝ shisshingtafa.
ACT 20:11 Ngǝrang Bulus inna huri afshi ɗǝkna chichandǝ njohmǝhi chiikǝn. Nakna shundǝ tǝkanda kǝ wenda ɓǝta kanapǝɗata.
ACT 20:12 Pǝɗakndǝ tǝ kimshi'iyu tǝ shisshingtafa nangnda kwalǝ kaǝn.
ACT 20:13 Kǝ natani sa'a'ndǝ kommbawal, yimkanisi kǝ Asus kǝthlǝm kǝ tǝrrani Bulussa mbǝnniyu nda i tahsandǝnhi, mǝllan yarkǝnwa tǝsar natna ɗǝta.
ACT 20:14 Kǝ ɓatna mbǝskani a Asus, tǝrkaninda hur kommbawal ɗǝkani kǝ Mitilin.
ACT 20:15 Thlaakani ɓǝnniyu ɓingǝtle a hur kommbawal ɓakani kǝllari Kiyos. Iskichitkǝn changani kǝ Samas ɗiffitǝ mundǝ ǝrtǝ paɗ saakani Miletus.
ACT 20:16 Tǝrkǝ Bulus hurwa ngu thlarǝhi Afisa wa, kǝthlǝm mǝ sǝɓɓaɗǝ han thlikchaɗa Asiya wa. Mǝlla weshi kǝ saaka Urshelima ma mbandǝsi a farǝ Pentikos.
ACT 20:17 A Militus thlǝntǝ Bulus, kǝ Afisa kǝ ang fichǝ pǝktecha, mbǝt hwanda kǝ ɓanda mbǝsndi.
ACT 20:18 Kǝ ɓatnda mbǝsndi ndangnakandǝwa: "Kunang tǝ inchengnuni a shinuni witǝ soki sokti tǝkuni, i'sǝka para njang tǝ kuni, thlata fari ɗǝfti sarengnǝ kǝ Asiya.
ACT 20:19 Nja sa tor Lǝmwanda tǝ amtita tǝ ɓahmwa'i'nda tǝ ɓahhi satti tǝmbǝɗa ɓǝɓi yarǝcha Yahudawecha.
ACT 20:20 A malawi mbwa'a i'chakuni le na kǝssanda kunisǝwa, paɗ lanaki sakandakunihar a hur nofcha ɓuɓwetǝfǝwa, tǝ paɗ la yimkǝ huraa hura'a.
ACT 20:21 Kahhaɗi hur'i'nda Yahudawecha tǝ punofcha kǝ tǝrndǝhi mbanitǝ Fara, paɗ kǝ fǝrndǝ kit kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwaɗengnǝm Yǝso Kǝrǝsti.
ACT 20:22 Nakǝnya ɗǝki Urshelima tǝ ɓǝɗa alchita Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ. Paɗ sinwi'i'na kǝsnja mbǝnniyuwa,
ACT 20:23 A nakǝn cheɗi Chiɗchiɗtǝ Shemeɗwa, i'sǝka hǝmta na pursunachita natsi, tǝ ɓahta le naka punji.
ACT 20:24 Chika tǝ kichu tǝrwi shisshintengnǝ nda ǝn ndiichinwa, ndu kapat ǝnkǝ fandengnǝwa, mani mbǝlla tuɓwandǝ tori fǝritǝ Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso, le naka ɓassǝ kweshcha kusheng shunda kǝ ɗar kafata Fara.
ACT 20:25 Nakǝnya a shiniwa ngusa hurnuni na ngǝrnatnjuwa, kunangti wiiyaandi kuni kǝni ɓassa kuturichita Fara kunisi.
ACT 20:26 Tǝpaɗ nja sǝnnanda kunisi ɓukweya, mwa'u fwara yunengnunisa ɗar indengnuwa,
ACT 20:27 Kǝthlǝm a sǝkwi lǝklǝkchit mbwa'a yaara Farakuni natwa.
ACT 20:28 Mbǝramsa inchengnuni, tǝpaɗ uf chaɓi ɗǝftǝ Chiɗchiɗchita Shemeɗ kuni, kǝnuni fa putǝhar kǝ ɗuni mban tǝ hǝrǝm nofcha, fa kuwur mbanda Fara, fichile mbǝssandǝna i'ndi'en tǝ mbǝɗa fwara hwe'en.
ACT 20:29 A shini tǝ ndatwa ma pǝɗeɗi funǝ ɓǝɓi nofcha nanda yimta hurnuni, paɗ ngunda malandǝ chaɓǝkǝnwa.
ACT 20:30 Tǝpaɗ funa hurnuni nanda thlata kǝnnda shuwun lekta, kǝthlǝm kǝ kahangndǝ fa kuwur mbanda Fara kǝ thlǝmmantnanda.
ACT 20:31 Kǝthlǝm ɗǝkǝn sokam tǝ tahhasǝffa, kǝ kuɗkuni, hurat mǝkkan fiɗiktǝsǝwa farǝsǝwa, mallawi mbwa'anda kuni natuni tǝ amtitwa.
ACT 20:32 Nakǝnya njang firi kuni ɓǝɗa Fara, paɗ tǝ shuwun kafat'en, le na mbǝlla tinandǝkuni, paɗ kǝ fǝrangka kuni i tahsandǝnhi nat tǝ fichile nakchiɗchiɗ.
ACT 20:33 A yahwi zinariya ndu azurfa ndu njelecha yunǝwa.
ACT 20:34 Kunang tǝ inchengnuni a shinuniwa a shiɗi tor tǝ harchi'engnǝya kǝthlǝm kǝ kwanayi indengnǝ i'yahtǝn tǝ fichile naka thlǝmmatna.
ACT 20:35 A hur ichi nat cheɗaɗi sakǝtkǝnakuni tǝ ndatwa, sokkǝn waat kǝsuni tor kicheya kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝssangnguni fichilesi nguchik tǝ alchitafa, kǝnuni kuɗuk pathla Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso mǝllanti ndakwa: "Fǝr'ǝnna pǝɗaɗa thlǝthi tǝ mbǝsta.'"
ACT 20:36 Kǝ mweshandǝ Bulus mbutǝkichu, kopkǝnhi hwakǝn nat tǝ kandang.
ACT 20:37 Mǝrkǝndǝhi tit ufnda, hǝmmangndafa kǝskǝndǝndǝhar i saktǝhi.
ACT 20:38 Nakndǝ tǝ sǝɓhura, kǝthlǝm shuni ndandǝnakandǝwa ngundangǝrnatndǝwa, thlaakǝnda ɗǝfkǝndǝndi kǝmbǝt kommbawal.
ACT 21:1 Kǝ maltanikandǝhi, yimkani hur kommbawaltǝkǝn pǝɗakani kǝ Kos, wendambǝt paɗ ɗǝkani kǝ Rodes, thlaakani mbǝnniyu paɗ kǝ Fatara.
ACT 21:2 Kǝ mbǝstani kommbawalti na ɗǝtǝ furut Finikiya, yimkanisi pǝɗakani.
ACT 21:3 Kǝ tǝrkaatani nat Sayifurus, malkanihi tǝ kukun hishingta, ɗǝkaniɓan tǝ pǝɗata hǝmmǝt Suriya. Tǝrkanihaya a Taya, kǝthlǝm a mbǝnniyu nat kommbawaltǝkǝnna harandǝ ichi'enna haya.
ACT 21:4 Kǝ mbǝstani fafǝrkit, sokkanihi mbǝnniyu mundǝmuɗ. Tǝ mbǝɗa shemeɗa ndangnda Buluswa mǝɗiɗa Urshelimawa.
ACT 21:5 Tǝ kichu kǝ saatǝ munchi natani thlata, kǝnkanihursǝ tǝ wita. Thlaakǝnndǝ ufnda tǝ nishcha tǝ hwecha ɗǝfkǝndǝ kani kǝ ɗǝffitǝ hǝmta, mbǝnniyu kopkanihi mi ama hwankani,
ACT 21:6 kanani saktǝhi tǝkanda. Kanani yimta hur kommbawal, kandang paɗ ngǝrangndǝ'ina huri.
ACT 21:7 Kǝ tuɓwandani witengnani a Taya, saakani kǝ Tolemayis, ndangani ǝnna fahchǝnani, sǝkani mundǝ ǝrta mbǝɗengnanda.
ACT 21:8 Wembǝtle thlaakani ɗǝkani kǝ Kaisariya, yimkani kǝ hura'a Filibus lǝ ɓassa, le nak ǝrta a hur fichile muɗ taatǝ fichǝharyu.
ACT 21:9 Hwechǝ'ensi fwaɗa kǝ hantarcha ngwanauchit fichǝkanda, lanaknda mbu'icha.
ACT 21:10 Ɗiffitǝ sǝt hanmuncha mbǝnniyu, ɓak yunǝ lenaka tapǝna'a nat thlǝmkǝnwa Agabus nakna Yahudiya.
ACT 21:11 Kǝ ɓat Agabussa thlǝmmatnani, tǝrkǝn sahǝt kǝnhura Bulus. Ndǝkǝn kǝnandǝn harchi'en, tǝ sarǝchi'en ndakǝnwa: "A i'ndat Chiɗchiɗ tǝ Shemeɗkǝnya, 'kichu Yahundawecha Urshelima, nanda kǝnandǝ lǝ sahǝt kǝnhuriya, paɗ kǝ fǝrndǝndi kǝ mbǝɗa punofcha."
ACT 21:12 Kǝ sǝktani kichu, kanang tǝ nofchi naka mbǝnniyu, hwanangani Bulus mǝ ɗiɗa Urshelimawa.
ACT 21:13 Ngǝmmang Bulus ndakǝnwa, "Kǝthlǝmmi natuni sǝtkichu? Kǝthlǝmmi natuni tita kǝnuni sǝɓandǝ hanɗǝkiketengnaɗi? A tehshifa nga kǝnitǝ ɗengwama, ndu kǝ ɓǝllikǝficha a Urshelima kǝthlǝm thlǝm Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso."
ACT 21:14 Mbǝla'uchikani tǝɓrandǝ yarǝ'enhiyu, ngaskani ɓa, ndakaniwa: "Suku sakta Lǝmwanda kǝ nǝhɗǝnhi."
ACT 21:15 Ɗiffitǝ munchǝkǝn tahǝskanifa pǝɗakani Urshelima.
ACT 21:16 Funǝ fafǝrkitsa Kaisariya ɗǝfkǝ kani, ɗǝkndǝ tǝ kani mbǝɗa Manason lenatani tǝrtahaya mbǝt'en, nifǝkǝn lǝ Sayifurustǝ nakǝn, nakǝn ǝrta a hur fafǝrkitti tǝrkakǝnyu.
ACT 21:17 Kǝ ɓatani Urshelima, thlǝk fahchǝnanikani tǝ mbǝnfat kaǝn.
ACT 21:18 Wendambǝta pǝɗakani tǝ Bulus kǝ mbǝɗa Yakubu, pǝktecha fafǝrkit kanda mbǝnniyu.
ACT 21:19 Ɗiffitǝ nda ichakanda, ndǝkǝn mbwa'andǝna kandǝ ǝrtǝ ǝrtǝ ichi sǝt Fara a hur punofcha, tǝ mbǝɗa tori sǝt Bulus.
ACT 21:20 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu, mwanangndǝ Fara. Ndangnda Buluswa, "Neɗnǝwa hwanmanani, terǝ nofchǝ oi a hur Yahudawecha firndǝ kit, ufndǝ fa sǝrǝh kuwur kussa Musa naknda.
ACT 21:21 A mbwa'a fichǝ kushengwa kandǝ ndatwa, sokǝn lasakagnga Yahudawechihar uf fichile naka hur punofcha wa muhang ndǝ kussa Musa ɗi. Paɗ la ndakuwa mǝ heshafichǝ hwechengnandǝwa, paɗ mǝ kurindǝ tormurteng nandǝwa.
ACT 21:22 Nakmasǝtwa kǝniya chu? Kǝthlǝm nanda sǝk kushsheng ɓaɗeku.
ACT 21:23 I naksi su i ndutani kǝ sǝna. Nofchengnanisǝ fwaɗa, fichile ak ichimi.
ACT 21:24 Haru nofchiniyu kǝ ɗuni sapandǝ faɗengnuniɗi, kǝ kwanǝ i la kwantǝficha, kǝthlǝm kǝ hǝssang ndǝ kanda. Tǝ kichu nat ficha sǝndǝ tǝ ndatwa, i mbwa'andǝ ficha kanda nga kitchitsuwa, paɗ nakndanat nda sokǝn naka kuwur i mbutǝ kustǝkǝn.
ACT 21:25 Paɗ punofchi fǝrkǝkit, a thlinani ɗelwer tepi thlaɗanihi, mǝngǝmiɗunifa kǝ sǝmmuni i'thlandǝficha ɗǝhhachiwa, tǝ fǝllawichitta, tǝ chi i'ɓekrandǝfichǝ ɓurat'en, paɗ tǝ chi thlu tǝ fwar'en.
ACT 21:26 Ɓingǝtkǝn Bulus tǝrkǝn nofchǝkǝn, sapangfichǝ kandaɗǝ ufnda. Yimkǝnnda kapat hura'a Fara, kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝnaǝn farǝ nǝhata saptengnandaɗi, a fari nat ficha fǝr poffǝn kǝthlǝm chikawuni.
ACT 21:27 Kǝ nat mundǝ muɗɗa yah nǝhata, Yahudawechi ɓaka hǝmǝt Asiya nakndǝ Bulus a kapat hura'a Fara. Ndǝkǝn chikandǝndǝ terǝ humkǝn ufnda, kǝssangnda.
ACT 21:28 Naknda hwata kannda ndatwa: "Nofcha Isra'ila, kǝssamnakanisi! Le nifiya lasakaǝn ɓǝɓi'ichaɗi kǝ ɗar nofchengnǝm chika ayi, kǝnambwa'anda chika wuni, kǝ njirndǝ kussa Yahundawecha. Lashuwungkǝn ɓǝɓi'icha ɗar kapat hura'a Fara, paɗ latǝkmaǝn kweshcha mbǝɗihi chiɗchiɗya tǝ mbǝɗa ɓattǝ punofcha hurkǝn.
ACT 21:29 Kǝthlǝm soh neɗ ndǝ Tarofimus lǝ Afisawata, kanda mbǝt ǝrta a hur hǝmta, tǝrkǝndǝwa Bulus yima kapat hura'a Fara tǝ ndi.
ACT 21:30 Chatkichuyu shekɗang in'ndǝ hǝmta, ɓaknofchǝ tǝ rahtǝ ufnda, kǝssang ndǝ Bulus kahkǝndǝnda kish, a hur kapat hura'a Fara, chatkichuyu ngǝllang fichǝ mikǝtǝncha.
ACT 21:31 Kanda ɗar yarǝ ɓǝllanda, saakǝ kushengkǝna mbǝɗa kapat lǝthlǝrhwata, ndatwa kim Urshelimahi tǝ thla hur in'nda.
ACT 21:32 Chatkichuyu harkǝn fathlǝrhwecha tǝ pǝktat fathlǝrhwecha Roma, rahkǝnda hai kǝ mbǝɗi nat ngomnofchǝkǝn. Paɗ kǝ natndǝ fathlǝrhwechǝkǝn tǝ kapat nanda malang ndǝ tǝp Bulus.
ACT 21:33 Ɓak kapatnandǝ nduk kǝssaǝn, ndakǝnwa kǝ kǝnnang ficha, tǝ chalalochǝ chap. Kanna sahtǝwa ndu wunnakǝn, tǝ i paɗ sǝttǝn.
ACT 21:34 Thlaakǝ terǝ nofchiyu naknda muh hanhara, ndakfunuwa kǝcha, nak funǝndatpaɗwa kǝcha. Kǝthlǝm yakat thlahur in'nda hullaɗa mbǝssandǝ ɗarshuwunkǝn, ndakǝnwa kǝ ɗafichǝ tǝnda hura'a fathlǝrhwecha.
ACT 21:35 Kǝ saatǝ Bulus kǝmi tǝrta, tǝrkǝ fathlǝrhwechǝkǝnndi kǝthlǝm thlahur'inda terǝ nofcha,
ACT 21:36 Yakat nofchǝ oi kuwurkǝkanda, kanda hwata tǝ ndatwa: "Ɓǝllamǝn!"
ACT 21:37 Kǝ natndǝ nduk yimtǝ tǝ Bulus kǝ hura'a fathlǝrhwechǝkǝn, ndǝkǝn ndandǝna kapatnandǝwa: "Ni mbǝlla shunutǝwa?" Ngǝrkǝ kapatnandǝtǝkǝnsuwa: "Awi la mbǝrku Helenanciwa?
ACT 21:38 Awi nga sokǝn naka Lǝmasarawatwa, naka a hurechi mbǝrkǝhi humang thlahur'indǝyuwa, kahkǝ nofchǝ aru kumchit kum fwaɗa fa ɓǝlfata kǝ loktarǝyuwa?"
ACT 21:39 Ndǝkǝn ngǝmmandǝ Buluswa: "Ə, njang Lǝyahudawata naki a Tarsus, a hachahai Kilikiya. Njang ɓaki hǝmǝɗi sǝntǝficha, nja hwanuta malitǝn kǝ shunayi nofcha."
ACT 21:40 Kǝ fǝrandǝn mbanda, thlarkǝ Bulus kǝ mbǝt thlara, thla'anghara kǝmbǝɗa terǝ nofcha kǝthlǝm kǝ ngasndǝ ɓa. Kǝ ngastǝ ndǝ ɓa, shunaǝn kandǝ tǝ mi Aramayata, ndatwa:
ACT 22:1 "Hanmanchina tǝ shinchina sǝkamnji, kǝ mbwa'ayikuni isǝka kǝthlǝm kǝ cheɗayikuniwa suwuni'ǝnwa."
ACT 22:2 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝndǝ shunaɗǝkandǝ tǝ mi Ibraniyanci, ngaskǝndǝ ɓa. Ndǝkǝn ndatǝnwa:
ACT 22:3 "Njang lǝ Yahudawat naki, ngǝtkǝfichinja Tarsus, a hachahai Kilikiya. Nat tǝkichu mwanki hǝmmǝɗiya, paɗ sakikǝfichǝ changkathar tǝ mbǝɗa Gamaniel, le sakikǝ ichǝhar uf kǝ ɗar sakta kakechengnǝm. Lǝ sǝrǝhki kuwur Fara, nda i uffuni lǝ sutuni a ɓukweya.
ACT 22:4 Ɓahhaɗi fa kuwur mbanda Yǝso, paɗ lanaki ɓǝllandǝkanda, lanaki kǝnandǝ nofcha nda hishcha tǝ nishcha, la muhki kanda hur pursuna.
ACT 22:5 Kapat pǝrist tǝ pǝktat fasakmicha, tǝ fa hǝmmbanicha, na sheta kǝ ɗarna. Mbǝɗengnandǝ thlitti ɗelwer kǝ mbǝɗa fahchinǝm Yahudawecha, thlaaki pǝɗakǝ kǝ Dimaska, kǝ thlǝm kǝ hari fichile naka mbǝnniyu, kǝ ɓitǝkanda Urshelima a kǝnnda, ɓah nanda fǝraa pwane kanda.
ACT 22:6 "Nja ɗar pǝɗata, kǝ saati nduk tǝ Dimaska, kana hur fara sata, chatkichuyu ɓak ɗwachita afshi, finikǝn.
ACT 22:7 Hǝmkǝnhi kǝ hachahaya sǝkki ɓurata ɗitǝwa: 'Shawulu, Shawulu, i'mi natu fǝri pwancha?'
ACT 22:8 Njang paɗ ngǝmayiwa, sokǝn wuni, Lǝmwanda?' Ndǝkǝn ɗitǝnwa: "Njang Yǝso Lǝnazaratta, le natu fǝra pwancha.
ACT 22:9 Paɗ fichǝle naka thlǝmmatna, neɗɗi ɗwaachikkǝn, nattǝkichu sukundǝ ɓurata lenaka shundǝ tǝ njiuwa.
ACT 22:10 Ndakiwa, mǝnati sǝtta Lǝmwanda?" Ndǝkǝn ɗitǝ Lǝmwanduwa, thla'u kǝ yimna Dimaska, a mbǝnniyu nat ficha mbu'u i tahsandǝ fichǝhi kǝ sǝnna.
ACT 22:11 Kǝ hullandi nat mbǝta kǝthlǝm ɗwaachit hwaɗiyu, thlaakǝ fichile natani mbǝt ǝrtǝyu kǝskǝndǝ harengna, saaki kǝ Dimaska:
ACT 22:12 "Yunǝsi nat thlǝmkǝnwa Hananiya, la kuwur Farǝ nakǝn nda iyarandǝ kus hi, lela shunang Yahudawecha nat kǝ sǝkndǝndi fichile nak tǝ sokta mbǝnniyu.
ACT 22:13 Ɓakna mbǝsnji, thlarkǝn nduk tǝ nji ndikǝnwa: "Shawulu hwanya thlu natmbǝɗeku." Chatkichuyu naki nat mbǝta nakindi.
ACT 22:14 Ndakǝnwa: "Tǝɗ Fara kakechengnǝmsa kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝnnǝ sakti'en, kǝ nana lǝ kachita kǝ sǝknǝ shunda mi'en.
ACT 22:15 Kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝnna lǝ sheta'en kǝ mbǝɗa nofchǝ nat kǝ ɗar i'natu, tǝ'i'sǝktu.
ACT 22:16 Nakǝnya mǝnatu puta? thla'u, kǝ sukǝ fichǝ baptisma kǝthlǝm kǝ sapang fichǝ ɓǝɓifaɗekuɗi, tǝ mbǝɗa at thlǝmkǝn."
ACT 22:17 "Kǝ ngǝrandi'ina Urshelima, naki hwanda a kapat hura'a Fara, ɓak ǝn nda sǝnnata mbǝsnji.
ACT 22:18 Naki Lǝmwanda, nangna nditǝwa: "Suleɗleɗ kǝ chenakisha Urshelima, kǝthlǝm ngunda thlǝt sheta e'ku kǝ ɗarnǝwa."
ACT 22:19 Njang paɗ ndakiwa: "Lǝmwanda, kandang tǝ inchengnanda a shinnda i sǝka kǝtǝn humta Yahudawechǝhi, a kǝnnaɗi fichile fǝrkǝkit kǝmbǝɗeku, paɗ a tǝppaɗi kanda.
ACT 22:20 Kǝ thlǝrandǝ fichǝ fwara Istifanusa ɗi, lǝ sheta ti e'kuyu, njang ma njang kitta mbǝnniyu, nja kuwur i sǝt ficha, nja pu njelecha fichilehar ɓǝlangyu."
ACT 22:21 Ndikǝnwa: "Thla'u puɗu, ni thlǝnsa langna kǝ mbǝɗa punofcha."
ACT 22:22 Terǝ nofchǝkǝn naknda kathlǝmata Bulus, ɓakna mbu shuniniyu, mǝlla ɗar mbu'ichiniyu, thla'ang ndǝ hwata kanda ndatwa: "Ɓǝllamǝn! Sakamǝn witǝ nifihiya tǝkishita, kamusi kǝ nan tǝ shisshingtǝwa!"
ACT 22:23 Naknda hwata nak nda muhandǝ ɗǝsupchengnandaɗi, naknda thla'andǝ tǝnnata,
ACT 22:24 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn Lǝmbanita fathlǝrhwata shuwunkǝn tǝ ndatwa, kǝ ɗa fichǝ tǝ Bulus kǝ mbǝɗi la soktǝ fathlǝrhwata, kǝthlǝm kǝ tǝpangnda kǝ sǝnndǝ isǝk nat nofcha hwanda kicheya.
ACT 22:25 Kǝ kǝnnandǝnda kǝthlǝm kǝ tǝppangnda, ndang Bulussa kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝnna Roma lenak kit nduktǝndi: "Awi, hur kus keekesi kǝ sangnǝ ǝn ndu kǝ tǝpang ficha nifi naka hanhura'a Romawecha nga tǝ sang fichǝ kitasǝwowa?"
ACT 22:26 Kǝ sǝktǝ kapat lǝthlǝrhwata Roma kichu, ɗǝkna mbǝs lǝmbanikǝn ndaǝnwa: "Mǝnatu yarǝsǝta? Nifiya hwan Roma nakǝn."
ACT 22:27 Ɓak kapat nanda mbǝs Bulus ndaǝnwa: "Mbu'i'tǝn kit, sokǝn hwan hachahai Roma wa?" Ndang Bulus, "Ə."
ACT 22:28 Ngǝmmang kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝnwa: "njang tǝ hanɗǝɓǝltǝ oi mbǝsti nata hwanhǝmta. Ndang Buluswa: "Njang ɗǝkǝn ngǝttǝfichǝ nji."
ACT 22:29 Fichile naka yarǝ tawasǝndi chatkichuyu mbahkǝndǝ ɗifi'in. Kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝn kǝsǝntǝnwa Bulus lǝ hwan hachahai Roma nakǝn lechǝkǝn, paɗ teppa kǝnnaɗa.
ACT 22:30 Kǝ wentǝ mbǝtta, ɓak kapat lǝthlǝrhwatakǝn yahkǝnsa sǝn kachit i sǝk ɓat Yahudawecha muhhanhar Bulus, ɓakna kwasandǝhi, mbukǝn tǝ kapat ɓurat ndatwa, i sǝka pǝrischa tǝ fasakmicha kǝ ngomndǝhi. Ɓakǝn tǝ Bulus kǝ thlarnka mbanitǝnanda.
ACT 23:1 Thlaakǝ Bulus nakna kǝlandǝ fa sakmichǝkǝn, ndakǝnwa: "Kunang hwanmanchina, kǝ ɓukweeya a hur hanɗǝkiketengna mwa'u ǝn'sǝ ngweɗechin ndu ǝnat thlahur'i'ndǝ kǝ ɗar naɗengnǝhi a mbanitǝ Farawa."
ACT 23:2 Kǝ sǝktǝndǝ kichu, thlaakǝ Hananiya kapat pǝrist, ndǝfkǝn fichile nak nduk tǝ Bulus, kǝ tǝpndǝnda mi.
ACT 23:3 Ndak Buluswa: "Sokǝn kohat nifa! Sokǝn thlari pa'andǝ fichi fur kurrata, sokǝn ma na Fara tǝpsa! Sokkuhi kǝnna si kitasi kǝ ɗar sakandaɗa Musa, a landǝfku kǝ tǝpfichi nji, i nguchik keeke a hur sakakǝnnaɗi."
ACT 23:4 Fichile nak kikit mbǝnniyu ndangnda Buluswa: ''Kapat Pǝristsa Farǝ natu era?''
ACT 23:5 Ndak Buluswa: "Hwanmanchina, a sǝnwiwa mǝllan naka kapat Pǝristwa. Kǝthlǝm a yeraɗficha a hur shunda Farǝ, ndatwa: "Mǝ erinǝ lǝhǝm mbanita nofchǝwa."
ACT 23:6 Kǝ sǝntǝ Buluswa, funǝ Sadukiyawecha funǝ paɗ Farisawecha, thla'a'ǝn ɓurata hur fasakmicha, ndakǝnwa: "Hwanmancha, njangma lǝ Farisiyawat naki, Hweya Farisiyawa. Andiya kǝthlǝm ɗifi inndǝ kǝ ɗar thlata mǝmatcha ndǝkǝn sǝk natuni sakimiya."
ACT 23:7 Kǝ mbuɗtǝn kichu, thlaakǝ halǝ'i'nda tinnda Farisiyawecha tǝ Sadukiyawecha, sakkǝ ngomnofchǝkǝnhi kurutkǝn chap.
ACT 23:8 Ndak Sadukiyawechuwa, thlata mǝmatchǝsuwa, mala'ikachisǝwa, ndu Shemeɗa. Farisiyawecha kandang ngǝmmandǝwa neesi nat mǝkkanwa.
ACT 23:9 Thlaakǝ kapat sheka'inda naknda shundǝ kǝ afshi, funǝ malndǝmchǝ fa sakandǝ kussa Musaɗi, Farisiyawecha thlarkǝndǝhi kit, naknda halǝ'innda, ndakndǝwa: "Kanang a mbǝssawani ɓǝɓi i'sǝt nifiyawa. Mbahya yunǝ Shemeɗa ndu mala'ika shunangnga."
ACT 23:10 Kǝ thlaatǝ halǝ'inkǝn kaǝn, lechik kapat lǝ thlǝrhwatkǝn kǝthlǝm mǝni nda thlǝthlahhandǝ Bulus hi. Fǝrkǝn mi tǝndatwa, fathlǝrhwatkǝn kǝ tǝrndahaya kǝ thlǝndǝ Bulussa ɗǝ tǝ alchita, kǝ ɓandǝ tǝndǝ kǝ mbǝt sokta fa thlǝrhwata.
ACT 23:11 Sǝk fiɗikta thlarkǝ Lǝmwandǝ nduk tǝ Bulus, ndakǝnwa: "Ɗu mban tǝ alchit hanɗǝkiketa, nda i fǝrtu sheta kǝ ɗarna a Urshelima, kichu paɗ kamkǝsi kǝ fǝrnǝ sheta ɗarna a Roma."
ACT 23:12 Wendambǝta, Yahudawecha tahǝskǝndǝfa kǝthlǝm kǝ ɓallangndǝ Bulus. Akndǝ ichǝmi tǝ ndatwa, ngunda sǝmtǝwa ngunda satwa, se ma ɓǝllandǝ Bulus.
ACT 23:13 Fichile sǝk ɓǝɓi tahasinifiyu, pǝɗanda nifǝhi kumchit fwaɗa.
ACT 23:14 Ɗǝknda mbǝɗa pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ fa hǝmmbanita, ndakndǝwa: "A eɗɗani kapat ichimi tǝ ndatwa, ngani sǝm'ǝnwa ngani sat'ǝnwa sema ɓǝllaɗani Bulus.
ACT 23:15 Kǝthlǝm kichu, nakǝnya kunang tǝ fasakmicha, hwanamǝn kapat lǝ thlǝrhwatkǝn, kǝ ɓaǝn Bulussa kuni, nda tǝ yahunisi kǝ ngǝruni sahamihar kaǝn, kanang paɗ tehshanifa kǝ ɓǝllangngani kana sata."
ACT 23:16 Kǝ sǝktǝ hweya hwanman Bulus witǝ tahasifǝ nanda sita, ɗǝkna yimta mbǝt sokta fathlǝrhwatkǝn mbwa'angna Bulus.
ACT 23:17 Bulus akǝn yuna hur kapat fathlǝrhwata Roma, ndakǝnwa: "Ɗu tǝ hwankimshi'iya mbanitǝ kapat fathlǝrhwata, shundǝsǝ yahtǝnsa mbwa'anda."
ACT 23:18 Kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝna Roma tǝrkǝn hankimshikǝn, ɗǝkǝn tǝnda mbǝɗa kapatnanda. Kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝnna Roma, ndakǝnwa: "Bulus hwan pursunatiyu, aknji, hwanikǝnwa kǝ ɓitǝ hwankimshi'iya mbǝɗeku, kǝthlǝm ǝnsǝ natna mbu'uta."
ACT 23:19 Kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝn kǝskǝn hara kimshikǝn, kahkǝnda kǝlar, sahaǝn miya ɓuɓweeta: "Mǝnani yahtusa mbwi'itiyu?"
ACT 23:20 Ndang kimshikǝnwa: "Pǝktecha Yahudawecha tahsandǝhi, nanda hwanuta kǝ ɗangnǝ Bulussa kanda mbanitǝ fasakmichǝ ishki, nda yahkǝndǝ kǝ ngǝrndǝ tausandǝ shuwunkǝn'enhi kaǝn.
ACT 23:21 Paɗ mǝ ngǝmmana kandǝsǝwa, kǝthlǝm pǝɗaɗa nifǝhi kumchit fwaɗa kanda ɗuwetndi kanda kat kǝ ɓǝllangnda, paɗ tepa eɗndǝ i'chimi ndatwa, ngunda sǝmtǝwa ngunda satwa sema ɓǝllanda. Nakǝnya a tehishndǝfa, ngǝmteku ndak nannda puta."
ACT 23:22 Kahhang kapat Lǝthlǝrhwatkǝn thlǝmata hwankimshikǝn tǝ ndatwa: "Mǝ mbwa'ana yunuwa mbu'i'nǝ shuniyawa." Kalkǝndǝhi kǝ pǝɗan.
ACT 23:23 Kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝn akǝn pǝktat fa thlǝrhwechǝkǝnna Roma chap, ndangnakandǝwa: "Tahsamfa ɗukuni Kaisariya, hwanthlikǝn hanherta i'fiɗikta tǝ fa thlǝrhwechǝ kumchitkum chap, tǝ kumchit muɗ fa pǝrpirishcha, tǝ fa thlǝrhwat kumchitkum chap fa mbat tǝ pela."
ACT 23:24 Kǝ kuni pirshihar le nat Bulussa pǝrtǝsi, kǝ ɗunitǝnda mbǝɗa Ngomna Felis ngwalngwal.
ACT 23:25 Yarakǝn ɗelwer nda iya:
ACT 23:26 "Thlata Kalaudiyas Lisiyas, Kǝ mbǝɗa lǝ mwandǝ Ngomna Felis. Ndat ǝn oi.
ACT 23:27 Nifiya kǝsandǝ Yahudawecha, ndukndǝhi kǝ ɓǝllangnda, thlaaki leɗleɗ tǝ fathlǝrhwecha thlǝkindaɗi, kǝthlǝm a shikiwa mǝllan hwanhǝmǝt Roma nakǝn.
ACT 23:28 Yahkisǝ kǝ sǝki isǝtǝn nannda tǝramifa, ɗǝkitǝnda mbanitǝ fasakmichengnanda.
ACT 23:29 Ɓaki mbǝssandǝwa naknda tǝramifa kǝɗar shuwun sakandengna nda ɗaɗi, kǝthlǝm i'sǝtǝn saawa ɗǝffandafǝ kǝ kǝnangnda ndu kǝ ɓǝllangndǝwa.
ACT 23:30 Kǝ mbu'i'tǝfichiwa ɓǝɓi ǝnsǝ natficha yarandǝfa, chatkichuyu thlǝnukindi. Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ fichile muhkǝ hanharkǝnwa, kǝ ɗǝnda mbuta mbanituwa i'nat ndǝ sǝtǝn ndǝɗuwayu."
ACT 23:31 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn fa thlǝrhwatkǝn tǝrkǝndǝ Bulus, nda i mbwa'andǝ ficha kanda, ɗǝkndǝ tǝndi kǝ Antifatiris a fiɗikta.
ACT 23:32 Ɓingngitkǝn malkǝndǝ fa thlǝrhwatkǝn fichile la pǝr kǝ pirishcha kǝ ɗǝnda mbantǝndi, kandang paɗ ngǝrangndǝ'inna mbǝtsoktengnanda.
ACT 23:33 Kǝ ɓat fathlǝrhwatkǝn, fichile la pǝr kǝ pirihcha saakǝnnda Kaisariya, fǝrangndǝ ɗelwera ngomna, malkǝndǝ Bulushi a hurhar'en.
ACT 23:34 Kǝ changkandǝ ngomna ɗelwertǝkǝn, sahaǝn mi Bulus ndu ɓakna hǝmmǝt mi? sǝkǝnwa ɓakna Kilikiya,
ACT 23:35 ndakǝnwa: "Ni kathlǝmmata shundeku, a fari ɓatfichile muhkǝ hanharwa: "Ndǝkǝn fǝrtǝ ngomna shunda kǝ ngǝllangficha, a huri kuturichita Hiridus le tintǝn. Kǝ puufichindǝhar.
ACT 24:1 Ɗiffitǝ munndǝ ndurman kapat pǝrist Hananiya, ɓeɗ tǝ funǝ pǝktecha, Paɗ tǝ yunǝ lǝmbǝr shunda le nat thlǝmkǝnwa Tartulus. Kǝthlǝm kǝ muhndǝ hanhar Bulus a ɓanitǝ ngomna.
ACT 24:2 A yimang fichi Bulussi, Tǝrkaakǝ Tartulus muh hanhar Bulussa ɓanitǝ ngomna Felis, ndakǝnwa: "Nakǝn tǝ ɓǝɗa sǝndeku sandǝ fichi kachit nofchengnǝm, Paɗ kǝthlǝm lakǝllaku langnga, ndǝkǝn sǝk tahǝstǝ fichi ichi oi fichile sokka kachitta nofchengnǝm.
ACT 24:3 Nofchengnǝm chika ayi kanda su usoko nga sǝrtǝfuwa.
ACT 24:4 Paɗ kǝthlǝm mǝ sǝɓaɗi hanthlik chikǝn eku'ndǝwa, nja hwanuta hur kachiɗeku Kǝ kangnǝ thlǝmmata i nguɗǝh nattani ɓuta.
ACT 24:5 Mbǝssaɗani ndatwa nifiya lǝ ɓat tǝ thlahur'inda, lanakna ɓat tǝ thlahur'inda thlerǝ Yahudawecha, chika tǝteni a hur kishita, Paɗ mǝllan nalǝ mbanita i leki la atfichiwa Nazarawa.
ACT 24:6 Keɗ kǝ tǝkmaǝn kapat hura'a Fara ɗi, Paɗ a kǝssangngani.
ACT 24:7 Paɗ Lisiyas lǝ ɓanita, ɓakna thlǝtndaɗaɗi harengnani tǝ alchitta.
ACT 24:8 A ɗiftǝ fa muhhanhar nifiya kǝ ɓanda ɓanituwa. Ma usanǝ mihar sokǝn tǝ i'ndeku, nu mbǝlla sǝnda mbǝɗ'en nat ichi nattani muh hanharkǝn.
ACT 24:9 Yahudawecha kwiyirndǝ ɗiffitǝkǝn kichu. Ngǝmangndǝwa, nak ǝnnatkǝn kichu.
ACT 24:10 Fǝrang ngomna mba shunda Bulus, ndǝkǝn ngǝmandǝ Bulus ndakǝnwa: "Ni hǝrkandǝ indengna tǝ chiɗchiɗchit hanɗǝkiketa, kǝthlǝm shiniwa shiɗnǝ hurechǝ oi, sassa kiita nofchiya.
ACT 24:11 Ma tausanǝhi nu mbǝssandǝ wa, mbǝrawa munndǝhi kumngǝrǝnsǝchapwa, Kǝ pǝɗati Urshelima ka hwanda.
ACT 24:12 Fa muh hanharnǝtiya tamunda mbǝssitǝ nja halǝ'i'ndǝ tǝ nifǝwa, ndu nja thla'andǝ hur'i'nda nofcha kapat hura'a Fara ndu a mbǝt humta Yahudawecha, ndu a hur hǝmǝtkǝn.
ACT 24:13 Ichi nat'nda mbuta ɗar i'ndengnǝ nakǝnya ngunda mbǝlla fǝru sǝndǝwa.
ACT 24:14 Ən ǝrtǝ ngǝmandi, ndǝkǝn naka nja kuwur Fara kakechengnǝm tǝ mbanda nofchi la kuwurkǝ Yǝso, la atfichiwa Nazarawa, lǝnaki fǝrkitta ɗar ichi uf yarandǝ fichihi nda i lasakandǝ Musaɗi paɗ tǝ laulawecha Tapǝnecha.
ACT 24:15 Nja ɗǝf hanɗǝkiketa mbǝɗa Fara, nda i nat fichileya sǝta, ndatwa, naficha thla'andǝ mǝmatcha, fa kafata tǝ fa ɓah kafat nat.
ACT 24:16 Ndǝkǝn sǝk pware lanati kweetǝhi a hanɗǝkiketengna, kǝ soki nga kweeɗechinna mbanitǝ Farǝ tǝ nofchǝwa.
ACT 24:17 Paɗ ɗiffitǝ hanhurechǝ nguɗeh, ɓakiɗi kǝ Urshelima kǝthlǝm kǝ fǝripoffǝn kǝ mbǝɗa nofchengnǝm, paɗ tǝ thlǝr icha.
ACT 24:18 Nja hur sǝt kichu, mbǝssikǝnda shepiɗi a hur kapat hura'a Fara, nga tǝ ngomnofchǝwa, ndu thla hur'i'ndǝwa.
ACT 24:19 Funǝ Yahudawechǝsi a hachahai Asiya fichile naka mbǝnniyu, kandang kamkǝsi kǝ ɓanda mbanituwa ka muh hanharna, ma shundengnandǝsi kǝ faɗengna.
ACT 24:20 Mangakichuwa malamǝn nofchiya kǝ mbundǝ i mbǝssitǝndǝsi a fari thlartihi mbanitǝ fa sakmicha.
ACT 24:21 Manga kǝ ɗar i'ǝrtǝ mbwa'andi kish tǝ alchita fari thlartihi mbanitǝnandǝ ndatwa: "Lenaka ɗar thlaata mǝmatcha, sǝk nati mbanitǝnuni ɓukweya."
ACT 24:22 Felis paɗ nakǝn tǝ sakǝt sinnda kǝ ɗar mbanda Yǝso, thlaraǝn kandǝhi, ndakǝnwa: "Sema ɓeɗ Lisiyas lǝmbanitǝ kwaɗǝn kani thlandǝ kiita engnunihi.
ACT 24:23 Ndǝkǝn fǝrtǝ Felis shundǝ kǝ mbǝɗa kapat lǝthlǝrhwata Roma, kǝnna pu Bulus har, Paɗ kǝ fǝraɗǝ pwene oi wa, kǝ njaɗa shikechǝkǝn kǝ ɓanda mbǝɗ'enwa, ndu kǝ kǝssangndǝsuwa.
ACT 24:24 Ɗiffitǝ hanmunchikǝn ɓaknda Felis tǝ nuhkǝn Durusila, lǝ Yahudawata, a thlǝnkǝn kǝ ɓa fichi tǝ Bulus, a kaǝn thlǝmmata kǝ ɗar shuwun kitchita Yǝso Kǝrǝsti.
ACT 24:25 Tǝrkaakǝ Bulussa fǝr sakǝtkǝn kǝ ɗar kitchitta, tǝ pǝɗa yah ǝnat alchitta fat hi, tǝ farǝ ɓahhi naka ɓatyu. Sǝkkǝn kichu kǝsang lechit Felis, ndangna Buluswa: "Nakǝnya ngǝran'in. Ma mbisshi mbanda ni atsa."
ACT 24:26 Mǝlla ɗǝf hanɗǝkiketǝsuwa na Bulussa fǝraa hanɗǝɓǝlta, ndǝkǝn sǝknat Felissa nata atndǝ noknok kǝna shundǝ tǝndi.
ACT 24:27 Paɗ a ɗiffitǝ hurat chap, sǝk Fokiyus Festus kǝ ngomna kǝ kwar Felis. kǝthlǝm Felis mǝlla kat chiɗchiɗachita fwara mbanitǝ Yahudawecha, ndǝkǝn sǝk maltǝn Bulussa pursuna.
ACT 25:1 Ɗiffiti munndǝ mǝkkan, saakǝ Festus kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝssǝn tor ngomnachita, thlaakǝna Kaisariya pǝɗakna Urshelima.
ACT 25:2 Pǝktat Pǝristcha tǝ fa hǝmmbanita Yahudawecha, ɗǝknda muh hanhar Bulussa mbǝɗ'en.
ACT 25:3 Hwanangnda, kǝ ngǝrang fichi Bulus kǝ Urshelima, kǝthlǝm a tahsandǝhi wa nanda ɓǝllanda mbanda.
ACT 25:4 Ngǝmang Festus ndakǝnwa: Ndif fichi Bulus hi a Kaisariya, njang tǝ i'ndengna nja tǝrtǝhurwa ni ɗǝtta mbǝnniyu hanmunchiya.
ACT 25:5 Ɗǝkǝn ndatǝn paɗwa kǝthlǝm kichu, pǝktechengnuni kǝ ɓandǝ tǝnji, ma nifiya ǝnsǝ sǝttǝn nga keekewa, Kǝ ɓanda muh hanharkǝn.
ACT 25:6 Mbǝrawa mundǝhi foɗfoɗǝ ndu kum a mbǝɗengnandǝwa, ndǝkǝn ngǝrandǝn'ina Kaisariya. Ɓingngitkǝn sokǝnna mbǝt soktǝ'en i'kiita, thlǝnkǝn kǝ ɓa fichi tǝ Bulussa mbanitǝkǝn.
ACT 25:7 Kǝ ɓat Bulus, Yahudawechi ɓaka Urshelima thlaakǝnda taurangndǝhi, naknda ɓattǝ muh hanharengnandǝ oi kǝɗarkǝn, naknda cheka fǝra pwanchǝ kaǝn, ichi mbutǝnda ngunda mbǝla mbu kakatitǝkǝnwa.
ACT 25:8 Paɗ Bulus hǝrkaǝn fat'en ndakǝnwa: "Njang sawi ɓǝɓi'ǝn sakta Yahudawechuwa, tǝ paɗ sawi ɓǝɓi'ǝn kapat hura'a Farǝwa, paɗ sawi ɓǝɓi'ǝn Kaisarwa chika nguɗehwa.
ACT 25:9 Yahkǝ Festussa tǝraandǝ hanɗǝkiketa Yahudawechǝhi, sahaǝn mi Buluswa: "Ndunu ngǝmtǝfa kǝ ɗǝna Urshelima kǝ sukǝ fichi kiitasa mbanitǝna kǝ ɗar ichiniyu.
ACT 25:10 Ndak Bulus wa: "Njang kitta mbanitǝ kiita Kaisar, a mbǝɗya kamkǝsi kǝ sikǝ fichi kiitasi. Sawi ɓǝɓi'ǝn Yahudawechiwa, sokǝnma shinnǝ kichu kaǝn.
ACT 25:11 Ma njang la sǝk i kamuchiksi, paɗ mashiɗi ɓǝɓi'i saaka kǝ ɓǝllikǝ ficha, ngi cherifa kǝ ɓǝllikǝ fichǝwa. Paɗ manga kitchitsǝ kǝ ɗar muhhanhari nat nda muhta ɗarnǝwa, Paɗ nga nifǝsi na mbǝlla fǝrnja mbǝndengnandǝwa. Nja hwanda kǝ thla'ang fichi muh hanharengna mbanitǝ Kaisar.
ACT 25:12 Ɗiffitǝ yarandǝ icha nda Festus hi tǝ fa sakmichi'en, ngǝmkǝn ndakǝnwa: "Makichu hwanu kǝ thla'ang fichǝ hanhareku kǝ mbǝnitǝ Kaisar paɗ natu pǝɗata."
ACT 25:13 Ɗiffitǝ hanmunchǝ ɗimek, Agiriffa kutura tǝ Banis ɓaknda Kaisariya kǝthlǝm kǝ sangndǝ marapa Festus.
ACT 25:14 Nakǝn nanda sǝt hanmunchǝ oi a mbǝnniyu, ndǝkǝn ɓat Festus tǝ shuwun Bulus kǝ mbǝɗa kutura. Festus ndakǝnwa: "Nifǝsi malitǝ Felis hi a pursuna.
ACT 25:15 Thlahmbǝɗi nati a Urshelima pǝktat Pǝrischa tǝ fa mbanicha Yahudawecha ɓikǝndǝ muh hanhar nifiya, hwanikǝnnda kǝ thlang fichi kiitasi.
ACT 25:16 Paɗ ndayi kandǝwa, kanang Romawecha sǝnwanihi tǝ sa kiita le sǝk ɓǝɓi'ǝnwa, sema ɓeɗndǝtǝndi kǝ mbǝɗa fa muh hanharkǝn hwanitǝ tǝ hwanita, paɗ sema fǝraa fichi mbanda kǝthlǝm kǝ hǝrkaǝn i'ndi'en kǝ ɗar muh hanhari sǝt ficha.
ACT 25:17 Kǝthlǝm kichu, ɓak nda mbǝɗya rǝmmǝ tǝ ndi, a sǝɓawi hanthlikǝnnaɗǝwa, ɓingnetkǝn sokki mbǝt soksakmiya, ɗǝfki ke ɓafichǝ tǝ nifǝkǝn.
ACT 25:18 Kǝ thlaatǝ fa muh hanharkǝn, ɓundǝ tǝ muh hanharkǝn kǝ ɗar ɓǝɓi i nati yarǝ kǝ ɗarkǝnwa.
ACT 25:19 Nakǝn shuwunchengnandǝsi le fǝruchit ndǝ kitsi kǝ ɗar Bulus, kǝ ɗar tǝr mbandengnanda, tǝ yunǝ wa Yǝso le mǝrka, Paɗ le thlartǝ Bulus tǝ alchitwa mǝllan tǝ shisshingtafa.
ACT 25:20 Njang paɗ mbahki i nati tausandǝ ichihiya, sahayi Bulus ndu nan ngǝmtǝfa kǝ ɗǝka Urshelima kǝsang fichǝ kiitasi kǝ ɗar ichiniyu.
ACT 25:21 Paɗ kak Bulus kǝthlarang fichǝ shundǝ'enhi, Kaisar kapat kutura kǝ thlaǝn kiita enhi, fǝrkǝn shunda kǝnna ficha pundǝhar kǝ fari nati thlǝnnda kǝ ndang ficha Kaisar.
ACT 25:22 Agiriffa kutura ndangna Festus wa: "Njang ma ni ɓata kathlǝmmata nifiya tǝ i'ndengna." Festus ndakǝnwa: "Nu sǝkndǝ ishki.
ACT 25:23 Wendambǝta Agiriffa tǝ Banis yimkǝndǝsi tǝ mwanda witǝ i kuturcha, ɓak ndǝ tǝ pǝktat fa mbecha tǝ pǝktecha hǝmǝtkǝn. Fǝrkǝ Festus shundǝ tǝndatwa kǝ yimang fichǝ Bulus kǝ kǝttǝn sakmiya.
ACT 25:24 Ndǝkǝn ndat Festuswa: "Agiriffa kutura, nattǝ nofchi natǝm tǝ kandǝ rǝmma, a nifi ɓitǝ nofcha Yahudawechǝ hanharkǝn kǝ Urshelima, tǝ mbǝɗya paɗ, Kanda hwattǝ ndatwa Kammusǝ kǝ malfichi ndi tǝ shissingtǝwa.
ACT 25:25 Paɗ njang nuwi i sǝttǝn le saaka i ɓǝllandǝwa. Nakǝn paɗ mǝllan tǝ i'ndi'en keɗ tǝ ndatwa kǝ ngǝrang fichi kita'enna mbanitǝ lǝ mwandǝ Kaisar, ndakiwa ni thlindǝ tǝndǝ mbǝɗ'en.
ACT 25:26 Paɗ nga kakati tǝ shundǝsi nati yaranda kutura Roma lǝ mwandǝsǝwa. Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn ɓaki tǝ ndi kǝ mbanitǝnuni, kapatkǝnna mbanitǝwa sokǝn Agiriffa kutura, kǝthlǝm ɗiffitǝ usamihar ndu ni mbǝs i nati yarata ɗarkǝn.
ACT 25:27 Kǝthlǝm njang a na ndengna, mbomchita kǝ thlǝn fichi hwan pursuna, nga tǝ cheɗ fichi ɓǝɓi ichi sǝtǝnwa."
ACT 26:1 Ndang Agiriffa Bulus wa: "Fǝrrufichi mbanda ke hǝrkangnǝ i'ndeku." Thla'ang Bulus hara, tǝrkaakǝn shunda ndakǝnwa,
ACT 26:2 A shiɗi sa'a, naki hǝrkandǝ i'ndengnǝ ɓukweya a mbanitǝ Agiriffa kutura kǝ yakat shuwunchi mbutǝ Yahudawechǝ kǝ ɗarna.
ACT 26:3 Sokkǝn lǝ mbǝrtǝ naku sǝn ǝ'nat sǝtta Yahudawecha tǝ ichi lanatnda halǝ'i'nda ɗarkǝn. kǝthlǝm kichu nja hwanuta kǝ kikǝnnǝ thlǝmmata tǝ kǝrǝsta.
ACT 26:4 Nat Yahudawecha shinndǝ witǝ soki sokti njang kǝ hwankimsha'a, thlata tǝrkakǝnna hǝmtengna paɗ tǝ Urshelima taakǝ ɓukweeya.
ACT 26:5 Shinndǝ nji kǝ soh, paɗ ma yehndǝsi nanda mbǝlla fǝr sheta ndatwa, naki hur humihi sherkǝ tǝ kuwur kus a hur tǝr mbandengnǝm, sokki kǝlǝ Farisiyawata.
ACT 26:6 Nakǝnya njang kitta mbanitǝnuni kǝthlǝm kǝ sikǝ fichi kiitasi kǝthlǝm ɗiffi hanɗkiketengna kǝ ɗar nǝhhata ɗǝf shuni fǝrandǝ Fara kakechinǝm.
ACT 26:7 Ɗǝfshuwunkǝn naka kachitnǝm kumngǝrǝnsǝ chap ɗǝfkǝndǝsi mbah nanda nat nǝhatǝ'en, paɗ nak nda kǝn hursi tǝ kuwur Fara nda fiɗiktǝ tǝ fara. Sokǝn kutura, kǝthlǝm ɗiffi hanɗǝkiketa ɗar nǝhata ɗǝfshuniniyu, sǝk nat Yahudawecha tǝrimifa!
ACT 26:8 Mǝ sǝka a naɗengnuni ɓahwanatwa na Fara thla'andǝ mǝmatchǝwa?
ACT 26:9 Njang tǝ i'ndengnǝ soh kǝllayi nda keeke kǝ si ichǝ oi, kǝnji shunda Yǝso lǝ Nazaratta kǝ ɗǝka mban.
ACT 26:10 I sǝti hacha a Urshelima, a mbishi alchita mbǝɗa pǝktat pǝrist cha, kǝthlǝm kǝ kuɓlayi fa tǝr mbandǝ oi kǝ pursuna. Tǝ Paɗ fari nat ficha ɓǝlandǝ kanda nja kuwur ɗiffitǝnanda.
ACT 26:11 Lafǝrayi pwancha kanda mbǝt humta Yahudawechihi lǝɗǝfki kandǝ kǝ shuwunndǝ ɓǝɓishundǝ kǝ ɗar thlǝm Yǝso. Kǝthlǝm lanaki kǝs komlǝ tǝ kandǝ kaǝn, lǝ naki kuwur kandǝ kǝ funǝ hǝmchǝ somsomǝn kǝni sa pwanchǝ kanda.
ACT 26:12 Ficha hur sǝtkichu, farǝle nja pǝɗata Dimaska, tǝ yahta pǝktat pǝristcha tǝ yarat ɗelwerti fǝritǝnda.
ACT 26:13 A hur hwatfara mbanda, Sokǝn kutura kǝ nanǝhi, neɗi ɗwachita le sherangnga ɗwachita hwatfara, finkǝnna afshi taurikǝnhi njang tǝ shikechi witengna.
ACT 26:14 Uffani hǝmkanihi hachahaya, Sǝkki ɓurata nditǝ tǝ mi Ibraniyanci, 'Shawulu, 'Shawulu, Kǝthlǝmmi natu fǝri pwancha? Nanna fǝra pwene i'ndeku tǝ sǝt atikrechit tǝ nji.'
ACT 26:15 Ndakiwa, 'Wunnaku Lǝmwanda? "Ndikǝ Lǝmwandǝwa, 'Njang Yǝso le natu fǝrapwancha.
ACT 26:16 Paɗ thla'u kǝ thlarnǝhi kit. Cheɗki fandengna mbǝɗeku kǝ ɗǝffisa kǝllasi tora, paɗ kǝ fǝrnǝ sheta kǝ ichi natu kǝ ɗarna, paɗ tǝ ichi nati cheɗutǝ kǝ mban.
ACT 26:17 Ni hǝrkuta mbǝnda nofcheku tǝ punochǝ paɗ. Ni thlinsa mbǝɗa punofchǝkǝn,
ACT 26:18 Kǝthlǝm kǝ i'nangnǝ hwanichengnaɗǝhi, Kǝ tǝɓǝrndǝhi a hulta kǝ ɗwachitta, paɗ tǝ thlata alchita sheɗan kǝ alchita Fara, tǝ kichu nannda mbǝskaɓiɗi ɗar ɓǝɓichitfecha, tǝ mbǝs'ǝnhar nat tǝ fichile sokkǝ chiɗchiɗ kǝthlǝm a firndǝ kit kǝ mbǝɗengna.
ACT 26:19 Kǝthlǝm kichu, sokǝn Agiriffa kutura, a cherwi kǝ fǝrayi mwanda ǝnnda sǝnnatǝwa ɓaka haiya afshi kǝ mbǝɗengna.
ACT 26:20 Tǝrkaaki ɓasanda nofchisa Dimaska, kani sanda nofchǝsa Urshelima chika ayi a thlet hǝmmǝt Yahudawecha, sayi punofchǝsǝ paɗ, ndatwa kǝ tǝrɗǝhi kǝ tǝmǝrɗǝhi kǝ mbǝɗa Fara, kǝ sǝndǝ ichi nachetǝwa tirɗǝhi.
ACT 26:21 Ndǝkǝn sǝk kǝssitǝ Yahudawecha a kapat hura'a Fara, naknda kat kǝ ɓǝllikǝnnda.
ACT 26:22 Paɗ kǝssikǝ Farǝsi kǝ nakǝnya, ndǝkǝn nati mbǝɗya kǝni fǝr sheta kǝ ɓǝɗa pǝktecha tǝ hwecha. Nga ǝnsomǝn nati mbutuwa, se i nat Tapǝnnecha tǝ Musa ndatndǝwa nan sǝta,
ACT 26:23 Keekesi Kǝrǝsti kǝ san pwane, kǝ sokka tǝrka thlata mǝmatcha, Kǝthlǝm kǝ ɓan tǝ ɗwachitta mbaɗa nofcha, Yahudawecha tǝ punofchǝ nat."
ACT 26:24 Bulussa ɗar hǝrkandǝ fat'en Festus thlaǝn ɓurat tǝ alchita ndakǝnwa: "Bulus, luwurchǝ naka tǝrutǝwa! Yakat changngandeku tǝb'raɗǝ i'ndekuhi!"
ACT 26:25 Ndak Bulus paɗwa: "Festus lǝmwanda, nga luwurchǝtǝrikǝwa. Kit nati mbuta a hur i'nda.
ACT 26:26 Paɗ kutura shintǝ ichi natya, lǝ naki shunandǝ lechitfǝwa. A shinisǝwa kileesa ichini natyu, kǝthlǝm nga ɓuɓweetǝ sǝt fichiwa.
ACT 26:27 Agiriffa kutura, a firnǝ kit tǝ Tapǝnnecha? A shiniwa firnǝ kit."
ACT 26:28 Ndang Agiriffa Bulus wa: "A hur hanthlikchi ɗimekya yahtusa lǝmnji kǝsi Kǝrǝsta?"
ACT 26:29 Bulus paɗ ndakǝnwa: "Chika hanthlikchǝ ɗimek, ndu njang ndu nga njangwa nja hwandǝ tǝ ndatwa kǝɗǝf Fara mǝniɗa sokǝn ɗengwa, nat tǝ fichile naka sǝknji ɓukweya, kǝnandǝ nda i'nati, nga nat tǝ chalalotiyawa."
ACT 26:30 Thlaakǝ kutura, kichu paɗ ngomna tǝ Banis tǝ fichile natndǝ ɗǝndassa mbǝt ǝrta.
ACT 26:31 Cheknda kishsha mbǝt kiita ndangnda ndaniwa: "Nifiya sutǝ i'kamkǝsi kǝkuɓlang fichǝwa, ndu kǝ ɓǝlang fichǝwa."
ACT 26:32 Ndang Agiriffa Festus wa: "Ma nga i'nakǝn nifiya thla'a ɗǝ muh hanhar'enna ɓanitǝ Kaisar wa, ma kǝ kalfichǝndǝhi."
ACT 27:1 Kǝ tahsandǝ fichi kanihi hur kommbawal kǝ thlaani kǝ thlet hǝmmǝt Italiya, Ndekǝn fǝrtǝɗǝ Bulus tǝ funǝ hwanchǝ pursunacha a hara kapat lǝthlǝrhwata Roma le nat thlǝmkǝnwa Yuliyus, ǝrta hurfa thlǝrhwatkǝna Kaisar Augustus.
ACT 27:2 Yimkani kommbawal tǝ le i Adiramitiyum, le tahǝskǝ thlaata kǝ thlet hǝmchi naka kǝllarǝ Asiya, Tǝrkaakani wita. Aristarkus lǝ Tasalonikata i hachahai Makidoniya, mǝllan tǝkǝm.
ACT 27:3 Ɓingǝtkǝn kana Sidon. Yuliyus chendaǝn kafata Bulus, kǝ ɗǝka nat shikechikǝn, kǝ kǝssangndǝsi.
ACT 27:4 Thlaakani mbǝɗya hur kommbawal nak rǝnna'a ɓahhandǝ kani. Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn ɗǝkani tǝ ɗiffitǝ tingring Sayifurus mbǝɗi nguchit rǝnnaa tǝ alchitsi.
ACT 27:5 Ɗiffitǝ cheɗǝngnanikishsha hawurkǝn le nak nduk tǝ hachahai Kilikiya tǝ Famfiliya, Saakani Mira hachahai Likiya.
ACT 27:6 A mbǝnniyu kapat lǝ thlǝrhwata Romawecha mbǝskǝn kommbawalla Alekzandariya lǝ ɗǝta hachahai Italiya, Sikǝnkani hurkǝn.
ACT 27:7 Sǝkani mundǝ tǝ muncha kweekani nata witǝ hǝɓakka, tǝ kweetǝ saatani nduk kǝ hǝmǝt Kinidus. Kǝ njandǝ rǝna'a kani ɗǝta mban, Kuwurkani tǝ kǝllar tǝ mbǝɗi nguchit rǝnnasi, tǝ ɗiffitǝ tingring Kirit nduk tǝ Salmoni.
ACT 27:8 Nakani kwee mbǝrandǝhi, kǝ mbǝɗi lǝ atfichiwa Kwescha mbǝt thlara kammbawalcha, nduk tǝ hǝmǝt Lasiya.
ACT 27:9 Nakǝn sǝɓafichi hanthlikchaɗi oi, wikǝn paɗ sokkǝn tǝ mboro, kǝthlǝm a hanthlikchiniyu shiɗ hurat langnga har kǝ farǝ kǝr kwisshimta i farǝ ɓǝɓichitfata mbirhi. Tiɗɗang Bulus thlǝmmechengnanda.
ACT 27:10 Ndangna kandǝwa: "Shisshingchengnuni kǝ sǝn tolla, Kǝllaɗi wiiya nannat tǝ mboro paɗ tǝ kuɓat ichi oi, nga kuɓat icha kommbawal ndengwa nat tǝ Shisshingchengnǝm."
ACT 27:11 Kapat lǝthǝrhwatkǝn ngǝmaǝn tǝ i mbutǝ Buluswa, Kǝthlǝm kichu kan thlǝmata shunda lǝ koharǝ kommbawaltǝkǝn paɗ tǝlǝ kommbawal tǝkǝn.
ACT 27:12 Nakǝn mbǝt ngomta kommbawalcha Lasiya su keeke kǝ sok kommbawalchi fekta mbǝɗyawa, nakǝn yakat funengnani ngǝmkǝndǝfa kǝ ɗaficha mban tǝ wita, Paɗ kǝ kweefichihi kǝ saa ficha Finiks manan sǝtta, kǝthlǝm kǝ sokɗǝ fekta mbǝnniyu. Finiks mbǝt humta kommbawalchihi a chicheng Kirit le naka kǝllaɗǝ kukuwun hishingta tǝ mbǝt hǝmfara, paɗ tǝ kukuwun harsǝmta tǝ mbǝt hǝmfara.
ACT 27:13 Tǝrkaakǝ rǝnnaa thlata tǝ kukkuwun harsǝmtǝ ngunngundeh, saǝn nofchifiyuwa nanda mbǝlla sǝt i naka handǝkikechengnanda, kahangndǝ tǝppasiɗǝ kǝskǝ kommbawal tǝkǝn har, kuwurkǝndǝ tǝ chicheng Kirit, nduk tǝ mi hawurta.
ACT 27:14 Su tolluwa ɓak kapat rǝnna'a tǝ kukuwun harsǝmta tǝ mbǝt chet fara, thlaakǝ rǝnnǝkǝna tingringta.
ACT 27:15 Kǝtǝptǝ rǝnnikǝn kommbawaltǝkǝn, hulangna kǝllaɗǝ rǝnnikǝn, ndǝkǝn malandani nak rǝnnikǝna pǝkkani.
ACT 27:16 Kuwurkani tǝ ɗiffitǝ hantingringta le nat thlǝmkǝnwa Kauda, mbǝɗi tahtǝ alchita rǝnnahi, kweekani kahhandǝ kommbawal tǝkǝn ka ɗǝfta mi chichengta.
ACT 27:17 Ɗiffitǝ kahhandǝ hwan kommbawal tǝkǝn kǝ hur kapat kommbawaltǝkǝn, ɗathlkǝnda kǝnang ndǝhi kǝffa kapat kommbawaltǝkǝn kǝthlǝm mǝninda fǝffathlaɗi. Tǝrangndǝ kuwurta kommbawaltǝkǝnna haya mbah na rǝnna'a njek nda kǝllar kǝthlǝm mbǝlla'undǝ koharǝkǝnwa, sǝkndǝ kichu kǝthlǝm kanda lechita mǝniɗa muh kanda hansohhi Sirtis lela mǝhɗang ichi uf.
ACT 27:18 Kǝthlǝm rǝnnikǝna ɓahandǝkandǝ kaǝn, ɓingǝtkǝn tǝrkaakǝndǝ harandǝ ichihaya hur kommbawaltǝkǝn, somkǝnnda hur ama.
ACT 27:19 A farǝ mǝkkatǝkǝn kandang tǝ harchengnanda sommangndǝ ǝnat tor kommbawalchikǝnnaɗi.
ACT 27:20 Kǝ sǝtani munchǝ oi nuwani farǝ tǝ hanndǝrechuwa, paɗ kapat ɗǝf er tǝ rǝnna'a nakna tǝppandakani, kǝtangani hanɗǝkiketakish tǝ ndatwa ngani hǝrǝktǝwa.
ACT 27:21 Nakǝn mwinndǝhi sǝmunɗǝ ɗǝsǝmtǝwa, thlaakǝ Bulus kit a hurnanda, ndakǝnwa: "Nofcha, mamashikuni shundengna, tǝndatwa mǝ thla'iɗuni a tingring Kiritwa, ma hǝmwuni hur mboro tǝ kuɓat'ichiyawa.
ACT 27:22 Nakǝnya nja kahhandǝ thlemaɗengnuni sam alchit fata, kǝthlǝm nga yunǝsǝ nasǝt mboro tǝ shisshingtǝ'ena hurnuniwa, kommbawaltǝkǝn natficha sǝt mboro tǝkǝn ndak.
ACT 27:23 Kǝthlǝm a fiɗiki ɓǝraayu mala'ika Fara le nati kǝ'ikǝn nati mwananda, thlarkǝn nduk tǝ nji,
ACT 27:24 ndakǝnwa: "Buluswa, mǝlechinuwa. Sokǝn waat kǝthlarna mbanitǝ kaisar. Andiya paɗ tǝmbǝnda kafata Fara nan hǝrkandǝ shikechǝ witeku."
ACT 27:25 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn sam alchitafa kunang nofcha, kǝthlǝm firikit kǝ mbǝnda Farǝ tǝndatwa i'mbwi'itǝfichǝyu, nakna nat kichu.
ACT 27:26 Sokkǝn waat kǝ muhang rǝnnaa kǝmmaɗi kǝ ɗar hansohi tingring le."
ACT 27:27 A fiɗik kumgǝrǝnsǝ fwaɗa tǝkǝn, nak nda njekkani a hawur Meditereniya. A ɗarfiɗikta fa koharǝ kummbawaltǝkǝn tǝrkǝndǝwa nakani nduk tǝ hachahaya.
ACT 27:28 Kikeɗangndǝ hwengngǝchitta amkǝn, mbǝssangndǝ a shee ishtǝ sarǝ aru tǝ kumchitchap. Ɗǝkkani mban kuɗeh ngǝrkǝnda kikeɗanda, mbǝskǝndǝ ishtǝ sarǝ kumchit hanherta.
ACT 27:29 Kǝthlǝm rahlechita mǝɗi kommbawal egnani kuk ngwichǝwa, kalkǝndǝ ǝnnat thlarandǝ kommbawaltǝkǝn hi fichile nak lǝklǝk fwaɗa, tǝ ɗǝffitǝ kommbawaltǝkǝn kǝthlǝm kǝ njaǝnwita. Hwankǝndǝ Fara kǝthlǝm kǝ wenmbǝt leɗleɗ.
ACT 27:30 Paɗ fa koharǝ kommbawaltǝkǝn kakndǝ mba hǝrǝkta. Tǝrangndǝ hwan kummbawaltǝkǝnna haya naknda sǝt ɗathla nda nanda tǝrandǝ tǝppasi hai lǝklǝkyu kǝ mbanitǝ kapat kommbawaltǝkǝn.
ACT 27:31 Ndǝkǝn ndandǝ Bulussa kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝna Roma tǝ fathlǝrhwechǝkǝnwa: "Ma thlaru nofchihiya hur kommbawaltiyawa, nga mbandǝsǝ natuni hǝrǝktǝwa."
ACT 27:32 Thlithlang fa thlǝrhwatkǝn sahǝt hwan kommbawal tǝkǝnaɗi kalkǝndǝhi kǝ pǝɗaka ɗar ama.
ACT 27:33 Kǝ nat mbǝt nduk wenda, hwanang Bulus kandǝwa kǝ sǝmndǝ ɗǝsǝmta ndakǝnwa: "Ɓukweya mundǝ kumngǝrǝnsǝ fwaɗa kuna puta, sǝmwuni ǝnwa.
ACT 27:34 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn nja hwanandǝkuni kǝ sǝmmuni ɗǝsǝmta kǝthlem ngwalngwalchit faɗengnuni paɗ yunǝsa hurnuni na mɓah hwasǝ'en chika ǝrtǝwa."
ACT 27:35 Kǝ mbutǝn kichu, tǝrkǝn njohma saǝn usoko Fara a mbanitǝnanda chichaǝnhi tǝrkaakǝn chiita.
ACT 27:36 Natnda mbǝskǝndǝ alchit sǝmɗǝsǝmta.
ACT 27:37 Uffani hur kommbawaltǝkǝn nakani nifǝ aru kumkum chap tǝ kumchit muɗ ngǝrǝnsǝ tehethl (276).
ACT 27:38 Kǝ sǝmtǝnda ngelnda, tahhandǝ lǝkta kommbawaltǝkǝnhi, naknda som alkama hur ama.
ACT 27:39 Kǝ wentǝmbǝta, fa koharǝ kommbawaltǝkǝn mbǝsaundǝ furuɗi nanndǝwa, mbǝtsi nguɗuk tǝ hansohitǝsi. Tahaskǝndǝfa kǝ ɗǝndǝ tǝ kommbawaltǝkǝnna ɗar hansohikǝn manansǝta.
ACT 27:40 Thlithlang ndǝ sahǝt tǝppaskǝnaɗǝ malkǝnda hur ama. Chatkichu paɗyu nangnda kwasandǝ sahchǝkǝnhi a fa i latǝprang kommbawaltǝkǝnhi. Thla'angndǝ kuwurchi naka kommbawaltǝkǝn keeke tǝ mbayi natrǝnnaa njekanda mban ɗǝffanndǝ innda kǝlarǝ hawurkǝn.
ACT 27:41 Kǝ saatani mbǝtkǝmta ama, tǝpkǝ kommbawaltǝkǝn hansohita yimkǝ'innda kommbawaltǝkǝna hur hansohikǝn mbǝlla'utǝ hǝhǝrtǝfuwa. Tǝrkaakǝ kommbawaltǝkǝn fǝfathlǝɗi tǝ ɗiffi kǝthlǝm rahha'a.
ACT 27:42 Tahǝskǝ fathlǝrhwatkǝnfa kǝthlǝm kǝ ɓǝllangndǝ pursunechǝkǝn, mǝni yuneng nanda kun'ngoftǝ kǝ hǝrkǝn.
ACT 27:43 Nakǝn kapat lǝthlǝrhwatkǝnna Roma yehsa hǝrkandǝ Bulus, njangnakanda. Fǝrkǝn shundǝ tǝ alchita ndatwa: "Nat fichile mbǝrkǝ ama kǝ pǝparnda hurkǝn kǝ chang ndǝ kǝ mi chicheng le."
ACT 27:44 Tahhǝt pursunachǝkǝn kǝ tǝrnda ɗar chichet afchǝkǝn ndu hur chichet kommbawaltǝkǝn. Tǝkichu chetndakish kǝ mi chichengkǝn ngwalngwal.
ACT 28:1 Ɗiffitǝ hǝrǝktengnani, sǝkaniwa, awi thlǝm tingringǝyuwa Malta.
ACT 28:2 Nofchi mbǝnniyu cheɗangdǝkafata kani kaǝn. Thlǝkndǝ kani natani, njihangndǝ hwatakani kǝthlǝm ersi paɗ mbitǝsi.
ACT 28:3 Ngomkǝ Bulus afcha nakna sǝtta hwaɗiyu, chek hwithlnda kissha hur hwaɗiyu lenat yethaftǝ'en thlerthler, njo'aǝn hara Bulus.
ACT 28:4 Kǝ nat nofchi naka mbǝnniyu hwithlinkǝnna hǝhhǝrtǝfa hara Bulus wangarra, ndangnda ndaniwa: "Kitchitkǝn nifiya lǝɓǝlfatanakǝn! Andiya, chikanakǝn hirikka hurhawurta, nattǝkichu alhaki enna kuwurndi nan mǝrta.
ACT 28:5 Bulus paɗ saktaǝn har'en muhaǝn hwithinkǝnna hur hwata, mbǝsutǝ ndinditwa.
ACT 28:6 Naǝn kandǝhiwa nan hǝthlta ndu kǝ hǝmǝnhi chat kǝ mǝrrǝn, sǝkndǝ tolla nunda saǝnwa, ngǝrkǝndǝ yarǝtǝ ndatwa mǝllan witǝ farǝ mǝ nakǝn.
ACT 28:7 A mbǝɗǝ ndukya mbichisi i lǝ mbani tingringkǝn lǝ at fichiwa, Fubiliyus. Mǝllan thlǝk kani, fǝraǝn mbǝt munda kani ndiichin, kǝllakndǝsa kani, i'mundǝ mǝkkan.
ACT 28:8 Shin Fubiliyus nduk tǝ hafat kakǝnnda tǝ i ɗǝlǝhta. Yimkǝ Bulussa thlǝmatken hwanaǝnsi, ɗǝffaǝn hara in, kǝnkǝ nifǝkǝnaɗi.
ACT 28:9 Paɗ kǝ sǝkǝn kichu, nat tahǝt haacha fichile naka thlet tingringǝniyu naknda ɓata nak ficha kǝnandǝ kandaɗi.
ACT 28:10 Fǝrangndǝ poffǝna kani oi. Nakani thlata kommbawal tǝkǝn, ngomangndǝ icha kani lenatani yahta.
ACT 28:11 Ɗiffitǝ ndǝraa mǝkkan, thlaakani a tingring Malta hur kommbawal Alekzandiriya le tumbang fekta tingringkǝn. Tahsa fichi mirshing mǝhɗat hwanmanchisi nda farǝcha.
ACT 28:12 Ɓakani Sirakus munkani mǝkkanna mbǝnniyu.
ACT 28:13 A mbǝɗya paɗ pǝɗakani kǝ Rikiyum. Ɗiffitǝ mundǝ ǝrta, thlaakǝ rǝnnǝ kukuwun harsǝmta, Wendambǝt paɗ saakani Futiyoli.
ACT 28:14 A mbǝnniyu kǝmkani tǝ hwanmancha fa fǝrkit, hwanangndǝ kani kǝ sani mundǝ muɗ tǝ kanda. Tǝ kichu saatani Roma.
ACT 28:15 Kǝ sǝktǝ fa tǝrmbanda Roma kusengnani, ɓaknda sa marapa kani a lumo Affiyus, tǝ paɗ mbǝndi la ndat fichiwa mbǝt tǝrtahai Mǝkkan. Nak Bulus kanda saǝn usoko Fara, ngǝrkǝn mbǝs alchitafa.
ACT 28:16 Kǝ yimtani Roma ngǝmang ficha Bulus si kǝɗa sokta a huri haiya rǝmmǝ tǝ lǝ thlǝrwhaɗi naka pundǝhar.
ACT 28:17 Ɗiffitǝ mundǝ mǝkkan, Bulus akǝn pǝktat Yahudawecha ngomkǝndǝhi ndǝkǝn ndandǝna kandǝwa: "Kunang hwanmancha, chika nakǝn sawi ɓǝɓi'ǝn nofchengnǝmwa, ndu ɓǝɓi'ǝn i tǝrmbanda kakechengnǝm, nat tǝ kichu a kǝssi ficha a Urshelima fǝrkǝfichi nji kǝ Roma kǝkǝnnikǝnda.
ACT 28:18 Kandang paɗ kǝ usitǝndǝmihar, Yahkǝndǝsi kǝ kalndǝ njihi, kǝthlǝm mbǝsiwundǝ tǝ ɓǝɓi'ǝn le saaka ɓǝllitǝwa.
ACT 28:19 Paɗ cherkǝ Yahudawechi ngǝmtǝfa, ɓakna soktǝ waat kǝ tǝrayi muh hanharengna mbanitǝ Kaisar, chikanakǝn ngatǝni muh hanhar nofchengnǝmwa.
ACT 28:20 Ndǝkǝn sǝk kati kǝ nikuni, paɗ kǝ yaraam ichihi tǝ kuni, kǝthlǝm le ndǝftǝ Isra'ilawechǝ hanndǝkiketa natnda pu'ɓat'en sǝk kǝnitificha tǝ chalalocha."
ACT 28:21 Ndǝkǝn ndaɗǝɗǝwa: "Kanang mbǝswani yarat ndelwer a thlet hǝmǝt Yahudiya kǝ ɗarwuwa, nga yunǝ hwanmananisi ɓak tǝ kushengwuwa ndu kǝ mbu'un ɓǝɓi shunda ɗarwuwa.
ACT 28:22 Paɗ yahkanisi kǝ sǝkani yareku amiyeku, kǝthlǝm i sǝntani, yuwa humǝhi i lekiyu chikawuni mǝla shuwun ɓǝɓi icha ɗarkǝn.
ACT 28:23 Ɗǝfkǝndǝ fari natnda humtǝhi tǝ Bulus, ndǝkǝn ɓatnda mbǝt tǝrtǝ'enahaya, ɓakndǝ kaǝn. Thlata ɓingta kǝ farǝhufta mǝlla mwa'anda kanda tǝ sǝna kuturichita Fara kandǝsi, nakna kweetǝhi kǝ kahǝn kanda ɓǝɗa Yǝso tǝ mba sakanda Musaɗi tǝ ɗelwercha Tapǝnecha.
ACT 28:24 Funa ngǝmmangndǝ i mbutǝn, funa paɗ cherkǝndǝ fǝrkitsi.
ACT 28:25 Kǝthlǝm kichu halǝ'indǝsa thlerǝnanda. Naknda malǝ mbǝnnihiyu shunang Bulus kandǝ ǝrta ndatwa: "Awi Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ mbwitǝ kit, Shunandǝn kakechinuni tǝ miya tapǝnaa Ishaya ndatwa:
ACT 28:26 "Ɗu mbǝnda nofchiya, kǝ ndangna kandǝwa, Sǝkta, nuni nata sǝkta, Paɗ nguni sǝndǝwa, Nat paɗ nuninatanata, nguni mbǝssandǝwa.
ACT 28:27 Kǝthlǝm hanndǝkiketa nofchiya shiɗ kwaakwaa, resh thlǝmechengnandaɗi, ngǝlangndǝ hwanichengnanda, kǝthlǝm mǝ nindǝ tǝ hwanichengnandǝwa kǝ sǝkndǝ paɗ tǝ thlǝmechengnanda, kǝ mbǝsangndǝ tǝ hanɗǝkikechengnanda, kǝ tǝɓǝrndǝhi mbǝɗengna kǝ kǝnayi kanda ɗi.
ACT 28:28 Paɗ, kǝ sǝnuniwa, Fara a thlintǝ kuseng hǝrǝkta kǝ mbǝnda punofcha. Kandang paɗ nanda kat thlǝmatsi.
ACT 28:29 Kǝ mbukǝn kichu, thlaakǝ Yahudawecha mbǝnniyu tǝ halǝ'indǝ kaǝn a hurɗiffitǝnanda.
ACT 28:30 Bulus sokǝna huriini natna kwandǝyu hurat chap mǝlla thlǝt fichile ɓaka mbǝɗ'en.
ACT 28:31 Nakǝn njawundǝ ɓasǝwa, nakna ɓasǝ kuturichita Fara, nakna sakandaɗi kǝ ɗar Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso Kǝrǝsti nga lechitsuwa.
1CO 1:1 Yarat ɗelwertiya ɓakna mbǝɗengna njang Bulus, at Fara tǝ ngǝmtǝ'en kǝ naka lǝthlǝnda Yǝso Kǝrǝsti. Paɗ yaraki ɗelwertiya tǝ hwanmanǝm Sastanis.
1CO 1:2 Nakani yarat ɗelwertiya kǝ ɓǝɗa fa tǝrmbanda Fara hur Korinti, tǝ mbǝɗa fichile taɗtǝ fichihar a hur Yǝso Kǝrǝsti, atfichǝ kandǝ kǝnandǝ chiɗchiɗ, nat tǝ fichile chika ayi la ak thlǝm Lǝmwaɗengnǝm Yǝso kǝrǝsti, Lǝmwaɗengnanda tǝ inǝm:
1CO 1:3 Kafata tǝ yuyurchita mbǝɗa Shinnǝm Fara tǝ Lǝmwaɗengnǝm, Yǝso Kǝrǝsti kǝ mbǝɗengnuni.
1CO 1:4 Kǝnding la naki sandǝ Farǝ usoko kǝthlǝm kunang, kǝthlǝm kafaɗi Farǝ fǝrandǝna kuni tǝ mbǝɗa Kǝrǝsti Yǝso.
1CO 1:5 Chika tǝ mba yeni fǝraɗǝ hurmichita kuni a fat'en, hur shuwunchengnuni tǝ sǝn'ǝn paɗ nat,
1CO 1:6 kǝthlǝm ɓeɗ ficha mbǝsandǝ sheta engnani kǝ ɗar Kǝrǝsti a hurnuni.
1CO 1:7 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn ɓahwuni chika witǝ fǝr shemeɗ muwa, nda i natuni ɗǝf hwanita ɓata Lǝmwaɗengnǝm Yǝso Kǝrǝsti;
1CO 1:8 Le na kǝskunihar tǝ alchita kǝ mweshitkǝn, kǝthlǝm kǝ sokuni nga fa chithansarǝhiwa a farǝ ɓata Lǝmwaɗengnǝm Yǝso Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 1:9 Fara, lǝ nǝhɗandǝ ɗǝfshundǝhi mǝlan ak kuni kǝnuni ɓweet tǝ hwe'en Yǝso Kǝrǝsti Lǝmwandengnǝm.
1CO 1:10 Hwanaɗi kuni, hwanmancha, a hur thlǝm Lǝmwaɗengnǝm Yǝso Kǝrǝsti ndatwa: "Natuni kǝ ngǝmuni tǝ ndani mǝni saktǝhi sa hurnuniwa, kǝ humangnguni inda kǝna yarengnuni ǝrta, hanndǝkikechengnuni paɗ ǝrta."
1CO 1:11 Hwanmanchina mbu'i nofchi hura'a Kuluwi yu, ndatwa mbatsa thlerǝnuni.
1CO 1:12 I nati yarǝ ndatwa, chika wuna hurnuni mǝla mbu ǝn somǝn, ndatwa: "Njang i Bulus, "Yuna ndatwa, "Njang i Afolos, "Yunǝ paɗwa, "Njang i Kefas, "Yunǝwa" Njang i Kǝrǝsti."
1CO 1:13 Awi a shek Kǝrǝsti hiwa? Ndu Bulus kukwandǝfichihi kǝthlǝm kunang? Ndu sang fichi baptisma kuni hur thlǝm Bulus?
1CO 1:14 Saɗi Farǝ usoko sawi baptisma yuna hurnuniwa, nda Kirisbus tǝ Gayus ndak sandi kanda,
1CO 1:15 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn yunǝsǝ na ndatwa sangfichi baptisma hur Thlǝmnǝwa.
1CO 1:16 Kit a saɗi baptisma nofchi hura'a Istifanus. Ɗifitǝ ndǝkǝn kuɗukwi ndu saɗi baptisma yunǝ paɗwa.
1CO 1:17 Thlǝnu Kǝrǝsti njiwa kǝ si baptisma wa, paɗ kǝ ɓassi laulawata nga tǝ mbǝr sǝn'ǝna nifǝwa, kǝthlǝm mǝ sǝɓa fichi alchit palita Kǝrǝsti ɗǝwa.
1CO 1:18 Pathla palita ɓomchita mbǝɗa fichile naka mba thlǝrǝttaɗi, paɗ kǝ mbǝɗengnani kanang ti hǝrǝkka alchita Fara.
1CO 1:19 Kǝthlǝm yara fichǝhi ndatwa: "Ni wuwelandǝ sǝn'ǝna lǝ sǝnda ɗi, kǝ sayi ɗathla lǝ ɗathlaɗi kǝ'ǝn pofǝn."
1CO 1:20 A ai fa ɗathla? A ai fa sǝn'icha? A ai fa halǝ'inda kisshi'iya? A chawu Fara kishwa ɗathla kisshi'iya ɓomchitwowa?
1CO 1:21 Sokkǝn a hur ɗathla Fara, sǝnu kisshitǝ Farǝ tǝ mbanda ɗathlǝ'enwa, mbǝnangna Farǝ fa kǝ hǝrkaǝn fichile fǝrkǝkit, tǝ mbǝɗa ɓomchit ɓassǝ laulawatkǝn.
1CO 1:22 Keɗ Yahudawechǝ kǝ nandǝ sakǝtkǝn, Helenawecha naknda kat ɗathla,
1CO 1:23 kanang kana ɓassǝ Kǝrǝsti kukwandǝ fichǝhi, i sokka ǝnat chithansarǝhi mbǝɗa Yahudawecha, ɓomchit paɗɗaa mbǝɗa punofcha,
1CO 1:24 A nakǝn mbǝɗa fichile at Fara, ndu Yahudawecha ndu Helenawecha nat hwaa, Kǝrǝsti alchita Fara tǝ ɗathla Fara.
1CO 1:25 Kǝthlǝm i tǝrtǝ fichǝwa shiɗ Farǝ ɓomchita, sheraɗa ɗathla nifa, paɗ ɓah alchita Fara, sheraɗa alchita nifa.
1CO 1:26 Hwanmancha yaramǝn naɗengnunihi fari at fichi kuni. Nga terchǝnuni nak tǝ sǝn'ǝn witǝ i nifǝwa; nga terchin nak tǝ mwandǝwa, paɗ nga terchin ngǝttǝ fichǝ nda kuturchǝwa.
1CO 1:27 Farǝ taɗkǝn i har naka ɓomchita kish, kǝthlǝm kǝ harangfat fa ɗathla, taɗkǝ Farǝ i nak ɓukɓukka hur kisshita kǝ harangfat fa alchita.
1CO 1:28 Taɗkǝ Farǝ ǝnat kuɓanda fata tǝ i njirtǝ kisshita nat tǝ ichi nguchǝksi kǝthlǝm i la nat nofcha tǝrtǝwa ndiichin kǝ saǝn nga'ǝnwa.
1CO 1:29 Nat ichiniyu, sǝkǝn kǝthlǝm mǝ tǝri nifǝ tǝ hwasa'inwa ǝn nakǝn a mbanitǝ Farǝ wa.
1CO 1:30 Farǝ sǝka natuni hur Yǝso Kǝrǝsti, le sokka ɗathlengnǝmma mbǝɗa Fara, mǝllan sokka fǝrkit engnǝm, chiɗchiɗchita tǝ hǝrǝktengnǝm.
1CO 1:31 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn nda i natna hur yaratkǝn: "Chikawun na thla'a'ndǝ inda kǝ thla'angka hur Lǝmwanda."
1CO 2:1 Hwanmancha, ma ɓeɗi mbǝɗengnuni, ɓuwi kǝthlǝm kǝ mbwa'aikuni i naka ɓuɓweeta Fara, tǝ mbǝr shunda ndu tǝ sǝn'ǝnwa.
1CO 2:2 Kǝthlǝm tepi tirihur yahwisa sǝn'ǝn somǝn naki tǝ kuniwa, Yǝso Kǝrǝsti ndak, le kukwandǝfichǝhi.
1CO 2:3 Ɓaki mbǝɗengnuni hur ɓah alchita tǝ lechita, paɗ tǝ saktatfǝ kaǝn.
1CO 2:4 Lǝmfatsi ndu ɗathla hur shuɗengnǝ tǝ ɓassengnǝwa, tǝ cheɗndǝ alchita Shemeɗa,
1CO 2:5 Kǝthlǝm fǝrkitchiɗengnuni mǝniɗa ɗar sǝn'ǝna nofchǝwa, kǝ naka ɗar alchita Fara.
1CO 2:6 Chika tǝ kichu, la shuwunkani sǝn'ǝna kǝ mbǝɗa fichile mwanka hur fǝrkit, nga sǝn'ǝna kisshi'i nakǝnya ndu i kuturchi nakǝnya, fichile naka thlǝrǝttaɗǝwa.
1CO 2:7 La nakani shuwun sǝn'ǝna Fara hur ɓuɓweetǝ yu, le naka hur ɓuɓweetǝ soh, sǝn'ǝni fǝrtǝ Farǝ soh kǝ tǝrka nathi kǝthlǝm mwaɗengnǝm.
1CO 2:8 Hur kuturchi nakǝnya ngusǝ mbǝsang sǝn'ǝniyawa, mamuwa mbǝsanda, ma kukwawundǝ Lǝmwandǝ le nak mwanchinwa.
1CO 2:9 Nda i nat yaratkǝna hur laulawatkǝn: "I tahsandǝ Fara fichilesǝ la mbǝnkǝfatkǝn, tamu hwanita natwa, thlǝmatsǝ tamka sǝktǝwa, hanndǝkiketa nifǝsǝ tamka yarandǝhiwa."
1CO 2:10 Kanang cheɗandǝ Fara kani tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗ'en. Shemeɗ la kaǝn chikamǝnat, chikamǝ naka hwengngǝchit icha Fara.
1CO 2:11 Wuna hurnofcha sǝnkǝ yara nifa, manga Shemeɗi nifǝkǝn ti naka fi'enwa? Kichu paɗ nifǝsǝ sǝnkǝ yara Farǝ wa Shemeɗa Farǝ ndak.
1CO 2:12 Thluwani shemeɗa kisshitǝwa, Shemeɗi ɓaka mbǝɗa Fara thlǝtani, kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝnani ichi fǝrandǝ Fara kani pofǝn.
1CO 2:13 La mbwa'angani ichiya kuni, nga tǝ shuwunchǝ le sakandǝ fichaɗi tǝ mbǝɗa sǝn'ǝna nifǝwa tǝ shuwunchi sakandǝ fichaɗi tǝ Shemeɗa, tǝ mbu i naka kitchita shemeɗa a hur shunda Shemeɗa.
1CO 2:14 Nifi nguchit Shemeɗa fi'en thlutǝ ichi ɓaka mbǝɗa Shemeɗa Farǝ wa, kǝthlǝm nakǝn kǝ ɓomchita mbǝɗ'en, paɗ ngu mbǝlla sǝn kandǝwa, kǝthlǝm tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗ la sǝntǝfichǝ kanda.
1CO 2:15 Nifi nat Shemeɗsa fi'en la sǝnkǝ ichǝ nat, mǝllan tǝ indi'en nifǝsǝ na kikeɗandǝwa.
1CO 2:16 "Wun sǝnkǝ yara Lǝmwanda har natna sakandǝhar?" Kanang yarengnani i Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 3:1 Hwanmancha, ngi mbǝlla mbwa'a' ǝna kuni nda nofchi naktǝ shemeɗa fǝwa, nda nofchi naka kisshita, paɗ nda hangwa'yarcha hur tǝrmbanda Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 3:2 Yah fǝrandǝ kuni nga ɗǝsǝmtǝ kwaakwaawa, kǝthlǝm sǝkwunisa sǝm'ǝn kwaakwaa kwaɗǝnwa. Chika nakǝnya sǝkwunisǝwa,
1CO 3:3 Kǝthlǝm paaya mwakuni hur fata. Makuna sǝrǝh ndani paɗ thlangǝtmisa thlerǝnuni, nga mwakuni hur fatwowa? Ɗǝsǝchengnuni nga nda tǝ fatwa?
1CO 3:4 Kǝthlǝm ma ndeɗ yunǝwa, "Njang i Bulus", "Ndak yunǝwa", "Njang i Afolos", Nga tor fat natuni sǝtyuwa?
1CO 3:5 Wun naka Afolos? Wun naka Bulus? Nga mafechǝwa fichile fǝrtuni kit tǝ mbǝɗengnanda, nda i fǝrandǝ Lǝmwanda tora chikawun engnanda?
1CO 3:6 Njang hǝfkǝ hanwǝtǝkǝn, thlǝrkǝ Afolos amsǝ, paɗ Farǝ mwanangnga.
1CO 3:7 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, lǝ hǝfkǝn tǝ le thlǝrkǝ amsi nga naknda mi ǝnwa, Farǝ ndak mǝllanti la mwanangnga.
1CO 3:8 Lǝ hǝfkǝn tǝ lǝ thlǝr amkǝnsi nakndǝ ǝrta, chika wuna hurnanda nakficha kwanandǝ keeke tǝ tor'en.
1CO 3:9 Kǝthlǝm kanang shikechǝ fa torcha Fara, kunang hita Fara, tinda Fara.
1CO 3:10 Tǝ mbǝɗa kafaɗi fǝritǝ Fara, a ɗǝfi thlorǝ tindǝhi kǝ lǝ mbǝr tinda, ɓakyuna nata chekandǝ tinkǝn kǝ ɗarkǝn. Chikawuni kǝ sǝn hǝɓaakǝ tǝ witǝ tindǝ'en.
1CO 3:11 Kǝthlǝm nifǝsǝ na ɗǝf thlorǝ tinda kǝ pǝɗangka le hi ɗǝftǝ fichǝhiwa, le naka Yǝso Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 3:12 Nakǝnya ma tin yunǝ kǝ ɗar thlorǝ tinkǝn tǝ zinariya, ndu tǝ azurfa, ndu tǝ ngwichǝ ɗiichin, ndu tǝ afcha, ndu tǝ hwelaa, ndu tǝ kofcha,
1CO 3:13 na tora chikawuna chetakish, kǝthlǝm fariniyu nan chetakissha ɗwaachitkǝn. Nak tora chikawuna chetakish tǝ hwata, hwatkǝn na kikeɗandǝ tora chikawuni.
1CO 3:14 Ma tini sǝtficha kǝ ɗar thlorǝ tinkǝn hiriki iwaɗǝwa, le tinka nan thlǝt kǝnikǝn.
1CO 3:15 Ma iɗ torkǝna ɗi, le tinka nan sat ɓahta, mǝllan tǝ indǝ'en nan hǝrǝkta nda nifi kuwurkǝ tǝ hur hwata.
1CO 3:16 Awi sǝnwuniwa kunang tǝ inchengnuni naka kapat hura'a Farǝwa, paɗ nak Shemeɗa Farǝ tǝ sokta a hur hanndǝkikechengnuniwowa?
1CO 3:17 Chikawun sǝɓang kapat hura'a Fara ɗi, na Fara sǝɓandaɗi; kǝthlǝm kapat hura'a Fara la nakǝn chiɗchiɗ, kunang naka kapat hura'a Farǝkǝn.
1CO 3:18 Mǝ lǝmiɗuni inchengnuniwa. Ma yunǝsa hurnuni la yarkǝwa ɗathlchin a hur kisshi'i nakǝnya, kǝ saǝn fat'en nda ɓoma, kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝka lǝ ɗathla.
1CO 3:19 Ɗathla kisshi'iya ɓomchita mbǝɗa Fara. Nda i natna hur yarat laulawatkǝn: "La kǝsaǝn fichile nak ɗathlchin a hur ɗathlengnanda."
1CO 3:20 Tǝpaɗ: "A shin Lǝmwandǝwa yara fa ɗathlǝ nga ǝnwa."
1CO 3:21 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn mǝ hupa nifǝ hǝsǝr tǝ nifǝwa. Kǝthlǝm chikamǝ nat innuni,
1CO 3:22 ndu Bulus, ndu Afolos, ndu Kefas, ndu kisshita, ndu shisshingta, ndu mǝrtaɗi, ndu ichi nakǝnya, ndu ichi naka mban, nat innuni.
1CO 3:23 Kunang paɗ i Kǝrǝsti, Kǝrǝsti paɗ i Fara.
1CO 4:1 Tǝkichu kemsi kǝ tǝruni kaniwa mafecha Kǝrǝsti, tǝ fichile ngǝmandǝ fichǝ kǝnandǝ tǝ ichi Farǝ naka ɓuɓweeta.
1CO 4:2 Sokkǝn waat nifi malandǝ fichǝ ichahar kemsi kǝ mbǝsang fichǝ tǝ kitchita fa.
1CO 4:3 A mbǝɗengna, hanhwan'ǝna kǝ nda fichǝwa kunang na sakimiya ndu mbǝt sakmiya chikawun nifa. Kitchitkǝn, njang mangi sakamiya faɗengniwa.
1CO 4:4 A shini hur indengniwa naki yalfar, chika kichu ngu soktǝwa chiwi hansarǝhiwa. Lǝmwandǝ na kikeɗita.
1CO 4:5 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn mǝ thlaɗuni sakmihi kǝ ɗar yunǝ pofǝn sa'u hanmunchikǝn kwaɗǝnwa; pwa'ama kǝ farǝ nat Lǝmwanda ɓata. Mǝllan na chandǝ ichi kissha ɓuɓweeta kǝ ɗwachitkǝn, kǝ cheɗin yara hanɗǝkikecha. A farǝniyu chikawun nan thlǝt hamtǝ'ena mbǝɗa Fara.
1CO 4:6 Nakǝnya hwanmanchina, fǝrki sakǝt ichi natya kǝ faɗengnǝ tǝ Afolos kǝthlǝm kunang, kǝ sakuni ǝn tǝ mbǝɗengnani kǝ ɗar shuni ndatfichǝwa: "Mǝ mbǝraɗuni ihi yarandǝ fichihi hur laulawatkǝnwa." Mǝ thla'a yunǝ inda hurnuni kǝ mbǝrangka lehi kǝ ɗar yunǝwa.
1CO 4:7 Wun sukǝ somǝnhi tǝ tahhǝt nofcha, mǝnakseku le thluchitu? Sokkǝnma tǝ thlǝna, mǝsǝk natu thla'a'ndǝ inda nda nga tǝ thlǝnǝwa?
1CO 4:8 Tepi mbǝshuni nat ichi yahtuni! Tepi shokuni kǝ hurrumcha! Tepi shokuni kuturcha nga tǝ kanangwa! Mayahtengna kǝ sokuni ka kǝ kuturcha, kǝthlǝm kanang ma kǝ sokani kuturichitkǝn tǝ kuni.
1CO 4:9 A naɗengna cheɗ Fara a ɗwachitkǝnwa, kanang fathlǝncha njirandǝ fichǝ kaniɗi kǝ ndukwatkǝn chika mi, nda nofchi thlandǝ fichǝ sakmi mǝrtaɗa kandǝsi, sangfichi kani kǝ ǝnat nata kisshita, tǝ mala'ika cha nat tǝ nofcha.
1CO 4:10 Shokani kǝ ɓomcha Kǝrǝsti, kunang nakuni kǝ fa ɗathla hur Kǝrǝsti! Kanang fa kuɓanda fata, kunang nakuni kwaakwaa. Ficha natkuni tǝ kapatichita fa, kanang nga ǝnnakaniwa.
1CO 4:11 Paa kǝ nakǝnya, nakani hur mita tǝ kusshimta, thlǝthlah njelecha naka fechengnani, ficha tǝpanda kani paɗ hurechengnanisǝwa.
1CO 4:12 La sani tor kaǝn tǝ harchengnani. Ma erndǝ kani, ndǝfangani mbǝs'ǝnhara kanda; ma fǝrandǝ pwancha kani, kǝrǝskani.
1CO 4:13 Ma sǝɓandǝ thlǝmchǝnaniɗi, la shunangani kandǝ tǝ kachita. Paaya sokkani nda chirǝfta kisshita, i nat chikawuna wuɗekta.
1CO 4:14 Nga yaraki iya kǝthlǝm kǝ harangfat kuniwa, kǝ tahsayi kuni nda hwanchi yahti.
1CO 4:15 Chikama sokkǝn fasakchengnunisǝ aru kumchitkum (10,000) a hur Kǝrǝsti, shinchǝnunisǝ terchinwa, kǝthlǝm njang naka shinnuni a hur Yǝso Kǝrǝsti tǝ mbǝɗa laulawata.
1CO 4:16 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn nja hwanandǝ kuni kǝ sakuni nji.
1CO 4:17 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn nja thlǝna Timoti kuni, hwe'engna le la mbǝntifatkǝn, le nak tǝ kachita a hur Lǝmwanda. Nan kuɗkanda kuni tǝ mbanda naɗengnǝhi a hur Yǝso Kǝrǝsti, nda i soktǝn keeke tǝ i sakandi ɗaɗi chika ayi hur chika yen mbǝt tǝrmbanda.
1CO 4:18 Funa thla'a'ndǝ inda nda ngi ɓata mbǝɗengnuniwa
1CO 4:19 Ma ngǝma Lǝmwanda ni ɓata mbǝɗengnuni chetchetya, kani tausandǝ alchiɗi mbǝstǝ fa thla'a'ndǝ iniyu kish tǝ shuwunchengnanda.
1CO 4:20 Kǝthlǝm kuturichita Fara nga pathla shundǝwa pathla alchita.
1CO 4:21 Mǝ yahtunisi? Kǝ ɓi mbǝɗengnuni tǝ kuɓwerǝwa, ndu hur mbǝnfata paɗ tǝ ngwallǝchit shemeɗa?
1CO 5:1 Shikiwa fǝlawichitsa hurnuni, witǝ le tamuchit ficha sǝta chika hur fa sǝt tor ɗǝhhacha, yuna sok fǝlawichit tǝ nuh shinkǝn.
1CO 5:2 Nakuni thla'a'ndǝ inda! Nga kwesh sǝtuni sǝɓhurwa? Chikawun sǝk iniyu kǝ chang ficha kissha hurnuni.
1CO 5:3 Chika sokkǝn njangsǝ tǝ iɗengna mbǝnniyuwa, njang tǝ kuni hur hanɗǝkiketa. Tepi sakaɗi miya nifi sǝk witǝ iniyu, nda njangsa mbǝnniyu.
1CO 5:4 Ma hwimunihi a hur thlǝm Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso njang tǝ kuni mbǝnniyu hur hanɗǝkiketa, paɗ alchita Lǝmwaɗengnǝm Yǝso mbǝnniyu,
1CO 5:5 witǝ nifiniyu kǝ fǝranguni Sheɗan kǝthlǝm kǝ ɓǝllang ficha hur fata, mbah na shemeɗ'ena hǝrǝkta farǝ ɓata Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso.
1CO 5:6 Thla'a'ndǝ inchengnuni ndǝɗuwa. Sǝnwuniwa, mehndǝ nguɗehkicha la huppang humbat tahasǝ njohmǝ wowa?
1CO 5:7 Pa'amǝn ɗohhǝt mehniɗiyu fechengnuni, kǝ sokuni kǝ yuwa ɗokyeta le nguchit mehndǝsa fi'en, kǝthlǝm kittǝkǝn nakuni kichu. Kǝthlǝm teppa thlafichi ɓurat hwan shohraɗengnǝm i chohhǝm tala, mǝlan naka Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 5:8 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn kǝsam chohhǝmtengnǝmhar nga tǝ ɗohhǝt mehndǝwa, mehǝn sǝɓfata tǝ ɓǝɓifata. Kǝla sǝm chohhǝmtengnǝm tǝ njohmi nguchit mehndǝsi, ndǝkǝn naka njohǝm kachita tǝ kitchita.
1CO 5:9 Yaraɗi kunisa hur thlǝn yarat ɗelwer engna ndatwa mǝlla humiɗunihi tǝ fǝlauchiwa.
1CO 5:10 Nga yarengnǝwa nofchi kisshi'iya naka fǝlauchiwa, tǝ fa yah'ichǝwa, tǝ fa ɗathlanda nofchifǝwa, tǝ fa sǝt tor ɗǝhhachǝwa. Kǝthlǝm ma nakǝn kichu sokkǝn waat kǝ chunikissha hur kisshita.
1CO 5:11 Yarayi kunisi mǝ sokiɗuni tǝ chikawun la at fichiwa hwanmanda lǝ tǝrmbanda, ma la sǝkǝn fǝlawichita, ndu lǝ yah'icha, ndu lǝ mwanandǝ ɗǝhhacha, ndu lǝ erǝfata, ndu lǝ sat icha, ndu hara. Chika sǝm'ǝn mǝ sǝmiɗuni tǝ witǝ nofchiniyuwa.
1CO 5:12 Mǝ kǝmikǝ tǝ sakamiya fichile nguchika hur tǝrmbanda? Nga fichile naka hur tǝrmbandǝ natuni sakamiya kandǝwa?
1CO 5:13 Farǝ na sakamiya fichile nguchika hur tǝrmbanda: "Chamǝn ɓǝɓi nifa hurnuni."
1CO 6:1 Ma yunǝsa hurnuni naka thlangǝtmi tǝ shekkǝn, mǝ ɗiɗa muhhanharkǝna mbǝɗa fa ɓah fǝrkitwa, nga kweshkǝn kǝ mbǝɗa fa fǝrkitwowa?
1CO 6:2 Awi sǝnwuniwa fa fǝrkit na sakamiya kisshitǝwowa? Makunang na sakamiya kisshita, nguni mbǝla sakmi ichi top-topyawowa?
1CO 6:3 A sǝnwuniwa kǝmnang na sakamiya Mala'ika chiwowa? Kana cheta ichi natma soktǝsa kisshi'iya!
1CO 6:4 Ma witǝ muhhanhar chini engnunisiyu, mǝsǝk la ɗǝtuni tǝkǝna mbanitǝ fichile nguchika miya ǝna mbanitǝ fa tǝrmbanda?
1CO 6:5 Mbuki iniyu kǝthlǝm kǝ harangfat kuni. Sokkǝnyawa yunǝsa hurnuni ǝrtǝ nak ɗathlchin na tahsandǝ thlerǝ fa fǝrkitaɗǝwa?
1CO 6:6 Paɗ mǝsǝka hwanmanda la ɗǝtna muhhanhar hwanmankǝn a mbanitǝ fa ɓah fǝrkit?
1CO 6:7 Muhhanhar ndani ti la muhtuniyu kǝttǝhi mbǝɗengnuni. Nga kweshkǝn kǝrǝstuni kǝ nuni ɓomchǝwowa? Mǝsǝk nguchituni kǝrǝstǝ kǝ ɗathlang ficha kuni fa?
1CO 6:8 Kunang tǝ inchengnuni kuna ɗathlanda ndanifa kuna puppuk ndanihi, ta hwanmanchǝnuni la sanduni ichiniyu kanda.
1CO 6:9 Awi sǝnwuniwa fa ɓah fǝrkit ngunda mbǝs yimta kutǝrichita Farǝwowa? Mǝ lǝmi fichi kuniwa, kǝthlǝm fa sǝɓtaɗaɗisi ndu fa sǝt torɗǝhhacha, ndu fa sǝt fǝlauwichita, ndu hishchǝ fa che fechengnanda, ndu hishchi fa mundǝ tǝ hishcha,
1CO 6:10 ndu harcha, ndu fa yahta, ndu fa sat'icha, ndu fa erǝfata, ndu fa ɗathlanda nofchǝfa na mbǝs mbǝta hur kuturichita Farǝwa.
1CO 6:11 Nak funengnuni kichuyu. Anakǝn sapa fichǝ kuniɗi, tahsafichǝ kuni, chafichǝ kuni kish a hur thlǝm Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso Kǝrǝsti, paɗ tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗa Farengnǝm.
1CO 6:12 "Chikamǝ ngǝmifichǝsi", Paɗ nga chikamǝ na kǝsitisǝwa. "Chikamǝ ngǝmifichǝsi", Chika kichu ngi sokta mafata chikamǝwa.
1CO 6:13 "Ɗǝsǝmta kǝthlǝm hura, hur paɗ kǝthlǝm ɗǝsǝmta" Farǝ nan thlǝrtandǝ kandaɗǝ hwaa. Sufichǝ fata kǝthlǝm kǝ i fǝlawichitwa, kǝ naka i Lǝmwanda, Lǝmwandǝ paɗɗaa i fata.
1CO 6:14 Thla'ang Farǝ Lǝmwanda hur mǝmatcha tǝ alchit'en, paɗ chika kǝm nan thla'a'ndǝ kǝm.
1CO 6:15 Awi sǝnwuniwa fechengnuni njarǝ fata Kǝrǝsti tǝ indǝ'enwowa? Kemsǝ hachiya kǝ hari njarǝ fata Kǝrǝsti kǝ humayi kandǝ tǝ ɓǝɓimanda? Ngu tamtasǝtwa!
1CO 6:16 Awi sǝnwuniwa nifi humangfat tǝ ɓǝɓimanda sokkǝndǝ fat ǝrtǝ tǝ ndǝwowa? Kǝthlǝm nda i nat yarat laulawatkǝn: "Chapndǝyu naknda soktǝ kǝ fat ǝrta."
1CO 6:17 Le humang fat'enhi tǝ Lǝmwanda, sokkǝndǝ ǝrta hur shemeɗ tǝ ndi.
1CO 6:18 Rahamna fǝlawichithar! Tahhǝt ɓǝɓichitfechi nat la sǝt nifa nakna kisshitǝ fat'en, paɗ le sǝk ɓǝɓichitfat tǝ mbanda fǝlawichita sǝkǝn ɓǝɓichitfat kǝ fa fat'en.
1CO 6:19 Sǝnwuniwa fechengnuni kapat hura'a Fara le naktǝ Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, naka a hanndǝkikechengnuni, le thlǝtuni ɓǝɗa Farǝ wowa? Nga nakuni tǝ alchit inchengnuniwa.
1CO 6:20 Hikkǝ fichǝ kuni 'yang'yang. Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn mwanamǝn Farǝ tǝ fechengnuni.
1CO 7:1 Nakǝnya kǝ ichi yaratuni ɗarkǝn, ndiichinsi hishnifǝ mǝ kahindǝ kanwa.
1CO 7:2 Kǝthlǝm rahhanda fǝlawichit har, chikawun hishnifǝ kǝnan tǝ nuhkǝnsi, paɗ chikawun nuhnifǝ kǝnan tǝ sǝmahsi.
1CO 7:3 Hishnifǝ kǝ fǝraǝn i kamkǝsa nuhkǝn i reta, nuhnifǝ paɗ kǝ fǝraǝn i kamkǝsa sǝmahha i reta.
1CO 7:4 Kǝthlǝm nuhnifǝ alchit'ensǝ kǝ fa fat'en ichitkǝnwa, sǝmah ndak. Kichu paɗ sǝmah alchit'ensǝ kǝ fa fat'en ichitkǝnwa, nuhkǝn ndak.
1CO 7:5 Mǝ njaɗuni ndaniwa, kǝnan tǝ ngǝmtengnuni hwaa, kǝ fari ɗǝftuni kǝthlǝm kǝna hur'inchengnuni hur hwanda kanuni ngǝr kǝmta, kǝthlǝm mǝ limi sheɗan kuni a ɗar ɓah kǝrǝstǝwa.
1CO 7:6 Mbuki iya i kamkǝsi yarandǝhi, nga waatwa.
1CO 7:7 Mamuwa nansǝta kǝna nofchǝ nat nda njang. Nakǝn chikawun hishnifa tǝ i fǝrandǝ Fara, leya tǝ witǝ i fǝrandǝn leyu paɗ tǝ witǝ ikǝn.
1CO 7:8 Kǝ mbǝɗa fichile kahuchikkan tǝ ndǝllat nishcha fichile mǝrtǝ hishchengnandǝyu, a kǝllaɗengna keekesi kǝ soknda kahundǝ kanwa nda i nati.
1CO 7:9 Ma ngunda mbǝla kǝs fechengnandǝ harwa, kǝ kahndǝ kan. Kweshkǝn kǝ kah nifǝ kan mǝni ita ɗi tǝ yahta.
1CO 7:10 Kǝ mbǝɗa fichile kahkǝ kan nja ndandakuniwa, nga njangwa Lǝmwanda, ndatwa: "Nuhnifǝ mǝ sakindǝhi tǝ sǝmahwa."
1CO 7:11 Ma ɓeɗa saktǝhi tǝndi, kǝ sokǝn kichuyu kǝnretsǝwa, manga kichuuwa kǝ tahsangndǝ thlerǝnandaɗi tǝ sǝmahha. Hishnifǝ paɗ mǝ sakiɗǝhi tǝ nuhkǝnwa.
1CO 7:12 Kǝ mbǝɗa tahchikǝn paɗ ndakiwa: "Nga Lǝmwandǝ mbukǝwa." Ma yunǝ hwanmandǝsi nat nuhkǝn kǝla ɓahfǝrkit, ngim nuhnifǝkǝn kǝ sokǝn tǝndi, mǝ cheriɗǝndǝwa.
1CO 7:13 Ma nuhnifǝsǝ nat sǝmah kǝ lǝ ɓahfǝrkit, ngim hisnifǝkǝn kǝ sokǝn tǝndi, mǝ cheriɗǝndǝwa.
1CO 7:14 Kǝthlǝm hishnifǝ lǝ ɓahfǝrkit, tahsafichǝ chiɗchiɗ tǝ mbǝɗa nuhkǝn, paɗ nuhnifǝ lǝ ɓahfǝrkit, tahsafichaɗi chiɗchiɗ tǝ mbǝɗa sǝmahha. Manga kichuwa, hwechengnuni naknda nat tǝ putafa, nda i natǝn nakǝnya, nakndǝ chiɗchiɗ.
1CO 7:15 Ma lǝ ɓahfǝrkittiyu yahkǝsa saktǝhi tǝ shetkǝn kǝnan kichu. A witǝ mbǝnniyu, hwanmandǝ kǝ nuhnifǝ ndu kǝ hishnifǝ nga waatsa sokkǝnwa. Kǝthlǝm Farǝ akǝn kǝm kǝ sok yuyurchit tǝ ndani.
1CO 7:16 Sokǝn nuhnifa, shinnǝ ndu mbahya sokǝn na hǝrkandǝ sǝmatuuwa? Sokǝn hishnifa, shinnǝ ndu mbahya sokǝn na hǝrkandǝ nuhwuwa?
1CO 7:17 Chika witǝmǝ natma hurkǝn, chikawun kǝ sokka mbǝɗi ɗǝftǝ Lǝmwandǝndǝsi a nat'enhi, kǝ i at Farǝ ndi. Ndǝkǝn naka mbutengna kǝ mbǝɗa fafǝrkit nat.
1CO 7:18 Wun taɓkǝ kǝ heshang ficha kǝ fari at fichǝndi? Mǝ sokiɗǝ kǝ lǝ ɓah heshiwa. Le heshuchika kǝ fari at fichǝndi, mǝ kiɗǝ heshiwa.
1CO 7:19 Hesha tǝ ɓah hesha nga ǝn nakndǝwa, kuwur kussa Farǝ ndak naka ka'ǝna.
1CO 7:20 Chikawun kǝ nan nda i natǝn kǝ fari at Fara ɗi.
1CO 7:21 Naku kǝ mafat kana ficha atsǝwa? Mǝ kǝmu ǝnwa. Manu ɓǝs alchit iɗeku, sǝku tor tǝ mbayiniyu.
1CO 7:22 Chikawun naka mafata kana Lǝmwanda atndi nakǝn kǝ nifi ɓǝske alchit iɗi'en a Lǝmwanda. Kichu paɗ le nguchika mafata kana ficha atndi nakǝn kǝ mafata Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 7:23 Hikkǝ fichǝ kuni 'yang'yang mǝ niɗuni mafecha nofchǝwa.
1CO 7:24 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn hwanmancha, chika hur witǝ sokmǝ atfichǝ chikawuni, kǝ sokǝn kichu nda i at Farǝndi, kǝnan tǝ Farǝ'en.
1CO 7:25 Kǝ ɗar nishchi tamuchika kan, fǝriwu Lǝmwandǝ alchit shuɗe kǝ ɗarkǝnwa, paɗ naki fǝr i naka yarengna kǝ ɗar ndatwa njangti ngǝmitǝ fichǝsi a ɗar shisshetfata Lǝmwanda.
1CO 7:26 Ma yarengna, kǝthlǝm ɓahhi natma hurkǝn nakǝnya, keekesi kǝ soknifǝ ichitkǝn nda i natǝn.
1CO 7:27 A kehnikanwa? Mǝ kǝnǝ saktǝhiwa. Ma kahunikanwa, mǝ kǝnǝ nuhnifǝwa.
1CO 7:28 Ma kehnikan sunǝ ɓǝɓichitfatwa, ma keh nuhhwekan sutǝ ɓǝɓichitfatwa. Fichile kahkǝkan nanda yimta ɓahtǝ somsomǝn a naɗihiya, njang tǝ yahhisǝ kǝnan paapa'a mbǝɗengnuni.
