1CO 7:29 I yarti hwanmancha, ndatwa hanmunchikǝn nguɗeh. Thlata nakǝnya kǝ mban fichile nat nishchengnandǝsi kǝ sokndǝ nda ngusengnandǝwa,
1CO 7:30 Fa tita nda nga tǝnnda titwa, fichile naka mbǝnfata nda nga kanda mbǝnfatwa, fichile hikkǝ'ǝna kǝ nandǝ nda nga ichengnandǝ kǝ kǝsndǝharwa.
1CO 7:31 Fichile naka sǝt tor tǝ ǝnat kisshita mǝ ɗǝfindǝ fatsǝwa. Kǝthlǝm kisshikǝn a naɗi nakǝnya, tǝ naka mbǝrtǝhi.
1CO 7:32 Yahkisi kǝnuni cha'a hur thlahur i'nda. Nifi kahhuchikkan nak yarǝ'ena ɗar torcha Lǝmwanda, i natna sǝta kǝ tǝraǝn hura Lǝmwandǝhi.
1CO 7:33 Le kahkǝkan nak yarǝ'ena nata ɗar ǝnat kisshita, mbayi natna sǝt kǝ tǝraǝn hura nuhkǝnhi.
1CO 7:34 Paɗ shek hur'indǝ'enhi. Nuhnifǝ kahhuchikkan ndu nuhhweya nak yarǝ'ena ɗar torcha Lǝmwanda, la ɗǝfkǝn indǝ'en kaǝn kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda a hur fat tǝ shemeɗa. Nuhnifi kahkǝkan yarǝ'ena ɗar ǝnat kisshita, mbayi natna sǝt kǝ tǝraǝn hura sǝmahhi.
1CO 7:35 Naki mbu ichiya kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝsangka kunisi, ngauwa kǝ ɓweshikuniwa, kǝthlǝm soktengnuni kǝnaka mbandǝ ndiichin mǝ saki yarengnunihi hur mwanandǝ Lǝmwandǝwa.
1CO 7:36 Ma yaraa yunǝhiwa i natna sǝt kǝ ɗar nuhhwani ngwantǝn nga keekewa, a nakǝn hurrecha nuhhwankǝna mbǝrtǝhi paɗ a fat'en kemsǝ kǝ kahhǝnkan, kǝ sǝn kichu nda i yahtǝn. Nga tǝna sǝt ɓǝɓichitfatwa, kǝ kǝnangndǝ reta.
1CO 7:37 Nifi thlarkǝ kit kǝ ɗar yara hanndǝkiketǝ'en ndatwa ǝnatkǝn nga waatwa paɗ nan mbǝlla kǝs indǝ'enhar, paɗ tira hanndǝkiketǝ'enwa ngu kahhandǝ nuhhwaniyuwa, mǝlan ma shiɗtǝ i nak keeke.
1CO 7:38 Nifi kahhang nuhhwani ngwantǝn shiɗ keeke, paɗ nifi kahhauchik nuhhwani ngwantǝn shiɗtǝ i kamkǝsǝ kaǝn.
1CO 7:39 Nuhnifǝ nakna kǝnda kǝ mbǝɗa sǝmahha ma tana mweehi tǝ shishingta. Ma mir sǝmahha, cheɗa kissha sahta kǝ kahhǝn chikawun yahtǝn, sokkǝn waat kǝ na hishnifǝkǝna i Lǝmwanda.
1CO 7:40 A thlandǝ shuɗengnǝhi, nan nat tǝ mbǝnfat kaǝn manan soktǝ ichitkǝn nda i natǝn. Paɗ la sikǝnfǝ Shemeɗa Farengnǝsi.
1CO 8:1 Nakǝnya pathlǝ ɗǝsǝmi fǝrandǝ ficha ɗǝhhacha: "Shinǝmwa nattǝm sǝɗengnǝmsi." Sǝndǝ la ɓakǝn tǝ thla'inda, mbǝnfata la tinaǝn.
1CO 8:2 Ma tiryunǝwa shintǝ'ǝna, paaya sǝnu nda i kamkǝsi kǝ sǝnǝnwa.
1CO 8:3 Ma yuna mbǝnfat Fara, shin Farǝ ndi.
1CO 8:4 Pathlǝ sǝm ɗǝsǝmi fǝrandǝ ficha ɗǝhhacha: "A shinǝmwa ɗǝhhata nga ǝnnakǝnna kisshitǝwa paɗ Farǝsǝ somǝnwa ǝrta."
1CO 8:5 Chika sokkǝnwa funisǝ la atfichǝwa farǝcha a Afshi ndu kisshita (nda i nat, "farǝchǝsǝ" ka'ǝn "shinchǝsǝ" paɗ kaǝn),
1CO 8:6 Chika kichu a mbǝɗengnǝm Farǝ ǝrta, le naka Shinda, ichi natya ɓakna mbǝɗ'en, naɗengnǝmhi kǝthlǝm mǝlan. Lǝmwandǝsi ǝrta Yǝso Kǝrǝsti, tǝ mbǝɗ'en chet ichi kish natya, kǝmnang paɗ naɗengnǝmhi tǝ mbǝɗ'en.
1CO 8:7 Nga chikawun sǝnkǝ iyawa. Funǝ paaya sǝɗengnandǝhi tǝ tor ɗǝhhacha, la saǝn kandǝfǝwa ɗǝsǝmi la sǝmtǝnda nda i fǝrandǝficha ɗǝhhata. Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn nguchikndǝ kwaakwa'a hur hanndǝkiketa la tǝrkǝndǝwa shiɓndaɗaɗi.
1CO 8:8 Ɗǝsǝmtǝ ɗutǝkǝm nduk tǝ Farǝwa. Ma sǝmwumwa ngǝma tahtǝhiwa, ma shimǝm ngǝma chektǝwa.
1CO 8:9 Kǝ ɗǝfuni indǝsi, mbǝs thlǝt indengnuni mǝ sokiɗa ǝnat chit hansarǝhi mbǝɗa fichile nguchit alchiɗengnandǝsi.
1CO 8:10 Kǝthlǝm ma neɗ yunǝsa le nguchik kwaakwa'a hur fǝrkit, sokǝn tǝ sǝnka sa sǝm'ǝna kǝtǝn mwanandǝ ɗǝhhacha, fǝrauni alchit sǝm i tahsandǝ ficha ɗǝhhachǝwowa?
1CO 8:11 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn hwanmani nguchik kwaakwa'a na sǝndeku sokta mba hǝmtǝ'enhi, le mǝrtǝ Kǝrǝsti ɗi kǝthlǝm mǝlan.
1CO 8:12 Ma shiɗnǝ ɓǝɓichitfat kǝ mbǝɗa hwanmanchiwa, tǝ mbǝnniyu paɗ ɗǝfau ndindita kandǝ kǝ ɗar ɓah kwaakwaa chiɗengnanda, tǝ sǝnǝ ɓǝɓichitfat kǝ mbǝɗa Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 8:13 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, ma sǝm'ǝn na ɗǝf hwanyaa kǝ yimka hur ɓǝɓichitfata, mwawi tamta chi thlu paɗwa, kǝthlǝm mǝ ɗǝffiɗǝ ndǝ kǝ hǝmǝnhiwa.
1CO 9:1 Njang mbǝs thlǝt indengnǝsǝwowa? Njang nga lǝthlǝndǝ nakiwowa? Anuwi Yǝso Lǝmwaɗengnǝmwowa? Kunang nga kǝni torengnǝ nakuni a hur Lǝmwandǝwowa?
1CO 9:2 Chika sokkǝnwa nga lǝthlǝndǝ naki mbǝɗa funiwa, kittǝkǝn mbǝɗengnuni njang lǝthlǝnda, kǝthlǝm kunang naka sheta tǝ tor lǝthlǝɗengna a hur Lǝmwanda.
1CO 9:3 Tǝ ndǝkǝn la chandǝ faɗengna kish a mbǝɗa fa tauwasǝnji.
1CO 9:4 Alchiɗengnanisǝ kǝ fǝranguni sǝm'ǝna kani tǝ satwowa?
1CO 9:5 Nga alchiɗengnanisǝ kǝ tǝrani kan kǝ wi'yani tǝ nishchengnani fafǝrkit nda i la sǝt tahhǝt fathlǝncha, tǝ hwanmancha Lǝmwanda tǝ Kefas yuwowa?
1CO 9:6 Nga njang tǝ Barnabas ndak sokkǝ waat kǝ sani tor sǝma'ǝn inchengnani kǝ nanihiwa?
1CO 9:7 Wun la sǝk tor thlǝrhwata kana sǝma'ǝn indǝ'en? Wun na pat affǝt inabi kǝ cherka chi hwanchikǝn? Wun na hǝrǝm chaɓa kǝ cherka sat yahkǝn?
1CO 9:8 Naki mbu ichiya ɗar yara nifǝwa? Ndu kustǝkǝn kichuwowa?
1CO 9:9 Yarang fichǝhi a hur kussa Musa ndatwa: "Mǝ panǝ hwan sokroka latami mamǝla sǝt tora hurhitǝwa." Lat ndak la hǝrǝmtǝ Farǝwa?
1CO 9:10 Nga shuwunkǝn kǝthlǝm kǝmnangwowa? Aa kǝthlǝm kǝmnang yarandǝ ficha. Kǝthlǝm lǝ huɗata, nakna huɗat tǝ ɗǝffatsǝ nan mbǝs ǝna, le naka ɗǝktǝ paɗ nakna ɗǝktǝ tǝ yarǝ mbǝs'ǝna hur ɗǝsǝmi hitǝkǝn.
1CO 9:11 Ma hifani hanwitǝ shemeɗa Fara hur hanɗǝkikecheng'nuni, kapat ǝnwa ma mbishani icha mbǝɗengnuni?
1CO 9:12 Mana funa mbǝs mba sǝt kichu mbǝɗengnuni, sherawani kandǝ tǝ mba sǝt kichuwowa? Chika kichu suwani tor tǝ mbayiniyuwa, kǝriskani tǝ chikamǝ kǝthlǝm mǝ ɓiɗani tǝ i na njat tor laulawata Kǝrǝstiwa.
1CO 9:13 Sǝnwuniwa fichile la sǝk tora kapat hura'a Fara, la mbǝskǝndǝ ɗǝsǝmtengnanda kapat hura'a Farǝkǝnwowa? Fa sǝt tora bagadi la mbǝskǝndǝ ɗǝsǝmta hur ichi la fǝrtǝ fichi i fǝr pofǝnwowa?
1CO 9:14 Kichuyu paɗ mbutǝ Lǝmwanda ndatwa, fichile naka ɓassǝ laulawata kǝ thlǝndǝ ǝnat nathi engnandǝ tǝ mbǝɗa laulawatkǝn.
1CO 9:15 Njang tamwi sah ǝn kuni hur ichiniyuwa, paɗ nga naki yarat'iya tǝ ɗǝffatsǝwa kǝ sikǝ fichǝ kichuwa. Kweshkǝn kǝ mǝri, mǝni yuna nji wilwirtengna tǝ ndǝkǝn.
1CO 9:16 Chika kichu ma ɓesshi laulawatkǝn, ngi wilwirtǝwa, kǝthlǝm ɗǝfkǝ fichǝnji waat kǝ ɓassi. Ai engna ma ɓasswi laulawatkǝnwa.
1CO 9:17 Mamuwa la ɓasski a ɗar yahtengna mala kwanikǝ ficha. Sokkǝnwa nga ɗar yahtengnǝwa, tǝni sǝt i malitǝ fichǝhi.
1CO 9:18 Mǝnaka kǝnikǝn engna? Kǝnikǝn engna ndǝkǝn naka ɓasse laulawatkǝn, kǝ ɓassǝ pofǝn. Sǝwitor tǝ cheta mbǝɗengnǝ nat a hur ɓassǝkǝnwa.
1CO 9:19 Chikama sokkǝn naki kweɗeleng nga hara chikawunwa, saɗi faɗengna mafata nofchǝnat, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsi nofchǝ oi.
1CO 9:20 Kǝ mbǝɗa Yahudawecha, naki nda lǝ Yahudawata, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝla'i kahhandǝ hur'incha Yahudawecha. Kǝ mbǝɗa fichile nat kussa alchiɗengnanda, naki nda le naka kakǝn paɗ (chikama sokkǝn njang tǝ indengna nga naki ka kustǝkǝnwa) kǝthlǝm kǝ kahhayi hur'incha fichile naka ka kus tǝkǝn.
1CO 9:21 Fichile nguchika ka kus tǝkǝn sokki nda kandang (chika sokkǝn nga naki kisshitǝ kussa Farǝwa naki ka kussa Kǝrǝsti) kǝthlǝm kǝ kahhayi hur'inda fichile nguchika ka kus.
1CO 9:22 Kǝ mbǝɗa fichile nguchit alchitsi njang ma naki alchitsǝwa, kǝthlǝm kǝ kahhayi hur'incha fichile nguchit alchiɗengnandǝsi. Sokki kǝ ichinat kǝ mbǝɗa nofchǝ nat kǝthlǝm chika tǝ kǝni kǝ hǝrkayi funa.
1CO 9:23 Sǝki ichini natyu kǝthlǝm kusheng shundǝ mbinchin, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsi ǝnhar hur mbǝs'ichihar.
1CO 9:24 Sǝnwuniwa hur fa teri rahta, nat fa teri rahkǝn la kweekǝndǝhi kǝ pǝɗangnda ndanihi, ǝrtǝ ndak la thlǝk kǝnikǝnwowa? Yimamma rahkǝn kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsuni kǝnikǝn.
1CO 9:25 Nat fa yimta terriyiniyu, la fǝrangndǝ ɓahta fechengnandǝ chika tǝteni. La sǝkndǝ kichu kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝsndǝ kǝnikǝn lena sǝɓtaɗi, kǝmnang paɗ la sǝkǝm inǝm kǝ mbǝsǝm kǝnikǝn le nguchika sǝɓtaɗǝ kǝpwaree.
1CO 9:26 A rahwi pofǝn nda nga mbǝt ɗǝtsǝwowa, a tokwi fat nda lela tokkǝ rǝnnawa.
1CO 9:27 Tǝ fǝrayi ɓahta faɗengna kǝ sayi mafata, kǝthlǝm ɗiffitǝ ɓassanda nofchǝsi njang tǝ indengna mǝ nji fichǝ mbǝs kǝnikǝnwa.
1CO 10:1 Yahkǝsi kǝ sǝnuni, hwanmancha, ndatwa kakechinǝm nat wikǝnda ka husomba'a, paɗ natndǝ ɗǝkndǝ tǝ hur hawurta.
1CO 10:2 A ka husombi'iniyu tǝ hur hawurkǝn sandǝ fichǝ baptisma kandǝ uf kǝ kuwur Musa.
1CO 10:3 Natnda sǝmkǝndǝ ɗǝsǝmta shemeɗa.
1CO 10:4 Natnda sakndǝ ama shemeɗa, kǝthlǝm sheɗndǝ ama a ngwiya shemeɗa le wiikǝ tǝ kanda. Ngwikǝn Kǝrǝsti nakǝn.
1CO 10:5 Chika tǝ kichu, sǝku Farǝ mbǝnfat tǝ funǝ oi a hurnandǝwa, tǝkang fichǝ kandǝhi a loktara.
1CO 10:6 Sǝk ichininatyu kǝ naka sakchikǝna mbǝɗengnǝm, kǝthlǝm mǝɗi hanndǝkikechengnǝma ɗar ɓǝɓi ichǝ nda i sǝtndǝwa.
1CO 10:7 Mǝ sokiɗuni kǝ fa sǝt tor ɗǝhhachǝ nda i sǝt funengnandǝwa, nda i natna hur yarat laulawatkǝn ndatwa: "Sokkǝ nofchikǝnhi kǝ sǝmndǝ kǝ sanda, thlaakǝnda naknda rǝɓta a hur sǝɓtaɗǝ i fǝlawichita."
1CO 10:8 Mǝ yimindǝma fǝlawichit nda i sǝt funengnandǝwa, ɓaka sǝt nifǝ aru kumchitkum chap tǝ aru kumchit mǝkkan (23,000) mǝrka farǝ ǝrta.
1CO 10:9 Ngǝma kikeɗandǝ Lǝmwandǝwa nda i sǝt funengnandǝwa, ɓak hwithlincha tǝkandǝ kandahi.
1CO 10:10 Mǝ hurmiɗǝm nda i sǝt funengnandǝwa, Mala'ika tǝ ɓǝlta tǝkaǝn kandahi.
1CO 10:11 Kǝskǝ ichini kandǝyu kǝ naka sakǝtkǝn, yarang fichǝ kandǝhi kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝka ǝnat kah thlǝmaɗengnǝm, kǝmnang ti ɓat ndukwat kisshikǝna mbǝskǝm.
1CO 10:12 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn chikawun yarkǝwa nakǝn kit, kǝ mbǝrǝnsi mǝ hǝmiɗǝhiwa.
1CO 10:13 Kiketǝsi tamka mbǝskuni le mbǝsuchitǝn nifǝwa. Farǝ lǝ kachita, ngu tamta ngǝmtǝ kǝ kikeɗang fichǝ kuni tǝ i na sheranda allengnuniwa. Ma kikeɗa fichǝ kuni nan mbǝssa mba chetakissha kuni, kǝthlǝm kǝ mbǝla'uni kǝrǝskǝn.
1CO 10:14 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn shikechina, rahamna tor ɗǝhhachihar.
1CO 10:15 Shuwunki tǝ kuni kunang fa hur'incha, kǝ yarangunihi kunang tǝ iɗengnuni i mbuti.
1CO 10:16 Kop i mbǝs'inhar le la sǝtǝm usoko kǝ ɗarkǝn, nga ndǝkǝn la ɗǝfkǝkǝm kǝnǝm ǝrta a hur fwara Kǝrǝstiwowa? Njohmi la chichaɗǝmhi nga ndǝkǝn la ɗǝfkǝkǝm kǝnǝm ǝrta a hur fwara Kǝrǝstiwowa?
1CO 10:17 Kǝthlǝm njohmiya ǝrta, kǝmnang ti nak terchin fat ǝrta, kǝthlǝm nattǝm njohmǝ ǝrtǝ la chiitǝm.
1CO 10:18 Kǝlamǝn Isra'ilawecha: Fichile la sǝmka hur i fǝrtǝ ficha, nga la humndǝhi tǝ ndani hur sǝm ichi fǝrandǝ ficha Fara a bagadi tǝ fǝr'ichǝwowa?
1CO 10:19 Mǝ nati yarǝ hachiyu? Ɗǝsǝmi fǝrandǝ ficha ɗǝhhacha naka ǝnwa, ndu ɗǝhhakǝn naka ǝna?
1CO 10:20 Auwa, yarengnaa i la fǝrtǝ fa sǝt tor ɗǝhhacha la fǝrangnda lǝwurcha nga Farǝwa. Yahwisǝ kǝ la nuni humtǝhi tǝ lǝwurchǝwa.
1CO 10:21 Nguni sat tǝ kop a Lǝmwandǝ kǝ suni paɗ tǝ i lǝwurchǝwa. Nguni sǝm'ǝna a mbǝt sǝmɗǝsǝmta Lǝmwanda kǝ sǝmuni paɗ a i lǝwurchǝwa.
1CO 10:22 Nǝma ɗǝf Lǝmwandǝ kǝ sǝrǝhtǝwa? Sheraɗǝm tǝ alchitwa?
1CO 10:23 "Nat icha ngǝmaficha kǝmsi", Nga nat ichǝ na kǝsanda kǝmsǝwa. "Nat icha ngǝmaficha kǝmsi." Nga nat ichǝ la tinangwa.
1CO 10:24 Mǝ si nifǝ ǝn ndiichin kǝ ɗar indǝ'en ɗengwa, kǝsǝn kǝ ɗar'inda funǝ paɗ.
1CO 10:25 Chi'u chikawitǝ thlumi, la hi'yandǝ fichaɗa mbǝt hi'yandǝ thluwaɗi, nga tǝ sahmi mbǝɗi ɓat thlukǝnwa, kǝthlǝm mǝni yarengnuni nata mbǝɗi chet thlukǝn.
1CO 10:26 Kǝthlǝm: "Kisshitǝ i Lǝmwanda nat tǝ ichi naka hurkǝn."
1CO 10:27 Ma eɗ lǝ ɓah fǝrkit sa sǝm ɗǝsǝmta, ngǝmkufǝ ɗǝkuni, sǝmu i ɓandǝ ficha kuni nga tǝ sahmiwa, kǝthlǝm kǝna hur'indǝ ngwalngwal.
1CO 10:28 Ma ndu yunǝwa: "Ɗǝsǝmiya i ɗǝhhata", Mǝ sǝminǝwa, kǝthlǝm le mbukǝ paɗ kǝna hanndǝkiketǝ'en yuyur tǝ sokǝn.
1CO 10:29 Nga yarkiwa hur'iɗekuwa, ikǝn. Yunǝ nan ndatwa kǝthlǝmmǝ nat ficha nji i yahtǝ faɗengna, kǝthlǝm yuyurchit hanndǝkiketa yuna?
1CO 10:30 Ma saɗi Farǝ usoko, kani sǝm ɗǝsǝmkǝn, kǝthlǝmmǝ nat ficha ishnji kǝ ɗar i sandǝ Farǝ usokosi?
1CO 10:31 Ndu tǝ sǝmna ndu tǝ sana, ndu chika witǝmǝ natu sǝta, su nat kǝthlǝm mwanandǝ thlǝm Fara.
1CO 10:32 Mǝ siɗuni kǝ ǝnat chit hansarǝhiwa, ndu Yahudawecha, ndu fichile nguchika Yahudawecha ndu nofcha Fara.
1CO 10:33 Naki kweetǝhi kǝ tǝrayi hura nofchihi nat chika tǝteni. Nga tǝni kat i na mbǝnanda faɗengnǝfǝwa, paɗ i na mbǝnanda nofchǝfǝ oi, kǝthlǝm kǝ hǝrǝknda.
1CO 11:1 Sakamnji nda i nati sak Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 11:2 Nja hamkuni kǝthlǝm la kuɗukkuni nji chika hurmi, kishshuni ichi sakandǝ kuni har ɗichin nda i fǝrandi kuni.
1CO 11:3 Yah kisi kǝ sǝnuniwa le naka inn chikawun hishnifa Kǝrǝsti, le naka inn chikawun nuhnifa, hishnifa, le naka inn Kǝrǝsti Fara.
1CO 11:4 Chikawun hishnifǝ hwanka ndu tǝ mbu'ǝn icha Fara indǝ'ena supta, njirtǝ Kǝrǝsti le nak mwanchinna mbanitǝkǝn.
1CO 11:5 Chikawun nuhnifǝ hwanka, ndu tǝ mbu'ǝn icha Fara supwawutǝ i'ndǝwa, njirtǝ sǝmahha le nak mwanchinna mbanitǝkǝn, nakǝn keeke tǝ hǝsandǝ i'ndǝ'enaɗi.
1CO 11:6 Ma cher nuhnifǝ supwandǝ i'ndǝ'en, kǝ hǝsaǝn hwasǝ'enaɗi. Manakǝn harǝfatsi ma hǝsa nuhnifǝ hwasǝ'enaɗi ndu kǝ hǝsangkaɗǝ tukulmur, kǝ supwaǝn.
1CO 11:7 Kamusi hishnifǝ kǝ supwa'ǝn i'ndǝ'enwa, nakǝn kǝ mirshingta paɗ mwanda Fara. Nuhnifa paɗ mwanda hishnifa.
1CO 11:8 Kǝthlǝm a tǝrkakǝn hishnifa nga chekna fata nuhnifǝwa, nuhnifǝ cheka fata hishnifa.
1CO 11:9 Su fichǝ hishnifǝ kǝthlǝm nuhnifǝwa, nuhnifǝ sǝt fichǝ kǝthlǝm hishnifa.
1CO 11:10 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn sokkǝn waat nuhnifǝ kǝ kǝnǝn ɗankwali i'ndǝ'en, che sakǝtkǝna sǝmah nak mwanchin, paɗ kǝthlǝm mala'ikacha.
1CO 11:11 Chika tǝkichu, a hur Lǝmwanda nuhnifǝ nga somǝnhi tǝ hishnifǝwa, hishnifǝ paɗ nga somǝnhi tǝ nuhnifǝwa.
1CO 11:12 Nda i nat nuhnifǝ chekna fata hishnifa, kichu paɗ nuhnifǝ ngǝtkǝ hishnifa. Ichi nat paɗ ɓaknda mbǝɗa Fara.
1CO 11:13 Yaramǝnhi tǝ inchengnuni, keekesi nuhnifǝ kǝ hwanaǝn Farǝ tǝ indǝ'en chaawa?
1CO 11:14 Sakkawu nathi kǝmharwa ma mel hishnifǝ hwasǝ'en njang, nga ǝnat harǝfata mbǝɗ'enwowa?
1CO 11:15 Ma hwasa nuhnifǝ njang nga mwandǝ'enwa? Fǝrang fichǝ hwasǝ njang kichuyu kǝthlǝm kǝ ngǝlaǝn i'ndǝ'ensi.
1CO 11:16 Ma yunǝsǝ nat halǝ'indǝ'ensi kǝ ɗar iniyu, kanang sǝnwani ɗǝsǝchǝ somǝnwa, nakǝn kichu mbǝɗa tahhǝt nofcha Fara.
1CO 11:17 Kǝ ichiya hamwi kuniwa, kǝthlǝm ma hwimunihi nga i katkǝnwa i sǝɓkǝn.
1CO 11:18 A tǝrkakǝn, sǝkkiwa ma hwimunihi humta fa tǝrmbanda, a lanak saktǝhisa hurnuni. Ɓeɗi fǝrkita ɗar shuwunkǝn nguɗeh kicha.
1CO 11:19 Sokkǝn waat kǝ mbǝs fichǝ saktǝhi hurnuni, kǝthlǝm kǝ sǝnfichǝ fa kachita hurnuni.
1CO 11:20 Ma hwimunihi nga jibi Lǝmwandǝ la sǝm tuniwa.
1CO 11:21 Kǝthlǝm a chikǝn, chikawun la ɗǝkna mban tǝ sǝm ɗǝsǝmtǝ'en pu'utǝ nifǝwa. Yunǝ tǝ mita fa, yunǝ ngeli har tǝraɗa.
1CO 11:22 Nga hurechengnunisǝ kǝ sǝmuni kǝ suni hurkǝnwowa? Tǝ njiruni fa tǝrmbanda Fara, paɗ kǝnuni ɓahhandǝ fichile nguchit ichengnandǝsi? Mǝnati mbwa'anda kuni? Kǝ hamikuni kǝ iniyuwa? Auwa ngi hamkuniwa.
1CO 11:23 I fǝrandi kuniya thlǝki mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda ndatwa: Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso, a fiɗiki fǝrtǝ fichǝndi, tǝrkǝn njohma,
1CO 11:24 ɗifitǝ sǝt usoko'en, chichaanhi ndakǝnwa: "Faɗengnǝniya, fǝrtǝ fichǝ kǝthlǝm kunang. La sam kichu kǝthlǝm kuɗuktǝ tǝnji."
1CO 11:25 Mbandǝ ǝrtǝ paɗ, ɗifitǝ jibi tǝkǝn tǝrkǝn kop, ndakǝnwa: "Koptiya i yuwa ɗǝf shundǝhi a hur fwarengna. Sam kichu nat kǝ farǝ natuni sata kǝthlǝm kuɗuktǝ tǝnji."
1CO 11:26 Chika kwat natuni chi njohmiya, paɗ natuni sata a koptiya, nuni mbu mǝrtaɗa Lǝmwanda kǝ fari natna ɓata.
1CO 11:27 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, nat le chiikǝ njohmiya, sheɗɗa hur kop ti Lǝmwandǝya nga hur chiɗchiɗchitwa, shiɗtǝ ɓǝɓichitfat kǝ fata tǝ fwara Lǝmwanda.
1CO 11:28 Chikawun kǝ kikeɗaǝn fat'en, kana chi njohhǝmkǝn paɗ kana sata koptǝkǝn.
1CO 11:29 Kǝthlǝm chikawun chiika a sheɗ paɗ ngatǝ mwanandǝ fatkǝna Lǝmwandǝwa, paɗ saɗǝ sakmiya fat'ensi, tǝ mbǝɗa chi'ini tǝ saɗini'enyu.
1CO 11:30 Ndǝkǝn sǝka nofchǝ oi a hurnuni alchiɗengnandǝsǝwa, funǝ haachinnda, paɗ terchina hurnuni a mirnda.
1CO 11:31 Ma yaraɗǝm inchengnǝmhi poo, ngu ficha sakamiya kǝmwa.
1CO 11:32 Ma Lǝmwandǝ sakang miyakǝm, na ficha eltandǝkǝm kǝthlǝm mǝ thlandǝ kita kǝmsǝ tǝ kisshitǝwa.
1CO 11:33 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn hwanmanchina, ma hwimunihi kǝthlǝm sǝm'ǝna, kǝ pu'uni ndani.
1CO 11:34 Ma yunǝsǝ tǝ mitafa, kǝ sǝmǝn'ǝna huri, kǝthlǝm humtengnuni mǝ ɓandǝ thlet shunda kuniwa. Kǝ ɗar tahhǝt icha, ni mbwa'a mbachǝkǝna kuni ma ɓeɗi.
1CO 12:1 Nakǝnya paɗ hwanmancha, pathlǝ fǝr shemeɗ somsomǝn, yahwisǝ kǝnuni tǝ ɓahsǝndǝwa.
1CO 12:2 Shinuniwa fari natuni nga fa tǝrmbandǝwa, limfichǝ kuni paɗ shekɗang fichǝ kuni kǝ fa kuwur ɗǝhhachi nguchit shishingchengnandǝsi.
1CO 12:3 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn yahkǝsi kǝ sǝnuniwa nifǝsǝ na shunda hur Shemeɗa Fara na ndatwa: "Yǝso nga'ǝn nakǝnwa" paɗ nifǝsǝ na ndatwa: "Yǝso Lǝmwandǝ nakǝn." Manga nakna hur Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ wa.
1CO 12:4 Nakǝnya fǝrtǝsǝ somǝn somǝn, Shemeɗ ǝrtǝ la fǝrkǝ kanda.
1CO 12:5 Mbachǝsi somǝn somǝn i sǝt torcha, chika kichu Lǝmwandǝ ǝrta.
1CO 12:6 Torchǝsi somǝn somǝn, chika kichu kǝmka Farǝ ǝrtǝ la fǝrkǝ tori nat chikawuna sǝta.
1CO 12:7 Chikawuni fǝra Farǝ mba ɓata Shemeɗa kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝsangka chikawunsi.
1CO 12:8 Yuna fǝrang fichǝ Shemeɗ mbǝr shunda, tǝpaɗ yuna Shemeɗ shuwun sǝn'ǝna, natyu tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗ ǝrta.
1CO 12:9 Yuna i fǝrkit tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗ ǝrta, yuna i kǝnandǝ nofcha ɗi tǝ mbǝɗa Shemeɗini ǝrtǝyu.
1CO 12:10 Yuna fǝrangndǝ alchit sǝt ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa, yunǝ i mbu icha Fara le na sǝt kǝmban, yuna i mbǝla sakandǝ shemeɗchǝhi, yuna i sǝn hanshuwunchǝ somǝn somǝn, yunǝ paɗ mbǝla sǝn i nat hanshuwunchi somsomǝnna mbuta.
1CO 12:11 Ichini natyu tora Shemeɗ ǝrtǝ la sǝk kanda, le la sakangnga chikawun nda i yahtǝn.
1CO 12:12 Nda i nat fat ǝrta njarǝchi'en terchin, chikama sokkǝn njarǝchi'en terchin, nakndǝ kǝ fat ǝrta, nak Kǝrǝsti kichuyu.
1CO 12:13 Sangfichi baptisma kǝm nattǝm tǝ Shemeɗ ǝrta kǝ hur fat ǝrta, ndu Yahudawecha, punofcha, ndu mafecha, ndu fichile thlǝk inchengnandaɗi, nattǝm ɗǝfkǝ fichǝkǝm kǝsǝma hur Shemeɗ ǝrta.
1CO 12:14 Fatkǝn nga tahsang fichǝ tǝ njarǝ ǝrtǝwa, paɗ njarǝchǝkǝn terchin.
1CO 12:15 Mana sara ndatwa: "Njang nga har nakiwa, makichu nga naki fa fatwa." Mbutǝ kichu ngu ɗǝfndǝ kǝ sakndǝhi tǝ njarǝchikǝnna fatkǝnwa.
1CO 12:16 Ma na thlǝmata ndatwa: "Kǝthlǝm njang nga hwanitǝwa, makichu nga naki fa fatwa." Mbutǝ kichu ngu ɗǝfndǝ kǝ sakndǝhi tǝ njarǝchikǝnna fatkǝnwa.
1CO 12:17 Ma fatkǝn nat kǝ hwanita, nakficha la sǝkmbǝt tǝ mi? Ma fatkǝn nat kǝ thlǝmata, nakficha la sa mbǝt tǝ mi?
1CO 12:18 Kittǝkǝn Farǝ tahsang njarǝcha hur fata, chikayeni nda i yahtǝn kǝ nandǝsi.
1CO 12:19 Ma nak fatkǝn nat kǝ njarǝchǝ ǝrta, nak fatkǝna natwa kǝni?
1CO 12:20 Nda i natǝn, njarǝchǝ terchin chika kichu fat ǝrta.
1CO 12:21 Hwanitǝ ngu ndanda harwa, "Kǝmiwu'ǝntǝsǝwa." Ndu inda kǝ ndangka harchǝwa, "Kǝmiwu'ǝntǝkuniwa."
1CO 12:22 A mbandǝ somǝn, njarǝchi fafat la kǝlandǝ fichǝwa nda nga kwaakwa'a ndǝwa, kandang naka kechikǝn,
1CO 12:23 Njarǝchi fafat la kǝlandǝ fichǝ nda nga ǝnnakndǝwa, kandang la mwanandani kaǝn. Njarǝchi kamuchiksi kǝ nafichiyu, la kǝlak fichasa kanda,
1CO 12:24 njarǝchi'engnǝm nak ndiichinyu, nga ma safichǝ ǝn kandǝwa. Humang Farǝ njarǝcha fata, nda i ngǝrandǝn njarǝchi farawuchit fichi mwanda, sokkǝn tǝ mwanda fa.
1CO 12:25 Sǝkǝn iniyu kǝthlǝm mǝni saktǝhisa hur fatwa, njarǝchikǝn kǝ la tǝrndǝwa nakndǝ nat keeke.
1CO 12:26 Ma njarǝsǝ ǝrtǝ naka ɓahta, nat ndǝ nanda nata hur ɓahta, ma njarǝsǝ ǝrtǝ fǝrandǝ fichǝ mwanda, nat njarǝchikǝn kǝ mbǝnndǝ fata.
1CO 12:27 Nakǝnya kunang naka fata Kǝrǝsti, chikawun ǝrta hurnuni nakǝn kǝ njarǝchi'en.
1CO 12:28 A kǝtǝn mwanandǝ Fara hertǝ nofchǝhar, saǝn funa tǝrkakǝn kǝ Fathlǝncha, chapatǝkǝn Tapǝnecha, mǝkkatǝkǝn fa sakaɗaɗi, funǝ fa sǝt ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nifǝfa, funǝ fa kǝnandǝ nofchaɗi, funǝ fa kǝsanda nofchǝsi, funǝ fa kǝlandǝ tora nofcha paɗ funǝ fa shundǝ tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝn.
1CO 12:29 Nat fatǝrmbakǝn fathlǝnchǝwa? Nat fatǝrmbakǝn tapǝnechǝwa? Nat fatǝrmbakǝn fa sakandaɗaɗiwa? Nat fatǝrmbakǝn fa sǝt ǝnat pǝɗandǝ nofchǝfǝwa?
1CO 12:30 Nat fatǝrmbakǝn fa mbǝs fǝr kǝnandǝ nofchandǝwa? Nat fatǝrmbakǝn fa shundǝ tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝnwa? Nat fatǝrmbakǝn fa mbu sakǝt i shuwuntǝ fichǝ tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝnwa?
1CO 12:31 Paɗ kam fǝrtǝ somsomǝn tǝ rahta fichile nak ka mwanchin. Ni cheɗa mbanda kuni le sherkǝ nat tǝ ndata.
1CO 13:1 Chikama la mbǝrki shundǝ tǝ hanshuwuncha nofcha tǝ i Mala'ikacha, nakǝn mbǝnfatsa faɗengniwa, sokki nda pupwandǝra lǝ la tik kaǝn, manga kichuwa nda thlǝmra.
1CO 13:2 Chikama fǝrtengnǝsi i mbu'icha Fara paɗ la mbǝsayi ichi ɓuɓweeta tǝ sǝndǝ nat, ma fǝrkitchiɗengnǝsǝ kaǝn ni mbǝla mbasandǝ shohlachaɗi nga mbǝnfatsa faɗengniwa nga ǝn nakiwa.
1CO 13:3 Chikama ni fǝra ichi naksengnǝ nata fa ɓahcha kǝ fǝri faɗengna kǝ 'yangfichaɗi manga mbǝnfatsa faɗengniwa, ǝnsǝ nati mbǝstisǝwa.
1CO 13:4 Mbǝnfata kǝrǝstǝ'ensi, tǝ kafata, sǝrǝhtǝsa hur mbǝnfatwa, thla'andǝ'ensǝwa, mwa'indǝsǝwa.
1CO 13:5 Mbǝnfata thla'indǝsǝwa, yah'indǝsa hur mbǝnfatwa, sǝɓhursǝ paapawa, kǝs'ǝnsahurwa.
1CO 13:6 Mbǝnfata yahutǝ sǝɓfatwa, la mbǝnkǝnfat kǝ i sǝtficha ɗar kit.
1CO 13:7 Mbǝnfat la nakǝn tǝ kǝrǝstafa kǝɗing chika hur witǝmi, la nakǝn tǝ fǝrkit hur chikamǝ nat, la ɗǝfkǝn hanndǝkiketa ichinat, la kǝrǝskǝn tǝ ichinat.
1CO 13:8 Tamu mbǝnfata tuɓwatwa kǝparee. Mbu'ichi Farǝ na sǝt kǝmban nan thlǝrǝttaɗi, shundǝ tǝ hanshuwunchi somsomǝn nan shekata, sǝn'ǝna nan thlǝrǝttaɗi.
1CO 13:9 Sǝn'ǝnengnǝm nǝhɗuhiwa. Mbu'ichi chandǝ Fara kish ngǝ mbǝɗengnǝm nǝhɗuhiwa.
1CO 13:10 Ma ɓeɗ le nǝhhǝɗkǝhi, le nǝhɗuchikhi nan thlǝrǝttaɗi.
1CO 13:11 Thlahmbǝɗi nati kǝ hweya, la shuwunkǝ nda hweya, la yarki nda hweya, la mbuki ichi kamkǝsi nda hweya. Kǝ sǝkti nifa, malayi hwanchita.
1CO 13:12 Nakǝnya la nakǝm nda a hur shishing'ama, shummǝ shumma, farǝkǝn nakma nat hwanitǝ tǝ hwanita. Sǝn'ǝnengna nakǝnya nǝhɗuhiwa, a farǝkǝn na sǝɗengna nǝhhatǝhi nda i sǝntǝfichinji ndiichin.
1CO 13:13 Nakǝnya, ichi mǝkkanya shokndǝ kichu, fǝrkit, ɗǝf hanndǝkiketǝsi, tǝ mbǝnfata. Le nak mwanchina hurnanda mbǝnfata.
1CO 14:1 Kwe'yamhi kǝ kuni mbǝnfata, kǝ kuni fǝrta Shemeɗ Chiɗchiɗ, nda i yah mbu ichi naka yara Fara.
1CO 14:2 Kǝthlǝm le la shuwunkǝ tǝ hanshundǝ somǝn, nga tǝ nofchǝ natna shundǝwa tǝ Fara, nifǝsǝ la sǝnkǝ i natna mbutǝwa, la mbukǝn icha ɓuɓweeta mbǝɗa alchita Shemeɗa.
1CO 14:3 Le la mbukǝ ichi na yara Fara, na shunandǝ nofcha kǝ tinaǝn kanda, kǝ chekaǝn alchita kanda, kǝ saǝn sǝssi kanda.
1CO 14:4 Le naka shundǝ tǝ hanshundǝ somǝn naka tinaɗǝ fat'en, paɗ le naka mbu'ichi na yara Fara tinaɗǝ fatǝrmbanda.
1CO 14:5 Yahkisi natuni kǝ shununi tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝn, ɓureɗi yahtǝ kǝ mbu'uni ichi na yara Fara. Le la mbukǝ ichi na yara Fara, sheraɗa le la shuwunkǝ tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝn, ma mbwi yunǝ hanngalǝ i mbutǝn, kana tinandǝ fatǝrmbanda.
1CO 14:6 Nakǝnya hwanmancha, ma ɓeɗi mbǝskuni nja shundǝ tǝ hanshuwuncha, mǝ natna chekanda kuni ma mbwa'awi hangngalǝ shuwunkǝna kuniwa, ndu sǝnda, ndu ichi na yara Fara, ndu sakandaɗi?
1CO 14:7 Nakǝn kichu tǝ ichi nguchit shishingtǝsa fechengnanda, nda kǝla'a tǝ ǝnat pecha, ma chu ɓurechengnanda kish ɗiichinwa, wun na sǝn i nat ficha futa tǝ i nat ficha peta?
1CO 14:8 Ma pyawu fichǝ kutmetǝ keeke tǝ i nat ficha sǝndǝwa, wun na sǝhatǝfǝ kǝ mbata?
1CO 14:9 Nakǝn kichu mbǝɗengnuni, ma shununi tǝ hanshuni mbǝsauchit ficha, nakficha sǝn i mbutuniwa kǝni? Shuwunkuniyu mere pǝɗakna hur rǝnna'a.
1CO 14:10 Michisi somsomǝna hur kisshita, chika yen miya tǝ sakǝtkǝnsi.
1CO 14:11 Ma sǝnwi sakǝt mikǝnwa, naki nat kǝ roma mbǝɗa lǝ shuwunkǝn, lǝ shuwunkǝn paɗ nakǝn kǝ roma mbǝɗengna.
1CO 14:12 Nakǝn kichu mbǝɗengnuni, nakuni tǝ ɓwechit hura a ɗar mbǝs fǝr Shemeɗchi somsomǝn, fǝram alchiɗengnuni kǝ suni tor tǝ fǝr Shemeɗǝ na tinandǝ fatǝrmbanda.
1CO 14:13 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn, chikawun na shundǝ tǝ hanshundǝ somsomǝn kǝ hwanǝn kǝ fǝrang fichǝ mba sǝn i mbutǝn.
1CO 14:14 Kǝthlǝm ma hweni tǝ hanshundǝ somǝn, shemeɗengnǝ hwanka, paɗ yarengnǝ cheku tǝ ǝnwa.
1CO 14:15 Mǝnati sǝta? Ni hwandǝ tǝ shemeɗengna, ni hwandǝ tǝ yarengnǝ paɗ. Ni ǝn'imshi tǝ shemeɗengna, ni i'ndǝ tǝ yarengnǝ paɗ.
1CO 14:16 Manga kichuuwa, masa sǝt usoko tǝ shemeɗeku, tǝ kǝni le naka kuthlǝmata mbǝsauchik hanshuniniyu ndatwa: "Kǝ sokǝn kichu wa kǝnǝ." Kǝ ɗar usoko tǝ natu sǝta, ma sǝnutǝ i natu mbutǝwa?
1CO 14:17 Chika sokkǝnwa shiɗi usoko kaǝn, ǝnsǝ chekandǝna le nak nduk tǝsǝ le sǝnuchikwa.
1CO 14:18 Saɗi Farǝ usoko sheraɗi kuni tǝ shundǝ tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝn.
1CO 14:19 Chika kichu, a hur kǝtǝn hwanda kweshikǝn kǝ mbu'i ichi ɗurman tǝ hanndǝkiketengna kǝthlǝm kǝ sakayi funǝhar mǝni mbu ichi aru kumchitkum (10,000) tǝ hanshundǝ somsomǝn.
1CO 14:20 Hwanmancha, malamǝn yarǝ'ichǝ nda hwecha. Kǝnuni hwecha a hur ɓǝɓichitfata, kǝnuni pǝktecha hur yarengnuni.
1CO 14:21 A hur kus yara fichǝhiwa: "Tǝ mbǝɗa nofcha fa hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝn paɗ tǝ miya romcha nati shundǝ tǝ nofchiya, chika tǝkichu ngunda kithlǝmatwa, ndat Lǝmwanda."
1CO 14:22 Awi shundǝ tǝ hanshuwuncha nakndǝ kǝ sakǝtkǝn nga kǝ mbǝɗa fa fǝrkitwa kǝ mbǝɗa fa ɓahfǝrkit. Mbu yara Fara i fafǝrkit nga i fa ɓahfǝrkitwa.
1CO 14:23 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn ma hwim fatǝrmbandǝhi, kana chikawunna nata shundǝ tǝ hanshuwunchi somsomǝn, nakǝn funǝsǝ mbǝsaundǝ i nat ficha sǝtwa, ndu funǝ fa ɓahfǝrkit yimkǝsi, ngunda ndatwa nga nakuni hur'inchǝwa?
1CO 14:24 Ma chikawuna mbu yari Farǝ na sǝtta, kana lǝ ɓahfǝrkit ndu yunǝ roma yimtǝsi le sǝnuchik i nat ficha sǝtta, ɓak shunda chikawuna tǝka harfa a kakǝn tǝrtǝhi.
1CO 14:25 Naficha chaɗǝ ɓuɓwee ichi kissha hanɗǝkiketǝ'enyu, tǝ kichu hǝmkǝnhi mwanaǝn Fara ndakǝnwa: "Kittǝkǝn Fara hurnuni."
1CO 14:26 Mǝ natma mbuta hwanmancha? Ma hwimunihi yuna imshǝ'ensi i mwanandǝ Fara, yunǝ sakandaɗi, yunǝ mbu'icha, yunǝ shundǝ tǝ hanshundǝ somsomǝn, yuna fǝr hanngalǝ shunda. Sam ichǝnat kǝthlǝm tinandǝ fafǝrkit.
1CO 14:27 Mana yuna shundǝ tǝ hanshundǝ somsomǝn, mǝ sheraɗa nifǝ chap ndu mǝkkanwa, kǝ sǝndǝ ɗeɗerra paɗ yunǝ kǝ fǝrǝn hanngalǝ shuwunkǝn.
1CO 14:28 Manga yunǝsǝ na fǝr hanngalǝ shuwunkǝnwa, chikawun kǝ ngasǝn ɓa'a hur fatǝrmbakǝn, kǝ shunaǝn fat'en tǝ Fara.
1CO 14:29 Tapǝnechǝ chap ndu mǝkkan kǝ shuwunnda, tahchikǝn kǝ kikeɗangndǝ hǝɓakkǝ i mbutǝnda.
1CO 14:30 Ma yunǝsa mbǝnniyu ɗas ɓat sǝn'ichikǝna mbǝt'en, le naka shunda tǝrkakǝnyu kǝ ngasǝn ɓa.
1CO 14:31 Natuni nuni mbǝla mbu ichi na yara Fara ǝrtǝ ǝrta, kǝthlǝm kǝ sak chikawuni paɗ kǝ mbǝs chikawun alchita,
1CO 14:32 Tapǝnecha la mbǝllakǝndǝ hǝrǝm inchengnandǝ har.
1CO 14:33 Fara nga Farǝ la shekɗandǝ i'ndǝwa, i yuyurchita. Nakǝn kichu mbǝɗa fatǝrmbaɗǝ chiɗchiɗ,
1CO 14:34 kǝ ngas nishchǝ ɓa a hur kǝtǝn hwacha. Kǝthlǝm fǝrau fichǝ mbanda kandǝ kǝ shuwunndǝwa, kǝ kuwurndǝ ndak nda i mbutǝ kus.
1CO 14:35 Ma ǝnsǝ yahtǝnda sahta, kǝ sahhangndǝ hishchǝngnanda huri. Kǝthlǝm ǝnat harǝfata kǝ shuwun nuhnifa a hur kǝtǝn hwanda.
1CO 14:36 Tǝrkaakǝ shunda Fara ɓat tǝ mbǝɗengnuniwa, ndu kunang ndak sa'andǝn?
1CO 14:37 Mala yarkǝ yunǝwa tapǝnaa nakǝn, ndu le mbǝskǝ fǝrta shemeɗa, kǝ sǝnǝnwa ichi nati yaranda kunisǝya mbuta Lǝmwanda.
1CO 14:38 Ma cher yunǝ mbǝnnifiyu, mǝlan ma kǝ cherunindǝfa.
1CO 14:39 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn hwanmancha, namtǝ ɓweechit hur mbu ichi na yara Fara paɗ mǝ malaɗuni shundǝ tǝ hanshuwunchǝ somsomǝnwa.
1CO 14:40 Kǝ suni chikama a mbayi kamkǝsi, paɗ a hur tahhasǝkǝn.
1CO 15:1 Nakǝnya, hwanmancha, ni kuɗkanda kuni kwescha shuni ɓassandi kuniyu, le thlǝtuni thlartuni ɗarkǝn.
1CO 15:2 Tǝ mbǝɗa kwescha shuwunkǝn hǝrǝktuni, ma kisshuni shunihar mbwa'andǝ kuni kwaakwaa. Manga kichuuwa fǝrkit engnuni mere.
1CO 15:3 I kamkǝsi sǝnandi kunisi, ndǝkǝn naka i thlǝta, ndatwa: "Kǝrǝsti mǝrkǝnaɗi kǝthlǝm ɓǝɓichitfechengnǝm, nda i natna hur yarat laulawata Farǝ le mbutǝn,
1CO 15:4 ndatwa thloha ficha, farǝ mun mǝkkatǝkǝn thla'aficha, nda i natna hur yarat laulawatkǝn,
1CO 15:5 cheɗaɗǝ fat'ena Kefas kana fichile kumngǝrǝnsǝ chapyu.
1CO 15:6 Kana cheɗa fat'ena hwanmancha fichile sheranga aru ɗurman (500) a farǝ ǝrta, mweefunǝsi tǝ shisshingtafa, chikama sokkǝn funa mirnda.
1CO 15:7 Kana cheɗa fat'ena Yakubu, tǝ tahhǝt fathlǝnchǝkǝn nat.
1CO 15:8 A mweshitkǝn nat, cheɗikǝn fata, nda le ngǝttǝ ficha a fari kamuchiksǝ.
1CO 15:9 Kǝthlǝm njang naka mweshitmiya fathlǝncha, kamuchiksǝ kǝ afichǝwa lǝthlǝnda, kǝthlǝm fǝraɗi ɓahta fa tǝrmbanda Fara.
1CO 15:10 Tǝ mbǝɗa kafata Fara nati kǝ i natiya, kafat'en kǝ mbǝɗengna nga merewa. Shiɗi tor sheraɗi chikawuna hurnanda, chikama sokkǝn nga njangwa, kafaɗi Farǝ nak tǝ njiyu.
1CO 15:11 Ndu njang ndu kaɗang, ɓasskani kichuyu, tǝ kichuyu paɗ fǝrtuni kit.
1CO 15:12 Ma ficha ɓassǝ thlata Kǝrǝsti a hur mǝmatcha, mǝsǝk la ndat funengnuniwa thlata mǝmatchǝsǝwa?
1CO 15:13 Ma nga thlata mǝmatchǝsǝwa, sokkǝn chika Kǝrǝsti thla'awu fichǝwa.
1CO 15:14 Ma thlaawu fichǝ Kǝrǝstiwa, ɓassengnani pofǝn, fǝrkitchiɗengnuni pofǝn.
1CO 15:15 Ma tana nakǝn kichu, shiɗani fa lekta Fara, kǝthlǝm shiɗani sheta kǝ ɗar Farǝwa thla'aɗǝ Kǝrǝsti hur mǝmatcha, le thla'awuchitǝn, ma tǝ kitwa thla'awu fichǝ mǝmatchǝwa.
1CO 15:16 Kǝthlǝm ma thla'awu fichǝ mǝmatchǝwa, sokkǝn Kǝrǝsti ma thla'awu fichǝwa.
1CO 15:17 Ma sokkǝn thla'awu fichǝ Kǝrǝstiwa, fǝrkitchiɗengnuni pofǝn paɗ paaya mwakuni hur ɓǝɓichitfechengnuni.
1CO 15:18 Sokkǝn fichile fǝrkǝkitta hur Kǝrǝsti, kannda mǝrtaɗi thlǝrǝtkǝndaɗi.
1CO 15:19 Ma ɗǝfǝm hanɗǝkiketengnǝm kǝ Kǝrǝsti kǝthlǝm naɗihiya ɗeng, sheraɗima chikawun kǝ ǝnat haɗandǝ nifǝfa.
1CO 15:20 Kitchitkǝn thla'afichǝ Kǝrǝsti a hur mǝmatcha, mǝlan naka tǝrka thlata fichile mǝrkaɗi.
1CO 15:21 Nakǝn ɓak murtǝ tǝ mbǝɗa nifa ǝrta, tǝ mbǝɗa nifǝ ǝrta paɗ ɓat thlata mǝmatcha.
1CO 15:22 Nda i nat ficha mǝmattǝ kǝthlǝm Adamu, kichu paɗ kǝthlǝm Kǝrǝsti nat ficha thla'andǝ nofchǝ nat.
1CO 15:23 Nak thlakǝna nata ndera chikawun tǝ witǝ ikǝn, Kǝrǝsti na nata tǝrkakǝn, kana fichile naka ikǝn a fari natna ngǝrandǝ'in.
1CO 15:24 Kana mweshitmikǝna ɓata, fari natna fǝra kuturǝchita Fara Shinda, ɗifitǝ wuwwelandǝ fa kuturǝchitaɗi, nat tǝ kuturcha tǝ alchita.
1CO 15:25 Waat nan sok kuturǝchita, kana ɗǝf atikrechikǝn kǝ ka sarǝchi'en.
1CO 15:26 Hanmurtǝ naka mweshitmi atikretǝkǝn ti natna ɓǝllanda.
1CO 15:27 "Kǝthlǝm shiɗtǝ ichinat kǝ ka sarǝchi'en" Ma ɗeɗfichǝwa: "Shiɗtǝ ichinat kǝ ka sarǝchi'en", cheɗakissha ɗwaachitkǝnwa nga nat tǝ Farǝ tǝ indǝ'enwa, le ɗǝfkǝ chikamǝnat kǝ ka Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 15:28 Kǝ ngǝrandǝ Farǝ ichiniyu kǝ ka sarǝchi'en, hwankǝn paɗ sokkǝna ka Fara, kana Fara nata chikamǝ tǝ tǝmǝ nat.
1CO 15:29 Manga thlata mǝmatchǝsǝwa, mǝnat nofchiya sǝta, fichile sandǝ fichǝ baptisma kanda kǝthlǝm mǝmatcha? Ma thla'awu fichǝ mǝmatchǝwa kǝpware, kǝthlǝmmǝ la sandǝ fichǝ baptisma nofchǝ kǝthlǝm kandang?
1CO 15:30 Kǝthlǝmmǝ la natma ɗǝf inchengnǝma hur mboro chikayen hanthlǝkta?
1CO 15:31 Wembǝta nja miya hanmurta! Yarkiyaa hwanmancha, kittǝkǝn la thla'ayi'indǝ kǝthlǝm kunang hur Yǝso Kǝrǝsti Lǝmwaɗengnǝm.
1CO 15:32 Ma mbeɗi tǝ pǝktat hanthlucha a Afisa, kǝthlǝm yarengnǝ kǝ ɗar nifa, mǝ naka mbǝstengnǝhar? Mangu ficha thla'andǝ mǝmatchǝwa, "Nga kwesh kǝ sǝmǝm kǝ sǝmwa nakǝn ishki nǝma mǝrta?"
1CO 15:33 Mǝ lǝmi fichǝ kuniwa: "Soktǝ tǝ ɓǝɓinofcha la sǝɓaǝn ka hur'indaɗi."
1CO 15:34 Ɓamaɗi kǝ hur'inchengnuni ndiichin, kǝ malanguni sǝt ɓǝɓichitfata. Kǝthlǝm funengnuni sǝnundǝ Farǝwa. Mbuki iniyu kǝthlǝm kǝ harangfat kuni.
1CO 15:35 Paɗ funǝ nanda sahtǝ ndatwa: "La thla'ang fichǝ mǝmatchǝwa kǝni? Tǝ witǝ fatmǝ natnda ɓata?"
1CO 15:36 Ɓoma! I hǝftu ngu tiftǝwa se ma mirwa.
1CO 15:37 Ma hifna, nga cheta i hǝftu tǝ fatkǝn na tiftǝwa, hanwitǝkǝn ndak. Ndu i alkama ndu hanwitǝ ǝn somǝn.
1CO 15:38 Farǝ la fǝrang fata hanwitǝkǝn nda i yahtǝn, paɗ chika witǝ hanwitǝmi la fǝraǝn fatkǝn'en.
1CO 15:39 Nga nat thlu ǝrtǝwa, nofchǝ tǝ witǝ thlǝwengnanda ǝrta, ɗǝhǝrǝmchǝ tǝ witǝ innanda, ɗishchǝ tǝ witǝ innanda, tinchǝ paɗ tǝ witǝ innanda.
1CO 15:40 Tinɗǝsi i afshi neɗsǝ paɗ i kisshita, mwanda i afshi somǝn, mwanda i kisshitǝ paɗ somǝn.
1CO 15:41 Mwanda hwatfarǝ somǝn, i ndǝraa somǝn, i hanndǝrechǝ somǝn; kǝthlǝm yunǝ hanndǝraa somǝn mwandǝ'en tǝ le.
1CO 15:42 Nakǝn kichu tǝ pathlǝ thlata mǝmatcha. I hǝftǝ ficha nan yirataɗi, i thla'andǝ ficha yirat'ensaɗǝwa.
1CO 15:43 La hǝfkǝ ficha tǝ ɓah fǝr mwanda, thla'ang ficha hur mwanda. La hǝfkǝ ficha hur ɓah alchita, thla'ang ficha hur alchita.
1CO 15:44 Hǝfkǝ ficha hur cheta fata, thla'ang ficha hur fata shemeɗa. Nakǝn fatsǝ i cheta fata, fatsǝ paɗ i shemeɗa.
1CO 15:45 Nakǝn kichu hur yaratkǝn, "Adamu tǝrka nifa sokka nifǝ tǝ shisshingtafa, ndukwalat Adamu shemeɗa lela fǝrkǝ shisshingta.
1CO 15:46 Nga le naka i shemeɗ naka tǝrkakǝnwa, i punifǝchita, kana i shemeɗa.
1CO 15:47 Tǝrka nifa chekna hur furta a hur kisshita, chapatǝ nifa ɓakna hur afshi
1CO 15:48 Nda ini chet nifa hur furtuyu, nakǝn kichuyu tǝ fichile naka i furta. Nda i'ni nat leni hur afshiyu, kichu paɗ natna nata kǝ fichile naka i hur afshi.
1CO 15:49 Nda i'ni tǝrtǝm mirshingta leni cheka hur furtuyu, kichu paɗ natma tǝr mirshingta le naka hur afshi.
1CO 15:50 I nati mbwa'anda kuni, hwanmancha, ngusǝtta faɗengnǝm nda thlu tǝ fwara kǝ yimnda kuturǝchita Farǝwa. Kichu paɗ lǝ yirata ngu mbǝs ǝna a ratǝ le nguchika yiratwa.
1CO 15:51 Kamthlǝmathi, ni mbwa'a ǝna kuni ɓuɓweeta. Ngǝma mǝrtǝ natǝmwa, natǝm naficha ɓuɓweɗandǝkǝmhi,
1CO 15:52 Nda nakǝnya a tǝɓǝrta hwanitǝhi, a mweshitmi kutmeta. Naficha pyandǝ kutmeta, thla'ang fichǝ mǝmatcha tǝ faɗi nguchika yirata, kana ficha ɓuɓweɗandǝ kǝmhi.
1CO 15:53 Kǝthlǝm faɗi na yirata waat kǝ ɓuɓweɗang fichǝhi tǝle nguchika yirata, lela mǝrkǝ paɗ kǝ ɓuɓweɗang fichǝ tǝle nguchika mǝrta.
1CO 15:54 Le na yirata ma ɓuɓweɗa fichǝhi tǝle nguchika yirata, le na mǝrta kǝ ɓuɓweɗang fichǝ tǝle nguchika mǝrta, a mbǝnniyu nat i yarandǝ fichǝhi hur shunda Farǝ nan nǝhhatǝhi ndatwa: "Mǝhɗafichǝ hanmurta, shera ficha al'en."
1CO 15:55 "Ai hanmurta, mbǝs'ǝnekuhara ayi? Ai hanmurta, alchiɗeku ayi?"
1CO 15:56 Alchita hanmurta ɓǝɓichitfata, kus naka alchita ɓǝɓichitfata.
1CO 15:57 Usoko Fara le fǝrang mbǝs'ǝna kǝmhar tǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwaɗengnǝm Yǝso Kǝrǝsti.
1CO 15:58 Kǝthlǝm ndǝkǝn hwanmanchinǝ ti yahti, thlaramhi kit, mǝ fohha ǝnkuniɗiwa. Kǝnding kǝ fǝrunǝ fechengnuni nat kǝ tora Lǝmwanda, kǝthlǝm shinuniwa ɓahtengnunihi hur Lǝmwanda ngu nat pofǝnwa.
1CO 16:1 Nakǝnya pathlǝ kǝsaanda fichilesǝ nak chiɗchiɗ, sam nda i ndaɗi mbǝt ngǝlhwanichi a Galatiyayu.
1CO 16:2 A farǝ ladi, tǝrka chika yen mundǝ muɗ, chikawuni kǝla ɗǝfǝn hanndǝɓǝltǝhi kǝlar hur i la mbǝlaatǝn mbǝsta kǝ kǝsǝnhar, kǝthlǝm ma ɓeɗi mǝni hum'icha natsǝwa.
1CO 16:3 Ma she'i ni thlǝn fichile hartunihar, ngǝmtuni tǝkanda, tǝ yarat ɗelwer kǝ ɗǝndǝ tǝ fǝrpofǝn engnuni kǝ Urshelima.
1CO 16:4 Ma sokkǝnwa keekesi njang paɗ kǝ ɗi, natnda ɗǝfkǝɗǝnji.
1CO 16:5 Ni ɓata mbǝɗengnuni ma ɗiɗi tǝ Makidoniya, kǝthlǝm yahkisi kǝ ɗi tǝ Makidoniya.
1CO 16:6 Mbah kǝ si tolla mbǝɗengnuni, mbahya ma kǝ mbǝrayi fektǝhi mbǝnniyu, kǝthlǝm kǝ kǝsikunisi nat mbǝɗi nati ɗǝta.
1CO 16:7 Nga yahtengna kǝnikuni nakǝnya kǝ mbǝrihi ndakwa, ɗǝfi hanndǝkiketǝsi kǝ muni tolla mbǝɗengnuni, ma ngǝma Lǝmwandǝ.
1CO 16:8 Paɗ ni thlarǝhi a Afisa kǝ farǝ Pentekos,
1CO 16:9 Kǝthlǝm i'ni fichǝ mikǝnndǝsǝ hauyang i tor nat tǝ mbǝs'ǝnsi chika sokkǝn atikrechisǝ kaǝn.
1CO 16:10 Ma ɓeɗ Timoti, kǝ ngǝmangnguni kǝ kalǝn fathi hurnuni, kǝthlǝm mǝlan ma na sǝt tora Lǝmwandǝ nda i nati sǝtta.
1CO 16:11 Mǝ cherinduni thlǝtndǝwa, kǝ kǝsangngunisa hur witǝ'en yuyur, kǝthlǝm kǝ ngǝraǝn i'na mbǝɗengna, nja kǝlata mba ɓat'en tǝ hwanmancha.
1CO 16:12 Nakǝnya pathlǝ hwanmanǝm Afolos paɗ, hwanaɗi tǝ alchitafa kǝ ɗǝka mbǝɗengnuni tǝ tahhǝt hwanmancha, nakǝn nga yahtǝ'en kǝ ɗǝn nakǝnyawa. Nan ɗǝta ma mbish tǝ mbanda.
1CO 16:13 Sokam tǝ tahhasǝfa, kǝ thlaruni kit tǝ alchita a hur fǝrkitengnuni, kǝnuni nda hishcha, kǝnuni tǝ alchitafa.
1CO 16:14 I natuni sǝtnat kǝ suni hur mbǝnfata.
1CO 16:15 Hwanmancha, shinuni nofchi hura'a Istifanus kanda tǝrkakǝ tǝrtǝhi a hur hachahai Akaya, paɗ firndǝ fechengnanda kǝ sangndǝ tora fichile nak chiɗchiɗ.
1CO 16:16 Nja hwanandǝ kuni kǝ fǝranguni mwanda witǝ nofchiniyu, tǝ fichile naka shikechǝ torchengnani tǝ ɓahtengnani.
1CO 16:17 Shiki mbǝndǝfǝ tǝ ɓata Istifanus, tǝ Fartunatus, tǝ Akaikus, le sokkǝ nda kunang ɓaka.
1CO 16:18 Tǝrandǝ hurengnǝhi nat tǝ innuni. Witǝ nofchiniyu kǝla fǝranguni mwanda kanda.
1CO 16:19 Fa tǝrmbayi Asiyayu kanda nda'icha kuni. Akila tǝ Biriskila tǝ fa tǝrmbayi la humkǝhi hure'engnandǝyu, kanda nda'icha kuni kaǝn hur thlǝm Lǝmwanda.
1CO 16:20 Hwanmanchi natta mbǝnniyu kanda nda'ǝna kuni. Kǝ ndangnguni icha ndani tǝ chiɗchiɗ tǝ kǝsndanihar.
1CO 16:21 Njang Bulus yarak ndat'ǝnaɗiya tǝ harengna.
1CO 16:22 Ma yunǝsǝ nguchit mbǝnfat'ensi kǝ mbǝɗa Lǝmwanda, kǝnaka sǝɓkǝn. Lǝ Lǝmwada a ɓu.
1CO 16:23 Kafata Lǝmwandǝ Yǝso kǝnan tǝ kuni.
1CO 16:24 Malan mbǝnfaɗengna kǝnan tǝ kuni natuni hur Yǝso Kǝrǝsti. Kǝsokǝn kichu.
